/ /rang gi rnam par thar pa yul sna tshogs kyi bdud rtsi myong ba'i gtam du byas pa zol zog rdzun gyis ma bslad pa sgeg mo'i me long zhes bya ba bzhugs so/ /

/ /gsung snyan mgrin pa'i 'gyur khugs thos pa'i mod/ /zab gsal thugs kyi gsang ba mtshon nus pa/ /dbyangs can lha mos snying dbus padma'i khrir/ /rnam dpyod 'dab stong ze'u
kha phye mdzod/ /'dir chags khyod zhal zla 'od dmar ba'i 'dzum/ /'char ka zla shel dwangs par 'gran bzod pa/ /yid mkhar dran na srid zhi'i dpal ster ba/ /rnam gsum rtsa
ba'i bla ma 'dir spyon zhig /lha ngag dbang nyid kyi rjes bzung ba/ /yul 'dzin mar nyi ma ltar grags shing / /yid tsha gdung zla ba ltar bsil ba/ /skyabs bzang po bla mas
bdag skyongs shig /dbang bzhi ldan srad bus sbrel ba yi/ /rgyud rnams bshad nor bu'i 'phreng ba mdzes/ /rang mgrin par sbyin byed dge ba'i bshes/ /kun dga' byed mchog ldan
sa 'dir rgyal/ /g.yo zog rdzun dang 'ur gyis ma slad par/ /rang nyid brel bas

phar 'gro tshul 'gro'i gtam/ /chos ldan sbyin bdag dad sun mi 'byin phyir/ /mgyogs par bris la bla ma mkha' 'gros bzod/ /gang gzhan dad 'dun nyi zer gyis spros pas/ /bdag blo
ku mud zum pa ma bzod nas/ /rang snang so 'phreng ze'u 'bru gtsigs 'di la/ /ma dad mun rum khrel yang ga zha'i gnas/ /zhes mchod brjod dam bca' sngon du btang nas rang
gi lo rgyus ji ltar 'tshams pa sgro skur spangs nas cung zad brjod na/ byang phyogs gser gyi las byed mtho ba'i rigs/ /cho rigs rnam dpyod gtsang ba'i gzhon nu mched/ /zang
zang 'brong zhes ri thang mdzes pa'i cha/ /rkang 'thung do ra 'khrigs der skyes so lo/ /de yang 'di skad thos te kho bo'i rigs ni/ byang phyogs chos rgyal rim par byon
pa'i rigs ldan gang / /de dag gi gser 'don pa'i gser dpon zhes pa'i las byed khrom rigs mang po'i dpon du skos pa'i gser dpon gyi thog ma gser dpon lha mo skyabs/ de'i
sras gser dpon lha mo mgon/ de'i sras gser dpon lha mo don grub/ de'i sras pho lnga/ mo lnga ste bcu'i skyes

phran dpa' bo'i chas su zhugs pa'i gser dpon lha mo 'phan chen/ lha mo 'phan chung / gser dpon lha mo lnga dar te gser dpon spun gsum zhes byang phyi 'brog na grags pa thob
pa gsum du grags/ yang slob dpon chos skyong bsam 'grub dang / nyams rtogs ldan pa bzang po bkra shis zhes bya ba/ gos ser po'i rtags can bka' brgyud bstan pa'i sgor zhugs
pa/ rtogs ldan gyi rgyal po gtsang dbus gnyis sogs kyi zhabs zung bsten pas nyams rtogs 'gran zla ma mchis pa'i rnal 'byor pa chen po gnyis te/ sras pho lnga'i tha chung
gser dpon lha mo lnga dar la/ snga bu lnga dang / phyi bu gcig ste drug byung ba'i snga bu che ba de gzhon nu nas gshegs/ de yang ma des byang thang gi rang byung chu
tshan zhig la byon pas/ chu tshan gyi logs shig na lha bshos gtsang ma lnga rog ge 'dug pas gcig g.yog mo zhig la byin/ bzhi rang gis gsol bas de lta bu'i rten 'brel gyi
yin zhes gtam du grags/ snga bu 'tsho zhing gzhes pa bzhi'i che ba gser dpon lha mo gnyer ma/ de nas bi ri tshe dbang lhun grub/ de nas gser dpon lha phrug /de nas chung
ba klu rgyal nor bu zhes bod pa ni bdag go /phyi bu ma mi gcig pa khri tshang dkar rgyal/ de yang pha ni lha mo lnga dar/ ma sems ma rgyal 'dzom/ ma ma ayon bzang mo zhes
bya/ skye ba'i gnas ni/ zang zang chu byang brgyud kyi lung pa 'brong zhes bya ba/ nyin ri thams cad spa shugs la sogs pa 'khri shing sngo ljang grib ma snum zhing brjid
pa/ srib ri thamasacad spang rtsi sngo ljang gos su gyon pa/ gzhung thams cad chu klung dal gyis 'bab pa'i 'gram na ne gsing sngo ljang gi ral pa bun long nge bar khyab
pa/ de'i nang tshan gyi lung pa kha nub phyogs bde ba can la phyogs pa shel ltar dwangs bas 'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba shel lung zhes bya ba'i gnas su chu mo lug lo la kho
bo skyes so zer/ de yang rang nyid ma'i mngal

du chags pa'i tshe ma'i rmi lam du/ sbrul dkar po chung ngu mal du zhugs pa rmi/ de'i mtshan la yang dpags te/ rang gi khu bo rnal 'byor pa chen po des kyang klu rgyal nor
bu zhes btags/ phyis rab tu byung ba'i tshe kho bo'i mkhan po lcags thang pa chen pos kyang / khyod kyi ming gi zur gyi klu de chad na mi yong ba 'dug pas/ klu sgrub rgya
mtsho gyis shig ces bka' stsal bas/ skye ba kun tu klu'i ming dang ldan pa zhig dgos pa'i rten 'brel lung bstan pa yin nam snyam/ pha ma ne zla phu nu mched sogs dang /
/'khor g.yog nor phyugs rnam mang thos bu'i dpal/ /hor sog mon bod dgra yis 'tshe med par/ /bde skyong 'brog sde'i phun tshogs de yang myong / /bgrang gzhi bcu gnyis gzhon
nu'i rol rtsed tshe'ang / /rgyan po ri dwags 'tshe sogs kun spangs nas/ /'phongs skyen rtsed 'jor dga' yang chos kyi blos/ /lcog gra glegs bam khur dang 'bral ma myong
/ /bcu gsum lon tshe chos sgor zhugs kyi brdar/ /'chi med me lhas rang byung gtsug phud bzhes/ /de tshe pha dang ne zla mched rnams kyis/ /chos kyi skal pa yod ces gnang
ba stsal/ /zhes pa ste/ gser dpon spun gsum du grags pa des/ stod sogs rA ma Na'i g.yul ngo yang lan gsum du bzlog pas/ rang lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du hor sog bod sogs kyis
'tshe ba med cing bde ldan du 'tsho zhing gzhon nu rol rtsed kyi tshe yang / sho dang mig mang sogs la mi chags par 'phongs rtsod rtse ba la dga' zhing / rang gi pha khus
kyang ru thag 'then pa'i khul na 'phongs skyen zhing dpa' rtsal 'dzom pa'i grangs su bgrang pas/ pha'i 'phongs skyen pa lta bu yong zhes gtam du gleng yang / de'i tshe
rang nyid chos kyi 'dun pa la sha chags pas rtsed mo'i tshe yang / gnas

khang lcog bu dang / glegs bam chung ngu dngos sam/ tha na g.yam pa srab po la glegs bam bcos nas 'chang ba dang khur ba sogs byed/ kho bo la a jo bi ri zer bas/ pod chung
dkyus la khyid gang / zheng la sor gsum tsam yod pa zhig byin pa de 'bral med byed kyin yod pa la skabs shig rtsed mos g.yengs nas de bor ba tsal yang ma rnyed par ngu zhing
bsdad pas/ a jo che bas gser 'od kyi po ti zhig gdong du bskyur nas khyod la dpe cha dgos na de gyis zer na'ang blo kha ma tshim zhing mchi ma gtong gin yun ring bsdad
pas/ chos kyi bag chags cung zad sad par sems so/ /yang nged la mchod gnas bon chos gnyis yod pas/ lan cig khong gnyis chos gtam byas pas/ bon chos kyi kha 'dzin la ma
'cham par 'khrug pa byas/ nged kyi phas khyed gnyis mchod gnas byed du bcug pa la/ 'khrug pa byed dran na zer mda' gzhu bkug nas ded/ nged kyi mas pha bzung / mchod gnas
gnyis ri la shor zhag gcig 'khor ma thebs zer/ bgegs srung mched gnas chos dbon rnam pa gnyis/ /chos bon kha 'dzin kha brdal lag 'khrug byas/ /pha rgan thugs 'khrug mda'
gzhu'i 'phrul 'khor bcings/ /a mas ma bzod pha yi sked nas bzung / /chos bon zung de snying sdangs ri la shor/ /bon chos rtsod pa'i zar zir ri la yal/ /phyin chad chos gtam
rtsod pa'i zhi byed la/ /chos las 'phongs skyen 'phrul 'khor ngom pa bzang / /nged kyi ma de rang skyes nas nad kyi stabs kyis nu ma 'thung rgyu cher ma byung / deng sang
lus rid pa des lan zer/ ma des bu tsha 'di 'tsho na chos la 'jug zer ba zhig yod zer/ de nas chos la 'jug pa'i sad byed kyi rkyen ni/ dkar gur yangs po zhig gi dbus su
mchod

pa/ dkar mes g.yon phyogs su pha dang / g.yas su nged spun bzhi rim pa bzhin nyal bas/ dkar me dang nged thag ring yang / nged kyi spyi gtsug skra la dkar me lhab 'bar ba phas
mthong nas/ bu tsha 'di skra gcod pa 'thad par 'dug zer bas nye ba'i rkyen de kho nas byas par snang ngo / /chos kyi 'khor lo'i sgra dbyangs sgrog pa'i gnas/ /ngur smrig
dge 'dun 'du ba'i chos grwa cher/ /tshe rabs 'phreng bar brtse bas bskyangs pa'i mgon/ /'jam mgon phyogs las rnam rgyal de na bzhugs/ /chos grwa de mthong yongs 'dzin
de mjal tshe/ /ri byi'i gur khang mkha' la shar ba bzhin/ /gzung 'dzin rnyog ma'i dri ma rtsad nas bkrus/ /snying la rab dga'i 'od snang de tshe shar/ /zhes pa ste/ bcu
gsum pa lug lo'i ston/ nged spun bzhi char gyis bod la yongs gcung mdo spe chos sder zla ba bzhi tsam bsdad/ de phyogs kyi dgon gnas so sor rten mjal ngo mtshar gyi ltad
mo sna tshogs bltas/ de nas a jo spun gsum 'brog la thegs song / nged la gtsigs shin tu che ba yod kyang / rang chos byed bsam pa'i blo khong du bcangs pas/ khong spun gsum
thegs pa dang mi zug pa sogs sdug bsngal med par de gar bsdad/ de nas dpyid shar ba'i tshe chos 'khor gling nas 'jam mgon bla mas/ rgyal sras thugs rje dpal zer ba'i grwa
pa gnyis rta dang bcas pa'i bdag bsu ba la btang byung bas/ rang dang na mnyam pa'i 'brog phrug gcig dang bcas phyin pas/ dgon pa der sleb pa na khang phran thams cad
zho spungs pa ltar dka' ba/ sgo logs thams cad sa khra'i 'byed sna tshogs byas pa/ phyi nang thams cad grwa pas dmar mer khengs pa 'dra ba de mthong ba tsam gyis/

sngon chad yong ma myong ba'i sems la dga' bde dang / lus kyi ba spu ldang ba/ gzung 'dzin gyi rtog pa rags pa 'gags pa'i gnyis med kyi sems gsal le ba'i ngang du 'dzin med
du cham song ba 'dra ba brjod mi shes pa dang / nang du 'jam mgon bla ma dang mjal ba'i tshe yang sngar mdza' gcugs kyi gnyen dang 'phrad pa bzhin du/ zhal mthong ba tsam
gyis sems la dga' ba dang thugs brtse bas rjes su 'dzin pa 'bral mi phod pa lta bu byung / mtshan nyal ba'i nying 'khrul rmi lam na/ /rang dog mo'i g.yang la lhung snyam
tshe/ /rje bla mas spyi bo'i gtsug nas drangs/ /khong tshe rabs yongs 'dzin yin par nges/ /de nas skra gcod pa dang gos bsgyur ba sogs byas/ da khyod rab byung byed dgos
te/ mkhan slob dbus gtsang na grags che ba zhig gi drung du btang dgos gsung/ bcu bzhi pa sprel lo bshad gsar gyi gzhung 'dzin dang / sa gzhung ngo sprod sbyor ba sogs
kyi 'go btsugs/ sngar bshad gsar lo re dgos pa la phyis lo phyed re dgos pa zhig 'dug kyang / shin tu dam dog che ba 'tsher cha che ba rang nas/ bshad gsar 'di thongs na
gzhan slob gnyer las sla ba 'dra snyam pa shar/ lo de'i dgun chos steng du bshad gsar ba lnga bcu skor byung / nged snga ldang ba yin pa la/ las chen bkras bzang zer ba sogs
sgrob chen bzhi 'dug pa la/ phyi gzhung / phyogs chos de rjes khyab pa yi/ /gtan tshigs zhes pa'i gzhung bskyur byung bas/ kho bo tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi snga gzhung
phyi gzhung kun zin yod kyang / snga gzhung ma gtogs gzhan sbrel ba med mod/ sa gzhung sbyor ba sogs gra skor pa gzhan gyi sna chags tsam la brten nas rang sems gtad thub
'jigs pa med par bde sim me ba'i ngang nas gzhung de ka blangs sa

gzhung sbrel sbyor 'god gtsang sing ba byas pas/ gzhung bskyur ba'i tshe las chen rnams gre sug ling nge ba la/ kho bos sbyor 'god grub mtshams las chen rnams dbu gug pa dang
/ zhal 'dzum bag dang ldan par gyur to/ /de yang 'phrin las cung zad khyab che ba tsam yong pa'i rten 'brel yin nam snyam phyis shar ro/ /de nas rang lo bco lnga pa sa
mo bya mnyan yod bya gshongs btab nas lo drug cu skor gcig song ba'i tshe/ dbus gtsang yongs na grags pa'i dpal mnyan yod bya rgod gshongs zhes yongs su grags pa'i grwa
sa chen po de nyid du mkhan po'i mchog kun mkhyen lcags thang rab 'byams pa byams pa bsod nams dpal bzang po zhes snyan grags phyogs kyi rna ba'i rgyan du gyur pa des/ lo
grangs nyi shu rtsa bdun 'chad nyan mdzad/ blo gsal gyi slob bu grangs med bskrun par mdzad de/ bstan pa'i bya ba mthar phyin pa mdzad rjes dgung lo drug cu rtsa bzhi pa
la/ paN grub bzang po bkra shis gdan sar bskos pa'i lo 'jam dbyangs bla mas bdag la grogs bsod nams dpal 'byor dang / dge 'dun seng ge zhes bya ba gnyis dang bcas slob gnyer
la rdzong bar mdzad/ blo bde gong kar sleb tsam nas dgon pa khra phung nge ba g.yu thog dang bcas pa zhig mthong byung bas bo dong e pha gi na byas pas/ grogs gnyis
na re/ bo dong e min/ e dang bya gshongs la da dung thag ring zer/ de nas la chung der sleb la khad du bud med gos khra mo gyon pa zhig dang phrad/ bya gshongs gang na yod
byas pas/ la chung 'di'i phag na yod/ myur du sleb pa yod pas mgyogs se rgyug zer/ dga' ru tshor ba byung / dmag zor ma'i sprul pa yin pa 'dug zer ba'i 'ud byas kyang chog
pa tsam 'dug

/de nas la 'gar sleb tsa na/ lcang shol smug thib se ba'i gseb na dgon pa khra phung nge ba g.yu thog dang bcas pa/ zur dril sil chom me ba mthong bas/ rab tu dga' ba chen
po sngar dang cha 'dra ba byung / de nas grwa tshang gi gling du sleb pa dang / grwa pa rnams dga' ba'i glu len bro 'khrab cing 'dug / kun mkhyen lcags thang pa chen po gling
du spyan drangs byung bas/ rang yang dad pa skyes shing kun mkhyen chen po thugs shin tu dges/ ming la ci zer gsung / klu rgyal nor bu zer zhus pas cung zad zhal 'dzum
pa dang bcas pas/ khyod kyi ming zur gyi klu de chad pas mi yong ba 'dug /da khyed yon tan che ba 'dod dam/ grags pa che ba 'dod gsung rang 'dod zhu ma spobs pa la yon
tan che ba 'dod na klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ grags pa che ba 'dod na klu sgrub rgyal mtshan zer dgos te/ yon tan yod na grags pa lhun grub yin pas klu sgrub rgya mtsho gyis
gsung / de yang 'das ma 'ongs su klu'i ming can cig yin pa'i mngon mkhyen du 'dug /gsang ba'i lung bstan cig yin zer ba'i 'ud byas kyang rdzun du mi 'gro las che/ de'i sang
nyin mkhan po lcags thang chos rje/ slob dpon paN chen bzang bkras/ zhu ba po grib tshod dang bcas pa'i dge 'dun gyi dbus su rab tu byung / ming mang thos klu sgrub rgya
mtsho gyis gsung / de'i nub gcig gi rmi lam na kun mkhyen chen po chos khri chen mo'i steng na bzhugs/ grwa pa rnams byin chos grwa nas langs 'gro ba tsam 'dug /kho bo
la shog gsung chos khri'i mdun du phyin pas/ zhabs chen mo 'jad de ba de spyi bor bzhag /de'i steng du chos 'chad 'phro'i bseg ka li chen mo bzhag nas smon lam mang po 'debs
pa gnang gin 'dug /kho bo dga' spro dang dad pas mchi ma mang po shor/ da khyed lo bcu gnyis las sdod long mi 'dug go gsung

de nas bdag gang du 'gro ba gda' zhus pas/ de nas gang du 'gro nga la rgyus med do gsung gin 'dug /gnyid sad nas brtags pas phyis gdan sa'i rten 'brel sgrigs pa yin nam snyam/
ma 'ongs pa na gdan sa'i lung bstan yin zer ba'i 'ud byas kyang chog pa tsam 'dug /kho bo bya gshongs su slob gnyer la ni lo hril bo brgyad dgu tsam las ma bsdad/ gdan
sar khyi lo nas khyi lo'i bar lo ngo bcu gsum/ hril po bcu gnyis song 'dug pas/ lo bcu gnyis las sdod dbang mi 'dug gsung ba de/ de tsam lhag pa gdan sar bsdad na mi yong
ba'i rten 'brel zhig gzigs pa yin par nges so/ /dbus gtsang yongs grags mkhas pa'i grwa sa cher/ /lo skor gcig tu legs bshad 'doms pa'i khur/ /de tsam gyis kyang blo gsal
mig 'byed pa'i/ /ma 'ongs lung bstan yin snyam nges pa rnyed/ /de nas dgun chos dang po grol ba tshun bsdad/ slar ngam ring dgun chos la sleb/ khyi lo de la kun mkhyen
chen po ngam ring mkhan por gdan phebs/ kho bo dang nag tshang brgya phrug kun bkras gnyis tshogs chen du rigs lung la slang / kun mkhyen chen po thugs dgyes te/ de 'phral
shog gsung khong spobs pa mtho ste khyed yon tan che ba 'dug go gsung / rang lo bcu bdun pa phag lo kun mkhyen chen po la gsar lung bas sbyin bdag byas te/ dpyid chos
chen mo bteg /de'i dus chos rje chos dpal mgon po'i tsho 'og la kho bo yang yod pas/ dam bca' 'jog gin yod pa la kun mkhyen chen po tsho rnams la zhabs skor dang gzigs rtog
gnang ba'i tshe/ gser dpon gyi chos mdzad de/ da lta nas dge bshes chen por gyur 'dug ces gsung zer ro/ /nged

chos gling pa 'ga' dang bcas pa la bka' gdams lha bzhi'i rjes gnang mdzad/ khyed la 'jam dbyangs kyi sku zhig ster bar byas pa de 'di yin gsungs nas/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sku legs
po zhig gnang / bya gshongs su khyed 'jam dbyangs kyi sku dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi sku gnyis gang 'dam gsungs/ spyan ras gzigs 'dam zhus/ phyis 'jam dbyangs gnang pas
de dus 'jam dbyangs 'dam zer dgos rgyur snang / lan cig khyed la lcags thang rab 'byams pa'i sku zhig byin gyis gsungs nas/ rje rang gi sku 'dra gos thang zhig gnang /
nang gcig kho bo tho rangs kyi rmi lam na shar phyogs nas nyi ma yud kyis yong gin 'dug pa de zla ba la thim song / nyi zla 'dres pa des snang ba gsal du 'gro'am snyam pa
la cung mi gsal du song / skar ma khra chil mthong ba tsam byung / 'jam mgon bla ma la zhus pas bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu la lod par 'dug gsungs te/ byi ba'i lo kun mkhyen
lcags thang pa chen po dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pa de la lta bar 'dug /de'i tshe rang lo bco brgyad pa yin/ rang lo nyi shu lon gyi bar du 'jam mgon bla mas chos gling
du legs bshad kyi chos char 'bebs pa'i bdud rtsi myangs/ rnam rigs la gtso bor sbyangs/ rnam 'grel le'u bzhi la zin bris kyi shog bu phyed gsum brgya tsam yod/ 'jam mgon
bla ma shin tu mnyes te/ khyed la dus gsum khegs pa'i yon tan zhig yong ba 'dug gsung / de skabs shig chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes/ byams chos sde lnga 'dzin
sbyong gi 'go btsugs/ byams chos pa sum brgya tsam dpal ldan sa skyar byams chos kyi gra skor la btang / de'i zla la bdag kyang yod/ zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga la byams chos
lnga

zin kyang / byang ba dkar se byung bas/ sgrub lung zer ba'i dben gnas shin tu byams chos lnga sbyong dar la mtshams byas/ sngar 'brog phrug gi tshe sha dmar po mang po mthong
bas rkyen byas 'jigs skrag gi brgyal 'gro ba lta bu dang / brjod mi shes pa'i nyams snang sna tshogs 'char ba zhig yod pa la/ 'brog pa rnams kyi sha dmar po nang la khur
yongs tsa na nged la sbed dgos pa zhig yod zer/ mtshams kyi skabs de nas gnyid kyi rmi lam na sngar gyi snang ba de 'dra shar ba la 'jigs pa'i snang ba med par bde cham
'gro ba dang / dag ma dag gi yul snang lta ba'i 'dun pas/ dga' ldan du byams mgon mjal ba la 'gro snyam tsa na steng phyogs la ling ling 'phur/ lte 'og nas rtsa'i sbubs
nas rlung hu ru ru zhugs/ spyi gtsug tu sleb pa dang / rnam shes mthon 'gro ba snyam byed pa dang spyi gtsug tu rlung khyil li li cung zad 'khyil nas nyams sad yong ba de
'dra byung / de man rmi lam du nyams snang de 'dra rgyun chags la yong ba zhig byung / rmi lam nying 'khrul dag pa'i 'od gsal dang / dag dang ma dag yul snang lta ba sogs/
/sngon gyi las 'phro sad pa las byung ltar/ /rten 'brel sgyu ma'i rol rtsed ngo mtshar gnas/ /yang de lta bu'i skabs shig na/ grogs btsun chung drung skyabs zer ba zhig
dang gnyes chos gling dgon pa'i ltag ri sgang zhig tu/ slob gnyer byed sa brag phug brus pas re zhig nas glegs bam chung ngu zhig thon byung bas/ grogs de na re/ 'di khyed
kyi yin zer bas/ ngas kyang yin byas blangs nas bltas pas birWa pa dang gong ma lnga'i bstod pa par ma khra gsal le 'dug pas/ rje btsun gong ma'i byin rlabs 'jug pa'i
rten 'brel gyi thog ma yin snyam sems dga' ba tshad med pa skyes so/ /rang byung brag phug

brus tshe gong ma lnga'i/ /gsung rab glegs bam yid bzang gis byin bzhin/ /lag tu babs tshe sa skya'i bstan pa la/ /bya ba gyis zhes lung bstan yin nam snyam/ /yang lo bcu bdun
pa'i skabs shig /kho bo chos 'khor gling gi brang khang bde ldan zer ba zhig na nyal ba'i dus shig na tho rangs tshe na/ nged rang gi ma ma ayon bzang mo zer ba zhig
yod pa de yin no snyam pa'i bud med smug 'jol le ba zhig byung nas/ nged shAkya thub pa dang rgyun du mjal gyi yod na'ang khyed la sngar ma bstan/ da ltos shig zer bas mdun
gyi nam mkhar 'ja' gur gyi dkyil na bstan pa'i gtso bo sku gser gtso ma lta bu zhabs rdo rje skyil krung / phyag sa gnon mnyam gzhag mdzad pa/ zhal 'dzum bag dang ldan
pa/ sku bdos bcas ma yin par nam mkha' la 'ja' shar ba lta bu 'od zer ser po 'phro ba 'od kyi gur khang nang du lam mer mthong bas/ yid dga' ba spro ba dpag tu med pa skyes/
phyag 'tshal gsol ba btab pa'i snang ba shar ba zhig byung / de sangs tsa na sngas mgo mchi mas bangs 'dug pa zhig mthong / de tshe ston mchog zas gtsang sras po des
tshe rabs thog ma nas rjes su bzung zhing slar yang byin gyis rlob pa'i ngo mtshar gyi rtags yin nam snyam pa shar/ mkha' la 'ja' bzhin zas gtsang sras kyi sku/ /mngon sum
mthong tshe gzung 'dzin 'khrul snang nub/ /glo bur dri bral chos dbyings zla tshes gzugs/ /gsar du mthong snyam rang snang mthol lo bshags/ /de nas 'jam mgon bla ma dgung
lo so brgyad pa stag lo mnyan yod bya rgod gshongs kyi gdan seng ge'i khri la zhabs sen bkod/ bya lo'i bar lo grangs brgyad du rgyan drug mchog gnyis kyi gzhung lugs
chen po la legs bshad spel ba'i tshe bdag gis kyang gsung gi bdud rtsi

myangs/ sngar chos gling du phar phyin gyi sgrigs sog tsam byas kyang / zur bkor bzhi la dmigs rnams 'char ba dka' se byung / bya gshongs pa rang gi lugs la/ phar phyin gyi
gzhung shing shes kyang zur bkol mi shes na/ phar phyin mi shes pa'i grangs su 'dren pa zhig 'dug pas/ zur bkol la lta rtog nan tan byas pas/ zur bkol bzhi sogs kyi gnad
phyin ci ma log par khong du chud/ zur bkol mngon pa'i khri la bzhugs zer ba yin pas/ mngon pa gong 'og dang / sher phyin thun mong ma yin pa'i dmigs rnams gsal por phyed/
gzhan zur bkol shes zer khengs pa byed pa rnams kyang phyogs re tsam la spu khengs yin pa 'dra snyam pa shar/ skabs der kho bo ni shing rta'i srol 'byed gnyis kyi gzhung
lugs la shes 'dod chen po yod kyang / mngon pa mdzod dang 'dul ba 'di tsho/ theg dman gyi chos skad du 'dug pas mkho byed che rgyu rang med ba 'dra snyam pa zhig byung
/ khyad par sngar chos gling slob dpon pa/ mkhas pa chen po dge 'dun rgya 'tsho zhes pa phar tshad gnyis la ston bzangs su byed cing / gzhan stong phyogs la thugs yus po
gnang ba zhig la/ byams chos kyi gzhung TIka mang du nyan zhing / g.yas ru byang gi chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje yang gzhan stong gi bdag por byed pas de rnams
kyi blos sna khrid nas/ gzhan stong phyogs la shin tu dad mos che ba zhig byung / bya gshongs bla brang na bzhugs pa'i mdo sde de rnams zhib par ltas kyang gzhan stong
dang / byams chos kyi gsal byed du gang 'gro'i lung tshol ba dang / yi ger 'dri ba sogs kho na byas/ klu sgrub phyogs la shin tu mos kyang klu sgrub kyi dgongs pa'ang gzhan
stong du gnas snyam pa rlom tshod kyis dkrugs nas/ klu sgrub lugs

kyi lta ba thun mong ma yin pa la nges pa gtan nas ma rnyed par lam me zhig las ma byung / kho bo cag bza' btung dang / chos spyod sogs skabs gang du'ang gzhung lugs kyi don
la thos bsam gyi rtog dpyod rgyun ma chad par yong ba zhig yod pas/ ngam ring chos sder 'tshog pa'i skabs shig gung gral du ja 'thung ba'i skabs bsam mno gtong gin yod
tsa na/ yod snyam pa rtag lta dang / med snyam pa chad lta yin zer ba sogs kyi yom yom de 'dra ma yin par klu sgrub gzhung nas bshad pa'i rtag chad kyi lta ba dang / rtag
chad kyi lta ba las grol ba'i mtha' dang mthar 'dzin 'gog tshul la nges pa gting nas rnyed pa byung / thogs med kyi dgongs pa dang sbyar na/ gzhan stong yin byas kyang chog
pa tsam 'dug kyang / klu sgrub lugs kyi gzhung lugs la bsam gzh-ig bcug pas klu sgrub lugs la bden grub khas blangs na/ rtag chad kyi lta ba'i rtsa ba rang du go nas
sngar rang gi lta zhen wal wal thams cad chu bur bzhin du zhig nas mtha' bral dbu ma'i lta ba la 'phrog med kyi nges pa rnyed pa de man chad nas byung / spyir srol 'byed
rnam gnyis kyang gcig gis cig shos lta ba la skur pa 'debs pa kho na byung 'dug pas/ rjes 'jug mkhas pa rnams kyang dbu cung zad 'khor/ chal chol mang du smra ba dang byams
chos lnga ka'i lta ba sems tsam du gnas zer ba dang / dbu ma rang stong du gnas zer ba dang / rgyan dang rgyud bla'i dgongs pa dbu ma thal 'gyur du gnas zer ba dang /
phal mo che dag byams chos thog mtha' gnyis dbu ma rang stong dang / bar pa gsum sems tsam du gnas zer ba sogs cal col dang 'ar 'ur mang du sgrogs pa zhig 'dug kyang / kho
bo'i rnam dpyod kyis gzhigs pas rgyud bla ma'i dgongs pa yang sems

tsam du gnas par mthong nas/ sgrub byed lung rigs 'jam mgon bla ma'i rtogs brjod dpal gyi 'khri shing dang / klu sgrub stod 'grel du gsal bar bkod zin pa de yin no/ /'di la
rnam dpyod dang bral zhing thugs gzu bor mi gnas pa dag gi dpyod yul min pas smra ba skyungs na rang bzhin bzang mdog rnam pa yin la/ rgyan dang rgyud bla thal 'gyur lugs
su bsre ba ni/ srol 'byed so so'i dgongs don so sor 'byed ma shes par rnam dpyod phyang mo yug tu shor ba la mchor chas su ngom pa tsam du snang ste/ kho bos dpal gyi 'khri
shing du rnam dbye phye zin pa la gzigs shig /chos rgyan drug gi gzhung la sbyong dar byas/ /khong paN grub tsho'i dgongs don ma 'dres phyed/ /rang thos bsam byas pa
don yod byung / /nga sgom zhig byed snyam snying la gcags/ /de skabs shig 'jam mgon bla mas/ khyod 'dul mdzod la rtsol ba zhan par 'dug kyang de ltar byas pas mi yong pas/
'di gnyis la thos bsam rus thon pa zhig gyis gsung gsol ja dang gzan legs pa zhig gnang / de phyin chad 'dul mdzod kyi gzhung bzung 'dul ba rgya cher 'grel dang / mdzod
rang 'grel 'grel bshad dang bcas pa legs par ltas/ 'grel pa mkho che ba 'dra bzung thos bsam phul phyin byas pas phyis 'dul mdzod gnyis la rnam dbye legs par shar/ khyad
par mdzod rtsa 'grel la thag chod kyi spobs pa rnyog pa med pa shar ba yin no/ /yang gdong dga' nas chos mdzad spe gsar pa zer ba rnam dpyod kyi shes rab dang spobs pa
bzang thag chod pa zhig yod pa des/ kho bo la snyan ngag legs legs mang po dang / rigs gter gyi/ ldog 'gog chos rtags phyags gnyis kyi/ /rtsod pa bzhi yi gzhan lan

'khrul/ /zhes pa'i gzhung 'di'i rtsod pa bzhi ngos 'dzin dang / gzhan lan 'khrul tshul dang / rang lan 'debs pa ji ltar byed ces pa'i dri ba legs po zhig bskur byung bas/ kho
bos kyang snyan ngag blo la gang shar dang dri lan blo nus gang yod byas bskur bas spe gsar ba shin tu mgu nas khyed kyi 'di legs bshad rang du 'dug cing / sngar rang
gi gsung so so la cung zad 'gal 'du 'dug snyam pa'i gnad 'gag ma go ba'i dogs pa mang po la/ ma go ba brgya rtsa zer ba'i bstan bcos chung chung mang dag brtsams yod pa la
yang / khyed kyi de ma go ba brgya rtsa ru mi 'dug /legs bshad brgya rtsa rang du 'dug go zer byung / de nas kho bos kyang / rang gis mi shes 'dri na ha cang thal/ /rang
gi shes bzhin 'dri na gzhan la brnyas/ /the tshom nye bar zhi ba'i log rtog 'ga'/ /blo gsal khyod la 'dri yi lan smos shig /ces sogs dri ba mang po byas/ de nas bzung ste
rtsam rtsom la shin tu 'jug pa dang / rtsod pa yang gzhan la khyad gsod dang / sun 'byin gyi spobs pa ha cang mtho ba med kyang 'jigs pa dang zhum pa mi dgos par rang
gzhan grub mtha'i gnad khong du chud pas/ rang gi khas blangs tshugs thub pa dang / gzhan gyi khas blangs 'gog pa'i gnad phyin ci ma log par zin pas/ rtsod zla thugs gzu
bor gnas pa rnams kyang khyed dang bgro gleng byas pas blo skyed mi yong ba mi srid pa 'dug zer ba kho na byung / de dus chos 'chad 'dod kyi bsam pa ye med par gsung rab
kyi don la thos bsam gyi go ba phyin ci ma log pa chags phyin/ rang gi khu bo rnams kyang bka' brgyud kyi nyams len pa kho na yin pas/ 'chi ba la 'tsher med kyi bka' brgyud
kyi grar zhugs pa'i sgom rnam dag cig byed snyam pa de ga rgyun chags

la yod/ 'on kyang rang gzhon nu nas sa paNDi ta'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis ba spu g.yo ba'i dga' spro byung ba dang/ slob gnyer gyi tshe yang tho rangs snga mo nas bshar sbyangs
byas/ nam langs la khad la gnyid cung zad log pa na yang rmi lam rang zin la 'byung zhing / rmi lam dran pa gsum gyi nang tshan bla ma dran pa'i thog mar sa paN chen
dran pa 'byung zhing / shar mngon dgar sa paN mjal ba la 'gro snyam pa'i yul snang 'char ba zhig rgyun chags la yong gin yod pas/ bya gshongs la yong gong chos rgyal ma
dang / sgrol ma ston zhing grogs med pa dang / grogs bcas kyi sgo nas slob gnyer sha stag byed pa dang / sgom sha stag byed pa gang dga' zhes brtag pa lan gsum tsam byas
'dug kyang / slob gnyer kho na bzang ba'i lung bstan byung 'dug go /'chad rtsod rtsom la blo gros mi zhan kyang / /mi rtag 'chi ba dran pas rgyud bskul nas/ dben pa'i ri
khrod 'grim par sha chags kyang / /thos bsam chos grar 'khor 'di mkha' 'gro'i lung / /rang lo nyer drug pa sbrel lo nged dpon slob gnyis char gyis ri khrod chen po jo nang
du 'jam mgon kun dga' grol mchog drung du bka' chos zhu bar phebs pa tho rangs gnas tshang na yong ba'i tshe mi mang po ngu tshi theg pa 'dug /mi gces shi ba yin snyam
sems skyo ba zhig byung / jo nang pa rang gi chos lugs sbyor drug nyams 'ur gyi lugs de yin zer bar 'dug /de nas smin drug zla ba'i yar ngo'i tshes brgyad la rje btsun dam
pas dbang brgya'i gtso bo 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du smin byed kyi dbang thog ma thob/ gsang mtshan gyi tshe la lI ta badzra ste rol pa'i rdo rje
zhes bya ba'i 'di sa paNDita'i yang gsang mtshan yin no gsungs

'dogs pa gnang / de nas rnal 'byor ma'i sindhu ra'i byin rlabs/ rgyu sde lnga'i dbang / bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang / ni gu'i byin rlabs nyer lnga/ grub chen brgyad cu'i rjes
gnang / 'khrid brgya'i 'go brtsams 'khrid nyi shu tsam sogs dang / ni gu'i 'khrid srol mi gcig pa gsum sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbang lung byin rlabs gnang / kho bo
yang gnyag gser dpon gyi rigs yin la /rje dam pa yang gnyag gi rigs yin 'dug pas/ de'i dkar phyogs kyi kho bo la nye bo chos rje gsung zhing thugs gtsigs par mdzad/ khyed
gnyag pa la grub thob mang po byung / mkhas pa sngar byung ba med do gsung pa'i nyams ldan gsung / bdag gi bsam pa la grub thob mtshan nyid pa byung na mkhas pa don ldan
de ga yin snyam pa byung yang zhu ma spobs so/ /yang bdag lo nyi shu rtsa gsum lon pa'i skabs shig bo dong phyogs na 'brum pa 'dug pas bdag dpon chen byams pa blo gros
gnyis kyis 'brum 'dzem 'dar du zla ba gnyis tsam skyid gshongs dang ru spe gnyis su bsdad/ de'i tshe sdom gsum rab dbye sogs gzhung mang po 'dzin sbyong smar bar byung /
de snga rje tshar chen dang mjal ma myong / chos rje tshar pa zer ba de rta zhon ber gyon khyi khrid pa'i bla ma sgrob can zhig ma gtogs slob ma 'khrid pa'i bshes gnyen dam
pa zhig e yin nam bsam pa byung / dus gcig gi tshe rje bla ma de tsha lung skyid mo gshongs su spyan drangs pa'i tshe kho bos kyang mjal/ de'i dus mdo phyogs la dri ba
mang po gnang byung ba la bdag gis kyang lan rim pa bzhin phul bas shin tu dgyes/ khyed la dris pa'i thad la bshad rgyu 'dug /gzhan 'di tsho la dris pa'i don la bshad rgyu
med par ma dris pa'i sar phyam phyam 'phro ba zhig yong gin

'dug gsung / kho bo yang bla ma la dad pa tshad med pa skyes/ de nas skyed gshongs pa rnams 'dar grang chen du rje bla ma la dbang zhu ba la 'gro ba'i zla la kho bos kyang
phyin/ tshe dbang grub rgyal ma dang / sna tshogs yum gyi dbang rjes gnang thob pas dga' ba dang spro ba ci yang skyes/ bdag kyang dpal ldan sa skya'i chos 'dra zhu 'dod
yod pas rjes su gzung dgos zhus pas/ nga yis mthu min pa gzhan mi shes/ khyed mthu ni mi slob bam gsung / bdag gis mthu dang mthu min pa yang slob zhus pas zhal 'dzum bag
dang ldan par gyur 'dug go /de dus nyid nas thugs rje'i spyan ras kyis 'tsho ba'i rten 'brel gyi thog ma yin par shes so/ /de nas 'jam mgon bla mas dgung lo zhe lnga pa/
bdag gi nyer bdun lon pa bya lo dbyar chos gnyis pa la 'jam dbyangs bla mas bya gshongs kyi gdan sa 'jam mgon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la gtad nas/ khyi phag byi ba'i lo
gsum dben pa bsten nas thugs dam mdzad pa dang / gsung ngag sogs gsan pa yin la/ de skabs su yang kho bos 'jam mgon bla ma'i zhabs pad bsten pa yin te/ de yang 'jam mgon
bla mas gdan sa bkod pa'i gong dbyar chos dang po la kho bo rogs gsum dang bcas 'dar la log yongs pas/ don grub gling gi lcang ra'i 'gram der sleb tsa na byis pa mang po
paNDi ta sleb byung zer dir dir 'dug pa na zha lu bu ston la'ang de 'dra byung ba'i tshe/ byis pa'i kha la g.yang yod zer ba yin pas rten 'brel bzang gsung pa rnam thar
na 'dug pas/ byis pa tsho rten 'brel bzang po zhes nged rnams bzhad gad byed kyin phyin/ de nas khyi lo de la nged kyis 'jam mgon bla ma la bya gshongs su ni chos 'chad nyan

dang / chos gzhis 'gro smon can sogs dang bya gshongs rnying pa jo bo/ rnam sras lha khang / chos gzhis grong g.yog dang bcas pa sogs bya gshongs su thes shin tu che ba byung
/ da sngags chos shig gsan na dga' ba 'dra zhus pas/ kho bo ni sngar thob pa'i chos la nyams len byung na de gas chog thob thob mang po mi dgos/ khyed rang shes 'dod chen
po 'dug pas thog mar rje dpal 'bar rgyal mtshan drung du ni gu zhig zhu ba la phyin chog gsung/ khyi lo'i ston nged dpon slob gnyis dbon chen byams pa blo gros dpon po
'gar lung pa dang bzhi grogs dang bcas pas ra sa mtshal khung du mkhas grub dpal 'bar rgyal mtshan gyi drung du byon zla ba gnyis tsam bzhugs thog mar bde mchog lha lnga'i
dbang / rgyud sde lnga'i dbang / sgyu lus dbang mo che tsam gnang phyag chen ga'u ma'i 'khrid/ ni gu'i 'khrid rnam nyams 'khrid du bskyangs mdor na rtsa ba phyag rgya
chen po/ sdong po ni gu chos drug /yal ga lam 'khyer rnam gsum/ 'bras bu 'chi med 'phyug med/ me tog mkha' spyod dkar dmar sogs dbang bka' nyams 'khrid lung 'khrid/ bla
ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi lung sogs dpe lung gi rigs rnams dang / 'khrul 'khor lus sbyong nyi shu pa/ 'chi med 'khrul 'khor so gnyis rnams phyag len ltar 'phyug med du
sbyangs/ de rjes ma gcig zhus te thog mar mkha' 'gro sde lnga'i dbang / de rjes ma gcig zab don lugs kyi nyams 'khrid lung sogs cha lag tshang ma/ rgod phrug lugs kyi ma
'khrid chen mor grags pa/ 'ba' ra ba'i spyod yul gdan thog gcig ma/ 'bar ra ba'i mal gcod gdon chen bco brgyad ma sogs dang / do ha'i skor la/ do ha'i lo rgyus/ bshad lugs/
gdams lugs

dmangs do'i rnam 'grel chen mo/ do ha mdzod drug gi lung sogs dang / gzhan yang rgya gar gsang gcod chung ba/ rgwa lo'i gtum mo zhag bdun ma/ phyag chen yi ge bzhi pa/ lnga
ldan/ ro snyoms sgang dril sogs dang / khyad par rje mar pa'i snyan gyi shog dril bzhi/ de bzhi'i nang tshan rtsa rlung dra mig 'khor lo'i 'khrul 'khor bco lnga sogs lag
len la thebs par sbyangs pas/ bla ma de yang bka' drin che ba yin/ kho bo slob gnyer gyi tshe nyin mo gnyid log kyang rmi lam rang zin la yong bas mtshan mo lta ci smos
shar kyang mtshan mo'i dge sbyor rmi lam 'dzin pa las sla ba 'dug snyam pas/ mtshan mo nyal ba la spro sag ge ba zhig chung ngu nyid nas yod/ dmigs pa'i sgo nas rmi lam 'dzin
pa la/ ni gu las kyang lam 'bras ngos dmigs pa rno ba tsam byung / ra sa mtshal zhes dben pa'i ri khrod nas/ /mkhas grub chos rje dpal 'bar mtshan can bzhugs/ /dwags
shangs bka' brgyud gdams pa'i nying khu thob/ /re zhig bde ba'i stegs bu ngal gso brtsams/ /rnal 'byor gos dkar gyon pa'i do ra ru/ /rlung dang gtum mo lus kyi 'khrul 'khor
sogs/ /rtsa yig thig le'i rnal 'byor nyams su myong / /dben gnas ri khrod 'grim snyam sag ge byung / /de nas dpon slob rnams kyi khyi phag byi ba'i lo gsum gyi ngo la
'dar gyi brag khung / rmu brag shod/ mu gu lung rnams su bzhugs/ de yang thog mar mang mkhar rmu'i lho nub phyogs kyi grog po gang phug gsum yod pa 'dzin spras mdzad/ logs
rnams rtsig pas gru bzhir bcad nas zhal ba byas/ mdun dang shod du me tog ldum ra dang 'khrul 'khor rdegs sogs legs par bcos pa'i gnas shin tu spro ba zhig yod pa der
shas cher

bzhugs/ thugs dam ngag 'don/ sems 'dzin rlung 'khrul 'khor bslab sbyong sogs shin tu 'phel bar byung / nang gcig khong dpon slob rnams gzhung la spyan drangs song / kho bos
gcig pur rlung bum pa can 'dzin zhing bsdad pas/ gad phug gi nang thams cad du 'tshub kyis khrig mer khengs byung / nag po tshang du go me mched snyam sked pa la gzan dkris
nas ltar phyin pas thab kha ni skam krog ge 'dug /tshur log nang du sleb tsa na'ang du 'tshub ma bsangs ba zhig byung ste phyi rol gyi du ba ma yin par nang nas 'od gsal
du ba lta bu'i nyam shar bar 'dug /de phyin chad nas rlung gzung res kyi 'od gsal du ba lta bu'i nyams de rgyun ma la 'char gyin 'dug /yang nang gcig rlung 'dzin gyin
yod tsa na rtsig logs na sa paN gyi sku thang phyag gnyis chos 'chad mdzad pa zhig bkram yod pas gzhan mi 'gul bar phyag chos 'chad kyi sor mo rnams gul gul byed kyin 'dug
/mig 'khrul ba yin nam snyam thang sku'i 'khris su bltas pas kyang re zhig sngar bzhin 'gul gyin 'dug /de rigs kyang rlung zin pa'i nyams yin par 'dug ste/ de phyin chad
de 'dra'i nyams tho re ba yong gin 'dug /ya ga chos sdings dang bya bshongs kyi tshoms ka bzhi mar rlung bzung ba'i tshe yang ka ba rnams 'deg cing khyom khyom byed pas
khang pa rdib 'gro ba snyam byed pa la 'jigs skrag med pa cig byung ste/ nyams de rigs smig rgyu'i nyams yin zer ba lam 'bras gzhung bshad na 'dug /yang phug pa der 'jam
dkar dang sgrol dkar gyi bsnyen pa byas pa'i tshe tho rangs shig lung pa kha byang ltas skya seng ba zhig tu phyin pas lung pa de'i nang thams cad me tog dkar po mda' tshad
tsam pas khrig mer khengs pa/ de'i phyogs gcig na me

tog utpal sngon po tshad snga ma bzhin la/ 'dab ma rnams sngar bas shed cung zad chung ba 'dra ba mthong / de'i tshe sems la dga' spro dpag med shar/ lha dkar po rnam gnyis
kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma cung zad yin nam snyam/ blo shes rab 'phel byed dkar po bzhi/ /thugs brtse bas rjes bzung 'jig rten dbang / /mgon mkhyen brtse 'bral
med tA ra ma/ /lha khyed kyis bskyangs 'di skal ba bzang / /lha padma dkar po'i spyan ras 'dzum/ /sems ngal 'tsho'i lung bstan gsung dbyangs snyan/ /tshe sngon nas thugs
rje'i lcags kyus sbrel/ /dus da lta bde ba khyed kyi drin/ /gnas der gzhan yang lha phran mang po'i bsnyen pa yang byas/ gzhung lugs mang po la shar sbyangs dang lta rtogs
'phel po byung / rlung 'khrul 'khor sogs kyang rtsol ba chen po byas pas/ 'od gsal gyi rtags dang nyams snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / /de nas mang mkhar rmu'i
brag shod zer ba der zla gcig tsam bzhugs pas/ sngar btsan thabs ye mi thebs pa la phyis rlung bum can gzung tsam gyi btsan thabs rang thebs la 'byung zhing lus la bde
ba dang / sems la 'char sgo sna tshogs 'char ba/ mtshan dus rmi lam rang zin dang gnyid log pa la brod pa skye ba sogs dge sbyor 'phel po byung ba yin/ de nas mu gu lung
du dpon slob gsum gyi zla gcig tsam bzhugs/ de dus kho bo la gzhung mang po blo la yod kyang sdom gsum rab dbye nyin re la tshar re chag med byas/ gzhan dbu ma 'jug pa/ byams
chos lnga/ mngon pa mdzod/ rigs pa drug cu pa/ chos dbyings bstod pa/ brgyad stong don bsdu/ nyi shu pa/ sum cu pa sogs skabs skabs su re mos kyis bton/

der yang rmi lam gyi yul snang rlung gi 'od gsal gyi rtags sogs rgyun ma chad pa de ga byung ngo / /de nas phag lo dgun bzang ldan du rje dam pas gsung ngag sogs chos 'khor
bskor rgyu yin pas khyed rang dpon slob shog gsung / gong ma nam mkha' rin chen gyi phyag rtags byung / nged dpon slob kyis kyang byon/ zla ba gsum gyi ring la tshogs pa
sum brgya tsam la lam 'bras snga chos 'phyi chos dang / bla ma slob dpon sogs cha lag sgrig mkhan sum cu tsam la zur du thun re mdzad/ mthar rje mkhan sogs bdun la cha lag
yongs su rdzogs pa gnang / mdor na dbang / byin rlabs/ lam skor dgu'i 'khrid lung sogs de dus las rgyas pa ma byung zhes grags/ rgyu dbang dngos gzhi'i nub rmi lam du
rje dam pa khri mthon po zhig na bzhugs/ lam 'bras pa gzhan rnams gyel 'gro yin 'dug /kho bo la rjes la sdod gsung nang mchod ka pA la nas bdud rtsi spar ba gang tsam gnang
byung bas/ sngar myong ma dran pa'i ro bcud phun sum tshogs pa myong / bla ma'i byin rlabs de nas zhugs snyam byung / de dus lam 'bras rdzogs pa bdun gyi nang tshan la
kho bo ma chud pas phyis mang ring sgo spe na rje dam pa bzhugs pa'i skabs/ kho bos sngar gyi lam 'bras kyi lhag ma rnams zhus pas thugs dgyes pa chen po dang bcas kho bo
cag gcig pu la ngam ring sgo spe'i steng khang du bdag med phyi nang gi dbang / brda chig brgyud/ gsang bcu'i rgyas 'debs/ sgrub pa lung sbyin sogs dpyid ra tshes bcu gnyis
la rdzogs par thob/ sgrub pa lung sbyin gnang ba'i tshe nam mkha' srib se ba zhig la 'brug gi skad 'ur ba zhig byung bas rje bla ma'i zhal nas rten 'brel bzang nga'i
nye po chos rje la 'phrin las dang snyan

grags chen po yong ba 'dug gsung / sku gzhogs na yod pa'i dpon drung 'phan dang / dge slong rin cen sogs kyang de ga mchis so rten 'brel legs zer ro/ /nag po spyod pa'i rnam
'phrul dam pa rjer/ /nyer brgyad lo la gsung ngag lam skor bcas/ /dbang 'khrid byin rlabs dpe lung ma tshang med/ /rdzogs par thob 'di skal ba bzang ngo snyam/ /de nas
nyer dgu pa byi ba'i lo 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse dang 'dab 'byor ba chos 'khor yang rtse'i bla brang du bka' drin mtshungs pa med pa 'dren mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i drung
gis/ nged dpon slob 'dar nas sku mdun chos rje/ chos kyi rje rab brtan dpal 'bar sogs lnga bcu skor la gsung ngag lam 'bras gnang / kho bos zin bris bgyis pa'i dpe rnams
spyan lam du gzigs phul bas shin tu thugs dgyes/ khyed la tshe rabs snga ma rnams su gsang sngags la sbyangs pa byas pa'i las 'phro bzang po zhig 'dug /gzhan tshe 'di
la sngar sbyangs pa chen po ma byas pas go ba 'di 'dra chags mi yong gsungs/ yang skabs shig zin bris 'dra 'bul du phyin pas shin tu dgyes/ nga'i lam 'bras slob bshad 'di
khyed min pa gzhan gyis ji lta ba bzhin mi go /snying po'i bcud bsdus pa tshi lu dang 'dra ba'i lam 'bras pa de khyed yin no gsung / mdor na rje bla ma des thog mar lam
'bras tshogs bshad tshar gcig de nas lam 'bras slob bshad bzabs bshad gnang / byin rlabs 'phro cung ma rdzogs pa 'dra 'jam mgon bla ma la zhu dgos pa byung ba yin no/ /mdor
na rje bla ma blo gsal rgya mtsho de la snga phyir shes rab bskyed pa'i lha dkar po rnam bzhi sogs rjes gnang

gi rigs shin tu mang ba/ rje bla mas bsgrigs pa'i be bum nang bzhin gyi dpe lung / de nas dmar po skor gsum/ dmar mo skor gsum/ dmar chung ma skor gsum sogs gser chos bcu gsum
gyi thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rjes gnang / dmar po skor gsum gyi po ti gsum gyi lung rje bla ma'i dkar chag nang bzhin dang / mgon po che chung gi rjes gnang
/ mgon chen gyi phyi nang gi 'khrid/ mgon pod me 'bar ma'i dpe lung rje bla ma'i dkar chag nang bzhin dang / gzhan yang nga'i mgon po'i man ngag 'di khyed snod ldan du
'dug pas rdzogs pa rang gcig byed do gsung bka' gnang phebs/ skabs shig kho bo la shog gsung khyed lam 'bras pa 'di rnams kyi nang nas lam 'bras 'chad mkhan gcig yong ba
'dug go gsung ba phebs te/ 'jam mgon bla ma dang / rje rab brtan pa gnyis kyis kyang lam 'bras gnang mod/ rje bla ma'i khri thog tu kho bo 'ba' zhig gis lam 'bras bshad
pas de tsam la dgongs sam snyam/ yang skabs shig mgon po khro bcu'i rjes gnang gnang pa'i nub mo/ bya rog snum stong ba bcu tsam gyis bdag la skor ba byed pa rmi/ srung skyob
byed pa'i rtags su go /byi lo de la chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes 'jam mgon bla ma blo gros rnam rgyal ngam ring chos sde'i rgyan du che ba 'dug pas chos
sde'i dbu mdzad dang / gra tshang gi gtsug rgyan yin pas ya ga chos sdings kyi 'dzin bdag la yong dgos gsung yang yang phebs pas de ga mdzad pa'i dgongs par 'dug /kho bo
cag sngar yin na srol 'byed gnyis sogs gzhung lugs chen po la yin min gyi 'gro ldog byed pa tsam byas/ rang gi khu bo gnyis kyang bka' brgyud pa yin pas/

bka' brgyud gong ma'i rnam thar la zhugs/ bka' brgyud kyi nyams len byas/ ri khrod 'grim pa'i rnal 'byor pa zhig byed bsam pa kho na yod kyang / rje tshar chen chos kyi rgyal
po la gsung ngag thob phyin 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa la phan pa zhig byed na dpal ldan sa skya pa'i chos lugs 'di kho na lhag
pa 'dug cing / khyad par nyams len cha tshang ba'i nyams len snying po chig dril byed nus na lam 'bras slob bshad 'di las lhag pa mi 'dug cing / gzhan rnams nyams len phyogs
re ba tsam du 'dug pas gzhan la 'gram chu mi ldang zhing ltos mi dgos par ri khrod 'grim thub pa'i chos 'di nyid yin snyam pa'i nges pa gting tshugs pa skyes/ chos
slob bshad snying la 'phos pa'i tshe/ /gzhan rtsab rtsob som nyi'i mdud pa grol/ /rje sa skya'i 'jam mgon brgyud pa las/ /skyabs gzhan na med do mched grogs rnams/ /de nas
bla ma'i gsung gis gseng 'di la gzhi bsnyen yud kyi btang na legs/ zla ba drug gdan thog gcig tu sdod pa 'di gnas gang dgar long mi yong zhing byed mi thub/ khyed rang
mtshan nyid pa rnams kyi gra skor thongs pa dang 'dra gsung pas bka' lung de ma 'ongs mkhyen pa'i mngon mkhyen du 'dug /de dus ma byas na bya gshongs bzhag nas gzhi bsnyen
byed zer ba las mi yong ba yod/ de tsa na lam 'bras 'chad thub pa yang dka' ba 'dug /de nas kho bos kyang bla ma'i gsung bzhin de ga byed zhus/ grang mo che'i grang khang
kun gyi yang rtse mthon po gcig tu mtshams bcad/ gzhan rogs gcig kyang med pa byas bla brang nas snga ja 'phyi ja re skyel ba gnang

gzhan spros pa ci yang med/ tshod ma yang rang gis skol/ mtshams zla ba bdun tsam song ste/ yab yum gnyis char gyi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg dang bcas pa grub mtshams de la 'gal
rkyen gyi tsher ma med cing mthun rkyen 'dzom pas blo bde sing nge ba mtshan dus rmi lam mi zin pa ci yang ma byung / rmi lam zin res kyi 'od gsal cung zad dang / dran pa
rnam gsum tur gyis byung dran pa'i tshe yang 'jam dbyangs bla ma dang sa paN mi dran pa mi srid/ dag ma dag gi yul snang lta ba sna tshogs 'byung / lan cig rgya gar rdo
rje gdan la 'gro snyam pa dang / nub phyogs la yud kyis 'phur rdo rje gdan yin snyam pa'i gtsug lag khang chen po zhig tu sleb/ rgya mthong gi thad na dril bu mang po zhig
dril gdang byas btags 'dug pa na dbus na nas phung zhig 'dug pa de nas nas gtor bas dril bu rnams la phog ste sel khrom zer ba'i sgra chem chem chen po zhig byung / lha'i
rnam pa gsal po ni mi dran yang lan cig rmi lam bzung nas byams mgon mjal ba la 'gro snyam tsa na nam mkha' la gyen du yud kyis 'phur song / dga' ldan du sleb snyam pas
lha dang lha mo sogs mang po mthong / byams mgon dang mjal snyam ste phyag btsal smon lam btab pa'i nyams snang shar ro/ /gzhan yang rmi lam nyams kyi snang ba la/ dran
pa rnam gsum 'byongs pa'i rnal 'byor pa/ /bar do'i grong khyer bcom zhes zhal lung yin/ /lus 'di mkha' spyod 'gro ba'i gtam 'di snyan/ /yang sa paN dang mjal du 'gro snyam
pa yang yang yong gin 'dug pa la lan cig shar phyogs la 'phur nas phyin pas/ lung pa yangs po shing rtsi nags tshal thib se ba na dgon pa skya chag ge ba zhig mthong
/

'di yang ma dag pa'i zhing yin pa 'dug/ shar phyogs mngon dga' yin snyam 'phur nas phyin pas ri med pa'i thang yangs po na khang ba gru bzhi pa zhig gi nang du sleb/ sa paN
yin snyam pa'i na bza' chos gos/ sa zhu bsnams pa zhig dang mjal/ de ga sa paN yin snyam nas phyag btsal na bza' la 'jus mchi ma shor nas mal khengs snyam pa zhig byung
/ yang lan gcig khang pa zhig gi nang du kye rdor gyi sgrub mchod byed pa'i nyams shig shar gzhan rogs ni mi 'dug kye rdor gyi dkyil thang bar snang na khra gsal le ba bkram
'dug pa zhig mthong / yang skabs shig rje dam pa bar snang na khri chen po zhig gi steng na bzhugs kho bo la bo dhi rtsi'i phyag 'phreng legs po zhig gnang byung bas
dga' spro shin tu che/ gzhan pa ru yin no snyam pa brjod mi shes pa zhig gnang ste dga' ba che yang de ni gang yin rngo ma thogs/ yang lan cig rje tshar chen chos kyi rgyal
po bir srung gnang du phebs pa yin zer/ lho phyogs kyi nam mkha' nas byang phyogs kyi nam mkha' la seng ge la chibs nas bir srung gi sngags 'don cing phebs pa zhig byung
/ kho bos bir srung gi byin rlabs nyan 'dod kyi rjes zlos byas gsol ba btab pa'i snang ba shar/ de'i tshe yang dngos mjal lta bu'i dad pa dang dga' spro dpag tu med pa
skyes so/ /yang lan cig gi tshe lho phyogs kyi nam mkha' na rnal 'byor dbang phyug bi rU pa sku'i cha lugs dang / zhabs kyi bzhugs stabs/ phyag gi rnam 'gyur sogs mi 'dra
ba dbu skra ral pa'i thor cog dang / lcang lo smug shig ge ba nam mkha' gang ba tsam zhig mthong / sems dga' ba dang spro

ba dpag tu med pa byung / 'di 'dra ba ri mo la bri thub na dga' ba snyam pa shar ro/ /yang skabs shig lce bde mo ma byung bar sems nong par yod pa la/ mtshan dus rmi lam zin
tsa na sngags 'dren pa'i 'dun pa byas pas/ sngags mgo oM zer ba byas tsa na sngags thams cad rang shugs kyi nar ra ra rgyun chags kyis rtsol bar ma ltos par thon song bas
sems dang sing nge ba zhig byung ngo / /yang lan gcig rmi lam zin 'bum phrag gsum pa'i sku mang po 'chos pa'i snang ba shar nas/ 'bum phrag gsum pa'i sku mang po par la
brkos te shog bu la btab nas shar phyogs kyi gyang logs shig la brgyab pa'i snang ba shar te/ phyis bya rgod gshongs kyi gdan sa byed pa'i rten 'brel gyi snga ltas su 'dug
go /mtshan dus nyid 'khrul bseng ba'i 'od gsal na/ /yul snang sna tshogs rnam bkra'i ri mo shar/ /ngo mtshar ltad mo sna tshogs de tshe mthong / /mtshan bsnyen mtha'
ru 'khyol snyam dga' ba skyes/ /dngos sam rmi lam nyams kyi snang ba la/ /phra rags 'char sgo bsam gyis mi khyab kyang / /phal cher dran lam mi gsal gsal na yang / /mangs
pas 'jigs phyir bkod kyang gad mo'i gnas/ /de nas dgyes rdor yab yum gyi bsnyen pa rdzogs/ de rjes kha skong bsnyen pa mdzad pa'i phyag srol gzhan la 'dug kyang rang lugs
la mi snang kha gso ba'i sbyin sreg gi tshe dbon rab 'byams pa blo gros mtshams nang na yod pas sbyin sreg gi rogs la bos/ thab thig dang thab kyi rdul tshon sogs drung
chen bzang pos bas byas/ gced mdes me sbor ba'i tshe gced ma de khur ba tsam gyi me tshang gi ong ba'i ras mde des/ gced mde'i me phrogs pa bzhin du me tshang

la me 'bar nas/ gced mde'i me de me khang la yal song ba mngon sum du byung bas rten 'brel ngo mtshar che snyam pa byung / kha skong sbyin sreg byas tshe me lha yis/ /me lce
rang 'bar bsreg rdzas bdud rtsi bzhes/ / 'gal rkyen sdig bsregs tshe dang bsod nams 'bar/ /'od gsal me lces ma rig mun bsal snyam/ /zhag drug bar la kha gso'i sbyin sreg
grub/ mtshan dus rmi lam 'od gsal char sgo'i ngang / /grangs dus mtshan bsnyen rab 'bring tha ma gsum/ /gdan thog gcig tu tshang ba'i drin dran nas/ /phyag 'tshal thugs
rjes gzigs shing blo gsal rje/ /mtshams la hab 'grol mi rung gsung pas zhag 'ga' ci bder gnas/ de nas rje bla ma dgyes bzhin du bla brang du shog gsung phyin pas de'i nyin
ngor pa'i zur 'chad pa chos rje sangs rgyas seng ge 'byon rgyu yin zer gdan gshom grub 'dug /de la phyag 'bul e dgos zhus pas/ ngor la 'byon 'dod yod na byas pas rung
/ gzhan mi dgos gsung nas ma byas/ de nas 'jam mgon bla ma yang byi lo dgun chos thog tu chos sde'i dbu mdzad dang / ya ga chos sdings pa'i phyag 'bul bzhes grub nas nged
kyi mtshams grol dang bstun 'dar du phebs/ rje bla ma yab sras mjal phrad gnang ba'i tshe rje bla ma rang las bzhugs gdan mtho ba bcas 'dug pa la/ 'jam dbyangs bla mas mi
bzhugs gsungs kyang rje'i drung de skad ma gsung / khyed mtho ba de gang mtho ba yin no gsung / de nas chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje'i kho bo la chos gling slob
dpon la shog gsung phyag rtags phebs/ 'gro 'dod med tshul zhus kyang bla ma yab sras kyis

g.yas ru byang ba 'di chos rgyal yin pas de'i gsung bzhin byed dgos gsungs nas/ bla ma yab sras kyi bka' ma chogs par rang lo sum cu pa byi lo'i mjug glang lo'i 'go brtsams
pa'i dgus chos steng du chos gling slob dpon byed dgos byung / de'i tshe chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes re zhig chos gling slob dpon gyis shig /phugs ma dbu mdzad
blo gros rnam rgyal 'di chos sde chen po'i rgyan yin pas 'di yang bzhugs brtan pa'i thabs su 'gro ba dang / khyed rang la yang bya rgod gshongs kyi mtshams nas ya ga
chos sdings las 'chad nyan byed sa lhag pa med pas blo la zhog gsung pa phebs/ bdag gi de 'dra mi lcogs chos gling slob dpon lo gnyis gsum byas/ de rjes grol cha gnang dgos
zhes zhus/ de nas glang lo de'i dpyid ka man chos gling gra tshang du slob gnyer pa yang shin tu mang ba blo gsal ba yod pas 'chad nyan shin tu 'phel bar byung / chos
rgyal chen po yang shin tu thugs mnyes/ gser dpon lnga dar gyi bu 'di bstan pa la phan pa zhig yong ba 'dug gsungs zer/ chos rgyal nam mkha' rin chen gyis kyang deng sang
dbus gtsang gi gzhung na/ gser dpon lnga dar gyi bu 'di las yon tan che ba med gsungs/ bo dong nas rgyugs kyang lo 'ga' yar gnang / de'i tshe byams mchu ba zer ba'i dpon
skya 'di tshang gis kho bo btsun chung nas chos gling slob dpon/ ya ga chos sdings slob dpon gyi skabs thams cad du gus zhen che zhing mkho ba'i yo byad thams cad bsgrub
pa zhig yod/ chos sde chen por yang rang re 'ur shog bdag po bzang po byed pa'i spobs pa chen po med pas grags pa chen po byung ba ni lkog /blo gzur gnas

rnams don gyi yon tan 'dug zer bar thag gcod pa byung / dgun chos gcig gi tshe deng sang thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi mkhan po byed pa'i chos rje byams pa rab brtan zer ba de
gra skor la byung / nged la phar phyin la gzhung zhu byas/ rgyun zhugs zhugs pa rgyun zhugs chos can zer ba'i bcad skyon byas nas rnam thar sgo gsum du rgyug 'bral byed cing
'dug /byang ngam ring chos sder spyir bcad skyon dang / khyad par bstan bcos phar phyin skabs su bcad skyon byed mkhan la 'phyas smod ma gtogs/ yon tan gyi grags pa sgrog
pa'i shes ldan gzur gnas su yang med/ deng sang khong gi rnam thar slob dpon pa zhig gis byas pa na/ khong pa rgyal ba'i rgyal lugs kyi rdzun mang po bris 'dug zer ro/
/yang skabs shig sde gung pa'i slob dpon chos rje mgon rin ba zer ba zhig kho bo cag la gzhung zhu byed du bcug /bgro gling mang po byas pas sems can thams cad sangs rgyas
pa med pa dang / rgyal po don grub kyang sangs rgyas pa med zer ba byas pas/ chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes slob dpon klu sgrub de skad byas cung mi yong ngam
gsung pa la/ bsam grub dga' ldan pa'i slob dpon snar thang dbu mdzad zer ba'i chos khrims pa zhig yod pa de na re/ nga dpal ldan sa skya pa'i grub mtha' yin/ sa skya
pa'i lugs la khong spu tsam yang 'chugs pa med do zer/ de'i dgongs dga' ldan pa'i chos khrims pa zhig yod pa de bdag gi rtsar byung / chos rje mgon rin pa zer ba de deng
sang bkra shis lhun po na ston pa bzang shogs yin pa la/ de thub pas dga' tshad yin no zer mthe bo bsgreng ba byung / yang chos rgyal kun

dga' rin chen gyi bzhugs gral du dbu ma la/ zhal snga nas dam chos pa dang gnyis bgro gleng rgyun ring pa byas/ bgro gleng sod sogs shin tu smar ba phan tshun gnyis char blo
tshad mar byas pa byung / chos rgyal gyi zhal nas bgro gleng zer ba de khyed gnyis kyi de 'dra ba zhig yong ba yin gsung / gzhan dpang po dang ltad mo ba rnams kyang de
ring las ltad mo che ba ma byung / kun gyi rgyud mi 'khrug pa g.yag 'khrug lta bu rgyun ring po byas na yon tan gyi bshan mi phyed ka med yong ba 'dug zer ba byung ngo /
/thub bstan phyogs kyi chos rje lung rgya ma chung ba zer ba'i sku yon shin tu che ba zhig yod pa de na re/ khyed dang bgro gleng byas pas blo bskyed mi 'byung ba mi srid/
gzhan dang bgro gleng byas kyang tshig 'gre tsam ma gtogs don gyi bgro gleng ni mi yong rgyud 'khrug pa las med zer ro/ /yang mtshal gung pa'i slob dpon/ chos rje bkra
shis 'od zer ba de na re/ bzang ldan chos sder gong ma nam mkha' rin chen gyi ngam ring chos sde'i gra shar drag pa rnams bos/ chos sde gnyis rtsod pa byed du bcug pa'i
tshe nged ngam ring pa rnams kyis ma thub pas nga rang yang mtheng skyes pa de 'dra byung ste/ khyed po ti mtha' dag la mkhas/ thub bstan lugs kyi gzhung don gyi bgro gleng
yang shes/ bya gshongs lugs kyi bar shun gyi bgro gleng yang shes pas khyed kyi kha ya byed pa 'jigs por 'dug zer ro/ /gzur mi gnas pa'i phyogs gzhan mi dga' yang / gzur
gnas sa dge'i phyogs gzhan drang thig 'debs/ phyogs lhung rmongs pa'i rtsod las rnam grol ba'i/ /rigs smrar dpyod ldan dam pa re re tsam/ /glang lo de'i ston 'dar du yong
/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho

la bdag zla gcig sdod long yod ba 'dug pas/ de bar gsung chos shig gnang dgos zhus pas/ 'o na ni gu e byed gsung / ni gu sngar yang thob/ ni gu'i chos 'di dwags shangs bka'
brgyud kyi bla ma zhig la zhu ba rigs/ 'dir dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zab chos shig zhu snyam nas 'khor lo bde mchog gi 'khrid cig gnang 'tshal zhus pas/ de zla ba gcig la
cung mi 'gro/ 'jigs byed kyi 'khrid cig e byed gsung / kho bos 'jigs byed la sngar 'khrid zab mo de yod pa nya mgo ma non/ drag po mngon spyod sogs las tshogs chen po byas
pa zhig yod pa 'dra snyam/ de yang min pa zhig zhu lags zhus pas/ 'o na dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gsung ngag che chung du grags pa'i shin tu spros med kyi 'khrid 'di zab po
zhig yod pas de e byed gsung / dga' ba dang spro ba chen po byung / de ga bka' drin che zhus pas spros med la ngor nas brgyud pa dang / theg chen chos rje nas brgyud pa'i
brgyud pa gnyis ka tshang ba'i rgyas pa zhig bzhugs 'dug pas/ thog mar gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang / spros med rang rkang la skal ldan cig car ba rjes 'dzin/ rdzogs rim
gyi 'khrid kho na yin 'dug kyang rje e waM pas bskyed rim gyi 'khrid kha bskang ba bzhin bskyed rdzogs kyi 'khrid cha lag yongs rdzogs brgyud pa'i lo rgyus dang / bskyed
rim bshad pa sogs la zin thun/ byin rlabs kyi skor/ spros med rgyun gyi byin rlabs/ 'od gsal 'char ba'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi byin rlabs sogs rgyas par thob/ kho bos kyang
de rnams la zin bris byas gzigs phul bas thugs dgyes par gyur/ de'i lo phyi ma yang chos 'khor phug

tu gshed dmar gyi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg dang bcas pa grub/ de nas rje bla ma'i drung du yongs/ mang mkhar rmu'i gzims khang gsar par sleb/ bka' gdams kyi chos skor mang po dang
lam dbang gcig gnang / de 'dus kyi phyag dril hor log ra log rtse lnga ma zhig 'dug pa de/ lam dbang gi ring la kho bo la gnang / 'di khrol thugs dam dang bshad pa sogs
'phrin las gyis gsung / dril bu de deng sang ya ga chos sdings na 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i sku gdung ring bsrel bzhugs pa'i dngul gdung gi drung na yod/ slob dpon byed ring
la mjal phrad la kho re yongs gser zho re zho do 'bul rgyu yong gin yod/ khyed nga'i gser dpon yin no gsung / snam sbyar gtur bu dang bcas pa sogs gnang / rgyud man ngag
gi mnga' bdag tshar pa rje/ /thugs 'bral mi phod par brtse bas bskyangs/ /drin 'khor med kyi 'dren par yid ches rnyed/ /khyed yang yang dran no thugs rjes gzigs/ /glang
lo dgun chos steng du mkhan chen bzang po bkra shis kyis mkhan po dang / 'jam dbyangs bla ma phyogs las rnam rgyal gyis las slob mdzad/ mdo rtsa bar skal ba dang ldan pa'i
rang bzhin can la bar chad ma dris par yang ngo zhes gsungs pa ltar de dus gsang ston med/ grib tshod kha skong dang bcas pa'i dbus su ngam ring chos gling bla brang
du tshigs phyi ma bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa thob/ sdom rgyun de ni mkhan slob gnyis kyi lcags thang chos rjes las bsnyen par rdzogs/ lcags thang chos rjes ya ga chos sdings
su sgye chu ba byams pa dkon cog dpal las bsnyen par rdzogs/ des ngam ring mkhan chen rin

chen rdo rje la bsnyen par rdzogs/ de yan gyi brgyud pa ma rnyed/ phyis lhas sdings slob dpon shes rab me lce ba'i gsung gis khyed kyi thugs la mkhan chen rin rdor bas sems
dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog la bsnyen par rdzogs sam dgongs pa zhig 'dug ste/ de min pa'i mkhan brgyud kyi yi ge zhig kho bo la yod de gzigs 'bul gsung ba byung kyang
phyis lag tu ma byung / de nas kho bos chos gling du glang stag yos gsum phar tshad la 'chad nyan yang 'phel po byung / byams chos lnga gsar 'dzin pa sum cu tsam byung
ba rgyugs 'bul la 'gro snyam yod pa/ chos rgyal chen pos ya ga chos sdings slob dpon la rdzogs bda' byed pa'i dgongs pa yod 'dug pas 'brug lo phyag rtags rim pa gnyis tsam
byung / kho bos kyang de ka shes nas ma phyin pa la brjid che ba dang bcas pa'i phyag rtags gsum pa zhig byung / kho bos kyang byams chos pa rnams kyi rgyugs 'bul dang
bcas 'gro rtsis byas pa la/ grwa pa bying gis kyang shes nas nged kyang 'bod zhus la 'gro zer byams chos rgyugs 'bul dang bcas lnga bcu skor gyis yongs rgyugs 'bul legs
par grub/ nged chos gling rgan pa bzhi dang bcas chos rgyal chen po'i drung du gsol ja zhus/ byams chos rgyun 'don 'dzugs pa'i rten du sngar gra tshang nas gser gyong zho
do re sde srid gzims chung du lo star gyi 'bul dgos 'dug pa de 'chag pa zhig bka' drin bskyangs dgos zhus pas/ chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje zhal 'dzum mdangs
dang ldan par byas/ gser gyong zho do po 'di gzims chung du 'bab rgyu

yin pas 'chag tu mi rung yang da lan khyed zer ba de yang ngas dang du len/ nged zer ba de yang khyed kyis dang du len dgos gsung / nged rnams the tshom log ge ba zhig gi ngang
las log nged rang rnams kyi lkog lab la gsung gi mdangs de la ni gser gyong zho do char 'chag gsung pa 'dra ba zhig byung ste/ sngar gra tshang gi slob dpon sku yon
che ba sde srid kyi thugs la 'dogs pa paN chen legs pa'i blo gros dang / 'jam dbyangs blo gros rnam rgyal lta bus kyang sne re sne gnyis las ma chogs pa yin/ da lan zho gang
tsam phyogs na'ang rab zer gyin yongs gra khang du sleb dang bstun/ gser gyong zho do la mgur zho gsum tsam yong gin 'dug pa de rtsa chag yong ba'i phyag dam skyel du
drung 'khor zhig gnang byung / gra pa rnams ni dga' mgu yi rang / khyed gra tshang gi slob dpon thes che shes/ rgyal sras thugs rje dpal las kyang lhag pa zhig byung zer/
nged gdan mthon po brtsigs pa'i steng du bzhag /nga dang dkar bcol bzang po byed kyin 'dug /nged la rtser shog gsung chos rgyal chen pos gsol ja dang gnang sbyin bzang
po mdzad/ da dgos gra tshang la yang byams chos kyi gzhi rten dga' mo sbyar yod/ khyed kyang ya ga chos sdings su 'chad nyan la phyin na rang gi yon tan gyi rgyan du che/
spyir mkhan slob gnyis gnyis byas pa 'di legs tshogs che rgyu yang mi yong 'dug ste/ khyed dpon slob gcig gis gcig gi grogs su che ba las/ gzhan mthun mi mthun yong ba'i
tshad du mi 'dug gsung byung bas/ rang gi 'khos ka 'di la chos rgyal chen po 'di lta bu'i brtse skyong mdzad pa ngo mtshar che bsam dga' ches/ mchi

ma bro lhug ge ba ma gtogs gzhan zhu ma spobs/ de nas 'jam dbyangs bla ma yang ngam ring du phebs byung / 'brug lo'i dpyid de ya ga chos sdings dpyid chos steng du ya ga chos
sdings slob dpon gyi go rar sleb/ phyag 'bul gyi tshe nged khri dngos ma'i steng dang / de'i gong du khri mthon pa'i steng du 'jam mgon bla ma bzhugs/ gra pa rnams kyis
phyag 'bul dga' spro dang bcas mdzad/ de yang sngar rmi lam du tshogs chen por nged dpon slob khri gnyis la bzhugs pa yang yang rmi ste/ chos gling ya ga chos sdings/ bya
gshongs/ ngam ring chos sde rnams su bla ma'i gdan khrir rang gis kyang yang yang 'dzegs pa 'di la lta ba yin par 'dug /'brug lo nas bya lo'i bar lo bco brgyad kyi bar
du ya ga chos sdings su 'chad nyan byas/ skabs shig byang khang gsar ba mgon po rnam rgyal la snyan tshig cig phul bas shin tu mnyes shog gsung zhag 'ga' bsdad/ khyed 'di
lta bu la dgyes pa 'dug gsung nas gzims chung mchod gral nas gong ma lnga tshar gyi sku shin tu legs pa zhig gnang / ches dga' ba khyad par can thob/ rang gces pa'i bu
dang chung ma sogs/ /yid phongs med sbyin gtong sngon rabs kyi/ /rgyal dri med rnams la co 'dri ba'i/ /byang khang gsar mgon po rnam rgyal khyed/ /'bangs ngan pas bslus pa'i
mdzad pa la/ /gzhan 'phya smod sgro skur bden na yang / /rdzas longs spyod 'khor la ma chags par/ /kun sbyin gtong tha mal spyod las 'das/ /sngon sa skya gong ma'i thugs
rjes sbrel/ /lha dkar phyogs srung ma'i lcags kyus

drangs/ /khong gong ma mched lnga rog ge byon/ /bdag skal pa bzang snyam dga' spro 'phel/ /yang mi dbang des sa paN gyi phyag bris kye rdor gos thang dang shin tu mkho ba'i
po ti bcu sogs kyang gnang / sbrul lo'i mgo de tsam la chos rgyal chen pos mus pa tab tob pas bris pa'i kye rdor lha dgu'i bris thang gsar pa legs pa zhig gnang 'chad nyan
gyis shig gsung / khong sngon med kyi chos rgyal ngo mtshar can/ /bstan 'gro la phan pa'i lhag bsam che/ /chos slob gnyer byed 'dod bu bzhin skyong / /khong bsams shing
dran tshe yid rab 'phyo/ /dus lan cig kho bo drung du bos/ /khyod gzhung lugs che la blo gros bzang / /chos legs bshad 'chad la 'bad cig gsung / /lha dgyes pa rdo rje'i
ras bris thang / /yid tshar du dngar ba'i ri mo 'di/ /byed chos 'chad dran pa'i rten du 'bul/ /sems ma brjed sa le zhog cig gsung / khyed legs bshad bshad pa'i mkhas pa
rnams/ /lus ci bder nyal de skyid pa min/ /shes don gnyer 'dzom pa'i blo gsal la/ /chos legs bshad 'chad na skyid do gsungs/ /lan cig mjal phrad kyi tshe che bsgres slob
dpon gzhan rnams skas la sus thob byed cing sngon la 'gro/ kho bos ga le yongs nas gral gzhug cig tu bsdad/ de chos rgyal chen pos gzigs nas sku 'dun dar tsho ba btang /
kho bo la yar shog gsung gral mtho sar bzhag /dam bca' zhog cig gsung dam bca' bzhag /skad 'phangs rang bzhin gyis zhan pa la skad gzengs mtho ru chug gsung / bgro gling
mang pos btang kyang 'gro song cher ma byung / chos rgyal chen pos

kho bo la rjes la sdod gsung / gsol ja gnang thugs dgyes dgyes mdzad/ gzhan slu med nam mkha' tshe dbang des/ /khong blo gsal yongs la thugs brtse na'ang / /sgos rang la dgyes
pa'i spyan zur g.yo/ /don slu ba med 'di ngo mtshar che/ /'chad nyan de yang phar tshad gnyis/ 'dul mdzod gnyis/ dbu sdom gnyis/ byams chos rigs gter rnams la 'chad nyan
rus thon byas/ de yang slob gnyer ba grwa pa brgya skor byung / tho rangs chos rnga snga bar btang ste thor skyongs la yang rang gis skor ba byed cing bsdad/ zur chos
zhu ba la chos bshad/ nam langs nas dpe 'dzin gyi tshe gra pa slob gnyer ba gra khang du nyal chog pa rnams kyang dpe 'dzin la bsdus/ tsha ba'i gaNDe byung byung rang gis
kyang bsdad/ tsha ba grol nas snga chos tshar gnyis gnyis/ de nas gung sangs cung zad byas/ de mtshams dgongs chos kyi gaNDi brdungs te dgongs chos tshar gnyis/ de nas
chos spyod rigs lung / de grol mtshams brang bdag ma yin pa'i slob gnyer ba rnams 'du khang du nyal dgos pas srod skyongs rgyun ring po'i bar la rang gis kyang bsdad/ chos
khrims pas snang gsal dang bcas skor ba byed dgos de lta bu 'chag med du dpyid chos/ stod bcu tshig bzhi 'am lnga/ smad bcu tshigs bzhi ston cag stod bcu tshigs gnyis/
smad bcu tshigs gnyis/ ston chos bcu tshigs gnyis sam bco lnga tshigs/ de dag gi gong du gser chos bcu tshigs gnyis sam bco lnga tshigs re 'chag med du yong bas/ de dag la
kho bo rang gi zha chag med par phyin pas slob gnyer ba

rnams kyang rgyud 'byongs nas 'chag med du khrig khrig yod/ chos khrims pa 'ga' res khyod rang 'o brgyal nged chos khrims pas chog zer te/ nged rang ma phyin na btsun chung
re re gcig gnyis las chos gra se ster re las mi yong 'dug /de lta bu lo bco brgyad kyi bar du 'chag med du byas pas slob gnyer ba rnams kyang hur thag che zhing nyams 'char
ba/ chos sde dang gra tshang du spyi sgyur yang yang lang dgos pas rigs lung mchod yar/ gzhan la smon mi dgos shing rang nyid mngon par mtho ba kho na byung / gra pa
rnams kyang bya gshongs dang slob gnyer mnyam/ gra sa gzhan las lhag zer ba'i 'dzin btang byed pa zhig yod/ chos rje las chen chos don grub pa'i gsung gi ya ga chos sdings
pa'i slob gnyer ba 'di rnams bsod nams bsags par 'dug /rje khyed lta bu'i 'chad nyan byed mkhan yod/ spyi sgyur lang ba'i tshe yang po ti 'di la lang zer ba ma gtogs gzhung
'di dgos kyi dmigs bsal mi dgos/ gra skor sogs dad can rnams kyang rmig med par byed/ gra sa nas 'ongs pa'i slob gnyer ba nga yin zer ba rnams kyang nged ya ga chos
sdings pa zhig dang slong dgos/ gzhung 'di dgos zer langs pa'i dus su skad ngar chag pa zhig ga yong gin 'dug gsungs/ yang lan cig ya ga chos sdings pa'i grangs chen rab
'byams pa shes rin zer ba de kho bo'i ngag rgyun rang gzhan gyi grub mtha' so so la/ 'thad mi 'thad kyi dgag sgrub byas pa zhig yod pa de la chos sde chen por bshad pa byas
pas che bgres slob dpon rnams bshad pa shin tu snyan pa byung / 'on kyang

gtsub bshad tho re ba 'dug pa 'di khyed kyis bslabs pa yin pa 'dug zer/ lan cig ya ga chos sdings kyi mang ja'i thog tu kho ba'i ngag rgyun sdom gsum gyi bshad pa zhig yod
pa de la bshad pa byas pas khong smra lce bde zhing bshad pa byed mkhas pa zhig yod pas/ gung gral la chos khrims pa dpal 'byor gzi brjid zer ba ma gcig gi gcod byed pa zhig
yod pa des phaT zer skad chen po zhig rgyab byung bas/ gra pa rnams bzhad gad thag ge ba zhig byung / kho bos chos khrims pa de la de 'dra ci yin byas pas bshad pa'i
dga' ba la snyam pa 'dzin pa chen po zhig skyes byung ba de gcod snyam nas phaT shor song zer ro/ /yang de'i tshe 'jam dbyangs bla mas dgung grangs re gcig pa glang lo ngam
ring chos sde'i mkhan po mdzad/ de rjes dbon gnas gnyag phur chos nyan pa sum cu skor la gsung ngag thog ma gnang / de'i tshe'i dkyil 'khor gyi thig dang / rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs pa sogs bdag rang gcig pus byas/ sngar rje tshar chen la ma thob pa'i gsung ngag gi cha lag cung zad yod pa rnams kyang zur du ci thob byas/ 'jam
dbyangs bla mas gsung ngag lan gsum gnang ba'i bar pa la dkyil 'khor bris thig sogs mchod g.yog ma gtogs gsung ngag rang la ma zhugs/ lan gsum pa de bdag bya gshongs na yod
pa'i skabs su gnang bar 'dug ste/ thub bstan mkhan chen chos rje sangs rgyam pa dang / chos rje dpal sras pa sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po byung bar 'dug /yang kho
bos chos mtshams shig la bla brang du mtshams shig

byas pas/ nyin mo rlung bum pa can bzung bas sa paN gyi sku thang chos 'chad ma de'i chos 'chad kyi mtheb mdzub gnyis po krab krab byed kyin 'dug /gzhan ni ci yang 'gul ba
mi snang de yang smig rgyu'i nyams yin par 'dug ste/ chos 'chad nyan gyis shig pa'i brda yin zer ba'i 'ud chen po byas kyang chog pa 'dug /yang lan gcig bla brang ka bzhi
ma'i ka ba bzhi po phar yom chur yom byas ka ba dang gzhu bral 'gro ba snyam byed pa'i nyams shar de'ang smig rgyu'i nyams yin par 'dug/ yang lan cig rlung bum pa can bzung
bas thog mar btsan thabs rgyab pa'i nag thib pa zhig byung / de rjes gsal la dngas pa'i nyams kyi snang ba la bar snang nas rten khegs dum sgrigs ma ri mo sna tshogs
bkra ba kha dog zangs mdog lta bu gcig rjes la gcig rim pa log log lag pas 'dzin thub pa lta bu'i snang ba 'char ba dang / yang res 'ga' rma bya'i sgro mdongs lta bu ri mo
sna tshogs bkra ba/ kha dog sna tshogs byas pa mig lam du khor mor 'khor ba dang / res 'ga' ri mo ltar mi bzod pa lta bu byas pa'i yol ba gsar pa bkra yal le ba de 'dra
mdun du kho re rgyab pa dang / res 'gar ri mo rtsing tshal le ba kha dog rnying song ba lta bu'i yol ba rgyab pa'i snang ba shar ba byung ste/ khams thig le dngas snyigs
kyi khyad yin pa 'dra snyam/ res 'ga' lcer sngar myong ma dran pa'i ro zhim po sna tshogs myong ba dang / sngar ma myong ba'i dri zhim po snom pa dang / rna bar sgra sna
tshogs thos pa dang / mi'i gleng mo sna tshogs rna bar shib shib yong ba dang / res 'ga' nam mkha' sngo sang nge ba la skar ma khra thag ge ba'i nyams 'char ba dang /

res 'ga' mig gi steng tsam na nyi ma shar ba lta bu'i 'od lhag ge ba'i nyams 'char ba byung ste/ lam 'bras rdo rje tshig rkang las sgra sna tshogs dang dri ro zhes sogs kyi
don yin par snang / rlung gi nyams de lta bu sna tshogs ni rlung 'dzin nus na de'i bar du rgyun ma chad par yong ba zhig 'dug /rlung dang rmi lam zin pa'i nyams snang la/
/ngor mtshar ltad mo sna tshogs mthong dang thos/ /rdo rje lus kyi rten 'brel ya mtshan snyam/ /yid la rab dga' skyes pa bla ma'i drin/ /yang dgon pa lu phu de na sa paN
gyi sdom rgyun bzhugs pa'i bla ma rim par byung ba la/ skabs shig bla ma gcig la sa paN gyi sdom rgyun de mi zhugs pas/ chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rjes khyed kyi
sdom rgyun de sa paN gyi sdom rgyun yin pas de chad na phongs/ sdom rgyun bzhugs pa'i sgrub chen mkhyen pa yangs pa zhig la sdom rgyun de long zhig ces bstan pa la gces
spras su che ba'i bka' stsal phebs/ de ltar byas pas dgon pa de na sa paN gyi sdom rgyun rgyun ma chad par yod pa de thos nas/ bdag gis 'jam mgon bla ma la bdag sa paN
gyi sdom rgyun cig zhu 'dod pas ji ltar legs zhus pas/ sa skya'i gra dgon gzhan gang na yang de 'dra yod par mi 'dug /lu phu na yod pa'i nges pa brtan po yod na rang re dpon
slob gnyis char de ltar byas pas chog gsung / bka'i gnang ba thob nas lu phu'i mkhan po sangs rgyas 'od zer la/ mkhan slob dge slong 'dra dang / ya ga chos sdings kyi
dge slong gtsang ma 'dra bsags blon po chu tshan khar dkar gur yangs po'i nang du dpon slob gnyis kyis bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ sngar

gyi sdom ro rnying pa la 'bul chog ma byas na sdom pa blangs kyang mi chags pa 'dul ba'i lugs yin te/ mdo rtsa ba las blangs pa la slar blang ba med pa'i phyir ro/ /zhes gsungs
pas shes/ des na kho bos dge slong gi bslab pa phul/ dge tshul dge bsnyen gyi bslab pa gnyis ni kun mkhyen lcags thang pa las thob pa yin pas ma phul/ de'i tshe slob
dpon dang gsang ston gyi 'os su gyur pa gzhan ma rnyed pas/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas 'od zer bas mkhan po dang las slob gnyis char mdzad/ gzhan dge slong gtsang ma gsum dang
bcas te dge slong bzhi'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs so/ /mkhan slob gcig gis byed pa ni bu rin po ches/ mkhan slob gcig gis byed pa 'di bod kyi 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams la
ni snang / gzhung nas bshad pa ni ma mthong gsungs te thugs mad/ dam chos 'dul ba'i lugs la bshad tshod yod kyang lag len med pa dang / lag len yod kyang bshad tshod med
pa'i dmigs bsal mang po yod pa de'i dmigs rnam phyed dgos so/ /yang 'dul 'dzin kha cig dge slong bzhi las bsnyen par rdzogs su mi rung gsung ste/ 'dul ba tshig le las/
gal te bzhi ni las brjod mkhas/ /tshul khrims ldan par gyur na ni/ /bsnyen rdzogs ma smad gyur pa ste/ /lha yis kyang ni phyag byar 'os/ /zhes bshad pa 'di ma gzigs par zad/
kha cig dge slong bzhi'i steng du las brjod mkhan bsnan pa'i lnga tshang pa la dgongs zer ba'i 'bru skyog gnang mkhan yod de/ gal te bzhi dang las brjod mkhas zer pa
yod na de skad rigs na'ang / gal te bzhi ni las brjod mkhas/

zhes pa'i tshig gi nus pa ma rnyed par zad do/ /mdor na gsang ston yod na gsang ston bsko ba'i las dgos/ bskau ba'i las la lnga tshang dgos te/ bsko ba'i yul dge slong gcig
/bsko mkhan dge slong bzhi tshang dgos pa'i gnad kyis yin/ gsang ston med na dge slong bzhis chog pa'i gnad ma go bar bab col ma mdzad cig /kha che paN chen nas brgyud sdom
rgyun la/ /rdor byang gnyis dang sa skya paN chen gsum/ /sa paN nas brgyud legs kyang dkon mthong nas/ /'bad pas bsgrubs 'di kho bo'i dpal du shar/ /lugs gang la'ang
gnad 'gag ma shes na/ /gtam chal chol mang pos rang gzhan bslu/ /chos 'dul ba skra shad 'dzings 'dra la/ /gnad ma zin 'chol lo 'dul 'dzin rnams/ /des na kho bos kyang ya
ga chos sdings su rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs mkhan po mang po dang / kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi rdul tshon du dbang bskur ba kha re dang / rjes gnang phran tshegs mang
po dang / chos rje bstan pa dar rgyas dang / chos rje nyi ma bkra shis gnyis la lam 'bras 'khrid kyang thal tsam zhig thog mar byas/ chos rje sangs legs ba sogs ya ga chos
sdings pa bdun tsam la gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang dang brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi spros med kyi 'khrid cha lag tshang ma zhig byas/ gzhan mdo phyogs kyi 'chad nyan gtso
bo yin/ rtsom pa'i rigs mdzod kyi spyi don chen mo dang / rigs gter dka' 'grel dang / phar phyin zur bkol kha re dang / sdom gsum so thar gyi dka' 'grel sogs yig cha cung
zad dang / bstan rtsis shog bu brgya tsam byas pa de/

dpyid ka chos dbar cig la lcog bu'i nang du mtshams byas brtsams pas bla ma so so la dad 'dun yang chen po byung / byin rlabs kyi rten 'brel yang yin nam shes rab yang gsal
du song pa snyam byung / de dus nub dgon nas kyi slob gnyer ba shes 'dod can shin tu mang pa yod pas/ de rnams kyis phar tshad/ sdom gsum sogs la zin bris byas pa mang du
byung / 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i ngo mtshar rtogs brjod dpal gyi 'khri shing yal 'dab bcu bdun pa yan grub/ yal 'dab bco brgyad pa/ bcu dgu pa/ nyi shu pa/ nyi shu rtsa gcig
pa rnams de snga ma grub pa mi dbang 'dar nas dgra 'dul don grub dang / mi dbang grag pa la sogs kyis 'di dpag bsam 'khri shing gnyis pa yin pas 'phro rdzogs pa zhig rtsom
dgos zhes gser gyi me tog dang bcas bskul nas shing mang dgon par grub/ mi dbang gdong dga' ba rnam rgyal pas rnam rig rtogs brjod kyi yal 'dab dang / dbu ma rtogs brjod
kyi yal 'dab gnyis po 'di la 'grel pa re byung na mkhas pa dpyod ldan gyi rgyan du che ba 'dug pas rtsom dgos zhes snyim pa me tog dang bcas bskul nas dpal ya ga chos
sdings su grub pa yin/ rong 'tsho nas mi dbang dpal 'byor don grub kyis yal 'dab gzhan rnams dang / khyad par yal 'dab nyi shu pa 'dul ba'i thad kyi 'grel ba yang rtsom
dgos gsung ba zhig byung kyang sngar phan ma grub/ yang mkhas pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan pas dpal ldan ngor phyogs la/ sems bskyed brgyud pa med pa dang / zhes sogs kyi skyon
brgyad 'phangs pa la/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub pas de'i lan mdzad/

slar yang de'i lan mkhan chen bzang po bkra shis kyis mdzad pa la kho bos de'i lan/ bdud rtsi sman sbyor gyi bstan bcos zhes pa zhig chos gling slob dpon byed skabs su sbyar
nas phul bas/ don la dpyod pa'i lan ni cher ma byung / 'on kyang na tshod gzhon nu la/ legs bshad 'di 'dra ngo mtshar che/ gsung ba sogs thung tsam gnang byung ngo / /ya
ga chos sdings chos kyi skyed tshal du/ /blo gsal blo la blo gros kha phye ste/ /zab don gnyer la zab 'khrid brda don btsal/ /blo gsal mkhas la legs par bshad pa'i gtam/
/bstan rtsa tshul khrims ma smad bsnyen rdzogs sdom/ /sa skya'i 'jam mgon las 'ongs pad dkar dri/ /snom byed skal bzang bung ba'i mgrin rnga yis/ /thub bstan ngur smrig
skyed tshal khyab gyur cig /de nas stag lo ba santa'i zla ba gsum pa la nged dpon slob gnyis car gyis 'dar du byon/ rje blo gsal rgya mtsho chos 'khor yang rtse'i bla brang
spe ser na bzhugs pa dang mjal/ lam dbang tshar gcig /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs bcu gcig zhal gyi rjes gnang / smyung gnas kyi chog khrigs/ gnyag phu ba bsod nams bzang
pos mdzad pa de'i lugs gting skyes bya bral ba kun dga' mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa'i smyung gnas chog khrigs kyi lung / dge slong ma dpal mo'i rnam thar / smyung gnas brgyud
pa'i bla ma so so'i rnam thar gyi lung sogs thob/ de'i tshe rje bla ma'i gsung las da lo dog cha chen po yod zer ba 'dug kyang da lo lo drug cu rtsa drug pa yin te/
da lo rang mi 'chi tsam yong las che gsung pa zhig yod na'ang gshegs pa de glo

bur sku tshe'i bar chad kyi rnam pa zhig byung ngam snyam/ gang na'ang nged dpon slob kyis thob pa'i gsung chos de rnams 'da' kha ma'i chos rang du 'dug pas skal ba bzang zer
ba byung ste/ de ga rang du 'dug ste/ de nas dag pa'i zhing du ma gshegs bar du su la yang bka' chos kyi rim pa ma byung 'dug pas so/ /drin 'gran bral gyi rje btsun blo
gsal ba/ /chos thob thob slob bu mang na yang / /spyan zur mig gzigs pa'i 'da' ka'i chos/ /don zhal gdams thob pa re re tsam/ /yang ya ga chos sdings su 'brug lo sleb pa'i
lo de mtshan gyi rmi lam la shar phyogs nas zla ba skya rgyang byung ba de nyi ma la thim/ nyi ma de yang nub phyogs kyi ri zhig gi phag tu thim song ba zhig rmis/ de
nged rang dpon slob la yod pa yin nam snyam/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma la zhus pas/ dbus gtsang gi sde dpon chen po gnyis la lta ba e yin gsungs/ de ka bzhin sbrul lo la sngon
la chos rgyal nam mkha' rin cen gshegs/ der rjes lo de ga la chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje gshegs pas de gnyis la ltas par 'dug go /khong 'khrul med kyi chos rgyal
yab sras gnyis/ /bstan 'gro la srog bzhin gces na yang / /gdon bsam ngan sbyor rtsub lang shor mkhan/ /las ngan byed ngo sor byed ces grags/ /dus deng sang gi ban skya
snying rul rnams/ mthar mngon mtho sgrub zer lam gzhan gol/ /ri mtho la 'dzeg 'dod thur la 'gril//don log pa spongs shig thar 'dod rnams/ /yang skabs shig 'jam dbyangs
bla ma 'dar la phebs/ kho bos gnyag phu bla brang du zla gcig tsam bsdad/ rogs chibs dpon dpal ldan bzang po zer

ba zhig min pa gzhan med/ nyin re la ja sbyor gnyis gnyis byas/ brtag gnyis snga sor nas blo la yod/gzhung bshad gnyag ma bzung dpe 'dzin dang shar sbyangs bsgrigs chug byas
pas/ shin tu skyid pa mtshan dus rmi lam rang zin dang / spel sbyong sogs ci rigs 'byung ba/ gzhung bshad la go rtogs shar bas brod pa skyes pa/ thun 'tshams rlung 'dra
bzung bas 'od gsal gyi rtags mang du shar ba yin no/ /yang skabs shig ja bsil bo zhig gis rkyen byas mig na ba zhag nyi shu skor byung / de'i tshe 'jam dbyangs bla mas gtso
mdzad dpon slob rnams kyis sgrol ma mtshan 'don sogs rim gro stobs che ba mdzad/ nub cig rmi lam du tshogs chen po zhig gi dbus su dbu mdzad yin snyam pa zhig gis chos
spyod bskul pa'i sgra 'brug ltar ldir pa zhig byung bas mtha' de nas mi skya shar gnyis 'jigs skrag chen pos g.yas la 'gros/ g.yon la 'gros byed pa zhig rmis/ de yang rim
gro de pa'i nus pa yin par 'dug/ zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga mun mtshams rang la bsdad kyang skyed cher ma byung / snga dro zhig 'jam dbyangs bla mas de ring nyi ma la mthon
no gsung / g.yabs su nyi ma la phyin pas mig skam thas kyis song / nye ring thams cad khra gsal le mthong ba zhig byung ba de bla ma'i byin rlabs kyi nyer len dang / rim
gro'i lhan cig byed rkyen 'dzom pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug snyam yid ches so/ /yang nub cig rmi lam du g.yag khyu chen po zhig yong gin 'dug pa de dang thug gi dogs lam steng
zhig la gzur phyin pas/ g.yag khyu de dang ched du gtad pa bzhin thug byung nas dkyil du 'thums/

bsdad na rmig pa'i 'og dang / langs na ra dang thug pa yong ngam snyam/ yun rings de gar bsdad pa zhig byung ste/ chos skyong srung mas srung skyob byed pa'i rtags su go /yang
nub cig lung pa rtsa bzang po byas pa zhig na g.yag mang po 'dug pa de rnams 'grangs kyang shin tu skom zer ba byung ste/ gtor ma la chab kyis sbyong ba brjed pa'am chab
nyungs pa yin nam snyam/ de phyin chad chab ma brjed pa dang ma nyungs pa byas/ yang nub cig g.yag rog po zhol chen dar sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa zhig 'dug pa de la zhon
pa'i 'dun pa byas/ g.yag mtho drags zhon mi khyod 'dug pa la g.yag de nyal byung zhon gyi brda yin pa 'dug snyam de la zhon/ yang lugs ji ltar byed snyam pa la sug rtse
rnams rim pas dal gyis bteg nas 'gro 'dug kha re byas pa zhig byung / de yang chos srung rnams thugs brtse zhing glo ba nye ba'i rtags su go /rang re ni gtor bsngo ma
chag tsam ma gtogs gtor tshogs chen po dang sgram chil chen po ni lta rtog sogs kyis g.yengs nas cher byed rgyu ma byung ngo / /khong phyi nang gsang ba'i srung ma'i tshogs/
/thugs brtse zhing bsrung skyob mi g.yel yang / /rang le lo che zhing rnam g.yeng gis/ /phyi rnga bsil gyi 'ur rding ma byas kyang / /gzhan g.yo zog gi sgrib g.yogs med
tsam la/ /nang thos bsam gyi rtog dpyod gcer bur shar/ /khong gsung rab kyi zab don gsal por mthong / /khyed chos srung gi thugs kyis ma btang tsam/ /yang byi lo dpyid
chos stod shin tu smar ba yod pa'i tshe nged kyi a jo che ba lha mo gnyer ma zer ba byang phyi 'brog na gces pa zhig yod pa de la 'brum pa byung zer nas

'bod du byung / de gces pa zhig yod pas mi 'gro zer yang ma nus/ chos bcag nas 'gro ba yang mi rigs sam nongs par yod pa la/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i gsung gi chos rje pa de 'dra'i
sems khrel mi dgos/ rang mi 'gro kha med yin de bar la ngas tshab byas chos 'chad nyan ma chag pa bya'i gsung / bka' drin bskyangs nged kyi 'brog khrod la phyin pas
