bar lam du sku tshes ma zin zer ba'i gtam sleb byung / sems la sdug bsngal bzod pa med pa byung kyang yab bgres po dang bu tsha rnams kyang sdug gi dogs gzengs bstod/ mi
snga 'gros la btang nye 'khor g.yog rigs dang bcas pa la khyed rnams sems khral dang mchi ma gtong ba sogs ye ma byed zer ba byas/ khong rnams nged rnams kyi gdong bsur
byung tshe gdong pham pa dang / nged sa dang 'dres zer ba tsam ma gtogs ngu chom ye ma byas/ pha rgan pos sna la byon chos rje 'o mi brgyal zer gzengs mtho ba rang 'dug /sngon
du chos rje bya btang ba sogs kyang 'pho ba sogs la byon tshar 'dug /nged kyis rus pa la sbyang khrus dbang bskur sogs byas/ dgyes rdor gyi cho ga de 'phral nas btsugs/
khong rnams ne rings su cho ga 'dzugs/ nged mgo ma la 'gro dgos zer ba byung kyang nged mi 'gro/ ne rings pa dpon slob dang / gzhan yang bla ma slob dpon sogs mang po
'dug pas de rnams la bsnyen bkur gang yong gyis zer ba byas ma phyin/ nub cig rmi lam du a jo ther slog gyon ngo nong nge byas byung bas chags zhen zhig yod pa 'dra snyam
a jo rang ga la yang chags mi dgos/ ngas bde ba can du bskyal gyi byas lag nas bzung aShta mang du bgrangs 'phur

'gro'i 'dun pa byas pas a jo gar song mi 'dug /mchod gnas 'dra yod ba rnams a jo mtho ris su sgrol thub pa 'dra zer/ g.yog dmangs ma mang po shi /g.yog gces pa 'chi ba'i sngas
mgor phyin pas nga khyod dang 'phrad 'chi ba la 'tsher rgyu med blo bde zer ro/ /yang skabs shig rang la mgo tshigs sogs na ba shin tu thu ba zhig byung / pha rgan yang
'brum pa yin nam snyam thugs khral shin tu mdzad/ sang nyin g.yog gces pa zhig yod pa de shi zer rta bzang po zhig gis gtso byas 'bul ba mang po byung ba de'i snga ltas
yin pa 'dug /yang kun skyabs zer ba'i g.yog drag pa zhig yod pa de la 'brum pa byung 'chi ba'i rtsar kho bos kyang phyin byin rlabs 'dra byas pas da khyod kyis byin rlabs
thob 'chi ba la 'tsher rgyu med zer ro/ /a jo'i bu spun gnyis sogs gnyen 'khor kun gyis 'brum pa thar/ snying phongs par gcags pa'i a jo de/ /sngon las ngan 'chi bdag
bdud kyis bzung / /sems ngar langs dag pa'i zhing du bskyal/ /da 'gyod pa med do gnyen 'khor rnams/ /zla gcig tsam zang bzang skam pa nas brtsams gzhung gong 'og shos pa
la ma bud kyi bar du zla gcig tsam bsdad/ de nas ya ga chos sdings su sleb/ de bar 'jam mgon bla mas 'chad nyan gnang bas gra pa rnams kyang yid spro seg ge ba byung 'dug
/de bar gyi bsngo rten sogs dngos spyad rnams nged la rtsis gnang / ngas skyas tshab byas pa'i nom pa yin no gsung / snga sor nas rang ston pa zas gtsang sras po la mi phyed
pa'i dad pa yod/ dpag bsam 'khri shing gi dpe 'byor na bsams pa lag tu ye ma byung / phyis

g.yas ru byang nas dpe g.yar po zhus/ drung yig dpal sdings pa chos grags gdan drangs khyi lo'i dpyid khong gis bza' bris byas/ yongs rdzogs bris grub stod cha'i mchan bu thebs
tsam la zhabs drung dus 'khor nas 'bod mi byung / smad cha ma thebs pa la yi ge su shes kyis bris pas mchan dngos gtsang po rang ma byung yang yongs su rdzogs pas sems
spro seg ge byung / khong ston pa'i rnam thar thos tsa na/ /lus ba spu g.yo zhing mchi ma 'khrug /las dkar ba'i bag chags sad do snyam/ /sems dga' spro'i ngang du nyin
mtshan 'das/ /de'i dkar chag kyang phyis kho bo rang gis brtsams/ rje bla ma'i zhal bzang nyi gzhon dang / /rang dad mos 'od dkar 'phreng ba gnyis/ /khong skal bzang mkha'
la lhan cig shar/ /rgyu 'bras bur snyam pa'i ngo mtshar ltos/ /bka' drin 'gran bral rtsa brgyud bla ma dang / /khrims ldan ngur smrig dge 'dun 'dus pa'i sde/ /dregs ldan
bka' srung rgya mtsho'i nus mthu yis/ /dngos po zhes bya shing pho khyi yi lo/ /dbus gtsang gra sa kun gyi gtsug gi rgyan / /legs bshad rgyud mangs sgrog pa'i chos gra
cher/ /lo grags snyems pa'i nga rgyal dang bral yang / /nga gnyis lo la kho bo gnas der 'phos/ /de yang 'jam mgon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan lo grangs nyi shu rtsa bdun du
mnyan yod du 'chad nyan phul du phyin pa mdzad/ gdan sa sko bzhag gi thus mdzad pa'i skabs de tsam du kho bo'i rmi lam du bya gshongs gdan sa la 'gro snyam pa'i bsam pas
chos gling steng gi rka rgyud de la brgyud de phyin pas rang gi rogs dang bsu mi sogs mang po 'dug /bya

gshongs bla brang gi sgo de na khyi chen po zhig btags 'dug kyang nged la 'gegs pa'i tshul ni mi byed 'dug rang gis kyang khog 'joms pa la 'phral thal le phyin pas khyi de
kho bo la 'dris g.yog dang / bkrab bkrab sig sig mang po dang chos gos la lce leg byed cing 'dug /rogs rnams khyed la khyi 'di snga sor nas 'dris 'dug pa zer chos srung gi
dgongs par bzhugs pa'i rtags su 'dug /de nas gnam sgo'i skas la 'dzegs pas skas gdang gcig gi tshab la thag pa gcig btang ba tsam las mi 'dug nang du bzhugs pa rnams kyi
sku khyer la snyam pa tsam byung / skas mgo nas gcig gis lag 'dren btang nas sgo khang der sleb/ de nas gnyid sad byung / de mtshams nub cig rmi lam na bya gshongs la 'gro
ba'i 'dun pas phyin/ shag lo tsam yin pa 'dra/ shar gyi spe'u dkar po zhig tu bsdad/ der 'jam mgon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan yang phebs mjal phrad byung / gsung gleng
ci gsung ni mi dran de nas rje sngon la phebs song / kho bos rjes la yongs pas bya gshongs mdun de na lo tog se chel le smin pa tsam 'dug /de phyin chad ci byas rmi lam dran
pa mi gsal 'dug rmi lam de ltar byung ba'i rjes zhag 'ga' yar nas bya gshongs nas che bgres mi sna dang bcas chos rgyal kun dga' rin cen gyi phyag rtags/ rje gdan sa
pa'i phyag rtags/ gra pa rnams kyi thus byas pa'i yi ge mgrin gcig tu byung zer ba'i shog dril rnams dang bcas phebs byung / kho bo rang gi blo'i gshis yin pas 'gro 'dod
pa rang ma byung / ya ga chos sdings pa rnams kyis kyang shar la mi

gtong zer rma bya shug khrod du 'bod zhus la thegs song bas btsan 'tshams pa 'chun che ba'i stabs kyis chos rgyal kun dga' rin cen thugs 'gyur/ brtag pa byas dus shar la ma
chug pas re zhig ya ga chos sdings su ka 'chad nyan gyis gsung ba phebs byung bas/ bya gshongs pa rnams shar la log dgos pa byung / slar bya gshongs nas bskyar zhus nan
can mdzad pa nas dgongs pa khrol/ bkod yig gi phyag rtags dang bcas pa 'bod mi gcang tshul khrims rgyal po sogs che bgres mi sna sogs bskyar nas byung / kho bos sngar bzhin
mi 'gro ba'i lugs byas kyang 'jam dbyangs bla ma phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi gsung las/ rang gi yon tan bslabs shes pa'i dgos pa yin pas 'chad nyan nus na bya gshongs lta
bur mi 'gro ba'i don med/ mi nus na ni de ga yin mod gsung bka' nan cher phebs pas mi 'gro zer ba'i bka' bzlog ma nus/ zla ba bdun pa'i dus tshes bzang po la gdan sa spo
len gyi dus yin pas de ga la 'gro bar brtsams/ zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu gnyis la dbon rams pa byams pa blo gros/ rang gi tsha bo mang thos rnam rgyal dang / rnam rgyal
klu sgrub sogs rogs du ma dang / ya ga chos sdings spyi sa nas dpe cha sogs 'gel ba'i g.yag bcu dang bcas yong bar brtsams/ 'jam mgon bla ma gra pa rnams dang bcas pas
khang gsar lcags kha thug skyel ma la byon/ lcags khar gsol ja dang gnang sbyin 'bul ba sogs mang du byung / de nas lcags thon chu lho ru yang khang gsar nang nas ja 'bul
ba sogs dang / dmangs mas kyang mar krog snod du ma zhos

gang ba sogs skya chil le ba rten 'brel legs tshogs shin tu che ba dang / lpags na'i thang la gra pa mang pos rjes 'brang byas/ 'u cag dpon slob la 'di 'dra'i 'gyes 'bral yong
ba zer zhing mchi ma phyung mi shi ba bzhin byas/ pho brang gi la rtsa nas phyi mig bltas pas 'jam mgon bla ma gra pa rnams dang bcas pa lcags khan dmar phung nge bzhugs
'dug pas/ nged kyang sems skyo nas mchi ma mang du shor de nub sbu mar bsdad/ de nas pho brang lha rtser chos rgyal nam mkha' rgyal po bzhugs pa dang mjal/ gsol ja gnang
sbyin sogs shin tu bzabs pa rang mdzad de dgyes dgyes gnang / bya gshongs khri thog tu sngar yang khyed pas yon tan che ba med da dung yang mi yong gsung ba sogs zol
bstod mang po mdzad/ der zhag gnyis bsdad/ rim pas phyin tshes bcu drug la blo ba der ja dang tsha bzhes byas/ sngon chad gdan sa la bsu ba ser sbreng sogs kyi khyud mi 'dug
na'ang de'i tshe dpon slob rnams thugs dgyes pas bsu ba ser sbreng sogs mdzad de bya gshongs su sleb/ tshes bco brgyad la bza' tshes bzang bas bla brang / g.yas ru byang
/ rgyal mkhar rtse/ bsam rtse sogs nas bsko ja dang bcas te gdan sar bkra shis pa'i me tog dang bcas te bskos/ mnyan yod bya gshongs de na gso sbyong / dbyar gnas/ dgag
dbye sogs gzhi gsum gyi lag len rma med pa yod pas gnam gang la dgag dbye mdzad/ de'i phyi de tshes gcig nas ston cag dang po btsugs/ de yang 'dul ba'i gzhung las/ rgyal
dang dbo dang sa ga dang / /chu stod khrums smad smin drug bcas/ /zla phyed gso sbyong bcu bzhi pa/

/zhes gsungs pa ltar khrums kyi gso sbyong de gso sbyong bcu bzhi pa yin pas/ 'jig rten lugs kyi nyer dgu de/ mar ngo'i tshes zhag bco lnga par sleb pas de'i nyer dgu la byed
pa 'dul ba'i gzhung dang mthun zhing 'bum phrag gsum pa'i dgongs pa yin pas de ga bzhin rigs kyang paN chen shAkya mchog ldan pas/ gnam gang la byed gsung pa'i sgrub byed
gsungs pa'i sgrub byed ltar snang ba mang dag mdzad 'dug pa dang / kun mkhyen chos kyi rgyal po lcags thang pas kyang de ga bzhin mdzad 'dug pas/ deng sang mar ngo'i
gso sbyong 'jig rten lugs kyi gnam gang la mdzad pa 'di phyag len la 'dug go /kho bos kyang chos gra phyir sleb pa'i tshe dga' spro shin tu che ba la 'du khang nang du sleb
pa'i tshe blo shin tu mun pa sems la sdug bsngal skye ba sdod mi 'dod pa lta bu byung / rogs rnams kyis de 'dra'i sems khral ma byed/ thog 'di spo len byed pa tshegs mi
'dug zer te/ phyis 'du khang gsar bzhengs grub pa'i snga ltas su 'dug /dpal mnyan yod chos khri'i pad lte la/ /rang rkang sen nyi 'od shar ba'i mod/ /blo gsal ba'i bung
ba legs bshad kyi/ /ro dngar ba'i sbrang rtsi bcud myong lo/ /gnas sngon gyi khang rnying mun 'thibs par/ /yid sdug bsngal slong rkyen drag po yis/ /phyis dga' ldan pho
brang 'gran bzod pa'i/ /dri gtsang khang 'byung ba'i skya rengs shar/ /de'i tshe ston cag dang po la slob gnyer ba gra pa sha stag mang po byung ste/ 'ga' zhig dad 'dun gyi
nyan 'don pa dang / kha cig chos bshad ji ltar 'byung gi nyan rna lta bur 'dug kyang rang nyid la 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i bka' drin dang / blo dang

rtsol ba mi zhan tsam yod pa dang / khyad par ya ga chos sdings su 'chad nyan rgyun ring byed bzhin pa yin pa nas po ti phyi nang gang la yang 'chad rgyu thogs med yod pa dang
/ gdul bya dang 'tsham pa'i 'chad lugs kyang sa paNDitas/ /blo chen rnams la zab rgya che/ /blo chung bzung bde go bla ba/ /de las bzlog na mkhas rmongs kyi/ /gdul bya
dga' ba skyed mi nus/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gang la gang mtsham gyi 'chad lugs shes snyam pa'i rlom pa yang cung zad yod pas/ gdul bya blo gsal rgan gzhon phal che yang
blo kha tshim zhing dga' mgu yi rang pa kho na byung zer/ legs bshad rjes chags dmar ba yis/ /myos pa 'chad mkhas rta ljang can/ /'tshams sprin gos dmar gyis klubs pa'i/
/zhes pa dpe'i gzugs can no/ /'char ka'i nyi gzhon la ni 'gran/ /lha rnams lha yi bdud rtsi za/ /blo gsal mkhas pa'i legs bshad myong / legs bshad bdud rtsi dgra dang bral/
/bzlog pa'i dpe rgyan 'di myongs shig /de nas kho bos ston cig dang po chos zhag tshang bar btang / /de rjes shar gyi sbyin bdag so so la mjal 'phrad la chas rogs drung
rams pa nam mkha' rnam rgyal chos 'phel zer ba'i rtse chen rab 'byams pa/ mang thos rnam rgyal sogs yod/ shel dkar gyi thad de tsam sleb pa na byang 'khris kyi zhing chen
po zhig na shel dkar rgyal chen pa 'u lag pa mang po dang bcas btsas 'go la phebs 'dug pas sngar mjal ma myong yang nged la gzigs pas brgyang ring po nas phyag 'tshal
zhing byon/ 'u lag pa mang po yang phyag 'bul thibs thibs byung bas sna 'dren gyi rten 'brel bzang bsam pa shar/ shar skya rengs 'od kyi mdangs tsam gyis/ /gling bzhi pa
gsal byed 'od

brgya pa'i/ /sna drangs nas rtsi bcud nags tshal smin/ /kun bde la bkod pa'i rnam thar ltos/ /de nub gnas su phyin gnas pa gzim lags kyis sna len bzabs ma dang / sngar yid
gcugs kyi grogs ltar mthun pa'i gtam gleng mo bag phebs par smra ba byung ngo / /de nas snar thang du phyin snar thang gi ri klungs chags tshul chos sde'i lcags ri sogs mthong
bas sngar gyi bag chags sad pa lta bu'i sems dga' spro sing nge ba byung / snar thang sde pa dang mjal dus sde pa de gzugs bzang po yin mdog rnam po zhig mi 'dug kyang
/ chos lugs la 'bel gtam gyi bgro ba gleng dus mdo sngags gnyis car la gsung rgyu yod pa/ gsungs pa de yang phal cher don dang mthun pa/ phan tshun gcig la gcig dag snang
yid 'drongs pa byung / yul snar thang gi phun tshogs gling chen du/ /gtam chos smar gyi sde dpon chen dang mjal/ /chos legs bshad skyes kyi dga' ston spel/ /nged phan
tshun du dag snang gi mjal 'phrad legs/ /de'i tshe sku mdun zhing bzhag rdo rje bsam grub rtse na mi bzhugs 'dug pas shangs la 'gro dgos shar/ gru khar sleb mtshams nyang
stod nas drung chen rin rgyam pa sku mdun la mjal du 'gro ba dang 'dzom/ sngar mjal ma myong yang bya rgod gshongs kyi sred pas sngar mthun par 'grogs pa'i mdza' bo bzhin
du dga' spro shin tu che ba byung / de nas drung chen dang sdebs mo byas phyin de nub shangs kyi mda' der bsdad/ sang snga bar langs phyin pas rnam rgyal gling gi mdun
shangs sreg zhing gi thad du sleb tsa na/ sku mdun zhing de thugs gcag dag po zhig yin 'dug pas nged drung chen gnyis char la rta dang /

rta khal mang po yang yod pas drung 'khor zhig nged kyi gdong du btang byung nas khyed 'dir bstad pa zhig yin nam phyogs la thegs rgyu zhig yin/ 'dir bstad pa yin na gnyer
pa de bos shog gsung zer/ drung chen gyis 'di bzhin yin tshul dang 'di khar bstad pa yin tshul zhus pas mi de gnyer pa 'bod par thegs song / de nas rtser mjal du phyi rang
gi bsam pa la rang la chos kyi gtam cung zad smra rgyu yod de de ni sku mdun gyis mi dgongs/ sku mdun la 'jig rten gyi gtam gsung mdzad yod de ni nged kyis mi go zhing
de'i lan smra rgyu yang med legs legs 'bal 'jam mang po yang zhu mi shes/ nged gnyis rang mjal 'phrad legs po zhig e yong na bsam pa byung yang drung chen rin rgyam pas snyan
brjod mang po dang legs sbyor mang po zhus pas thugs yid 'drengs pa yin nam/ mjal ma khod shin tu 'phrod pa'i gsung gleng dang bcas zhag 'ga' bzhugs gsung na'ang bya
gshongs kyi dgun chos 'dzugs pa sogs dgag dgos chen po yod pas sang nyin phyin chog dgos zhus pas/de ltar na dgongs pa dang sbyor gsung gnang sbyin sogs shin tu bzabs pa
dang bcas sangs nyin snga bar yongs/ shangs kyi mda' shangs mthong smon gyi phyogs gcig la skyed tshal yangs po zhig na phyin shol po'i ra ba/ de'i nang na lcang dkar gyi
ra ba/ de'i nang na lcang smug pa'i ra ba/ de'i nang na me tog gi ra ba yod pa'i skyed tshal zhig tu tsha ba la sleb/ dpon skya des nang du shog zer nang du ja la bos/
phug na tshoms ka bzhi ma rten mchod dang bcas pa zhig lam kha nang smig rtse 'breng chags su yod pa'i mdzod so so'i nang nor gyi gang sgo thams cad gdangs nas bzhag /spro
seg shin

tu che ba zhig 'dug /nang na gdan bzang po bting mchod gnas dga' ldan pa'i gnas brtan bgres po zhig 'dug /gra sa so so dang chos sde so so'i lo rgyus rnams brjod khyad par
bkra shis lhun po nas ngam ring chos sder gra skor la yong pa'i gra skor pa rnams kyi lo rgyus dang / gra skor pa yon tan che ba zhig gis chos sde'i gung gral gyi gdong gral
gyi dbus na gral yod pa gong dkar ba'i slob dpon yin zer ba'i bla ma zhig la dbu ma la gzhung zhus 'jog gi tshe bshad pa lam pa dang / khyad par sa dga' ldan gyi grub
mtha' mi mthun pa yod tshul/ dga' ldan pa rnams kyi zer lugs 'di 'dra yod tshul/ de la gzhan phyogs kyi lung rigs kyi skyon brjod 'di ltar gtong tshul/ sa skya pa go shAka
'bum sogs kyi bzhed pa 'di ltar yin tshul/ de la gzhan phyogs kyi lung rigs kyis skyon 'di ltar brjod tshul/ de'i lan rig pa la ma khyab mtshams 'dir ru byed tshul/ lung
gi dgongs pa 'di ltar yin tshul sogs sil bur bshad song bas gra skor ba de 'jigs chum pa zhig byung / bgro gleng gtong rgyu yang dkon pa 'dra ba zhig gi ngang nas thal
'gyur gsum tsam 'phangs/ de nas dbu mdzad chen mo de langs nas mchong yar gyis kyi brda byed kyi 'dug pas de ga bzhin byas/ bgro gleng mang po'i 'gro ldog byed ma nus zer
ba sogs smra kyin 'dug pas / nged kyi rogs rnams kyis de'i bla ma de 'di ga yin byas pas khong dga' ste rjes su yi rang bsngags brjod mang po byed kyi 'dug /ja zhim po
sbyor gnyis tsam 'thur lo rgyus mang po byas/ rje sa skya paN chen gdan sa mchog /shangs sreg shing dpal gyi dgon pa na/ /bka' zab chos 'doms pa'i chos khri

yod/ /khong phyag bris ri mo khyad par can/ /dbu rgyab bstan bris pa'i ri mo ni/ /khong sa skya 'jam dbyangs zhal bstan nas/ /chos pha rol phyin pa'i snying po mchog /bka'
zhen pa bzhi bral 'doms so lo/ /khri de na sa paN bzhugs pa'i tshe/ /chos rnying ma phur pa rtsa ba'i dum/ /phyag padmar babs tshe spro ba skyes/ /sgra rol mo bcas te spyan
drangs zer/ /gnas de na bzhugs pa'i rten gyi mchog /rje 'phags pa'i gdung la 'khrungs pa yi/ /khong rgyal ba rigs lnga yod ces thos/ /yid dad mos phyag dang mchod pa phul/
/dpon zhing bzhag rdo rjer grags pa de/ /sngon bsod nams bsags pas las 'phro can/ /bod dbus gtsang sa la dbang sgyur zhes/ /rje grol mchog lung bstan thog tu babs/ /shangs
mthong smon nas ru bzhi ma'i gru khar phyin/ de nas gru mkhan ral tshar ba zhig 'dug pa de na re/ 'di pa'i dkyid na gru skya g.yob shes pa e yod zer/ nged kyi rogs
blo gros thogs med zer ba zhig yod pa des nged kyis shes zer/ de nas gru la phyin pas khos gru skya g.yob ma shes gru mkhan ngar langs te mi gces po bla ma dge ba'i bshes
gnyen 'di 'dra bzhugs bzhin du gru skya mi shes bzhin du ngas shes shes zer ba de khyod kyi ltas ngan shes pa i yin/ ngas a shes ma shes lta'i zer ba yong / ngas shes shes
de ltas ngan shes pa i yin zer nan gyis yang yang lab cing grub skya phrogs nya mo hor stag pa yin zer ba'i mi gzhon cig la sprad song ba des kyang shes po ma byung /
de nas tsha bo mang thos rnam rgyal gyis byas pas a tho byung gru thongs pa lags so/ /chu chen por gru yis brgal ba'i tshe/ /

gru'i mkhan po lcags kyi ral pa can/ /'dir gru skya shes pa yod dam zer/ /blo thogs med shes zer nga blo bde/ /las byas pas ma shes mgo bo 'khor/ /gru'i mkhan po blo 'khrugs
tshig rtsub smra/ /sku gces pa bla ma bzhugs bzhin du/ /nges shes zhes rdzun tshigs ham gtam smra/ /khyod ltas ngan tsam zhig shes sam ci/ /shes mi shes lta zhes smra na
rung / /nges shes zhes ham tshig smra ba po/ /tshig 'di 'dra phyin chad ma smra zer/ /de nas phung po ri bo che'i thang chen po brgal stag grub kha la byas/ khyi 'phrang
rdo them gyi 'phrang dog mo bshags rgya po'i pho brang gzhis ka rin spungs su sleb/ de dus sde srid dbus dmag 'khor 'phral chab srid dar zhing rgyas pa go 'phang mtho ba'i
skabs rang yin te rin spungs rang na bzhugs 'dug mjal phrad thugs shin tu dgyes pa byung / khyed yon tan gyi grags pa chen po 'dug pas lcags thang rab 'byams pa lta bu'i
'chad nyan zhig rgyob shog gsung ba sog bka' bkod bslab bya mthil phyin pa gnang / byang la rings pa'i stabs kyi zhag po gsum min pa sdod skabs ma byung de nas yar lam
g.yung la byas g.yung la bud tsam de na 'brog yul rtsa kha bzang po byas pa zhig 'dug pas der bsdad pas kha ba chen po babs rogs rtse chen pa drung rams pa chos 'phel zer
ba des bla ma rin po che 'brog pa ru song bas thugs dgyes rang dgyes drags yod zer bzhad gad thag ge bsdad/ lha brgya byin gnas la co 'dri ba'i/ /bod rin cen spungs pa'i
pho brang mthong / /mi ngag dbang 'jigs bral spyan zur 'dzum/ /thugs dgyes pa'i bka' mchid mang du dar/ /g.yung la rtser ja skol mangs ba'i

mthus/ /la brgal tsam la sa skos 'bro bzang der/ /phyugs rta rnams skyid nas gcer nyal byed/ /nged mi rnams ra bar me lha mchod/ /yul kha ba bu yug mun ltar 'tshub/ /khyed
'brog rigs rnams la 'di rang skyid/ /thugs dgyes sam zer zhing grogs po rnams/ /nyams bzhad gad thag ge mtshan ring bsdad/ /nam langs tsa na kha ba yang chad nged rnams kyi
lhan skyes kyi mdun tshul chen zer ba der tsha ran la sleb/ tshul chen de na sngon dpal ldan sa skya pa'i yin zer ba'i lha khang zhig na rigs lnga bzhengs sku mi tshad
tsam pa rgyas sku shin tu legs pa rnams mjal/ de nyin dpal 'khor chos sder sleb/ bar tsho shag zer ba'i sngon drung chen rin rgyam pa'i gzims khang spro mo zhig tu bsdad/
de na thub bu chos mdzad zer ba'i phyug po ban gzugs can snang ba bde mo byas pa zhig 'dug pa des bya gshongs pa'i phyogs zhen gyis sna len shin tu bzabs pa byas/ de nas
rgyal mkhar rtser sde pa sku mched dang mjal yar tshugs bzang ba bsgrigs bkod ma nyams pa nyi ma'i grib tshod 'phyugs med kyi bkod pa ngo mtshar ba 'dug /sde srid che ba
des rje dam pa la gsung ngag thob pa yin 'dug pas lam dus 'chag med mdzad zer/ kho bo la shib bu'i tshul gyis deng sang phyogs 'di la lam 'bras yongs rdzogs thob zer/ 'o
na sgrub pa lung sbyin thob bam byas pas de 'dra rna bas ma thos zer/ 'di 'dra dag ci yin pa 'dug gi gsung / bdag gis slob ma nyams chung rnams la bla mas 'khrid rkyang
shar re ba re gnang des lam 'bras rdzogs so gsungs pa de la 'khrul pa yin mchis zhus/ de nas li ma lha khang gi rten mchod ngo mtshar ba rnams dang / khyad par rgyal

po ma skyes dgra'i gdung skal yin zer ba'i sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung/ tsandan dkar po'i dri gtsang khang gi dbus na shel bum gyi nang na bzhugs pa de dang / 'phags pa'i dngul
sku rgya nag ma dang / zi khyim las grub pa'i dril bu rtse lnga ma chung ba dang / theg chen ma che ba gnyis skad shin tu bzang ba dang / rgya zhwa rigs lnga ma dang
/ gzhan yang tsandan sogs kyi lde gu las grub pa'i 'phags pa'i phyag 'phreng / dgang gzar/ dgang blugs gser tshags dngul tshags ma/ spos rgya'i bar gser tshags dngul tshags
ma sogs ngo mtshar ba shin tu mang ba dang mjal/ shar rgyal mkhar rtse yi pho brang du/ /rigs chos rgyal sde srid mched dang mjal/ /sku yar gcod sgal tshigs bzang na
yang / /thugs bag phebs gsung gi bka' mchid 'jam/ /rten li ma lnga yi zhal sgo nas/ /gsung lhang lhang smra bar ma nus te/ /sku mdzes pa'i rnam 'gyur mnyen lcug ldem/ /gsung
smra 'dod zhal mchu 'dzum me bzhugs/ /zhes pa rnam phra'i rgyan te/ rten ngo mtshar can rnams kyis gsung byon pa min yang sku mdzes pa'i rnam 'gyur bzo khyad ngo mtshar
bas dngos mjal lta bu'i gsung chos thob pa dang 'dra ba'i dga' ba khyad par can skyes shes pa'o/ /sde pa sku mched gnyis car gyis gnang skyes gya nom pa dang / khyad par
sde pa rnam par rgyal bas zur du sgos mjal gnang / bya gshongs pa la khyad par du bdag rkyen gnang ba zhig 'dug pas sgos kyi gnang skyes sogs shin tu dgyes pa mdzad/ gzims
shag tu dpon sa brag kha ma dang mjal thugs shin tu grol ba'i gsung 'phros dang / 'bul skyes sogs legs tshogs shin tu

che ba byung ngo / /de nas chos sder yongs rten mjal rags pa tsam dang / sku drung blo gros pa zer ba'i chos sde'i chos khrims bya gshongs pa yin pa des bsnyen bkur 'bul skyes
shin tu bzabs pa mdzad/ de nas pho brang rtse chen du 'gro ba'i tshe bya gshongs phyogs kyi bla ma slob dpon gra pa drag pa rnams kyis rta khrom shin tu bzabs pa dang
/ rang re'i rtse chen phyogs kyi slob gnyer ba rnams kyis ser sgreng / sgra rol cha sogs kyi bsu ba byas pho brang rtse chen du sleb/ sde pa yum sras dang blon chen sde
pa 'tsho lags sogs dang mjal/ de snga rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa dang mjal phrad tsam ma gtogs yon mchod shin tu 'brel che ba rang ma byung 'dug cing / khyad par chos
dbar zhig la gdan 'dren mdzad rtsis phebs par zhal gyis bzhes nas phyag thog ma bkal bas thugs cung zad 'gal ba tsam byung ba yin pa 'dra zer/ 'on kyang rtse nas gnang
skyes sogs bdag rkyen shin tu bzabs pa mdzad/ 'tsho lags drung chos sde'i gra khang zhig tu phebs nas gsol ja 'bul skyes sogs dang / bya gshongs pa gra sa dngos gtsang rang
du 'dug pas chos dbar zhig la gdan 'dren 'dod yod gsung ba tsam 'dug /ri mthon po rtse chen pho brang du/ /rigs btsun po kun bzang yab sras mjal/ /byang rnam sras 'byor
par 'thab cing 'phya/ /rdzas longs spyod chos phyir gtong la dge /khong rgyal po'i blon po lhag bsam can/ /de bdag drung ched du gtad pa 'di/ /thugs dad 'dun lus kyi ba
spu'i tshogs/ /rigs sad nas ci yang g.yo ba'i rtags/ /zhes che'i rgyan no/ /de nas pho brang 'brong rtser phyin/ 'brong rtse hor rtse'i

sras bsod nams dpal 'phel drung dang mjal/ bzhugs gral du ja mchod che ba'i che mchog ma gyis gsung ba dang / gzhan yang bya gshongs kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i mtshan bstod sogs
byas/ dag snang thugs spro ba dang snyed bkur shangs len sogs dngos gtsang ba mdzad/ pho brang 'brong rtse spos ngad ldan ri ru/ /'dod yon gur gum spos kyi 'phreng ba dngar/
/dri la chags pa'i skyes phran bung ba'i tshogs/ /rnam g.yeng rlung gis g.yo ba med gyur cig /de nas chu shar la thon nyang stod stag rtse ru sleb/ sde pa stag rtse
chos mdzad pa dang mjal 'ar 'ur gyi gsung 'phros mang po dang thugs dkar ba'i bsnyen bkur dang 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung / yul stag rtse mkhar mig btsan po na/
/stag dpa'o mi yi seng ge bzhugs/ /gsung 'ar 'ur snyan dang mi snyan sgrog /sems dkar ba'i 'ur shom glu las snyan/ /de nas tshong 'dus khri khang du gra lnga nyin byed dbang
po dang mjal chos kyi 'bel gtam dang gang ci'i gsung gleng bag phebs pa gnang / de'i tshe gzims khang ka brgyad ma shin tu legs pa zhig 'dug pa der bzhugs gral bsgrigs
bzhugs gral na gser mdog can pa'i chos rje jo ba sogs gra ba 'ga' yar 'dug /gra lnga'i zhal nas da bgro gleng zhig mdzad dgos gsung / kho bos po ti so so la bshad pa lam
pa dang dogs gcod dang bcas pa'i dam bca' yod tsam byas/ jo bos bgro gleng btang grub mtha' so so'i gnad ma rig pa'i nga rgyal gyis phar mchong tshur mchong mang po byed
kyin 'dug /kho bos grub mtha'i gnad ma rig pa'i phyogs re'i mig can ma mdzad grub mtha'i gnad 'di ltar yin zhes zhib gsed mang du bya pas nga rgyal

zhi nas bsdad song / phyis sras che ba lhun chen dang mjal dus khong de 'dra mdzad pa zhig yod a lags kyang nya stong gi gso sbyong 'chag med mdzad pa la/ khong gis de la gso
sbyong gi sdom pa ni mi chags phan yon med zer ba byas pas phyis bcag nas da lta mi mdzad yod gsung ste de grub mtha'i skyon yin/ mkhas pa shAkya mchog ldan pas so thar
rigs brgyad la nyan thos cho gas blangs pa zhig dgos gsungs pa des 'khrul bar snang ste/ sdom gsum las/ byang chub sems dpa' nyid la yang / /so sor thar pa 'bogs pa yi
/ /cho ga 'ga' zhig yod mod kyi/ /de yi cho ga phal cher nub/ /gso sbyong rang gis blangs pa sogs/ /cho ga'i lag len 'ga' zhig yod/ /ces gsungs pa de spyan gyis gzigs kyang
thugs rnam dpyod kyis ma phyed pa'i skyon chen po ste/ de na da lta'i cho ga ni/ /bsam pa sems bskyed kyis zin pa'i/ /cho ga nyan thos lugs bzhin gyis/ /zhes pa des paN
chen pa thugs 'khrul bar snang mod lung de'i don ni/ dge bsnyen pha ma dang / dge tshul pha ma'i sdom pa rang gis blangs chog pa'i theg chen thun mong ma yein pa'i cho
ga zhig yod pa de nub nas med pas de rnams dang / dge slong pha ma'i sdom pa sogs nyan thos cho gas blang dgos zhes pa'i don yin gyi/ don yod zhags pa nas bshad pa'i theg
chen thun mong ma yin pa'i cho ga la brten nas bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa chags par gsal bar bshad kyi/ des cho ga'i go mi chod gsung ba dngos shugs gang las kyang ma bshad
'dug pa'i phyir dang / ci ste de la brten nas sdom pa mi chags su chug na yang blangs pa la phan yon med pa ma yin te/ mdzod rang 'grel las/ gal te de ltar na shan

pa dang byi byed pa dag gis nyin mo dang mtshan mo'i bsnyen gnas kyang 'bras bu yod par rung ngo zhes/ spyir bye smra lugs la nyin zhag ma tshang bar bsnyen gnas kyi sdom pa
mi chags kyang nyin mo tsam dang mtshan mo tsam bsnyen gnas blangs kyang phan yon med pa ma yin te/ bsnyen gnas sdom pa mi chags kyang legs spyad kyi dge ba yin pa'i phyir
zhes pa 'di zur tsam yang ma dgongs 'dug pa'i phyir/ spyir gra lnga nyin byed dbang po 'di kho bo gra sa 'dzin pa la shin tu bka' drin che ste/ lo star gyi 'jam thal
nyis brgya re sgo skyel gnang / lo gnangs chags kyis mjal du 'gro de skabs lhag por nyis brgya tsam re gnang / zhal nas kyang khyed khor khor 'byon pa 'di zhib thal slong
ba 'ba' zhig yin/ khyed rang dpon slob rdo bcal khar gshegs la bsngo ba zhig mdzod dang zhes nyams ldan yang gsung ngo / /rdzong tshong 'dus dbu rtse'i pho brang na/ /mchog
spyod ldan gra lnga nyin byed bzhugs/ /lugs gnyis la mkhyen pa'i spyan ras gsal/ /blo 'khyog bral tshad mar 'dzin pa yod/ /sngon las ngan smin pa'i mthu lhags na/ /yab
rgyal khab gzugs can snying po de'ang / /gnas phyag sbal nang gi mgron la btang / /pho ma skyes ma yin las kyi mthu/ /de nas snar thang / de nas gnas/ de nas bya rgod gshongs
su 'gyogs par sleb/ de nas g.yas ru byang la mjal 'phrad la phyin sde srid rnams ngam ring na bzhugs pa dang mjal/ shar phyogs la phyin pa'i lo rgyus dang skabs su
'bel gtam dogs dpyod sogs 'phel bar byung / lho ma la ya rlung gis reg pa'i/ /byang rigs ldan chos kyi pho brang cher/ /chos sgra sgrog nam yang mi chad pa'i/

/ngo mtshar ba'i chos rgyal mched rnams mjal/ /dmag ru mtshon bkod pa'i mchor sgeg dang / /sde phas rgol gzhom pa'i 'ur sding sogs/ /khong 'jig rten gzhan snang mi che yang
/ /sngon chos rgyal lugs bzhin sa chen skyong / /de nas nged rang gis sbyin bdag bya mchu nang du phyin sbyin bdag 'di tshang kho bo chos sgor zhugs phyin nas bu bzhin du
skyong / chos gling slob dpon/ ya ga chos sdings slob dpon sogs skabs thams cad du gus zhen che zhing / mkho ba'i yo byad bsgrub pa zhig yin pas der zhag 'ga' bsdad/ tshe
bka' sogs dbang rjes gnang mang du byas/ de nas nged rang gi 'brog sde rnams bu le'i rgyab 'di na bsdad yod zer 'bod du byung / dus sngon gyi sbyin po dad pa brtan/ /nged
gzhon dang dar babs rgan gyi bar/ /rdzas rnyed dang bkur sti'i mchod la brtson/ /khyed bu nor longs spyod dar babs shog /de nas bu le'i rgyab gangs kyi zil mngar char
bzhin 'babs pa'i gnas na la rtse zhes par sleb/ nged rang gi gnyen 'khor g.yog rigs rnams kyis dbang zhu byas/ dad 'bul gyi gser zho bco lnga skor dang / bya gshongs su
dkar me dang / ja sdor sogs la phan zer nas 'bri ma bu bdun cu skor zhig byin/ de nas 'brog sde dang bsdebs rgya tshor sleb/ de nas la la yongs pas nged rang gi tsha yug
dang sring mo sogs gzhon gzhon 'dras ngu tshi byed cing skyel ma la yong / nged kyi rogs rnam rgyal klu sgrub zer ba des kyang skad ston cing mchi ma phyung / de nas sman
gyi sbubs la byas 'dar skyid gshongs su sleb/ sred zhags pas bcings pa'i gnyen dang 'khor/ mar zho dar 'dzoms pa'i 'brog pa'i sdes/ /'phral yun du mkho ba'i longs spyod

stobs/ /'bral mi phod mchi mas skyel ma byas/ /de nas bya gshongs su dgun chos dang po 'dzugs pa la zhag gsum las med pa nyer bdun la sleb/ /gnam gang la kun mkhyen chos kyi
rgyal po'i dus mchod bla brang rang nas mang ja gtong dgos/ tshes gcig la bsdus gra ba dang / mi snas chos gtor dgongs phyogs/rigs 'bring lung 'bring pa'i rigs lung tshes
gnyis kyi snga dro rnam rgyal/ 'jam thon nas snga chos kyi rim pa la thog mar dpal gang drin ma/ rnam sras gtor chog /de nas tshad ma'i TIkka rigs 'bring yan la/ der rjes
phar phyin gyi TIkka lung 'bring yan la/ de nas 'dul ba'i 'go nas gzhung 'grel dang brda chad dogs gcod/ de rjes tshad ma'i rigs chen pa yan la zin thun byed dgos/ thog
mar rnam 'grel gyi gzhung gi thog ma nas gzhung 'grel dogs gcod dang bcas pa rang lugs kyi brda chad rnam gzhag /rigs pa'i sgo nas dgag sgrub kyi mtha' gcod pa'i rigs
pa'i 'phreng ba/ de nas lung chen pa yan la phar phyin zur bkol la thog mar gzhung 'grel rang lugs brda chad/ dgag sgrub kyi mtha' bcad pa'i rig pa/ de nas po ti phyi ma
yan la mngon pa mdzod kyi gzhung gang yin pa gzhung 'grel/ rang lugs kyi brda chad/ dgag sgrub kyi thal 'gyur/ de nas rigs chen/ lung chen/ po ti phyi mo ba rnams gyes/ de
nas rigs chung ba rnams/ de rjes lung chung pa rnams/ de rjes bsdus gra ba tsho bzhi/ de snga chos gnyis pa rigs chen pa nas bsdus gra'i bar/ de nas gung tshigs/ dgongs
chos la dpal gang drin ma/ dmag zor gtor bsngo/ de rjes tshad ma dang phar phyin TIkka/ de nas 'dul ba'i spyir bstan gzhi

smad sogs la sngar bzhin/ der rjes rigs che 'bring / de rjes lung che 'bring / de rjes po ti phyi ma'i/ de rjes dbu ma la sngar bzhin/ de nas po ti phyi ma gyes/ de nas rigs
chung / de nas lung chung / de nas bsdus grwa pa rim pa bzhi/ de nas dgongs chos gnyis pa la rigs che 'bring / lung che 'bring / de nas bsdus gra ba rim pa bzhi rnams rim
bzhin/ de nas dgongs mo'i chos spyod de grol nas rigs lung rnams kyi rim pa 'phyug med du yod pa yin no/ /de'i tshe dge 'dun rnams chos nyan pa la brod pa che zhing spro
ba che bas yid bzhin gyi nor bu mthong ba la sus thob byed pa bzhin chos nyan pa la sus thob byed cing rgyug 'dral byed/ rjes ma rnams snga ma'i steng du brtsegs shing
nyan/ nyan ma thag skyong ltar 'ur zing re ba byed mdor na nyin mtshan du skyong ltar dang rigs lung gi 'ur sgra dir re bas nyin mtshan dus 'da'/ rang la 'chad nyan byed
rgyu yod phyin 'di lta bu ru 'chad nyan byed pa ni tshe don yod yin snyam pas 'chad pa po spro/ nyan pa po nyan pa la sun pa med pas lung rigs bstan pa la bya ba byas pas
bla ma gong ma thugs dgyes shing / chos skyong srung mas bar chad sel ba'i stong grogs mdzod cig ces smon lam 'debs pa la brtson par gnas so/ /dpal mnyan yod chos grwa'i
dga' tshal du/ /khong blo gsal don gnyer kho na la/ /chos legs bshad sbrang char zim pa 'di/ tshe don yod yin zhes spro ba 'phel/ /legs bshad 'chad pa'i 'od brgya spros
pa las/ /gzhung lugs padma'i 'dab stong kha phye ste/ /zab don sbrang rtsi'i ro dang dri bzang gis/ /blo gsal bung ba tshim byed bla ma'i drin/ /don ma go tshigs tshogs
chos 'chad mkhan/ /rang 'o brgyal gzhan gyi blo gros 'gag /rang

nges pa rnyed pa'i legs bshad gtam/ /gzhan blo gros kha 'byed 'chad na mkhas/ /tshigs bcad dang sbugs zhugs 'phongs shor sogs/ /don bar zhun yin zhes 'chad rnams 'khrul/ /gzhung
nges pa rnyed pa'i rigs pa'i 'phreng / /gzhan rgol ba 'jom mkhas bar zhun yin//dbyar chos gra phyir chos 'chad kyi tshe/ chos khri lho zhes pa thog med pa zhig na chos
'chad byed dgos 'dug pas/ rang lus ngan pa la sa gzhi'i gnod pa yong ba ma bzod nas/ na tshod ldan zhes pa shing mo phag gi lo chos khri gsar pa thog 'bubs legs pa/ de'i
mdun du rdo bcal dang bcas pa thebs/ snga dro zhig drung rams pa zla 'od zer ba zhig byung nas/ sngar rin spungs nas bkod ja zhu ma thub 'dug pas 'di khag chen po yin
che bgres mi sna rang la skor yang e rigs zer byung/ che bgres mi sna rang la glengs pas gra pa gnyis bang chen la dmigs yod zer/ nged kyi zhu yig snyan ngag byas pa zhig
bskur nas btang bas shin tu mnyes/ bkod ja bkod yig dang bcas gnang / khyed rang skor cig 'phral du sleb pa gyis gsung ba phebs/ che bgres mi sna rnams bsags rin spungs
nas bka' shog 'di bzhin 'dug pa phyin na dpyid chos la dor yod pa 'dra ci ltar legs byas pas/ dpyid chos chos thog gcig chag na'ang phugs gra sa la khyed che bas byon pa
legs zer dpon slob kha cig mgyogs bshad phyin sde srid shin tu dgyes/ sku gzhogs na snar thang byang chen gyi mkhan po yin pa'i gser mdog can pa 'phags pa lha zer ba zhig
'dug /sde srid zhal nas sngar bod kha ba can du bstan pa dpang du btsugs pa'i rtsod pa byed mkhan rgyal po khri srong lde

btsan gyis dbang mdzad/ ka mA la shrI la dang / hwa shang gnyis tsam dang / de rjes sa paNDita dang / 'phrog byed dga' ba gnyis ma gtogs ma byung 'dug /rnam gnyis kyis kyang
gzhung lugs rnam dag la 'bel ba'i gtam cung zad rigs pa 'dra gsung / nged gnyis kyis bgro gleng gi ku co chen po ni ma byas/ byang chen pas dus 'khor la brten nas sangs
rgya ba ma gtogs/ rgyud sde gzhan la brten nas sangs rgyas ba med zer ba sogs mang zhig gleng gin 'dug /kho bos de skad mi gsung ba zhu de dpal ldan sa skya pa'i grub mtha'
ni min/ brtag pa gnyis pa las/ gang gis mi shes kye rdo rje/ /de yis ngal ba don med yin/ /zhes gsungs kyang de'i don dgyes pa rdo rje'i lam ma yin pa/ bla med kyi lam
gzhan la brten nas sangs rgya ba med zer ba rje btsun gong ma'i dgongs pa la med de'i don gang yin snyam na/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i thugs dag pa gnyis ldan gyi chos dbyings
de lta bu ni nges don gyi 'bras bu'i kye rdo rje yin pas de lta bu ma rtogs na 'tshang mi rgya zhes pa'i don yin/ dus 'khor rgyud dang rgyud 'grel las/ dus 'khor la ma brten
par sangs mi rgya zer ba lta bu'i tshig yod na'ang rgyud de'i che ba brjod pa tsam yin gyis grub mthar khas len pa ma yin zhes sogs zhib tu bshad do/ /de dus ngag dbang
'jigs bral sa paN gyi rnam thar rtogs brjod rtsom pa'i skabs yin pas snyan ngag la dogs gcod shin tu mang ba byung / rje grangs chen pas kho bo la byung ba'i snyan ngag
cig yod pa de gzigs phul bas a tho 'dug mtshan nyid pa spyi ba las drag tsam gsungs/ kho bos chos rje grangs chen pa la phul ba'i snyan ngag cig yod pa de gzigs phul bas
thugs dgyes/ de'i nang tshan shlo ka gcig

la gong ra lo tsA ba dang gnyis kas 'di 'dra shin tu legs gsungs nas/ sngon la bstan bcos rtsom pa po rang gi 'bru rgyob gsung kho bos 'bru rgyab/ sde srid nas de la 'bru khyad
par ba 'di lta bu zhig yong ba 'dug gsung 'bru zhig gnang / gong ra lo tsA bas de las kyang ches khyad par du 'phags pa'i 'bru zhig ngas brdeg gsungs nas 'bru zhig gnang
de sogs shin tu dgyes dgyes mdzad/ yang skabs shig rang re rtsom pa su mgyogs lta'o gsungs/ sde srid kyis gcig brtsams/ yar 'brog stag lung pas gcig brtsams/ gong ra
lo tsA bas gcig brtsams/ kho bos de myur bar brtsams/ sde srid kyi bris gsub mang po dgos pa la shin tu legs/ stag lung pas bdag gi de tsam mi yong gsungs/ skabs su babs
tsam gong ra lo tsA bas dpag bsam 'khri shing sogs gzhung gi 'bru brdeg pha la shin tu dngos gtsang ba/ brdeg lugs nyams 'char ba/ rtsom la thugs yus po rang mi gnang bzhugs
gral phal cher rtsom res kyis dus 'da'/ gsol gyi bzhugs gral dpon sa'i drung du yong zhing 'phros gleng pa sogs stag lung pas mdzad cing / lugs gnyis car la sku yon
shin tu che/ rang re la'ang bya gshongs pa'i sbyin bdag gi zhen gyis mthong bdag rkyen yang dag mdzad/ zhag bzhi lnga bsdad sde srid kyi gnang sbyin dar gos ja rdum/ ring
'gags shin tu legs pa/ dpon sa'i drung gis dar gos sogs gzan rong gi phrug po che shin tu dngos gtsang ba/ mtsher ja/ yar lam gyi lam brgyags/ lam ja/ ja sdor sogs yang
dag pa gnang / gnas rin spungs gangs can mdzes pa'i rir/ /mchog rgyal rigs tsandan dkar

po'i nags/ /dpal yal 'dab bskyod pa'i dri bsung gis/ /kun dga' ba bskyed par byed 'di mtshar/ /ces gzugs can gyi rgyu rgyan no/ /khyod zhal zla 'od shar bas rang gi 'khor/
/padma dkar po'i kha bye 'dod dgu yi/ /sbrang rtsi bcud zhim 'thungs pas phyogs kun gyi/ /bung bas glu dbyangs sgrog 'di rna ba'i rgyan/ /de nas bya gshongs su sleb/ phag
lo dgag dbye'i bsnyen bkur 'degs pa la bkras 'dzom mi dbang nam mkha' dpal 'byor rang phebs/ de snga mjal ma myong yang 'jam dkar gyi rjes gnang zhu ba gnang bsnyen bkur
gya nom pa mdzad/ de nas bzung da'i bar du thugs yid gcig tu 'dres mi 'phrog pa'i dad pa thob pa'i sbyin bdag legs pa'i gos zhim pa'i bza' ba yid du 'ong ba'i ja/ snying
nye ba'i gros sogs kyis sems la gcags pa'i sbyin bdag rang du gyur ba yin no/ /grogs med gcig pur ri bong can 'od kyis/ /phan bde'i skyed tshal bzhad par ma nus te/ /dad
ldan sbyin po'i brtse gdungs 'od brgya pas/ /phan bde'i dpal 'byor pad tshal rgyas so snyam/ /de dus gnas gsar nas bo dong la bzhugs pas 'phral rje tshar chen gyi slob ma
yin pas gus zhabs che snyam pa la/ phugs ruu nga bas gtser ba re mang bas blo mtsher dung nge ba byung / 'on kyang sde pa sras po deng sang chos mdzad pa 'dis thugs bsam
rnam par dag pa gnang / byi lo byang nas chos rgyal mched kyang lha dbang rtser phebs rtsod dus kyi rang gzugs shig ston pa 'dra zer shub bur 'dug /gdong dga' nas zhabs
drung chos rje lha dbang rtse nas bya gshongs su phebs sngar mjal ma myong yang thugs bag phebs pa'i gsung gleng mang

po mdzad/ sa skya steng 'og gdong dga' spe chung sogs pa 'di mdzod gsung ba'i bslab ston dang / khyad par bde gzar gyi 'phros bo dong phyogs su skyon cung zad yong ba 'dug
gsung de ga bzhin ston de bo dong du dmag gi mthil phab/ gnas gsar nas la bya gshongs su bskyas zhag gnang dgos byung / rtsa ba byang rang gi bzhad mthong smon nas yin pa'i
mdo sde po ti sum cu sogs dang / gzhan phyag rdzas gces pa 'dra bya gshongs bla brang dang gtsug lag khang du bcol mo mdzad/ de nas bdag gi sngar gser gser zho gang tsam
snga 'phrul phul yod pas gzims dpon nags kha ba brgyud nas sngar 'di 'dra zhig yod de de ni zhu spob pa mi 'dug /gra sa la phan pa'i rdzas 'dra zhus nas e khyab zhus pas
de los yong dgongs pa la gang 'dug zer/ dge sdings nas drangs pa'i rdo lha mtho re ba 'dra 'dug de zhu byas pas/ dpon sa yum drung gis de ga 'bul spro gsung / de ma thag
gra pa rnams bskul nas gnas khang so so na yod pa rnams chos rje a 'byor ba la dris nas tshang ma 'dren thub/ de yang mtshams su khel te cung 'phyis na bya gshongs su
yong ba'i tshad du mi 'dug khong rnams phebs skyel la khrom mda' bkra shis rtse thug kho bos kyang phyin nged yon mchod rnams rdzing lung gi'i gdong der sleb tsam nas sgra
chen po brag ral ba 'dra zhig byung ste/ phyis brtags na khong rnams la ngan pa'i ltas yin pa 'dra bsam/ snga sor rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i skabs su phra ma ba
sogs kyi 'go byas pa'i dmag gi dpon drung g.yungs pa bya gshongs gtsug lag khang gi steng du bkrong / gling so so la gnod pa chen po byas

che yang bya gshongs mgon khang mgon chen gyi shangs nas khrag mang po brdol/ dpon drung dkrong mkhan shangs pa rta mchog zer ba de gtsang po la gzings rdib nas 'das/ dro khud
bsam rgyal la nad ngan pa byung / bya gshongs nas thob ba nom pa'i lugs su byas pa'i kun mkhyen lcags thang pa'i thugs dam dmag zor ma'i gos thang la me 'bar/ bsten ma
nus par thang kha ja ldum sogs dngos spyad rnams bya gshongs su skyel du byung nas thang kha de deng sang rje sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan pa'i gzims khang rnam rgyal rtse
na yod/ bya gshongs nas tshogs dung dmag mi zhig gis khyer nas rong tsho'i ko ba la phyin pa dung gis skad bton pa phyis bya gshongs su phul 'dug /dmag mi'i gtso bo phra
ma ba sogs la'ang gnod pa chen po byung / lo 'di la yang phyag drug pa'i mgon khang du phyag drug sbrul zhag nas khrag 'dzag pa sogs cho 'phrul che tsam byung ngo / /dus
me pho byi ba'i bgrang bya la/ /yul bo dong sa yi thig le ru/ /yul bdag po 'pho 'phyugs dus gcig 'dzom/ /khong zla nyi 'pho 'phyug rten 'brel gshis/ /zla shel bsil zer gyi
reg padma'i kha/ /zum pas zhal skyengs shar ri'i 'phangs pa nas/ /nyi gzhon spyan drangs pad dkar bzhad pa'i ros/ /bung ba rgyags tshe khyung la 'gran bzod tsam/ /de nas
zhabs drung bkra shis stobs rgyas drung dang / bkras 'dzom mi dbang sogs kyis nyer sbyar nas khyed rang yang chos gzhis shig zhu ru byon na legs gsung / bdag rogs dang
bcas pas mgyogs par phyin chos rgyal kun dga' rin cen la gsol ja zhus 'bul bya dar gos ras sogs dang / nged rang gi kar dril rtse lnga ma/ mkhar rnga zhig rnams

phul bas mkhar rnga ma gtogs gzhan ni ma bzhes/ khyed gra sa dngos gtsang rang yin pas chos gzhis shig rigs gsungs nas bstan pa la phan pa'i lhag bsam thugs la bcangs nas/
shag blo ba bdag pa'i sa zhing sa skor dang bcas pa/ mnyan phug pa'i khang zhing / bon gnas zer ba'i grod g.yog dang bcas pa sogs bka' drin tshad med pa bskyangs/ chos rgyal
nor lha'i bu des bshad gra'i sder/ /dge 'dun gsos kyi 'tsho ba'i rkyen sman sbyar/ /pha rol stobs ldan sa 'og rim par bcings/ /rab dkar snying stobs dpung des yin nam
snyam/ gzugs can phul byung rab brtags kyi rgyan no/ /nag phyogs bdud kyi ru mtshon dpung brnyil nas/ /dkar phyogs srung mas rgyal mtshan ba dan bsgreng / /legs bshad chos
kyi rnga chen phyogs brgyar brdungs/ /mnyan yod bstan pa dar ba de nas byung / /de nas chos gzhis rnams rtsis len dus chos rgyal nor bu lags drung du bo dong phyag tu
byung 'dug pas phyag g.yog 'dras bsgyur kha la brten gnang yig nang bzhin grangs 'grig ma byung / rang gi bsam tshod la phyag g.yog rnams thugs bsam chung bas lan sde srid
la ni de tsam gyi gnod cher mi 'dug /bo dong 'di byang ba'i phyag tu rgyun chags yong pa yang dka'/ bya gshongs la gnang na sde srid su'i phyag tu byung kyang 'jags 'gro
ba 'dug ste bsam/ gzhan bsam pa ngan pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /yar sde srid go 'phang la gnod cing/ /mar rang nyid ngan 'gror mgyogs pa'i rkyen/ /ri mthon po'i rbab bzhin sgril
ba mthong / /rjes nas sde srid yid bzhin nor bus kyang chos gzhis la khral 'u lag sogs gtser ba gtan nas mi yong ba'i

phyag rtags shin tu btsan pa gnang / 'go 'dren bdag rkyen yang dag mdzad/ dbang phyug ces pa me mo glang la rtse chen la chos dbar gdan 'dren gyi pho nya yang byung / bo dong
gi drag rigs 'ga' zhig bya gshongs kyi grwa ris khyad par can 'di shar la gtong ba mi rigs/ rang re bo dong gi sa bcud nyams 'gro zer ba yang byung 'dug /rang re'i nyang
stod kyi grwa ris rnams kyang sngar yang chos dbar la phebs pa zhal gyis bzhes nas ma phebs pa de 'phyugs cung zad byung / da lan phyag tu khel ba zhig dgos so zer nan
gyi byung / de nas bya gshongs dgun chos dang po btang / chos mtshams la lha khang gsar pa bcu gcig zhal rnam sras mdung dmar can gyi lha khang sogs la dkar me lha bshos
phul/ bla brang nas zhogs ja bzang po zhig btang / slob gnyer ba nyis brgya tsam na bza' bzabs pa dpe khres 'ding lhung sogs dang bcas 'phreng byas bo dong e la g.yas skor
byas phyin pas gzhan gyi smon pa'i gnas su byed pa byung / de nub shel dkar du sleb shel dkar nang nas mang ja sogs bzabs par byung / dkar phyogs zla ba rgyas pa'i dus
tshes la/ /mnyan yod chos kyi skyed tshal ldum ra nas/ /shar phyogs rtse chen 'dod dgu'i pho brang du/ /chos kyi legs bshad gtam zer lam du chas/ /de nas khro phur spyan
'dren byung sang nyin khro phur dga' ldan gyi pho brang du sleb/ byams chen gyi zhal ras mthong ba tsam gyi yid phrogs pa byung / khyad 'phags bcu gsum gyi 'ga' re dang
mjal/ gdung brgyud zhal ngo rnams kyi thugs dgyes dgyes mdzad sna len sogs bzabs par mdzad/ khro lo tsA'i byams chen zhal 'dzum bstan/ steng dga' ldan lha yi

mdzes pa zum/ /sngon chos kyi sbrang char zim pa'i skyes/ /gnas ngo mtshar che snyam ba spu g.yo/ /de nas gangs can chos 'phel du sleb gling khrod kyi grang khang zhig tu sdod
sa byas/ de nub rmi lam du btsun pa mgo chen po thang theb gyon pa zhig dang chos gtam yun ring byas mthar nged rang rgyal khos zhwa phud phyag phul byin rlabs zhus ba
zhig rmis/ gnas gangs can chos 'phel chos grwa ru/ /mtshan nyal ba'i rmi nyams nying 'khrul la/ /gtam chos kyi bgro ba sna tshogs byas/ /brtag ma shes stag la'i la la 'dzegs/
/sang nyin snar thang du sleb sde srid kyi phun tshogs gling du nged rang 'bod pa gnang drung 'khor phal cher phyag 'bul byed du bcug 'bel ba'i gtam shin tu smar ba
byung / grwa pa rnams rab gsal 'og gi sla g.ye zhig tu spyan drangs mang ja gdan non sogs shin tu bzang ba/ snar thang gi rten bzang la mang pa 'dug pa mjal/ khyad par
byams pa mched lnga'i nang tshan yin zer sku shin tu mtshar ba zhig 'dug pa de'i mdun nar skor ba byas pas snyan dar phang phung mang po 'dug pa de kho bo'i mdun du 'tshar
byung ba rten 'brel dga' mo yin kyang dkon gnyer gyis mthong na mi rung snyam snyan la mgyogs par phul/ sngon mkhas pa grangs med byon pa'i gnas/ /rten bzang po grangs
med dga' bas mjal/ /rje byams pas dar phud skyes su gnang / /'di nyams 'char bzhad gad byas pa tsam/ /sang tshong 'dus dbu rtser sleb gra lnga nyin byed dbang po shin tu
dgyes/ nged rang yon mchod rab gsal zhig tu byas/ gra pa rnams mdun rdo bcal yang po der bos mang ja gnang chos spyod rigs lung sogs bya gshongs par rang gi lugs

gyis shig gsung / mang ja'i steng du dam bca' rigs lung sogs dang / de grol nas rigs lung gi tsho bcad sog 'khor rnam gsum/ chos khrims pas skor ba mthar gang dgyes stong pa'i
bar du byas pas/ 'di 'dra ba'i sgrigs bkod ngo mtshar che gsungs nas dgyes/ mang ja sun grangs 'di tsam gyi mang ba byed pa la sngar btang ba'i mang ja 'debs chung gsungs
nas phyin chad mang ja gnang ba rnams ja dngos gtsang rdum re gnang gin yod/ sang pa rnam du sleb de dus pa rnam na sde srid rong po'i rgyal po sku bgres pa dang mjal
ltag tshugs shin tu bzang / rang la bsngags brjod mang po mdzad kyin 'dug /gnas gsar nas kyang de na bzhugs 'dug pas mjal 'phrad dgyes dgyes kyi tshul du gnang / 'on kyang
phyag g.yog rnams la lkog tu brda zhig mdzad pa yin nam grwa pa rnams kyi rjes 'brangs la byang pa'i tshong ba 'dra yod pa dwags po sogs mi ngan 'dras 'dzin zer rgyug
'phral byas/ pa rnams nas sde srid kyi mi sna 'dras bzlog pa ma gtogs zir rkyen cung zad yong grabs byung / de nub nor bu khyung rtser sleb sde pa zhal ngo gcig gi mang
ja shin tu bzang ba byung mang ja la nged kyi yang phyir/ chos khrims pa rtsar byung grwa ba rnams mdo gtor ma sogs byed zer mi nyan 'dug pas ci drag zer/ de 'dra gtan mi
legs pas ma byed cig zer ba byas/ nged steng du log 'phral mdo sgrub dang / gtor bsngo byas pa'i gtor ma de mchod g.yog pas 'phangs pas gtor ma 'khyags bag la zug 'dug go
yang zer/ ngan byed kyi gtso bo dwags po de ring por ma 'gyangs par tshe'i dus byas zer ro/ /nged chos bar sde la skyabs bcol pa'i/ /khong rjes 'brang byang

phyogs tshong pa la/ /gtes gting 'dzin byed zer zar zir byas/ /sde dge 'dun thugs 'khrugs gtor zor 'phangs/ /mdo gtor mas drag po'i 'phrin las byas/ /gzhan gdug can snying
rtsa mi 'dar ram/ /khong grwa pa rnams ni de skad zer//mi kho bo de la mi gtogs so/ /sang snga bar langs phyin pas gnas gsar du rtse chen nas bsu mi sleb gsol thog tu mang
ja mdzad/ de nas rim par phyin pas 'brong rtse'i zhol du rtse nas ngos la ja zhim po rang zhig rgyugs byung / de nas pho brang rtse chen du sleb sde srid zhal ngo rnams
dang blon chen 'tsho lags sogs thugs rab tu dgyes/ nyang stod phyogs na yod pa'i slob gnyer ba rnams kyang 'dus pas dge 'dun slob gnyer ba sha stag sum brgya tsam byung
/ sde srid nas tshugs ston gung ston grol ston 'bul ba rnams gzhag /rgyun la mang ja 'chag med sogs chos dbar rgyun ring 'tshogs pa'i bdag rkyen de dus las bzang ba ma byung
zhes grags/ bdag rnams kyis kyang bya gshongs rang gi lugs bzhin snga mo tho rangs zhogs chos dpe 'dzin 'jam tshul/ de nas rdo bcal rdo lha dang bcas pa der chos grwa
byas/ snga chos tshar gnyis/ gung tshigs grol nas mang ja'i steng du sku rim mtshan brjod tshar re mdzad/ sde pa 'tsho lags de thugs lhag bsam che bas sku rim phebs pa rang
gis chog /khyed dge 'dun rnams chos 'chad snyan smar ba dang / grwa pa rnams thugs skyed che ba rang gal che gsung / de nas dgongs chos tshar gnyis/ dgongs mo'i chos
brjod rigs lung rnams 'chag med byas pa zla ba bzhi bzhugs/ slob gnyer ba rnams kyang blo skyed de dus las che ba ma byung

zer/ sde pa 'tsho lags drung gis nged la tshe dbang / dmar po skor gsum/ sgrol ma sngo dkar/ gur zhal gyi rjes gnang sogs rnam grangs mang po zhus/ mkhar rtse chen 'chi med
skyed tshal cher/ /nged ngur smrig gnyis skyes 'dus tshogs bos/ /chos legs bshad skyes kyi chos char dang / /khong 'dod yon sbrang char cig car babs/ /de dus chos rje bstan
pa dar rgyas rkyang 'dur slob dpon la bzhugs pas zhag 'ga' dge 'dun rnams dpal 'khor chos sder sku ngal gso dang / rten mjal sogs la phebs pa dgos gsungs/ rtser grol
cha zhu yin 'dug pa la 'tsho lags drung gis zhag mangs na tshong 'dus der grwa ba lad pa'i khag yong zhag gnyis de ka mdzod gsung / chos sder rkyang 'dur chos rje/ sku drung
blo gros pa sogs rang re'i grwa rgyun du gtogs pa rnams dang / rgyal rtse sde srid sogs kyis bsnyen bkur mchod pa tshad med pa byung / gtsug lag khang phyi nang rten
mchod mchod rten chen mo'i phyi nang rten mchod sogs kyang da ltar rang bcos ba 'dra ba so ma gsal yag ge ba/ nang gi rten mchod rnams kyang spabs rdul gtan ma chags pa da
lta rang phyis pa 'dra ba/ rgya sgo'i nang du chud tsam nas rig pa dang sing 'gro ba rang 'dug /khyad par rkyang 'dur grang khang / chos rje bstan pas gsar bcos lha'i khang
bzang 'dra ba 'dug /de yang dbang rjes gnang sogs mang po byas des mig phye ba bzhin song nas phyin chad chos sder grang khang gsar bcos dar po byung zer/ dpal 'khor
lo'i chos sde'i lugs gnyis kyi/ /chos zang zing 'dod dgu'i gling chen por/ /rten ngo mtshar can la dad 'dun phul/ /lus ngal dub bde ba'i ngal

gso byas/ de nas rtse chen mdun na mtsho gcig 'dug pa der nor bu dbyig 'gro 'dug byed pa byis pa mang pos mthong / chu sram bzhin yin nam snyam rdo mang du 'phangs/ 'tsho lags
drung 'khor dang bcas pas gang yin brtag pa'i phyir srod la chu nang nas btsal pa zin nas pho brang du sleb/ spyir nor bu dbyig de mis ma reg bar la 'gro 'dug byed kyang
mis lag tu thob nas 'gro 'dug mi byed zer/ bya gshongs pas rnam sras gtor bsngo'i cho ga rgyun du byed pa dang / sbyin bdag gi dad 'dun la rten gnod sbyin gang ba bzang
pos sbyin pa 'dra zer ba yang byung 'dug /lha rnam sras gtor 'bul gyis mnyes pa dang / /khong sbyin bdag gi dad 'dun dus gcig mdzom/ /'khor gnod sbyin gang bzang gi phyag
pad nas/ /rdzas nor bu dbyig gi char pa phab/ /yang mchod gnas rten dge slong yin pa skye sa 'o yug pa grwa sa 'bras yul ba spun gnyis yod pa des nged la dad mos kyis
dpon blon drung du legs sbyor byas 'phral phugs kyi dgos cha thams cad 'bad med du yong ba zhig byung / lan cig gsar du mjal ba'i ja nag po sing nga gsigs gcig 'dug pa dge
slong gis 'di la grwa pa mnyes cig yod zer bas 'tsho lags da ltar rang mang ja la thob/ khyod rang dpon slob 'chad nyan dang slob gnyer rigs lung hur theg pa mdzod gsung
/ mang ja thon byung tshe nged la yang khur shog gsung hub gang tsam bzhes/ grwa pa 'di tso ci byed 'di 'dra'i gar ba la zhim rgyu ni mi 'dug gsung phyi la pho gsung /
yang spu ja spob rtse gcig 'jal 'dug pa de yang 'di dge 'dun la mang ja gyis nged la 'phog che gsung / bla brang nas gsol ja zhus tshe yang khyed dpon slob 'di pa da dung
grwa rkyang

gi shubs nas ma thon 'dug /'di 'dra'i ja gar ba rang rgyu gzan pa 'thung mkhan 'phog che ba las med gsung / gzhan yang rtse chen pa'i phyag rdzas rnying ma 'di tsho ma rlag
pa rang gi ngo la gsar 'phel 'di tsho dge phyogs la gang 'gro byed gsung / khri zhabs la byams pa/ thugs tshad pa/ khrims snyom pa sogs yon tan bgrang gis mi lang ba yod/
lan cig 'bangs grong pa 'dra ma 'cham par gcig gis rtsib rdo'i lugs g.yu rna legs po zhig phul bas bsod de med khyod rang gi phugs na nor 'di las lhag pa med 'di nga la
phul nas khyod ci sgrub gsung bka' skyon dang bcas ma bzhes bshags bsher ba la drung 'khor btang nas rtsib rdo dang dgra 'dul gnyen skyong yong gsung nas rang gi rtsar bsags
nas mdzad/ rje la snying nye 'bangs rnams byams pas bskyangs/ /dkar phyogs la dgyes dge 'dun gtsug tu mchod/ /rdzas la spyan zur g.yo med phyogs lhung bral/ /de 'dra'i
blon po phyogs nas 'ga' yod dam/ /de nas dbyar thog tsam chos dbar bzhugs dgos pa'i zhu nan che bar byung yang de tsam la grol bya zhus 'gro bar brtsams/ 'tsho lags drung
'khor dang bcas pas brag kha thug skyel ma mdzad/ der gsol ja sogs mdzad nas de nub 'brong rtser sleb nged rang gis rtse dang / grwa pa rnams kyis 'du khang du bzhugs/
dbu mdzad chos khrims sogs kyang rtser bos ja mchod che ba'i che mchog ma mdzod gsung dgyes dgyes mdzad/ bsnyen bkur 'bul ba dngos gtsang ba mdzad/ spyan stong ldan lha
dbang rjes 'gro ba'i/ /mkhar rtse chen de nas lam du chas/ /ri mthon por 'brong rtse mi dbang gis/ /lus ngal 'tsho mchod sprin rgya mtshor skyil/ /de nas

khyung rtser nged kyis lha khang dang / grwa pa rnams kyis 'du khang der bsdad/ rtse bas sngar khyud mi 'dug gsung mjal 'dzom bzhin ni mi mdzad 'dug de ga legs snyam pa byung
/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs pa zer ba bya gshongs pa rang yin pa rtse ba'i dpon sa yum rnams kyi bla ma yin pa de sogs bya gshongs phyogs kyi grwa bu slob rnams kyis bsnyen
bkur legs tshogs che ba rang byung / khong khyung rtse 'byor pa'i pho brang cher/ /dpon dregs can de tsho'i mjal 'phrad bcad/ /gzhan dad ldan mjal 'phrad char bzhin babs/
/rang chos su song bas bde zhing skyid/ /de nas tshong 'dus su 'gro ba'i lam khar pa rnam du grwa pa rnams kyis ma 'khyogs par thal le phyin/ nged kyis pa rnam rtser rong
nas sde srid sku bgres pa dang mjal rtse ja rdum sogs gnang sbyin yang dag pa mdzad/ de dus rtse na chos rje rab brtan pa yang bzhugs kyin 'dug pas bzhugs shag tu bos
dgyes dgyes rang mdzad/ gnas gsar nas sde pa phun tshogs pa yang bzhugs 'dug /de'i dus byang nas bdag po chen po'i sku gshegs pa 'dra zer ba'i gtam myug myug 'dug /rtse
chen nas sde pa 'tsho lags de 'dra'i gtam 'dug pa 'dis bde gzar gyi rkyen byed gsung nas thugs khral chen po mdzad/ gnas gsar nas sde pas nged cag yang yang ja la 'bod pa
gnang gtam de la thugs dgyes pa'i gsung 'phros mang po mdzad kyin 'dug /tshong 'dus sde bas mi la skye 'chi los yong khos bsad pa ni min 'byung chung gsung / dus ngan pa
glang lo ngo nag la/ /mi gces pa mtho ris song yang zer/ /khong nyi zla khrag gi mchi ma 'dzag /gzhan shi ba'i gtam snyan sgug rnams blun/ /de'i

dus sa bcud cung nyams pa'i rtags su nam mkhal la skar ma mjug ring 'char ba dang / nyi zla khrag gis byugs pa bzhin song snga dro nyi ma shar ba'i dus gyang logs la khrag
bskus pa bzhin dmar chag ge ba de 'dra byung / de nub tshong 'dus dbu rtser sleb tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po la mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa'i gsung 'phros mang po mdzad/
rje mkhyen brtse'i drung la yang dad 'dun chen po mdzad/ 'on kyang gsung chos kyi tshe rnying ma sogs gzhan nas bsres pa'i rgya ha cang ches pas smin po rang mi yong /
de bas de dus mkhan po mdzad pa de ngos thugs rab chung ba de yon tan du song / brag rdzong ma'i 'khrid yid la 'jags pa tsam byung bas zin bris shig yod de gzigs 'bul lo
gsung / rdzong g.yer can tshong 'dus dbu rtse ru/ /mi dpyod ldan gra lnga nyin byed mjal/ /chos 'bel ba'i gtam la rdzogs dus med/ /grogs chos mthun yod na dga' ba la/ /sang
nyin snar thang du sleb sde srid dang mjal 'phrad dgyes pa sngar bzhin/ de nas gnas/ de nas bya gshongs su sleb/ glang lo dbyar chos dang po'i chos mtshams sogs skabs
gseng la chos gra phyi bkod pa byas pa yin/ sngar yang bya gshongs chos gra phyi ma 'di grwa sa gzhan la med ces ngom pa zhig yod na'ang slar yang chos grwa de'i nang gyang
gi gru bzhir bcad/ sngar chos khri chen mo'i g.yas g.yon la 'jam mgon bla ma blo gros rnam par rgyal bas lam 'bras nye brgyud deng sang lam zab brgyud par grags pa rang
re'i slob bshad brgyud pa'i rdo lha shin tu legs pa bkod pa gnang grub yod/ rdo lha de yang gnas gsar nas 'byon dgos byung ba'i tshe 'jam dbyangs bla mas byang chos rgyal
chen po la zhus te rdzong shar

nas drangs pa yin/ da lan yang bo dong e nas drangs pa'i chos khri'i lho'i g.yas phyogs nas lam 'bras ring brgyud bde gshegs so lnga/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas sogs kyi rdo
lha/ g.yon phyogs cung ma khengs par 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtser lugs gnyis kyi rnam dpyod zab cing lhag bsam rnam dag dang ldan pa'i sa skyong mi dbang rin chen dpal bzang
la zhus pas dgyes pa chen pos gnang / thub dbang gnas bcu'i rdo lha g.yon phyogs la legs par bkod/ de dag la lha g.yabs dang gung der me tog ra ba'i skyed tshal mthar ljon
shing gi ra ba rim pas bskor ba dang bcas pa legs par grub/ mchod sbyin brgya pa'i 'chi med dga' ba'i tshal/ /sa la 'phos pa mnyan yod skyed mos tshal/ /lung rigs rtsed
mo rtse la ngo mtshar gnas/ /mkha' nas lha rnams gnas 'dir byon par nges/ /de'i ston gsol bur shog gsung phyin tshe bka' brgya tshar sgrol dkar sogs rjes gnang mang po
dang / dgyes mdzad dbang / de steng tshogs 'khor bzabs ma re mdzad pa phyag len 'dug pas de bzhin gnang / gsol gral g.yabs chen dang / dgongs ja gsol ja khang du mdzad/
de steng du rab 'byams pa rnams bshad pa dang rigs lung dang dogs gcod sogs byed du 'jug 'bel ba'i gtam gyis dus 'da'/ mchog mi dbang nam mkha'i mtshan can mched/ /dad 'dun
pa rnam dpyod lhan cig 'dzom/ /chos 'bel gtam dang rkang 'thung btung ba dang / /sems gcig 'dres kyi mchod yon nyams re dga'/ /de nas dge 'dun slob gnyer ba dngos gtsang
'di la chos 'chad pa'i chos grwa dngos gtsang yid la bsam pa bzhin 'grub/ da 'du khang

dga' mo zhig bzheng thub na ci ma rung snyam pa'i bsam pa rgyun chags su yod pa nas snga gong nas 'jam mgon bla ma la bslab ston zhus pas/ khyed rang gi 'chad nyan la slob
gnyer ba rnams blo kha rdzogs pa rang yod 'dug pas 'chad nyan khag che de gas chog gsung gnang ba ma byung / phyis khyed rang la blo 'dod chen po 'dug pas 'chad nyan ma chag
pa'i gseng la gang yong gyis/ ngas kyang 'jam thal gyi mthud 'dra e yong lta gsung gnang ba thob/ chos rje bstan pa dar rgyas pa nged rang la dad 'dun che ba dang / mkhar
las la nyams myong che ba 'dug pas rogs la 'byon par byas/ grwa pa rnams la bskor bas 'di kham ches pas smra mi nus zer ba dang / kha cig bla ma gong ma'i rab gnas can
yin zer ba dang / phal cher 'chos khyod na de las dga' ba mi 'dug ste khyed rang gis chod zer ro/ /de nas stag lo 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan ngam ring dbyar
chos kyi gnam gang la mkhan por mnga' gsol 'dug kyang bya gshongs su ma thos par zhal dkar la 'gro ma thub/ dgun chos steng du 'gro rtsis byas na'ang ston cag sgang la dag
pa'i zhing du gshegs zer gtam byung / grwa pa slob gnyer ba sogs kyis mchod 'bul zla gcig bar du mang ja rgyun ma chad par btang / mang ja'i steng du'ang bla ma dgyes
pa'i mchod pa yin pas dkar me lha bshos sogs mchod pa'i sprin phung bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / khyad par gsung rab la dogs pa dpyod pa'i rigs lung rgyun ring ba 'ur chil
le ba byas/ mtshan ldan bla ma dgyes pa'i mchod sprin 'khyil/ /phyi yi mchod pa rkang 'thung btung ba'i chus/ /nang gi mchod pa rnam dpyod me 'bar bsam/ /lta ba ngan pa'i
bud shing ngo tsha nas/ /lung rigs

rlung gis khyer bzhin ga shed song / /stag lo de sogs chos mtshams byung res kyi phal cher gsol phu rong mtsho gnyis su kho re phyin/ rong mtsho'i gzims khang gsar pa maN gdang
gsar pa sogs la rab gnas dang / chos kyi thugs bzhed shin tu che bas klu sgrub lugs kyi dbu ma'i lta 'khrid/ thogs med lugs kyi sems tsam pa'i lta 'khrid/ sgrol dkar
tshe 'khrid/ grub rgyal ma'i tshe 'khrid/ kye rdor yab yum gyi dbang / gshed dmar gyi dbang sogs dang / rjes gnang gi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsan/ mdor na chos dang
zang zing skyes kyi dga' ston snol ma la dus 'da' bar bgyid pa yin no/ /gos bzang panytsa li kar 'gran bzod pa'i/ /ngur smrig gos dang li khri'i mdangs chags pa'i/ /gos kyi
klubs tshe zas gtsang sras khyod kyis/ /na bza' dmar zhes rab brtags kyi rgyan no/ /ser 'di na spungs min nam/ /de nas yos lo cung zad zir rkyen la brten nas byang nas
zhabs drung bkra shis stobs rgyas shar la phebs pa'i lam bar bya gshongs su zhag gnyis gsum sku ngal gsor bzhugs/ gla bo gang khar phebs skyel la phyin phan tshun du 'khor
ba la snying po med pa'i skyo shas nges 'byung gi skul 'debs tshad med pa byung / rigs 'khrul med chos rgyal bkra shis mtshan/ /rje padmA ka ra'i sprul par grags/ /gzhan
phyogs med 'gro ba'i don la dgongs/ /yul dbus gtsang zhabs 'chag de nas dar/ /rnam gnon zhes pa lcags pho 'brug gi dpyid 'du khang gsar bzhengs kyi ched du lcang gcod
byas de dus bde gzar gyi rnam pa zir re ba yod kyang ston bsam rtser chos dbar la 'byon dgos gsungs pho nya ba yang yang byung /

rang gzhan the tshom du gyur pa la de dus 'jam dbyangs bla ma 'dar skyid gshongs na bzhugs pas bslab ston zhur phyin pas bde gzar 'thug drag po yod 'dug na'ang khyed rang grwa
pa rnams kyis phar tshur thar pa gcig yong / phugs sbyin bdag gi khyad che bas phyin pa legs gsung / ston cag gi skabs yin pas slob gnyer ba brgya lhag las ma byung yang
lam du zhugs tshe lam bar gyi mi rnams da lo bsam rtse 'chor thag chod/ khyed rang yang mi chud chud srid na'ang gos zas dang 'ding lhung drag pa rnams bkra shis lhun
por bcol ba legs so zer/ bsam rtse rtse zhol rnams kyang bkra shis lhun po sogs su zhogs bdeg /bsam grub rtse yang stong sang nge yod pa lta bu'i tshe nged rnams sleb pas
lha'i gzungs bzhugs chud pa lta bur bag phebs par gyur/ sleb 'phral de'i nub tho rengs cha'i rmi lam du bud med rgan mo zhig byung nas da lo mi gces shi zer nas mchi ma
gtong sems khral shin tu che ba byed kyin nged la yang zhu ba mang po 'bul gyin 'dug /de mtshams mi zhig byung nas da khang pa la dar tshugs zer rang gi grwa pa rnams btang
nas dar 'dzugs su bcug /nged rang gi dar 'dzugs lugs ji ltar byas yod snyam ltar phyin pas khang pa de'i khor mor mdung dar khra thib se ba 'phreng ma chad par btsugs/
sgra rol cha sogs 'ur chil le ba 'dug pas sems spro sing nge ba byung / rdzong 'di la yang rten 'brel legs rang re'i chos dbar kyang legs tshogs cher yong ba'i rmi lam
du 'dug bsam blo bde cham me gnas so/ /de nas rgyun mi ring ba nas g.yas ru byang pa'ang dpung rogs la sleb pha rol gyi dpung tshogs phyir zlog zer ba'i gtam snyan dar 'phyar
dang bcas pa rgyas par

byung / de nas gtsang pa sku mched 'grig zer ba'i gtam snyan dar 'phyar dang bcas pa dang / kun spangs drung rang yang phebs dpon g.yog mchod yon thams cad shin tu dgyes shing
bkra shis par gyur to/ /gzhi'i bdag mo gdong pham gsol ba 'debs/ /khong chos srung zhal mtho bar chad bsrungs/ /nged yon mchod bkra shis phun sum tshogs/ /phyogs kun
tu snyan grags rna ba'i rgyan/ /de nas nged rang grwa pa rnams kyis kyang bya gshongs rang gi lugs bzhin tho rengs snga mo nas zhogs chos/ tsha grol la snga chos gnyis/ gung
tshigs thon nas dgongs chos gnyis/ chos brjod rigs lung sogs 'chag med du byas pas sbyin bdag dang phyogs kyi mi rnams ngo mtshar du rtsi zhing dad spro bsnyen bkur phun
sum tshogs pa grags dkar gyis brgyan pa byung ba yin no/ /sa 'dzin ri bo'i spo la brjid chags mkhar/ /bsam grub rtse zhes dpa' bo'i mdun nas bdar/ /ru mtshon ngom pa'i
mdun sar 'phya ba bzhin/ /legs bshad sgrog la bstod bkur bsngags pas brel/ /khyu mchog ces pa lcags mo sbrul gyi lo nyang stod 'brong rtse dang dbang ldan nas bzo rigs
pa bcu gnyis pos dpyid zla phyed bzhi'i bar la 'du khang gi skya dang / shing brtsegs nyi shu rtsa gcig dang bcas pa'i thog phubs/ 'du khang gi rgyug rnams rtse chen nas
gcod mi gnang ba rnam thug bskyal/ pa rnams nas snar thang thug tshong 'dus pas bskyal/ snar thang nas gnas thug snar thang pas bskyal/ de nas rdzi lung thug gnas pas bskyal/
de nas bya gshongs thug rdzi lung pas dang blangs byas bskyal/ gzhan lam bar gyi dpon chen rnams la zhu shog rten bcas re phul bas chog pa byung lags

so/ /gtsug lag khang dang / 'du khang gi spen bad dang bcas pa grub/ las byed pa'i tshe yang chos 'chad ma nyams pa byas/ chos kyi gung gseng dang mang ja'i ja gzhug la grwa
pa bsam pa dge ba rnams kyis dang blangs byas mgul ba ma gtogs khral skos byas pa'i gzhur yang gtan ma dgos/ spen bad spen ma rnams kyang phu gsum byang sems kyi g.yog
bskul rtsag skyel byas/ las mi rnams la ja gzhug gi ja re ma gtogs skyur gyi rdzi gcig kyang med pa byas/ 'du khang gi thog phub pa'i dga' ston la rong mtsho nas sa skyong
mi'i dbang po nam mkha' dpal 'byor yab yum phebs/ mang ja gor bur ston legs/ 'bul skyes bzabs ma dang bcas dge 'dun la mang ja zhib 'bo sogs mdzad/ de nyin bkra shis pa'i
gso sbyong mdzad de 'dul ba'i rab gnas/ dge 'dun blo gsal rnams kyi rigs pa dang lung gi rnam gzhag 'ur chi le ba dang / bkra shis pa'i mnga' gsol me tog rgyas par gtor
te mdo lugs kyi rab gnas/ de'i tshe 'jam mgon bla ma mkhan rin po che blo gros phyogs las rnam rgyal dgung lo bdun cu don bdun bzhes pas ya ga chos sdings nas spyan drangs
te sngags lugs kyi rab gnas mdzad/ 'du khang thog phubs mtshams tho rengs shig rmi lam du mi dkar po zhig byung nas 'du khang la rab gnas chags so zer ba lan gsum tsam
byung bas sems dga' spro chen po byung / 'on kyang rang gis kyang dgyes pa rdo rje'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs/ dngos sta sbrel ba'i sta gon nub gc-ig /dngos gzhi
nub gcig /de'i tho rengs nyi shar la rab gnas dngos gzhi ste/ rab gnas nub gnyis nyin gsum ma rgyas par byas pa yin

no/ /tshul ldan ngur smrig dri bzang gis byugs bzhin/ /bkra shis gso sbyong shis pa'i cho ga bstar/ /spyi bor dbang bskur rgyal po'i mnga' dbul ltar/ /bkra shis snyan grags
phyogs kyi rna rgyan mdzes/ /dgyes mdzad rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du/ /bzang drug cho ga rgyud mangs glu dbyangs kyis/ /utpal padma mandhar mya ngan med/ /bkra shis
me tog phon po'i char rgyun phab/ /mnyan yod bya gshongs skyed tshal gzhal med khang / /'di tsam gyis kyang 'dzam gling nor 'dzin khyon/ /dog par byas tshe byed po'i rdzu
'phrul gyis/ /stong gsum 'di dag yangs par byas so snyam/ /de tshe dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing sa cher/ /lung rigs rma med chos rnga 'di bsgrags pas/ /me tog gzhu ldan dpung
dang lhan cig tu/ /pha rgol log smra sa mthar bros par nges/ /sbrul lo'i ston snye mo nyang stod sogs nas lha ris pa dgu bos shing rtsi byed par brtsams pas rang gi
rogs rnams kyis thugs thung la rgyu cha rnams dang / bzo ris pa rdzong bdar gyi yo byad rnams kyang mi 'byor zer 'u thug po byed kyin 'dug na'ang de 'dra mi dgos rta gyad
gling btsong nas yo byad bsgrubs pas chog zer ba byas/ sbad chod kyi lag tu blangs pas shing rtsi legs par grub/ mgur nang so'i sbyin bdag byas nas mnyan yod bla rim dang
/ 'od dpag med kyi zhing khams kyang legs par grub/ gser cha zhig 'byor dgos pa 'dug pas da lta lag na ye mi 'dug rang gi 'brog sde la slongs shig byed dgos bsam pa yod
pa la lha rtse nas bkra shis lags kyi shing rtsi la gser cha bzhin 'bul mkhan e byung / gser cha dgongs par yod na nged la yang zho gang do 'bul rgyu yod

gsung / blo la 'dod cha che ba yod kyang sngar skyid gshongs dar chen pas zho do phul/ de tsam ma gtogs gzhan ye ma byung zhus/ phyis bo dong du phebs byung dus bya gshongs
su gdan 'dren tsam zhus pas mgul gyi dar mdud gseb nas gser dngos gtsang srang gang spungs nas phul/ spyir yang sbyin bdag chen po 'dis nged la thugs dkar ba rang mdzad/
snga phyir ja rtse mo rdum bzhi/ rtse ja nyag gsum bzhi byas pa'i thum mang du gnang grwa sa 'dzin pa la shin tu phan par byung / de 'phral bo dong nas sprul sku tshangs
pa bos gser shog brdung shing rtsi'i gser shin tu phyug pa phyogs kun tu snyan pas khyab pa byung / ming yang bkra shis gser khang zhes sbyin bdag gi mtshan gyi zur dang
ldan pa de nyid yin/ ngur smrig 'du ba'i kun dga' ra ba'i khyams/ /dzambu'i rkang 'thung nyer gcig 'chi med kyi/ /nor bu sna tshogs brtsegs la co 'dri bar/ /sna tshogs tshon
mdangs dbang po'i gzhu bzhin bkra/ /lhun po'i byang gi ba gam nyi 'od kyis/ /gzhu bzhin rin chen sa le sbram gyi mdangs/ /'od zer 'bar bas mtshan yang nyin mo bzhin/
/kun gsal bkra shis lhag bsam dge bas bskrun/ /sna tshogs zhes pa chu pho rta'i lo dbyar gyi cha la sprul sku rdo rjes gnas bcu si thang lugs mkhyen brtse'i phyag srol bzhin
dang / tshe dpag med rgyan drug gis bskor ba'i zhing khams gnyis/ mkhan rin po che blo gros rnam par rgyal bas gnang sbyin sogs bdag rkyen mdzad nas bzhengs/ sgo mchor
shing rtsi gser shog dang bcas pa/ chos grwa nang gi thog phub skyang nul dang bcas pa grub/ chos grwa phyir rkang 'thung gsar pa'i skyed tshal me tog sna tshogs bkra
ba'i bkod pa yang bgyis pa lags/ sa skyong zhes

pa shing mo bya lo ayon pa'i zhing khams sngon gyi lo paN gyis bskor ba dang / mi zad pa zhes pa me pho khyi lo grub thob brgyad cu'i zhing khams gser shog ma gnyis bzhad nas
khang pas sbyin bdag byas nas bzhengs/ ri mo mkhan ayon pa'i zhing khams sprul sku rdo rje'i mkhyen lugs dang / grub thob brgyad cu'i zhing khams sprul sku bstan rgyan
gyi sman lugs ri mo yin/ sa skyong zhes pa shing mo bya lo sa paN gyi sku brnyan shin tu legs pa/ 'phrog byed ral pa tshar bcad pa dang / hor rgyal po go brtan rjes su bzung
ba sogs kyi rnam thar zhing bkod gser shog dang bcas pa rong 'tsho nas 'byor lags sku mched kyi sbyin bdag mdzad nas bzhengs/ ri mo mkhan sprul sku sgang brgyud pas
sman lugs yin/ shing mo bya de la rje bla ma phyogs las rnam par rgyal ba'i zhing khams/ drung chen blo gsal dbang pos sbyin bdag byas nas sprul sku rdo rjes bzabs bris mkhyen
lugs shin tu legs pa yod/ rna ba'i bdud rtsi snying la 'dren pa yi/ /legs bshad gtam snyan mkhas pa'i mgrin par rgyu/ /mig gi bdud rtsi yid la sim byed pa/ /ngo mtshar
ri mo sor rtse'i rdzu 'phrul yin/ /mnyan yod bla rim 'od dpag med pa'i zhing / /chos kyi sgra sgrogs sbyin bdag zhing mchog der/ /padma'i ze 'brur skad cig brdzus te
skyes/ /gnas bcu'i bkod mdzes nor 'dzin mkha' la shar/ /bka' drin 'khor med dam pa'i phyag pad nas/ /lcags kyus drangs bzhin dad ldan 'gro ba'i tshogs/ /thub dbang zhing
der thogs med bgrod pas bde/ /tshe dpag med mgon rgyan drug mchog gis bskor/ /tshe yi dngos grub stsal nas rgyan drug gzhung / /so so'i

dgongs dpyid longs nas blo gsal ba/ /legs bshad chos char phab pa de nas byung / /'jam mgon bla ma'i zhing khams ngo mtshar rmad/ /bi shwa karmas gsar du bskrun pa bzhin/ /byin
rlabs bdud rtsi'i zil dngar snying la smin/ /ci bsams lhun gyis grub pa'i rten 'brel 'grig /lnga rig paN chen shar phyogs mngon dga'i zhing / /'dzam gling sa la gsar
du 'phos pa bzhin/ /sdom rig gnad 'gag nges don snying po'i bcud/ /'chad cing 'doms pa'i rnam dpyod spobs pa thob/ /padma ka ra auDDi yA' na nas/ /rdzu 'phrul gar gyis rol
bzhin mkha' las byon/ /nag phyogs bdud dpung bcom nas rgya mtsho yi/ /ska rags can 'di dkar phyogs lha mis bkang / /'phags pa'i yul nas grub chen bcu phrag brgyad/ /rang
rang rdzu 'phrul ngo mtshar ston bzhin du/ /mnyan yod dri yi gtsug lag khang 'dir 'phungs/ /byin rlabs bslu med 'dod dgu'i char gyis zim/ /sbyin po dad ldan 'tsho zhing
gzhes pa dang / /'jig rten 'di nas mtho ris son pa rnams/ /skye dang skye bar bde ba'i yon blangs nas/ /dag pa'i zhing du dga' zhing rtse bas rol/ /sa skyong zhes pa shing
mo bya dpyid kyi dus 'dar nas mi dbang lhun chen drung gis phyag rtags shig phebs dus der yang gsan yod dam rje mkhan drung sku khams cung zad bsnyel ba zhig yod pa 'dra
zer ro gsung ba zhig phebs/ nged de gong 'dar gyi sgrub mchod la shog zer 'gro rtsis su yod/ rje bla ma sku bsnyel na 'dir bang chen zhig mi yong ba'i sgo med ci yin
snyam pa shar/ de nas chos mtshams shig tu sleb pas gsol phu nas 'byor lags kyis chos mtshams la yong dgos gsung ba phebs/ da lan

'dar phyogs la 'gro dgos pa yod pas grol cha zhu byas kyang slar bskyar ma gnang nas da lan u tshugs yin pas cis kyang yong dgos gsungs/ nyer gcig la gsol phur phyin sleb 'phral
zhal ngo rnams la tshe bka' zhig phul/ de'i nam phyed tsam na bya gshongs nas bang chen byung / rje mkhan sku khams shin tu bsnyel 'dar du sleb pa yod zer nas bang
chen btang kyang 'dir ma 'byor ba 'dra 'phral du yong dgos zer nas tho rangs snga bar yongs/ gsol phu nas byang sems yum de de lo mi bzhugs pa'i snga ltas yin pa 'dra gzhan
gsol phur thug phrad dang 'tshub de 'dra mi yong yod/ de nub bya gshongs su bsdad/ yar lam sbas spro la byas rje btsun drung yang sku khams skor ba la 'byon gsung rtag
bstun ya ga chos sdings su byon/ snga 'phar zhig btang bas chos rje pa sleb yong na de ka bsgugs pa yin/ da nged la thogs med rdo rje gur khang du thogs pa med par 'gro
gsung / phyag g.yog pa dge slong bzod rin gyis bla ma rin po che la rdo rje gur khang de byang khang gsar pas phul ba lags sam zhus pas khang gsar ba la de 'dra 'bul ba'i
spobs pa med gsung / dag pa'i zhing khams shig gi gzigs snang yin pa 'dug /zla ba de'i yar ngo tshes bcu bzhi bco lnga skor la sku shin tu bsnyel/ bla ma rnam gsum byon
byung gsung ba'i dag pa'i snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa shar/ sku 'khor rnams kyi tshes bco lnga la phebs par thag bcad 'dug /da bar sku ma thim pa de kho bo cag thugs rje'i
lcags kyu'i drangs nas bzhugs par 'dug rang bu gcig ltar brtse'i bla ma rje/ /khong dag zhing gshegs la rings chas kyang / /bdag

thugs mtshor bcangs nas gdan la bzhugs/ /'di bsam zhing dran pa mig chu g.yo/ /de nas mjal ma thag khyed yun ring ba de brda ma 'byor ba yin pa 'dra/ da 'dir byon gsungs nas
sku zhogs g.yas kyi gdan zhig gi steng du bzhag phyag g.yas kho bo'i lag pa g.yon dang sbrel nas da kho bo la dgyes rdor dbang gong ma'i gsal 'debs shig gyis shig gsung
/ khyed nga'i slob ma yang yin bla ma yang yin dad mos shin tu che ba yod/ gzhan bla ma 'ar ma 'ur ma 'di rnams la dad rgyu rang med gsung / 'o na mchod bshom zhig dgos
sam zhus pas los dgos gsung / de nas ring zhig gi bar du bag phebs pa'i gsung 'phros mang po zhig gis g.yengs/ sa sros song tsa na da nga la dbang mi byed pa yin nam gsung
/ 'o na mchod bshom yang ma grub lags zhus pas da lam bsdus shig longs la dbang bskur de gas chog gsung / de nas gzims lam du phebs sku tshegs mdzad nga'i chos gos dang
snam sbyar khur shog gsung / phyag g.yog rnams kyi sku gzan sku chos sku rgyab la phul/ snam sbyar sku mdun la g.yogs 'dug pas 'di gang yin gsung / snam sbyar yin zhus 'dug
pas khyed la nyams rang mi 'dug /snam sbyar 'di skad byas su gyon rgyab la khob gsung / de nas kho bos dbang 'bul ba'i lugs byas pas bzang dar dmar po kha do 'brel zhig
gnang 'di dbang yon no gsung / maNDal dang brda sbyor mchod g.yog pa dge slong bzod rin gyis byas/ kho bos dbang gi 'jug pa sogs gang zhib 'bul ba'i lugs byas pas de 'dra'i
zhib zhib rang mi dgos gsung / kho bos thugs khrel gyi dogs bum dbang nas brtsams gang zhib phul/ mchod g.yog pas da dbang gi dngos

gzhi na sleb 'dug zhus 'dug pas/ dgod bro 'di la yang dbang gi nyams yod pa'i lugs byed kyin 'dug gsung bzhad gad mdzad/ de nas dbang rdzogs dus mchod g.yog pas dbang rdzogs
song zhus 'dug pas song song dgos pa 'dra'ang song / mi dgos pa 'dra'ang song gsung ste dbang gong ma tsam gyis chog rgyur 'dug /de nub sku khams shin tu bde dad ldan slob
ma'i dbang gis ma gtogs/ de nub dag pa'i zhing du gshegs par brtsams pa'i tshod du 'dug /sang nyin rab gsal du nyi ma la phebs/ 'tsho byed rnams ni phyag rtsa la ni skyon
ye med gsol ja nag rtse ni bzhes gsol ba gsol thug sogs ni dga' mo 'gro/ mnal du ni phebs sku mdangs ni dga' mo yod da lo rang sku skyon pa mi yong las che zer/ bdag
rang gis kyang de ga zhus pas kho bo da lo mi sdod tshe yang ring po byung / skyid po yang byas/ chos rnam dag byas zer ba la ni dka' se 'dug blo tshad po byas mi tshad
ma zhig yin gsung / drin 'gran zla bral ba'i 'jam dbyangs rje/ /gnas dus gsum gzigs pa'i spyan dang ldan/ /thugs bslu med mkhyen brtse'i nus pa ldan/ /dus 'da' ka'i zhal
gdams lhug par gnang / /sang nyin nyer lnga'i nam lang la phyag 'bul la phyin pas chos rje pa chos 'chag mi 'gro yam gsungs/ bdag sku khams kyi tshod zin zin mi 'gro lags
zhus pas khams kyi tshod de ring zin yong gsung / kho bo the tshom du gyur de ring sang sku gshegs gshegs ni mi 'dra sku khams cung bzang du 'gro ba ni e srid bsam pa tsam
byung / de nas da nyi ma la 'gro gsung shin tu snga bar nyi ma la phebs/ rje btsun drung yang phebs nas

phyag 'bul 'bul ba 'dra 'bul gyin 'dug /dge slong bzod rin gyis rje btsun drung shar la phebs pa'i phyag 'bul yin par 'dug zhus pas de ga mdzod rje btsun drung yang phebs/
nged kyang da lta 'gro yo gsung rang ni zhal skur yin nam snyam/ rje btsun drung spyan chab mang po sil bla ma rin po che phebs pas byung dogs med/ bdag cag yud tsam phyin
nas log yong zhus pas da yar 'gro mar 'gro zhabs brel ba las med ma 'byon gsung / bdag rang rlon po chu tshan la yongs 'dir yang yud tsam mjal zhu yin 'dug pas/ 'o na chu
tshan la 'byon na'ang byon gsung gin 'dug /rje btsun drung thugs ma bde log ge pa la phebs song / de nas nged rang dpon slob bzhugs gral la yod dus nged la spyan cher
ba zhig gzigs bla chen gyi sku mdangs kyi dga' ba la gsung/ cung zad nas chos rje pas lo brgyad cu lon ang gsung / ma lon zhus na rten 'brel la gnod dam bsam da lta ni drug
cu tsam ka yin lags zhus dbu gug tsam mdzad kyin 'dug /phyis mi rnams kyis de tsam la dpags nas khyod la lung bstan byung ba yin pa 'dug zer ba ni sgrog cing 'dug /de
nas nyi ma dgongs khyog pa la rje dpon blo gsal byung nas tshe ring drung dpal byin rlabs shig zhu ba la yong chog pa dgos zer zhu yin 'dug /'o na nga 'gro ba la ma thogs
pa da ltar rang shog gyis gsung gin 'dug /tshe ring drung dpal sleb gsol ja zhus 'bul ba 'dra byed kyin 'dug /drung dpal ka gdong na ja 'thung ring phyag cung zad 'dar ba
tsam 'dug /phyag g.yog pas ser ma yod pa ni min nam zhu dbu gug mdzad kyin 'dug /de nas drung dpal ja khang du btang nged rnams kyis a dkar dud pa

'dra sbyar ser ma 'phral la gdang byung / de nas gzims chung du gzims mal phyag phyi byas nged kyi gzims chung du ga lam bsdus blangs gtor bsngo'i skabs na yod/ dge slong pas
lam bsdus rab gsal du grub nas sku gzhog la sleb pa tsam 'dug /de nas dge slong bzod rin da 'dir mgyogs po phebs shig zer de ma khad phyin pas gzims mal na sku sir bsrang
bzhugs 'dug /dge slong pas 'di su yin pa 'dug zhu mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho yin pa 'dug da nged la gsal 'debs 'dra gyis shig gsung / kho bos mig chu mang du shor
skad 'dar re ba zhig la gsal 'debs 'bul lugs byas pas chos rje pa rtab rtob ma byed par lhod kyis gsung / kho bos bum dbang gi 'da' ka ma 'bul lugs byas pas dbu phrug mdzad
de mi dgos gsung gi brda yin pa 'dug /gsang dbang gi 'da' ka ma 'od gsal nas 'pho ba dang / sher dbang gi 'da' ka ma nam 'chi ba'i tshe na rdo rje sems dpa' 'byon par
'gyur ba dang / bzhi pa'i 'da' ka ma lam phyag rgya chen po nas 'pho ba gsum gyis gsal 'debs phul bas shin tu dgyes dbu gug gug pa mdzad kyin 'dug /de nas skabs shig nged
theg gsung gin 'dug bteg pas mi yong ba 'dug /'byung ba sa thim pa'i rtags yin pas thugs dam la 'jog pa zhu zhus pas re zhig mnyam gzhag la bzhugs/ slar yang theg gsung
rje dbon blo gsal gyis sos dal gyis skabs su'ang gzhan 'di tsho ni rdo rje skyil krung byas shi zer yags yags byed pa zhig 'dug /kho bo cag ni shAkya thub pa'i 'chi lugs
kyis yong gsung ba zhig yod pas sku'i bzhugs stabs 'di bcos na zer bas de ga bzhin zhabs rdo rje skyil

krung bkrol/ seng ge'i nyal stabs su bsgyur bas thugs dgyes/ da gsal thob cig gsungs/ gong ma gsum gyi 'da' ka ma slar yang gsal 'debs phul bas phal pa ltar na dar sog mgul
gyi mgrin pa na tong tong ba tsam 'dug kyang nged kyi gsal 'debs thugs la 'bab mi 'bab la dbu gug gug pa dang dbu sgril ba gnang gin 'dug /de nas tshangs phug cung mtho
