ba tsam dang / dbu zil pa khrom pa tsam 'dug pas 'od gsal ma bu zhal mjal ba'i nyams len phul du phyin pas rten 'di la grub mtha' snyogs par gdon mi za/ nged dpon slob phan
tshun chags na yang / /dus de tshe chags sdang 'ching thag chad/ /sems bde chen 'od gsal ngang nyid nas/ /lam so sor gyes kyang 'bral ma myong / /de'i tshe bdag cag gtso
'khor thams cad bde ba nas bde bar 'gro ba la mkhas pa su zhig sgyid lug byed ces dang / byams pas/ de yis chos kun sgyu ma lta bu dang / /skye ba skyed mos tshal 'gro
ltar rtogs nas/ /'byor pa'i dus dang rgud pa'i dus na'ang 'di/ /nyon mongs sdug bsngal dag gis gnod pa med/ /ces pa ltar rje bla ma ni skyed mos tshal rnying pa nas gsar
par 'pho ba ltar thugs dgyes pa chen pos zhing mchog dam par gshegs pa dang / 'khor rnams kyang lus sems la sdug bsngal gyi tsher ma med par sems spro sag ge ba dang / dga'
sag ge ba'i ngang la dus 'da' ba byung / skyid gshongs dar chen pas rang re dpon slob kun 'dzoms nas 'pho tshul rang dbang thob pa 'di lta bu yong bsam pa ma byung /
sngar bas kyang dad pa ches lhag pa thob/ da sdug bsngal byed rgyu spu tsam med do zer/ bka' drin mtshungs bral 'jam mgon bla ma rje/ /'od gsal ngang nas dkar

dmar snang ba'i tshe/ /rdo rje sems dpa' bde stong zhal mjal te/ /phyag chen lam nas 'phags pa'i grong du 'phos/ /bdag cag 'khor bcas sdug bsngal rgyun thag chad/ /dga' zhing
spro bas gsol ba 'debs la brtson/ /khyed nyid gar bzhugs rdo rje'i pho brang der/ /thogs med gzigs pa stsol zhig 'jam dbyangs rje/ /thub chen 'da' tshul bstan tshe nyan
thos 'khor/ /dgra bcom bye ba rang gis me sbar nas/ /lhag med mya ngan 'das la mtshar gyi yod/ /bde ba'i ngal gsor 'khor bcas bkod 'di mtshar/ /de'i sang nyin nas nged
kyis dgyes rdor gyi cho ga btsugs gdung gi 'khris su nyal kyang thugs dam la bzhengs pa'i rtags su mngon pa ni ci yang ma byung / gnam gang gi snga dro nged gzims chung nang
du bdag bskyed la yod pa'i skabs dri zhim po sngon tshor ma myong ba zhig sang sang byung / rab gsal na spos gced pa yin nam snyam sgo phye bas ni ci yang mi snang ja
khang du dri zhim po zhig gced pa yin nam snyam byung / nyi shar la rab gsal du phyi rol gtor ma la phyin tshe dri bzang ni sngar gyi de bzhin 'dug /'phags ma ngag dbang
dang / chos mdzad ma rin cen sogs gdung mjal la byung tshe rab gsal du sleb tsam nas 'di lta bu'i dri zhim pa zer/ gdung gi gzims chung na dri zhim po zhig gced yod pa 'dra
zer sgo phye nas snom gyin 'dug /mi phyi na yod pa rnams ni de'i tho rengs gling bu dang rnga sgra la sogs pa'i sgra snyan po yang thos me tog gi char yang 'bab kyin
'dug zer/ rang gi mngon du gyur pa la gnyag phu nas pho brang rtse'i bar la 'ja' dkar po zheng khru gang tsam byas pa zhig tha le mthong / dpyid zla

gnyis pa'i nyer lnga la chos dbyings su zhugs pa'i tshul bstan/ de yang don la nyer lnga nas gnam gang gi bar tshogs lam gsum nas sbyor lam bzhi'i bar sngar ma bgrod pa'i lhag
rnams bgrod/ gnam gang gi tshe rtsa mdud dang po grol grub mtha' 'khor 'das dbyer med snyogs/ sa dang po rab dga' rnyed par gdon mi za snyam pa'i nges pa brtan po yong
/ gzhan rnam shes bu ga dgu po gang rung nas thon pa'i rtags sku la dri nga ba dang / byang sems dkar dmar bud pa la sogs pa'i rtags ci yang ma byung / dbu'i tshangs phug
cung zad 'phags 'dug zer ba 'dug kyang tshangs phug 'bur tsam pa de ni snga mo nas yod/ phyis 'phags nas 'bur ba min par mngon/ gnam gang nas gdung sgam bcos gos dar gyis
gril mchod pa 'bul ba'i rten du bzhugs su gsol/ de nas ya ga chos sdings su gsol 'debs kyi tshe ya ga chos sdings dpon slob rnams kyis 'du khang du rnam par snang mdzad
kyi chog gra btsugs/ sgyi chu ba'i rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams kyis bla brang du dgyes rdor gyi chog gra btsugs/ dgon gnas gzhan rnams su rang rang gis chog gra btsugs/ kho
bo cag gi 'du khang du bsngo ba la yud tsam ma gtogs gdung gi sku mdun du dgyes mdzad cho ga lhur len byas/ gang sku'i dkyil 'khor dag zhing gshegs na yang / /thugs rje'i
lcags sgrog 'bral ba med mthong nas/ /mig la mchi ma 'dzag kyang sems la ni/ /rab dga'i ting 'dzin mi g.yo brtan par gyur/ /tshul ldan ngur smrig 'dus pa'i pho brang du/
/phyi nang dkyil 'khor zhal phye mchod cing bstod/ /ting 'dzin sngags rgya cho ga'i dbyangs snyan gyis/ /'jam mgon bla ma dgyes pa'i mchod sprin

bstar/ /gnas der g.yas ru byang nas zhal ngo rnams dang / sbyin bdag khag khag so so rnams dang / rje dbon blo gsal sogs sku nye rnams dang / drag rigs dad pa rnams kyis bsnyen
cing bkur ba dang / phyi nang gsang ba'i mchod sprin rgya chen pos legs par mnyes par byas pa yin no/ /de nas kho bos bya rgod gshongs su sleb/ dpyid zla gsum pa hor
zla bzhi pa'i sa ga zla ba'i dus bzang po la zhogs chos dang snga chos ma chag pa byas/ 'jam dbyangs bla ma mchod pa'i sprin phung 'dus pa'i tshogs la rkang 'thung btung
ba gya nom pa dang / gsol 'debs kyi shis brjod smon lam/ gsung rab zab mo'i don la tshig don gyi sgro 'dogs gcod pa'i lung dang rigs pa'i 'bel ba'i gtam 'ur chil le ba zla
ba de'i ngo gang la legs par bsgrubs/ de yang 'dar nas byams pa lags kyis mang ja/ nas 'bo/ rags rdzong nas chos rje bla ma thugs rje rnam rgyal gyis mang ja/ chos rje
spe ring pa dang / chos rje dbon rams pa dpal ldan gnyis kyis mang ja re yong gsung na'ang de steng ma sleb/ nye mkhar nas mang ja/ g.ye sde pa nas mang ja/ mus nas mang
ja/ nyang stod phyogs nas rtse chen sde pa dang / gzims lags kyi mang ja/ sde pa stag rtse nas mang ja/ tshong 'dus nas mang ja/ dbang ldan nas drung chen drung gi mang
ja/ bla brang nas mang ja zung nas 'gyed sogs zur zhus mang ja shin tu mang ba sogs chos thog de la dgong ja 'chag med/ skabs su zung 'brel sogs gtsang zhing gya nom pa'i
bsnyen bkur thos bsam gyi sgro 'dogs gcod pa'i legs bshad kyi dga' ston/ bla ma rab tu dgyes pa'i thos bsam gyi mchod pa'i sprin phung snyan grags kyi

char rgyun zim pas 'gro ba tshim par byed pa'i legs byas shin tu bstar ba yin no/ /rkang 'thung lo bcud zil dngar na bun gyis/ /rnam dpyod lha lam sgrib kyang dri ro yis/ /rnam
'byed ljags kyi glog 'khyug 'brug gi sgras/ /rgol ngan snying rab gas kyang legs bshad kyi/ /'chi med bdud rtsi snying la zegs pa yis/ /srog gi 'tshe ba slar log bag
phebs nas/ /sgra dbyangs rgyud mangs glu la yid chags te/ /sems kyi ri bo mi g.yo brtan par gyur/ /gong gi sbrul lo 'du khang gsar bcos grub ma thag snar thang nas mi'i
dbang pos 'du khang gsar bcos kyi dga' ston yin no gsung 'dus pa'i tshogs la mang ja bzang ba/ zhib thal nas khal brgya/ sger la dar yug gis gtso byas pa'i gnang sbyin bdun
tshan dang bcas pa bka' drin bskyangs/ chos lugs srol 'byed pa'i sde srid ches/ /'dir mnyan yod chos grwa dar 'di la/ /thugs dgyes pa'i dga' ston dpag med stsal/ /rgyal
sras bcas legs so'i rnga dbyangs sgrogs/ /yang gdong dga' nas mi'i dbang po rnam par rgyal bas kyang 'du khang gi dga' ston rkang 'thung rtse ja/ gnang skyes gya nom pa
dang bcas pa mdzad/ 'du khang bcos pa'i lo lam 'bras slob bshad dang mkhar las lhan cig tu btsugs pa'i tshe slob bshad kyi ming gi snyan gyi bu ga cung zad rtsub pa dang
/ ngos la thugs dgyes pa'i snyan tshig spel legs kyi 'phreng ba na bka' bstan bcos kyi mtho ba ma gtogs gzhan la med pa'i g.yer chos kyi mtho ba min zhes sogs slob bshad
la zur za ba'i tshig rigs mang po gnang byung kyang spyir slob bshad tshogs bshad kyi yin min 'gro ldog shes pa la thog mar

de skabs slob ma dang tshogs pa gnyis kyi khyad par shes dgos/ de nas de gnyis la bshad rgyu'i chos kyi rnam dbye shes dgos pa la brjod bya'i don la rtog dpyod ma shar bzhin
du ming tsam gyi thugs 'tshang ba bden yang nyan thos senta pas theg pa chen po'i chos bka' ma yin zhes smra ba la rgyal tshab byams pas/ thos rjes 'brangs te blo ldan
thob nas ni/ /gang zhig thos la rab tu brnyas byed na/ /rnam pa sna tshogs dpag tu med 'dus ni/ /rmongs pa gang gi phyir na nges par byed/ /ces khyed nyan thos senta pas
theg chen gyi chos bka' ma yin zhes skur ba 'debs pa mi rigs te/ de bka' yin min shes pa la theg chen chos kyi tshig mtha' dag rna bas thos shing / don la yin min gyi rtog
dpyod shar ba zhig dgos pa las khyed de lta bu ma yin pa'i phyir zhes gsungs pa 'di tshig dngos bstan senta pa la 'phangs kyang don gyi snying po mkhas rlom gzhan dag la
phog snang ba'i phyir dang / sa paNDi tas/ bsngo ba de yang mdor bsdus na/ /gnas dang gnas ma yin pa gnyis/ /zhes de dag gi lung sbyor dang bcas gsungs kyang bu ston rjes
'brang dang bcas pa sogs gnas dang gnas min gyi bsngo ba'i don thugs la ma chags shing mdo de dag las/ 'di gnas kyi bsngo ba/ 'di gnas min gyi bsngo ba zhes pa'i ming
byang zhig dngos su ma 'byar ba dang / rab dbye las/ de ltar bshad pa'i don ma dgongs bzhin du tshig de la skrag nas/ gnas dang gnas min gyi bsngo ba zhes pa bka' bstan bcos
gang nas kyang bshad pa ma mthong zhes sogs kyi mu cor smra ba dang sgra ji bzhin du mtshungs pa'i phyir ro/ /de lta bu'i lan yang thung tsam

'bul dgos byung ba yin no/ /chos slob tshogs bshad pa gces pa'i bu/ /rang nyams len 'phangs par mchis bzhin du/ /ma smyon mos bu ngo ma shes bzhin/ /khong mkhas rnams bzhad
gad thag ge ba/ /yang rang lo nga bzhi pa shing mo bya lo rin spungs nas dpon zhang ma mthun par bsam rtse sku mdun gyi zhal bdag gnang ba'i skabs phyogs kyi dbon rigs la
mjal phrad la phyin/ bsam rtser sku mdun dang mjal rigs lung dogs gcod sogs shin tu 'phel bar byung / sku mdun zhal nas chos thams cad bden par ma grub pa'i gnad kyis mtshan
nyid pa'i rigs pa 'di gang sgrub sgrub yin pa 'dug gsung / 'jig rten rgan po'i gtam shin tu ngo mtshar/ de nas rin spungs la mjal 'dod yod pa la gzhan rnams zer dus
sku mdun la zhus na mi dgyes pa mdzad zer/ rang gi gsang na mi legs bsam dngos bstan zhus pas shin tu phebs pas thus/ yang pa rnam na sde pa rgyal po bzhugs pas der mjal
tsam gnang na yang go chod gsung shin tu dgyes pa mdzad/ gnang sbyin zur gsos lam chas gya nom pa gnang yar lam yang 'dir byon cig gsung / bya bzang sogs la lam bde mi bde
ji ltar yod zhus pas dog ste dog po yod kyang skyon te mi skyon phebs yig byas pas chog gsungs nas lam yig gnang / thal le phyin pas lam bde mo byung rin sbungs su mjal
thugs dgyes par byung / phugs 'di phyogs na gnas dben po yang yod mthun rkyen yang 'dzom po yod khor re bzhugs pa zhig e yong de bdag gis lag tu mi longs zhus/ phyag g.yog
rnams na re gzhan drag zhan kun gyis 'gro 'tsham

byed pa zhig 'dug kyang khyed dpon slob rnams mjal du byon pa dga' mo yin zer/ khong mthon po'i mtha' ltung bsags pa 'dzad kyi don/ /gzhan drag zhan kun rang mal na mi 'dug
pas/ /khyed nga rgyal dang zhum pa 'di spang na legs/ /dus 'gyur ba la nam yong rang mi 'dug go /de nas yar lam bsam rtser khyogs phyin pas shin tu dgyes/ slar yang gnang
sbyin lam chas sogs gang ci nas bzabs par mdzad/ bya gshongs su sleb chos 'chad nyan shin tu 'phel ba byung / yang mjal phrad kyi re shig shar lam srad la byas dbang ldan
du shog gsung drung chen rin rgyam pas snga 'phar zhig byung / de ga gzhin rdzing lung bar chen bla brang sogs su sbyin bdag rnams kyi bza' bca'i cho ga skang 'thung gi
ngal gso 'bul skyes sogs bzabs par byas/ de nas yom lag gi mdun thang ka der sngar khong rnams dang zhal 'dris med kyang khro phu ba'i zhal ngor 'dug pas bya gshongs zhen
gyis gsol ja shin tu bzad ba/ rogs rnams la skom gyi ngal gso sogs shin tu smar ba byung / de nas de'i la bud mtshams srad kyi mda' der zhag gcig bsdad/ srad rdzong dpon
gyis gsol 'degs sogs bzabs par byas/ srad phu do dper zhag gcig bsdad khong sngar srad kyi bdag po lta bu yang byas zer ba'i grong pa shin tu bzang ba zhig 'dug pa des
chos zhus sna len sogs yang dag byas/ de nas srad kyi thang ka byang thang 'dra ba 'dug pa de dang la zhig 'dug pa de brgal nas dbang ldan du sleb/ srad lung pa dog kyang
dkyus thag ring / /sa rgyus med kyi mgron la ngo shes byas/ /thang yangs kyang ri bong 'gros kyis sleb/ /gnas dbang

ldan chos 'khor rtse mor son/ /de nas drung chen drung dang sde srid sku mched sogs shin tu dgyes shing zhag bcu skor bsdad/ drung chen drung gis bar tsho shag na rab gsal
gsar pa ka gnyis ma/ phug na gzims chung kun spyod dang bcas pa 'dug pas 'di khyed la ched gtad bcos pa yin bzhugs brtan pa dang / phebs bzhud kyi 'byon lam 'di rang la mdzad
dgos gsung / tshe 'khrid/ sgrol dkar 'khrid/ rnam sras gtor 'dzugs/ bskang gso sogs dang gzhan yang dbang rjes gnang shin tu mang ba zhogs ja gsum sbrel/ srod ja gzims
chung zur pa zhig tu me skor dang ja gsum sgrel sogs shin tu skyid skyid rang mdzad/ bza' btung gi cho ga shin tu bstar ba dang / chos 'chad/ mgur ma sogs spro seg ge
ba mdzad pa zhig 'dug /sde srid sku mched kyang res 'ga' bar tsho shag tu phebs/ res 'ga' nga cag rtser 'bod pa gnang chos dang zang zing gi rnam gzhag 'jig rten gzhan snang
gi blo'i ra ba las 'das pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i legs tshogs shin tu che ba byung / yul dbang ldan gyi rin cen rgya mtsho de/ /dpal 'byor pa rnam thos kyi bu dang 'gran/
/chos dad 'dun mi phyed lhag bsam brtan/ /sems dga' spro'i ngang du nyin mtshan 'da'/ /de nas skyid mkhar dgon pa rdzong thug drung chen gyis kyang skyel ma la byon/
de 'tshams rim pas rtse chen du sleb sde pa 'tsho lags thugs dgyes pa chen po dang bcas deng 'bum chen bstan pa gnyis la khyed rang dpon slob gnyis nga'i gzims chung du
shog /phyag phyi 'di tsho byang pa yin pas brkun ma brkus yong gsung bzhad gad mdzad/ gzims chung gi lam thams cad mar tshugs kyi

steng la 'gro dgos pa'i rab gsal zhig 'dug sleb tsa na gsol ja brgyugs byung bas mdog rgya mdog bltas pa tsam gyi yid tshim pa zhig 'dug /'bum chen thugs rab tu dgyes ja la
zur mig log ge gzigs ja'i mdog las gzigs 'di lta bu'i ja byang phyogs la mi yong lags hub gcig bzhes g.ya'/ 'di la dro ba 'di yin zhig ni mi 'dug zer nged rnams bzhad gad
thag ge byung / de nas 'tsho lags kyis khyed bya rgod gshongs pa la slob gnyer smar ba ma gtogs longs spyod che bsam pa su la yang med/ deng sang gi sde dpon skya sogs
la 'bul 'bul chen po 'byor yang mi 'byor byed yang mi byed ngo tsha med 'di tshos phul ba'i lan re yang byas mi yong gsung / bla ma rin po che'o brgyal na phongs 'di tsho
phul cig gsung / nged rang gis ja khug tsho ja rtse mos bkang dar ras sogs phung por spungs nas gnang / gzhan bzhin zal zal byas 'bul mi dgos gsungs/ yul rtse chen chos
blon 'tsho lags de/ /spyir lugs gnyis kyi srol la rnam dpyod bkra/ /sgos chos byed kyi mi la lhag par dad/ /bdag 'khos chung la ci 'dod sgrub pa bzhin lags/ /de nas rtse
chen dpon blon lhag par gzims lags sku mched khu dbon sogs kyis dad 'dun mthun sbyor phun sum tshogs pa da'i bar du rgyun bsrings nas mdzad pa zhig yin/ thugs snying nas
dad pa'i rtse chen nas/ /dus rgyun gyi zhib thal brgya phrag gnyis/ /skyes dam pa tshong 'dus gra lnga nas/ /dus rgyun gyi zhib thal brgya phrag bzhi/ /gnas dbang ldan dang
snar thang sde srid sogs/ /dus rgyun dang res 'jog gi zhib thal sogs/ /dus

snyigs dus kyi grwa sa 'dzin pa la/ /lha gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi cho ga bstar/ /de nas rim par bya gshongs su sleb/ sbrul lo 'du khang gsar bzhengs kyi rab gnas la rje
mkhan rin po che sbyan drangs/ yar lam rang gis kyang phyag phyi byas 'dar du yong 'dar nas sa skyong mi dbang a rin dpal bzang gis bya rgod gshongs su ni 'chad nyan smar
la 'du khang sogs thes che ba zhig byung 'dug /da sgos tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i chos rgyun skyong ba la khyed mi dgos kha med du 'dug pas khyed phebs pa zhig byung
na lo bcu yin na'ang bsgug nus pa de yin/ da 'dir yang cung zad 'phyug pa 'dug pas grang chen du phebs dgos rab rgyun bzhugs tha na'ang nyis 'dzin tsam gnang dgos gsung
nan chags mdzad/ bdag gis rab la rje tshar chen gyis thugs shin tu dgyes pa mdzad kyang gsung ngag lam 'bras/ spros med/ gser chos bcu gsum/ mgon po phyi nang gi 'khrid/
rjes gnang phran bu tsam ma gtogs gsung chos thob rgya med/ rje bla ma de'i bstan pa zin thub pa zhig mi yong lags zhus pas/ gsung chos de rnams kyis cis kyang chog pa 'dug
/rje bla ma'i chos lugs kyi bstan pa khyed kyi mi 'dzin na su yis 'dzin gsung bka' nan brji ba rang phebs kyin 'dug /rje mkhan rin po che'i gsung nas kyang 'dar nas zhal
ngo 'di tsho dang thog nas khyed rang la thugs dkar ba'i steng du zhabs drung rin cen dpal bzang 'di shin tu thugs zhen che ba 'dug pas phugs ma 'di khas len dgos/ 'on
kyang zhabs drung 'di sku khams bzang po rang mi 'dug pas 'di'i sku khams kyi shan phyed pa zhig byed dgos de ma phye na 'phrod mi 'phrod kyi thugs

phrad legs nyes yong gsungs/ 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i mi dbang mchog /dpon khu dbon yum sras 'khor dang bcas/ /chos lugs gnyis la dad pa rab tu brtan/ /bka' mi 'gyur brtan
pas bzlog ma nus/ /de nas zhabs drung sku khams cung bsnyel zer bya gshongs su phyag rtags byung 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i rtser sleb/ zhabs drung la tshe bka' sgrol
dkar sogs rnam grangs mang du phul/ zhabs drung chos lhun drung gis rje tshar chen la gsol ba 'debs pa'i bla ma mchod chog sbros med la brten pa zhig dgos gsung / spros
med bla ma mchod chog de yang de dus brtsams nas phul/ drung 'tsho rtsa brgyad pa'i drung gis sman dpyad bcos legs phul sku khams skyon med yong gsungs/ phu'i chab la yang
mchod yon lhan du byon chab mdzad pa'i nub nas zhal ras kyi gdong cung zad skrang snyam pa 'dug chab mi 'phrod pa min nam byas pas drung 'tsho ba'i drung 'dis bzod gsung
de'i 'phro la sku khams dga' mo byung / mkhar 'dar stod rnam rgyal stag rtse na/ /dpon dpa' brdar mdzangs 'dzom mang na yang / /lugs gnyis mkhyen dpyod ldan mgu byed pa/
/dpon rin chen dpal bzang sa 'di'i rgyan/ /de nas kho bos bya gshongs su chos 'chad la phyin/ rta lo de'i mjug zla ba bcu gcig pa la zhabs drung rin chen dpal bzang sku
tshes ma zin zer nged kyis kyang sku tshigs gcig gi bar 'dar du yong / bya gshongs dgun chos dang thug nas gzhan sdod skabs ni ma byung / gzhan mchor chas kyi drag mdog
mi che yang / /lugs bkur skyong la dam pa'i spyod pa mdzes/ /khong dpyod ldan gyi dgra gnyen kun gyis smon/ /dus 'gyur ba la mig chu'i

char pa 'bebs/ /zhabs drung chos dbang rin chen de yang sku btsun zhing lugs gnyis la mkhyen rab kyi spyan phye ba zhig yod pa des kyang grwa tshang gi 'dzin skyong lugs gnyis
thad nas phun sum tshogs pa mdzad/ rje tshar chen gyi bu chen rje mkhyen brtse/ rje rab brtan pa sogs la yang gus zhabs shin tu che/ kho bo cag la yang thugs bsam shin
tu dkar tshe bka' lam dbang sogs mang du zhus/ lo star gyi lam dbang ma chag pa zhig zhu yo gsung / grang mo che'i 'du khang gsar bzhengs tshar ba'i lo bdag gnyis car gyis
gzigs rtog la byon/ kho bos sngon la skor ba byas pas 'du khang gyang 'khris na chos rnga chen po zhig 'dug pa de'i rnga lde kho bo'i mdun du krog zer tshar byung kho
bos kyang rnga 'di brdungs zer ba'i brda yin pa 'dug byas rnga 'ur de ba zhig brdungs/ phyis bsams pas rje mkhan gyis kyang ngam ring chos sder grwa skor la byon pa'i lo
chos gling 'du khang du gzims/ chos gling gi rnga ril de brdungs pa'i mtshan lam byung ba phyis chos gling dpon slob mdzad dgos pa'i snga ltas su byung ba de dran/ kho bo
cag la yang de 'dra'i snga ltas shig yin srid na'ang bya gshongs gdan sa 'di 'jog thub na gzhan dgon pa'i 'dzin bdag blo thag chod bsam pa byung / phyis gdung bzhugs pa'i
lha khang gsar pa tshar ba'i tshe'ang mjal du phyin pas rnga ril gsar pa zhig 'dug pa de'i rnga lde mdun du 'tshar byung na'ang sngar gyi rtog pa sngon song des rnga ma
brdungs kyang phyis grwa tshang gi 'dzin bdag dgos pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug /blo sbub 'khums kyi zhen pa ltas pas na/ /gnas gsar pa la a gsar mi che yang / /rje bla ma dang
mkha' 'gro chos skyong gis/ /rgyud

yang yang bskul nas dbang mi 'dug /de nas 'dar rtse'i mi dbang chos skyong lhun grub khu dbon yum sras dang chos 'khor yang rtse'i che bgres rnams kyis mi sna bskul lcags yang
yang byung / khyad par bka' drin mtshungs bral 'jam mgon bla ma'i zhal gdams de yang dran/ lug gi lo ston ka 'dar du yong dgos shar zhal ngo rnams bka' bgros nas rje
tshar chen gyis kyang thog mar phu thub bstan dge 'phel gyi zhal bdag gnang 'dug pas de ka rten 'brel legs gsungs nas thog mar phu la phyin/ phu'i grwa pa rnams kyis ser
sbreng byas yul 'gros sogs kyang shin tu legs pa byung / phyag 'bul rtsis len sogs legs che ba'i rten 'brel 'grig /drin 'gran bral tshar chen chos rje des/ /gtam sngon med
chos 'khor bskor ba'i gnas/ /gling thub bstan dge 'phel chos kyi khrir/ /chos ngo mtshar rgyun gyi bstan pa dar/ /de nas nged kyis tsha lung skyid mo gshongs su sleb/ sang
nyin gza' skar 'dzom pas chos 'khor yang rtse'i phyag 'bul len pa la 'byon dgos gsung / nang par snga ba'i cha la mi dbang bsod nams lhun chen dang / dgra 'dul don grub
sku mched kyis gtsos pa'i chibs rags rnams kyi ser sbreng / dar gdugs sgra rol cha dang bcas phyin pas bya rog shin tu mang ba brgya phrag tsam 'phur zhing lding bas skyid
gshongs nas dgon pa'i bar la thibs thibs byung bas chos skyong srung ma rnams kyis bsu ba yin par 'dug zer ba yang byung / me tog gi char yang shin tu mang ba babs zer/
de'i nyin phyag 'bul gyi dga' ston legs tshogs shin tu che ba byung / rje bla ma'i 'jigs med seng ge'i

khrir/ /khong chos skyong srung mas mdun nas bsus/ /gzhan dad ldan 'phan gdugs rol mos bstar/ /chos slob bshad bstan pa de nas dar/ /khong lhag bsam gyi zla tshes snying la
'khrungs/ /thugs rab dgyes bdud rtsi'i thigs pa 'dzag /lam zab mo'i 'od dkar phyogs brgyar 'phro/ /gzhan phas rgol gyi mun btub sa mthar bros/ /de nas lug /sprel/ bya khyi'i
bar dgos gal che ba'i skabs re tsam ma gtogs bya gshongs su 'chad nyan 'chag med byas/ spre lo dpyid nged rang gi tsha bo snying la gces pa zhig yod pa de de snga yan
rang gi rtsar yod tsa na ku re dang bzhad gad byed kyin dga' sag ge yong ba zhig yod kyang / nang zhig zhogs chos steng nas bla brang du sleb tsam na nged kyi gzhogs su
gleng mo yang mi zer bar ngo mnan nas bsdad 'dug /sems la mi 'dod pa zhig byung 'dug bsam pa ma gtogs rang dpe lta la yengs nas ci yin zer ba yang ma byung / snga chos grol
nas nged kyi 'khris su byung sngar gyi nad thu mo de langs nas shin tu na ba zhig 'dug zer bas sems shin tu 'tshab drung 'tsho legs grub pa pos sman bcos 'dra byas/ rang
gis tshe dbang / tshogs su mang ja sogs rim gro ci lcogs byas kyang skyed mi 'dug sngar yin na tshe dbang la skyed thon tsam yod kyang da lan skyed ye mi 'dug bu tsha
'di 'tsho thub pa zhig mi yong ba 'dra byas pas/ drung 'tsho ba khyed rang sems chung bas yin 'di la de 'dra'i skyon ci yod zer/ drung 'tsho legs grub pas dgos med kyi stong
skad chen po zer ba la kho blo 'gro mo mi 'dug pas rog tsho byang pa rdor smyon yang spyan drangs/ dge 'dun rnams kyis rim gro yang tshad med byas kyang zhag bcu gsum
bcu bzhi song tsa na sman pa

gnyis gros bcas kyi sman zhig btang bas rig pa mog tu ka song / nyi ma dgongs song ba la sngar mig sdod pa ye mi yong ba la mig phra hrig pa zhig bltas byung cung zad drag
tu 'gro ba e yin bsam tsa na de'i 'phro la mig skya rlog byas song stobs gzhan ston rgyu ni ma byung / 'da' ka ma'i gsal 'debs rgyas pa zhig byas/ sang snga dro bltas pas
tshangs bug rus pa rim pa log ge ba zhig 'phags 'dug /de nas steng du phyin rje mkhan la thugs dam 'dogs kyi zhu yig cig bzhengs tsa na sems shin tu skyo kho chung chung
nas pha ma spun zla rnams rgyab tu bskyur/ nged kyi rjes la bsgyil bas ma thub par 'brangs g.yog go chod med thabs med pa zhig byas te me tog dbyar skam gyis dus 'di lta
bu byung snyam mchi ma yang mang du shor/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs pa sogs rogs rnams kyang de 'dra ma mdzad zer zhing mig chu mang du gtong gin 'dug /rang yid la gcags pa
gces pa'i snying / /kho 'chi bdag bdud kyis khral nas song / /sems skyo nas mig chu'i thigs pa 'bab/ /las bsags pa myong snyam sdug bsran bskyed/ /snying rje nas bzod thabs
mi 'dug kyang / /chos 'da' ka zab mo'i 'phrul 'khor gyis/ /sems skar mda' 'phangs bzhin gnas bzang bskyal/ rang de tsam yin snyam blos sna bsring / /rang dar rgyas kyi
rnam thar skyong tsa na/ /ci byas kyang bde bde 'dra lags na'ang / /dus 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal zhig dran tsa na/ /gnas ri khrod cig dran pas blos sna thungs/ /de nas bka'
lnga pa grags bzang dang thog nas gus zhen shin tu che bas rogs byas/ tsha bo'i don du mang ja

'gyed bcas sogs btang bu tsha 'da' ba'i gong tsam du bya gshongs gling khrod du nub dgon dge slong zhig 'da' ba'i sngas mgor 'pho ba la phyin 'da' ka gsal 'debs byas/ sang
snga dro rogs rnams kyis bltas pas tshangs bug brdol byang sems 'dzags/ mgo bo'i skra dang snyel tho gnyis 'byar nas 'dug zer/ nged rang gi g.yog rnam rgyal klu sgrub zer
ba zhig yod pa des rang re'i bla ma 'dis mi'i thod pa gcog na shes shes zer/ de nas rang gis kyang dpe lta dang bsam mno rgyun chags la btang bas po ti so so'i gzhung 'grel
gyi bshad pa/ rang lugs kyi brda chad zhib rgyas/ rang dang gzhan khul du dogs pa gcod pa'i lung rigs kyi rnam gzhag tshig tsam ma yin par nges pa 'grongs/ mkhas pa gong
ma dag gis dgag sgrub mdzad pa la yang legs nyes kyi shan 'byed pa'i rnam dpyod kyi spobs pa gzhan la ji mi snyam pa shar chos 'chad pa la yang spro sag ge ba byung /
slob ma rnams kyis kyang rang gis gang bshad kha nas lhung ma thag sus thob byas bzung zin ma thag skyong thar 'ur chil le ba byas pas rang gzhan spro sag ge ba zhig yod
kyang bya lo'i gzhug de tsam nas tho rengs skar ma khra chil le ba rlung po 'ur chil le ba la ldang dgos pa de la 'tsher bya shin tu che ba byung / chos khri'i steng du
sleb rang gi lam bsdus byed ring grwa pa rnams kyang sib sib 'dus shar sbyangs 'ur thag ge ba byas/ gaNDe byung 'phral gling so so nas grwa pa rnams chos grwa la sus thob
byas sgo thag zer zhing 'dus yong ba shin tu brod pa zhig yong / de stabs kyi gdan sa 'jog zer ba yang ma nus/ lo na tshod kyis lus sems khogs na yang / /yul dbus

gtsang gi blo gsal dad 'dus la/ /chos legs bshad 'chad la yid chags nas/ /dus nyin mtshan 'das pa ma tshor ro/ /de nas khyi lo'i tshe rang ltos kyi slob bu 'di rnams bskyur
mi phod kyang rang lo yang drug cu rtsa bzhir sleb/ bla ma gong ma rnams kyis kyang drug cu rtsa bzhi thal nas sus kyang 'di'i 'chad nyan pher ba zhig ma byung 'dug pas/
rang gis kyang 'di mtshams 'jog thub pa zhig legs pa 'dra bsam mang ja gcig gi steng du nged kyi lo drug cu rtsa bzhir sleb chos 'chad nyan hril po lo bcu gnyis song 'dug
/kun mkhyen lcags thang pa chen po dang / 'jam mgon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis kyang 'chad nyan lo nyi shu rtsa bdun re mdzad 'dug kyang dgung lo drug cu rtsa
bzhi pa la gdan sa 'jog pa gnang 'dug /nged kyis kyang lo drug cu rtsa bzhir sleb 'di yi 'chad nyan pher ba yang dka' mo 'dug /khyed rnams kyis go shes skyed gdan sa'i thus
bya rogs gyis zhes nan gyis glengs pas/ yar 'brog pa drung rams pa gsung rab zer ba zhig yod pa de ka gdong du langs nas bla ma rin po che de skad mi gsung ba zhu nged
grwa pa rnams kyis dad 'dun ci byas ni thugs la mnga'/ sa thag ring po nas 'bog khras re khur nas grwa sa dang / bla ma la gtad nas yongs 'di bskyur phod na grwa pa kha
dmar 'di rnams kyi mgo su yis 'don rgyu yin zer nas skad bton te mchi ma byung / de nas tshogs pa thams cad kyis langs nas phyag phul/ mchi ma phyung 'du khang gi nang thams
cad ngu tshi theg pa byung / rang gis kyang lan zlog ma nus/ dbu mdzad la chos spyod kyi brda byas pas dbu mdzad kyi langs nas

chos spyod bskul kyang lkog 'degs mkhan yang ma byung / dbu mdzad rang yang mchi ma shor nas mgo phur nas sdod dgos byung / rang yang grwa pa 'di rnams kyang bden rang shi
yang 'di tsam gyi ngu dbyangs byed mi nus snyam sems skyo nas mchi ma mang po shor/ rang gi rogs bzang nga zer ba 'dis nyung ja 'debs pa la yong tshe gra pa rnams de ltar
spyan chab bsil ba mthong sems skyo sdug drags nas sdod ma nus par bros nas phyin zer/ khong grwa pa rnams chos kyi 'dod pas gdungs/ /yid gdung shugs kyi dad pas mchi ma
'dzag /ngag mgrin pa rnams 'dar bzhin du dbyangs byas/ /rang dran 'dzin gyi bzung yang mchi ma shor/ /phu gangs kyi ri sul nyi mas bzhu/ /reg bsil ba'i chu klung phyogs
brgyar 'bab/ /gangs ral ba'i gad rgyangs rna ba rtsub/ /yid nges 'byung chu thigs bdud rtsi yin/ /de lta bu'i gtam rtse chen sde pa dpon po bas gsan pas de 'dra ngo mtshar
che grwa skyag gi mig nas mchi ma 'chor ba yid bzhin gyi nor bu bas dkon zer gyin 'dug go zer/ phyogs gzhan na yang de ltar thos pas bya gshongs pas de 'dra dga' mo yin
'di phyogs la bla ma lag 'don mas na rab yin zer gyin 'dug zer/ de nas mang ja de la thus de tsam byung bar grwa pa rnams sems mnong zhing 'gyes dgos byung / de nas khong
grwa pa rnams kyis gsol phu nas 'byor lags dang / phu gsum nas byang sems drung zhu ngo la sbran nas 'du khang du byas na sngar bzhin byung dogs bla brang du gsol ja 'bul
rten bzang po dang bcas lo rgyun mthud dgos pa'i bka' lung nan chags gnang gin 'dug /rang la yang byed dka' mo byung nas

gdan sa pa gcig thus su lhugs pa byas rang gis lo gsum 'di gar bsdad/ zhib thal mgron po'i kha 'dzin sogs sngar bzhin byas nas de tsam la thus don gnang dgos pa 'dra zhus/
khong rnams gnyis kyis kyang de bzhin skor yang byas pas grub don de la bsdus/ gdan sa'i thus byas pas chos rje byams bzang ba brtag pa dang po/ /'ga' rong pa gnyis pa yin
pas khong bzhis gdan 'dren la phyin chos rje byams bzang pa sku gzugs kyis mi lcogs gsung ma byon/ chos rje 'ga' rong pa 'byon par byas sngar 'khyud bzhin zla ba bdun pa
la bkod par byas/ rang gi bsam pa la de ltar byung na shin tu legs 'dug /'chad nyan gyi rkang gdan sa pas gnang rang gi sngar gyi yig cha rtsom 'phro rnams 'phro rdzogs
pa dang / slar rtsom dgos pa 'dra grub na'ang grwa sa la phan pa 'dug bsam pa'i blo bde 'bol la byas/ phyis gdan sa bskos nas sngar bzhin chad don la gnas pa zhig dgos gsung
yong ngam bsam byung tsa na/ de 'dra'i 'phros zur tsam yang ma byung bas rang bde sar thon blo bde 'bol le shig ge ba zhig de nas byung ba yin/ sngar kun mkhyen chen
po lcags thang pas rmi lam du brgyud byin gyis brlabs zhabs dang seg ka li spyi bor bzhag smon lam mang du mdzad khyod la lo cu gnyis las sdod dbang mi 'dug gsung ba de
bya gshongs su khyi lo nas khyi lo'i bar lo ngo bcu gsum yin kyang hril po bcu gnyis yin pas/ de nas 'dar grang chen du rje tshar chen gyi chos skyong gis rang dbang med
par bkug pa de'i lung bstan du yid ches par byas

pa yin no/ /khong sbyin bdag gnyis kyi bka' ma chogs/ /bdag g.yo zog med par dam bcas kyang / /rje tshar chen chos srung gnyan po yis/ /dam bcas pa'i ra ba brgal nas song /
/rang lhag bsam gyi 'ja' ris drang na yang / /gzhan 'gyu mang gi rdul dmar tshub se ba/ /khong thugs 'char gyi gzhan rlung dri ngan yang / /rang lhag bsam gyi dri bzang
'khor bas brod/ /ci gzhan bsam 'khrul pa min yang sla/ /'khor chos skyong srung mas blo kha bsgyur/ /bdag rang gi re ba rdzogs nas song / /khyed bu slob rnams rang sems ma
'pham zhig slar gdan sa gsar bskos kyi tshe mkhan chen bzang po bkra shis kyis mkhan blo gros rnam rgyal gsar bskos kyi tshe sbyin bdag kha kha so so la sbyor sprod la
phebs 'dug /bdag gis kyang 'jam mgon sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan la de bzhin phebs pa zhig dgos zhus kyang mi dgos gsung zhal gyis ma bzhes/ 'o na bdag mjal phrad la 'gro ba
la thugs rgyus kyi steng nas rab 'byams pa 'di dang 'di rgyug gsung ba zhig dgos zhus kyang khyed rang gis mdzad pas yong gsung ma mdzad/ de nas nged rang gis rtse chen
rab 'byams pa chos 'phel dang / byang pa rab 'byams pa nam mkha' sogs khrid nas phyin da lan yang chos rje gdan sa pas sbyin bdag rnams la sbyor sprod la 'gro dgos gsung
byung ba la sngar ci rigs 'dug kyang grwa sa la phan na cis kyang phyin pas chog zhus/ gnas mnyan yod chos kyi skyed tshal nas/ /gzhan gdan sa 'phrod pa'i dga' spror bcas/
/bdag dpon slob rnams kyang lam du chas/ /khong lha mi dad pas skyel bsu byas/ /de nas nged rang gi rogs drung

rams pa 'jam dbyangs/ drung rams pa nam mkha'/ rje dpon skyid gshongs pa ming dngos mang thos byams pa smra ba'i dbang phyug /ding sang 'gro mgon du grags pa rtags dbon bzang
nga / ri mo ba bstan rgyan rnams khrid/ bya gshongs nas rdzing lung du ja sbyor gsum tsam gyi bar bsdad nas ber chen bla brang du sleb/ gnas tshang rnams kyis dga' spro
dpag tu med pa byas tshe dbang dgos zer de ga bzhin byas/ lam bar gyi thab chas sogs kyang dngos gtsang phul/ de nas sang nyin gung tshig la srad rgod dang snar thang du
sleb/ phun tshogs gling du snar thang sde srid dang mjal 'bel ba'i gtam shin tu smra ba byung gnang sbyin zur gsos sogs shin tu bzabs pa mdzad/ yong khar sde srid rang
bzhengs nas khyed 'dzam gling mkhas pa'i nyi ma yin pas yang dang yang du mjal lo gsung byung kyang de man chad mjal ba gcig ma byung / khong snar thang mi yi dbang po des/
/chos 'bel ba'i gtam la shin tu dgyes/ /thugs snang ba dag pas dgag sgrub 'phel/ /yid dpyod ldan thal sbyar mdong gsol phul/ /de nas sang nyin bsam grub rtser sleb gnas
gtsang 'bum khang pa rnying pa rnams ni mi 'dug /grang chen pa la 'bum khang gnang 'dug pas der bsdad grang chen pas kyang gnas mgron gyi dam tshig gtsang ma bsrungs/ rtse
na sde pa kun spangs drung dang mthu stobs drung bzhugs pa dang mjal/ bu ram gor la sogs pa bzhes spro'i rnam grangs shin tu mang ba dang gnang sbyin zur gsos sogs bzabs
par gyur/ dpon sa rgyal

chen gling mas kyang gzims chung du gsol cha bzhes spro sogs gnang / sprul sku sman thang nas dang rtse chen sde pa phun tshogs pas kyang gsol ja shangs len sogs mdzad/ mkhar
ming can bsam grub rtse chen na/ /mi g.yer can gyi kun spangs mched dang mjal/ /srol 'jig rten gyi gzhung lugs de na 'dug /gtam snyan grags kyi dril rnga sgrog cing snang
/ /sang nyin tshong 'dus su sleb gnas po shar ba'i khang par bsdad/ tshong 'dus gzims khang rnying par sde pa lhun chen dang mjal/ 'phags pa'i sku 'dra 'bul thob ma sogs
rten ngo mtshar can mang po mjal/ sde pa lhun drung gis shangs len sogs shin tu bzabs pa mdzad/ gnas tshong 'dus kyi gzims khang rnying pa na/ /dus de tshe ngo mtshar
gyi ltas mo mthong / /dus deng sang sa phung gi shul yang med/ /gnas 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal 'dis yid rab 'phyo/ /gnas der gnas po shar ba'i gnas mo des shin tu gus par byed
gsol ja gsol thug sogs kyang gnas mo rang gis sbyor/ ja rtse rdum gcig nyos pa'i phud yin zer nas ja bzang po sbyar nged kyis ma phu bar lhag ma gzhan la ster grabs byas
pas ngas dad pas zhus pa yin gzhan la gnang bas mi yong zer ster du ma bcug /de nas nged kyis rgyan gong lha khang du rje sa paN gyis bsnyen rdzogs mdzad dus dbu skra
bsil ba'i rdo kyong yod zer mjal du phyin/ rje tshar chen zhwa lu'i mkhan po gnang dus bdag rkyen mdzad pa yin zer khri mthon po zhig gi steng na rdo gzhong chen po zhig
'dug /de nas phyag 'bul byin rlabs zhus tshon rtsi'i dar lcog btsugs smon lam gsol btab byas/ dpal ldan ma'i lha khang zer

ba'i lha khang mun pa gnag ge ba zhig gi nang nas dpal ldan ma bzhugs zer/ de dmag zor ma dang don gcig mtshan gyi rnam grangs su 'dug pas mjal du phyin/ skye dman gos smug
khra gyon pa zhig gis mjal sna byas mjal mchod gtor phul mchod sprin gsol btab sogs byas/ gnas nyang smad rgyan gong lha khang du/ /rje 'jam dbyangs sa skya paNDi tas/ /khong
kha che'i mkhan po paN chen la/ /don bsnyen par rdzogs tshe mig sman mdog /dbu lcang lo'i zur phud mchod pa'i tshe/ /lha gnas nas babs pa'i ganggA'i chus/ /gzhan ma
dag bkru ba'i zla shel gyi/ /snod tha gru yangs pa'i yol sgo mjal/ /khongs sa skya'i 'jam dbyangs gzhon nu de/ /thugs dgyes nas mngon dga'i zhing khams nas/ /bdag mdun du
dngos su byon no snyam/ /sems dga' spro'i ba spu ci yang g.yo/ /khong dpal ldan lha mo dmag zor ma/ /zhal mjal tshe skye dman tshul 'dzin de/ /gzugs gzhan bsgyur sprul
pa yin pa'ang srid/ /rdzas mchod gtor phul nas smon lam btab/ /tshong 'dus kyi zhol de na sngags pa'i tshul 'dzin lung bstan 'dra 'dra gtam chol le ba zer ba zhig 'dug pa
des khyed bya gshongs bla ma yin na phyag g.yog cig la mjal gyis zer/ gzhan 'phrad mkhan ni ma byung gsol dpon 'gro ba zer pa des 'phrad pas khyed kyis 'phrad ka mi gtong
'dug ste khyed bya gshongs bla ma yin na sa skya'i gong ma lnga dang mjal ba 'dug go zer/ de dus ni chol gtam du rtsis phyis brtags pas lung bstan dngos yin byas kyang
chog pa 'dug /de'i nyin pa rnam chu spe shar zer ba'i gnas tshang dga'

mo zhig yod pa der bsdad/ sang nam langs la phyin pas pa rnam gyi thang yangs po de la rna ba dang rkang pa shin tu 'khyags nyang stod sa dro zer ba rdzun yin pa 'dra snyam
pa byung / de nas nyang stod stag rtser sleb sde pa chos mdzad pas thugs shin tu dgyes dgyes mdzad skad chen po'i bzhad gad thag ge ba byung zhag gsum bsdad tshe dbang sogs
mang du byas/ de nas nyang stod mkhar kha rdzong du phyin chos sde'i mkhan po mkhan chen lung rigs pa dang mjal thugs dgyes shing gang ci'i gnang sbyin bzhes spro sogs
shin tu bzabs pa mdzad pa zhig 'dug /de nas jo gdan tshogs pa spos khang pa yang bzhugs 'dug pas tshogs pa'i rten mchod rnams dang mjal/ khyad par kha che paN chen gyi
rdza sku bzo rigs pa gcig gis nyin gcig la bdun bcos zer ba'i nang tshan gcig dang / rje btsun dam pa kun dga' grol mchog gis gnang zer ba'i sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel dri
gtsang khang chung ngu zhig gis nang gang ba zhig 'dug pa de dang mjal/ gnas nyang stod mkhar kha'i pho brang na/ /khong spos khang jo gdan tshogs pa bzhugs/ /mkhan lung
rigs dgyes pa'i dga' ston spel/ /rten ngo mtshar can rnams zhal yang mjal/ /de nas snga bar langs ras la chen po de la 'dzegs la mgor sleb tsa na rong nas yongs pa'i tshong
pa bong bu bzhi la mar khu zom brgyud bkal nas yongs pa dang phrad rten 'brel legs byung zer mar khu nas mchod yar sogs byas/ la mgor tsha bzhes bza' ba'i cho ga bstar/
rong de la lam bde mo mi 'dug kyang rkyen skyon med par rin spungs su sleb/ gnas tshang drag po che zer ba snga so'i gnas tshang

yin pa der bsdad/ gnas tshang pa de skyen 'dus dpon yin pas mda' pa rnams der 'dus chang ka sogs byed kyang ca co sogs ye mi nus pa zhig 'dug /gnas tshang pa'i o lo dpal rab
zer ba de mda' shin tu bzang / skyen 'dus dpon drag pa zhig yin pa des bla ma rin po che nga shi ba gsan tsa na se gol gtogs pa zhig mdzad rogs mdzod zer/ de nas gong ra
lo tsA ba rtse nas gnang byung nas khyed la nged sngar yang chos shig zhu bsam pa yod kyang gdan sa ma 'khod pas stabs ma bde/ da gdan sa yang 'khod 'dug pas nged la chos
shig gnang dgos 'di'i tshes brgyad la rgyal phur 'dzom pa sogs rten 'brel legs tshogs che bas chos 'brel gyi thog ma 'go tshugs pa zhig byed do gsung / nged kyis kyang
gzhan zhu ma spobs khyed lta bu'i sde srid chen po la dbang bka' sogs 'bul ba go nad che na'ang dgongs par yod phyin bka' bzlog mi bde zhus/ de nas tshes brgyad kyi bar
zhag lnga zhol du bsdad nyin par bzhugs gral la phyin 'bel gtam sogs shin tu smar ba byung / de'i tshes brgyad snga ma'i cha la phun tshogs gling pa/ byams brtse lags sogs
drung 'khor rags bsdus kyis spos sna byas phyin tshe bka' brgya rtsa'i thog ma'i tshe dbang phul/ de nas sde srid yab yum/ sras nor bu bzang po/ /zla ba bzang po/ /'jam
dpal grags pa/ drag po 'khor lo sgyur ba ste zhal ngo drug la tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ sgrol dkar brgya rtsa/ 'byung 'dul brgya rtsa/ dgyes rdor man ngag lugs kyi smin byed/
dmar po skor gsum/ rnam sras mdung dmar can/ gur zhal gyi rjes gnang sogs dgos gsung pa de

bzhin phul/ kye rdor dbang la kha 'byams mi rung bas phyag g.yog drag pa zhig dang bdun mdzad na zhus pas/ gzhan la mi yong mchod g.yog pas kha bskang bas chog gsung / mchod
g.yog pa rab 'byams pa 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i rgya mtshos byas/ dpon sa yuu ma drung gis khyed rang gsol thab zur pa mdzad na legs gsung / sde srid sku bgres pas khyed
rang dang thag nye gsol ja la thugs dad pas gsol ja rgyugs kyang chog gzhan la'ang gsol ja rgyug mi dgos gsung / dbang gi tshe sde srid drung gis dbrag 'di kha gsol ja rgyugs
pas e chog gsung dgongs pa dang sbyor zhus/ de nas dbang bka' brgya tshar sogs yun ring pa rnams la sde srid gsol thab gsum dang rang re'i gsol ja re ste gsol ja bzhi
tsam re yong gin 'dug /sngon tshe 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po la/ /mtho ba'i khri bshams skye bo 'bum gyi dbus/ /rgya mtsho'i chu blangs rin chen bum pa bzhis/ /spyi
bor dbang bskur bkra shis mnga' gsol bzhin/ /sa steng 'di na rgyal srid mang yod kyang / /chos lugs rigs byed smra ba khyod gcig pu/ /mkha' la 'od ldan grangs med 'khrigs
na yang / /tsha zer 'byin pa rta bdun las gzhan ces zla bo dngos po'i rgyan bzod nas su/ /lhag bsam rab dkar sgra snyan rig byed kyi/ /cha shas yongs rdzogs rin spungs rgyal
srid cher/ /bshes gnyen klu dbang gtsugs nas dbang bskur bas/ /chab srid rgya mtsho'i byings ltar 'phel gyur cig /de nas dbang bka' rnams rim pas grub/ rnam sras mdung
dmar can gyi rjes gnang gi tshe ngag dbang nor bu bzang po'i gsung gis khyed bla ma rnams la yang gsung chos smar zong mang

po yod pas da lan smar cher rang zhig dgos so gsung de ga bzhin gang yod phul/ gtor ma khang brtsegs de yang de 'phral gtor sgam bcos nas gzims chung du 'jug pa gnang song
/ de nas sngar yin na rin spungs 'dir sbyin sreg rgyun chags byed pa zhig yod na'ang phyis ye ma byung da khyed kyis zhi rgyas dbang drag bzhi'i sbyin sreg mdzad dgos gsung
/ rang res drag po ni ma byas drag po yang tshang ba yin pas las thams cad pa'i sbyin sreg dang zhi rgyas dbang gi sbyin sreg ste bzhi byas/ deng sang gi zha lu pa rnams
dang karma pa 'ga' zhig gi phyag srol mchod rdzas rnams kyang me la 'bul ba dang / khyad par sbyin bdag rnams kyang sbyin sreg byed sar yong dgos zer ba dang / dar gos
gser dngul sogs kyang sbyin bdag rang gis smon lam mang po btab nas me nang du bskyur gyin 'dug khyed kyang de ltar byed dam gsung / de ltar gzhan byed pa ni sreg rdzas
dang mchod rdzas kyi shan ma phyed pa 'dra khyad par zhal zas dang gtor ma rnams ni gong du me lha la phul zin pas ro ma gcig me nang du bcug pa la dgos pa ci yod/ gser dngul
sogs rin po che'i rigs 'di sreg rdzas la dgos pa'i skabs yod kyang rnam pa thams cad du min khong rnams phyag len zal snang srol du shor ba 'dra zhus/ zhabs drung sku
bgres pa'i phyag na sbyin sreg gi dpe mang du 'dug /khyad par karma zhwa dmar pa gong ma zhig gis mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg gi dpe par ma chog khrigs shin tu legs pa zhig 'dug
na'ang de tsho na'ang mi 'dug /sbyin bdag sbyin sreg tshe spyan 'dren pa ni bla med dbang gis smin pa yod na de ltar 'gal ba mi

'dug kyang ma smin pa la gsang sgrogs phan yon med zhus/ zhabs drung nor bu bzang po phyag len khyed rang gi 'di dga' ba 'dug pas 'di ga mdzod gsung thugs yid shin tu ches
par mdzad/ zhabs drung chen mo 'di sa skya pa'i yi ge na med kyang zhwa luu bu'i yi ge na yod/ cis kyang dgos gsung nas tshon si dmar po kha gang la smon lam mang po mdzad
me nang du bskyur gyin 'dug /zha lu pa'i zhi rgyas dbang gi sbyin sreg gi yi ge gsum tsam lag na yod pa na ni mi 'dug gzhan yod pa yang srid/ mkhar rin cen spungs pa'i
pho brang du/ /me zhi rgyas dbang gi sbyin sreg byas/ /khong zhi rgyas dbang gis dngos grub rnams/ /ci bzhed pa'i thugs dgongs 'grub gyur cig /sde srid nas bzhengs pa'i tshe
bum de la ni su la yang dbang bskur du mi snang / dpon rigs drag pa rnams rang rang gi tshe bum bshams nas/ lcags 'dam nas sku mched/ sog nas sku mched/ phun tshogs gling
pa sku mched/ 'a sras pa/ byams rtse yab sras/ dpal 'byor gling pa/ rnam sras gling pa/ bde skyid gling pa/ rdzong dkar drung chen gong ra lo chen sogs tshe dbang zhu
mkhan mang po byung / khyad par rdzong dkar nas grwa pa 'ga' re la lam dbang dgos zer ba dang / khams pa'i slob gnyer ba drag pa gnyis gsum la zhal gyi rjes gnang dgos
zer/ de dus rang re'i gdan sa pa yang yod pas khyed zur du bsdad na ja mi yong yong dbang gral gyi gzhogs 'di 'dra zhig tu sdod gsung / de nas gdan sa pa 'chad nyan stabs
kyis sngon la gdan sa pas 'byon kha der gnas gsar nas sde pa phun tshogs pa yang phebs byung / gdan sa pas ma

mjal ba la cung ma dgyes khong 'ga' rong bka' lnga pa zer ba'i dran skye chen po zhig yong gsung bdag gis shag lo mnyan phug sogs la yong byang rin spungs gnyis nas kyang phyag
rtags yod pa 'di nas kyang phyag rtags gnang ba dang / khyad par bya gshongs su bcol mo zhus pa'i mdo sde po ti sum cu po 'di yang byang nas mi sna rnams kyis 'di byang
rang nas yin pas dgos zer yang yang gtser gyin 'dug na'ang 'di bcol mo yin pas de ltar mdzad na mi yong byas bsran btsugs pa yin pas 'di yang bya gshongs su gnang bya
zhig dgos zhus 'bul rten bdun tshan gcig phul bas ye zhal gyis ma bzhes/ nged rang bo dong du sleb tshe ni nged rang la dgos gsung / rjes nas sde srid rnams kyis kyang dbang
zhu de ltar mdzad pas gnas gsar nas sde pas kyang sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang zhus nged gnas gsar ba'i mi rigs 'dis bla mar khur phyin bla ma'i bka' gcog pa zhig med pas
bla mas gang gnang byed/ 'on kyang gnyan phug 'di kho rang mi ngo yod phyin de ltar byas na kho mi dga' bas shag lo la de ltar byas chog gsung / mdo sde rnams kyang bya
rgod gshongs su phul ba yin pas gnas gsar ba la gus zhen ma dor ba dang sku rim mdzad dgos tshul gyi yi ge mdzad kyin 'dug /nged rang yang don chen po grub snyam sems bde/
khong la sha'i rigs 'khrungs lakShmIs/ /lan 'ga' tsam rna brtsub na yang / /dus snyigs ma'i dbang gi sa mthar 'khyams/ /mi bdag la gus pas btud nas song / rin spungs
su zhag nyi shu rtsa lnga bsdad de nas grol cha zhus/ sang yong ba'i snga nyin sde pa ma

nas bkra shis kha btags dkar po/ /'bras shel dngos gtsang / gos yug /dar yug sogs bdun tshan/ dpon sa'i drung gis bkra shis kha btags dkar po/ /bzan li khri ma sogs bdun tshan/
zhabs drung rgyal pos sang yong khar bkra shis kha gtags mar gad mdog can/ dngul dkar gyi gong ma lnga tshar ngo mtshar ba/ gon ma ras yug sogs lnga tshan/ yum drung
gis slar yang ja nag rtse thum mar rel zhib dngos gtsang sogs phul/ de dus rin spungs nas mngon brjod kyi rtsom pa chen po zhig gnang gin 'dug pa 'khrol yod na zhu byas
pas sde pa ma la med gsung / sde pa 'jam grags nas nged la bsdus pa zhig yod de mkho na 'bul gsung snang / mi dbang zhabs drung dza hu yi/ /bu mo'i dar gos lhab lhub can/
/nor bu'i tog can rgyal mtshan bsgreng / /mi mthun g.yul las rgyal gyur cig khyad par gyi gzugs can no/ /rta dang glang chen nor bu gos/ /gtong ba gzhan las ches lhag pa'i/
/'jam dbyangs gzhon nu'i 'ja' ris sku/ /me tog char bzhin 'di ru babs/ /nor 'dzin 'di yang ring du 'dar/ /nam mkha'i 'ja' ris gur khang phub/ /me tog gsil ma'i char zim
'bab/ /'di yi gtong bas yin phul byung rab brtags kyi rgyan no nam snyam/ /ngag dbang lha mo'i byin rlabs zhugs/ /nor bu dngul dkar sku brnyan phul/ /sku tshe 'phrin las
bzang po ni/ /dar zhing rgyas pa'i bkra shis shog /snga dro snga mo nas sku de rnams gnang byung dus mtshar po zhig yod pa 'dra na'ang 'jim pa las grub pa zhig yin bsams
pas zhol du gnas tshang du sleb khar bzang nga kho thal skad sang sang 'don

cing 'dug /nang du phyin pas dngul sku gong ma lnga tshar 'dug dga' ba la zer rang the tshom za se byung / rje dpon skyid gshongs pa dang / ma chen 'gro ba/ rab 'byams pa gnyis
sogs sag sag byed kyin 'dug /gong ma lnga tshar sku brnyan des/ /dngos dang mjal ba cis ma mnyam/ /tshong 'dus sngags pa'i lung bstan de'ang / /drang po'i thig snyam
dga' spro skyes/ /phyag g.yog dpon rigs byams brtse lags/ rnam sras gling pa/ dpal 'byor gling pa sogs rags rim zhig gis skye ma byas/ rgya mkhar rdzong gi mdun longs spyod
zer ba'i gzhis ka der gsol 'debs sogs byas/ skyel ma ba rnams phyir thegs/ ras lnga'i la thog tu ngal gso byas shing 'bras sogs bzhes spro bkye/ ras lnga'i la babs tsam
de na thur rgya mtsho zer ba'i rtse chen pa'i gzhis ka zhig 'dug pa'i dbon khang dga' mo zhig du de nub bsdad/ sleb 'phral sku brnyan rnams la bltas pas lta bas chog mi
shes pa dga' tshor chen po byung sku rnams gral la bsgrigs/ na bza' phul mchod pa bzang po bshams dkar me phul/ ja mchod dhIHyig ma de yang de 'phral brtsams pa yin/ de
nas khar kha rdzong gi byang ngos der tsha ba la sleb/ de 'tshams thang smad kyi mtsho lags drung gi gzhis ka der phebs bsu snang dkar bas gtsos pa'i stag rtse nas kyi nang
gzan rags bsdus byung der ja sbyor sbrel gyi bar la bsdad/ de nas stag rtser sleb sde pa chos mdzad pas sku 'dra rnams ston zer bstan pas 'di dngul rang e yin nam bsha'
tshe dkar po 'dra zer/ sde pa phun tshogs pa bsam rtse na bu gte la yod pa de yang deng sang sleb

rgyu yin pas zhag shas sdod dgos gsung zhag lnga 'gor/ sde pa phun tshogs pa yang byon byung gong ma'i sku 'dra gzigs sde pa chos mdzad pas phun tshogs 'di dngul e yin pa 'dug
zer phun tshogs pas dngul gyi nang nas hor dngul rang yin pa 'dug /bla ma rin po che gzhis ka ru sku nom pa che rang 'dug go gsung / gnas der phyag drug mgon po dkar
dmar mthing gsum gyi rjes gnang / dmar po skor gsum/ tshe dbang / sgrol dkar/ gtor sgrub sogs byas/ yong dus sde pa stag rtse ba drung 'khor dang bcas pas 'brong rtse'i thad
kyi chu shar kha thug phebs skyel byas/ mkhar stag rtse'i dba' bo stag shar de/ /khong chos srung rnams la bcol gnyer zhus/ /dmag stong phrag 'tshogs kyang mi brdzi ba'i/
/rbad stong 'ur sgrog pa de nas byung / /rtse chen nas sde pa dpon blon sogs chibs khrom shin tu che bas phebs bsu/ grwa tshang gsum gyi grwa ba rnams kyi'ang ser sbreng
sgra rol cha dang bcas phebs bsu byas/ rtse chen du sleb rtse chen sde srid yum sras sogs kyis kyang de dus tshe bka' sogs mang po gsan/ gzim lags zhal ngo rnams kyis
mgon po'i phyi 'khrid nang 'khrid sogs dgos gsung 'bul rtsis yod/ jo gdan bzhi sde dbu mdzad yon tan che ba ches zer ba de dang / sho ma ri'i bla ma gser mdog can pa yin
pa'i ri khrod dga' ldan gyi mkhan po yang byas sku yon yang che zer ba des kyang mgon po'i 'khrid de lta bu shin tu 'dod pa zhig yod pas sngar ye ma thob da lan gnang dgos
zer/ rags bsdus tsam la 'khrid byas shin tu smar ba byung / gzim lags drung yang de dus kyi dmigs pa de las gsal ba dang yid ches pa ma byung

gsung / khong gzhan rnams kyang blo kha shin tu rdzogs/ de lo rtse chen gyi lcags rig gsal pa/ spe lcog gsar pa mang po/ /chu spe gsar pa sogs la rab gnas dgos gsung / steng
gi tshoms chen der dar yol dang thang sku thog tshad ma gsar pa mang po bsgrigs/ rang re dpon slob rnams kyis kye rdor gyi cho ga rdul tshon ma sogs rab gnas rgyas par
byas/ sde pa nas dung chen/ rgya gling / 'phan gdugs sogs mang po'i sta gon byas/ spe lcog bzhi ru zhi rgyas dbang gi sbyin sreg byas/ sgo spe'i steng der sgom khang gsar
pa 'ja' ris/ dar sham sked bris sogs bzabs pa/ ka bdung rnams la gzhu ring thung / tshon rdzogs gser shog ma byas pa'i nang du rtse nas gsol ja mang po/ /phyogs phyogs nas
kyang ltir rgyugs mang po/ /tshogs 'khor bzabs ma dang bcas chu spe sogs la yang rab gnas byas yul khad shin tu legs pa sgra rol cha 'ur dir re ba dar gdugs khra thib
se ba byung / kho bo cag gi rmi lam du yang rtse chen yin zer ba'i ri mthon po zhig la 'dzegs/ grog srubs shig la dar po che mang po 'dzugs kyin rtse la phyin rtse mor dar
'phyar ba'i rmi ltas byung / rtse chen pa la rten 'brel legs snyam du bsam/ khyod kyi snyan grags dpal dang 'byor/ /gzugs can yin pa 'dir shong ba/ /nor 'dzin khyon 'di
byed po yis/ /yangs par byas pa don yod snyam/ /sngon med snyan brgyud zab mo'i gtam/ /skal bzang rna ba'i rgyan du byas/ /skal med brgyal yang srog 'tsho ba/ /sman blas
rdzu 'phrul byas sam ci/ /sa 'dzin mdzes ma'i dpung rgyan du/ /rab gnas bzang po'i gdu bu mdzes/ /'phan gdugs

sgra dang rol mo yis/ /stong gsum khyab la sus mi smon/ /de nas byang la thegs rtsis byas rtse chen nas dpon blon rnams kyis mi grong klu sdings thug phebs skyel byas/ dkar
gur chen mo phub gsol ja bzhes spro sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas/ de nub khro phu ma sangs drung gi sgos gzhis su bsdad/ sang nyin snga ba'i cha la khre'i la la byas
la babs rtsa na na gzhung spang gshongs sogs shin tu skyid pa der rtse chen nas gsol 'degs byas/ de nub dgon pa rdzong du dbang ldan nas gang ci'i mthun sbyor byas bsdad/
sang nyin dbang ldan du sleb par tsho shag gi gzims khang gsar pa shin tu nyams dga' ba der zhag bcu skor bsdad/ dbang ldan sde srid sku mched/ drung chen zhal ngo sogs
la tshe bka' sgrol dkar sogs rnam grangs mang ba dang / logs bris gsar pa la rab gnas rgyas par byas/ ja ser nag rtse mo la nan blud dang bzhes spro sogs bzabs par byung
/ mkhar dbang ldan gyi sde srid sku mched dang / /mi 'byor ldan gyi drung chen rin rgyam pas/ /dpal phun tshogs kyi yo lang zad med spel/ /dus bzang por lugs gnyis cig car
'dzom/ /de nas tang tang la la brgal srang phu do per zhag gc-ig bsdad/ sang nyin snga bar langs lo ma lag dgon pa'i bla brang du zhag gcig bsdad/ sang lhun rtser sde pa
gser ma la mjal rtsis lo gsar gyi 'bul ba sdud pa'i thugs brel chen po yod zer nas ber chen bla brang du sleb/ mkhar lhun rtse'i mi dbang ser ma ba/ sa 'bul sdud kyis brel
nas zhal ma mjal/ /bdag rang yul la rings pa'i dga' ba ches/ /sa bde 'jam gyi lam la thal le phyin/ /sang rdzing lung du 'gron khang dang phyug

po skyi lod kyi der tsha ba la sleb ja sogs shin tu mang ba byung / de nas bya gshongs nas grwa pa rnams kyis bo dong e'i bar du dar gdugs rol mo sogs kyi ser sbreng byas sleb/
bya gshongs su mang ja zung nas 'gyed phogs khal re/ sprod rnying pa gang yod kyi steng du sprod gsar shag lo/ gnyan phug gi gzhis/ 'du khang bkra shis gser khang /
chos grwa phyi nang / rdo lha lha g.yabs sogs rkang 'thung gi do ra 'khrigs pa/ bla brang tshe ring gur khang / tshe ring g.yabs dkar dang bcas pa gsar bcos/ lha khang gsar
rnying mgon khang dang bcas par mchod cha cha tshang / 'du khang du mdo sde po ti sum cu/ bla brang gi brtsams chos rnam 'grel la sgrub ngag nas gtan tshigs rab dbye'i
bar bshad pa shog bu drug cu skor/ dbang yid zur bkol/ khyad par gtan tshigs rab dbye la tshad ma mdo dang sbyar ba/ gzhung chung dang sbyar ba/ rnam 'grel rang rkang dang
sbyar ba gsum phar phyin zur bkol la dge 'dun nyi shu'i lugs gsum gsal byed/ rten 'brel gyi zur bkol/ chos 'khor gyi zur bkol/ mdzod spyi don chen mo/ /mdzod rgyu 'bras
kyi bshad pa/ spang gnyen gyi zur bkol/ dbu ma'i dka' 'grel shog bu sum cu skor/ 'dul ba'i dka' 'grel shog bu sum cu skor/ sman gzhi'i zur bkol sum cu skor/ thal 'gyur
gyi dogs gcod rigs gter dka' 'grel shog bu lnga bcu skor/ blo rigs chen mo shog bu sum cu skor/ sdom gsum so thar dka' 'grel/ sngags sdom 'go'i zur bkol/ de rnams phal cher
sprod la yod/ gzhan yang rang gi brtsams chos sdom gsum gyi phyag chen

rtsod spong / phyag chen rang lugs/ yul chen gyi rnam bshad/ drod kyi rnam bshad/ lugs gnyis kyi sems bskyed la 'khrid re re yod/ phyag chen rtsod spong 'di ri bo che'i rje
drung ngag dbang drung dbus nas yar lam bya rgod gshongs su phebs pa'i tshe sprul sku padma dkar pos phyag chen gan mdzod zer ba zhig yod de thugs mkho na bzhag gi zer bzhag
song / lo gsum tsam lta ba yang ma byung phyis rje drung 'gyur med sogs kyis gan mdzod de la khong gis lan cig mdzad pa rigs pa 'dug go gsung zer/ lan dgos pa'i gnad
ci 'dra yod dam bsam bltas pas rtsod spong gi thad du dngos su rtsod pa'i rtsod pa spang ba dang / don gyis rtsod pa'i rtsod pa spang ba gnyis mdzad nas/ phyi ma dri ba
lhag bsam rab dkar dang / snga ma sdom gsum la mdzad/ rab dbye las/ phyag chen pa la dogs gcod gnang ba'i skabs thams cad la ther chags kyi lan mdzad 'dug /'on kyang rab
dbye'i de don la zhugs/ phyag chen pa'i de don la ma zhugs pas/ padma dkar po 'gran zla dang bral yang 'di la lan thebs snyam kho bos kyang rtsod spong de ston cag cig la
brtsams pa yin/ sku gzhogs la 'gro myong pa kha re la sprul skus kyang sa paN la rgan 'chal gsung ba sogs mdzad 'dug pas/ de lan nyams 'char tsam byas na e chog byas pas
'ga' zhig de mi legs zer/ 'ga' zhig thugs yul shin tu yangs pas thugs dgyes pa min pa skyon mi yong zer/ kho bos kyang nyams 'char 'ga' re byas/ phyis yi ge spyan lam du
'byor 'dug pas 'phral mi dgyes pa mi 'dug kyang sgar pa rnams thugs 'khrul po 'dug zer/ kho bo'i rtsod spong gi 'go tho re

ba la mchan bu'i lan tsam gnang byung ba de la yang lan spyan dbye'i cho ga zhes pa zhig brtsams/ rje nA ro paN chen sprul pa'i sku/ /gzhan 'gran zla med cig los yin mod/ /rje
sa paN rnam dpyod spungs pa la/ /ci 'gran yang rnam dpyod long dang mtshungs/ /rje sa paN rnam dpyod grib bsil gyis/ /snying tsha gdung mun pa bsal bar nges/ /mkhas gzhan
la spyan dbye'i cho ga byas/ /thugs sdug 'thums dgongs dbyings ma 'khrungs shig /'di'i rtsod pa rtsod lan rnams rje grang chen rab 'byams pa'i spyan lam phebs pa'i lan
du/ mang du thos pa'i tshon brgya gsal ba'i lam/ /rnam dpyod me long yangs par shar 'di des/ /mkhas rlom phal la smra bcad gdams pa byin/ /chos kun snying por bsdus pa
dpal gyi mgur/ /legs bshad dal bur ston la ngo mtshar ci/ /nyams 'gyur stong gis spras pa'i legs bshad sgra/ /thos par gyur pa'i rna ba 'di ya mtshan/ /de slad yongs rdzogs
bstan pa'i khur chen po/ /snying stobs phrag par lon pas mi ngal ba'i/ lhag bsam rab dkar lha yi glang po khyod/ /mkhas pa'i skyed tshal mdzes pa'i rgyan du mdzod/ /phyag
chen rtsod spong thad rnams rgyal 'pham ji ltar byung dpyod ldan gzur gnas yod na rtsod pa rtsod lan la gzhigs pas gsal bar shes/ zhes pa yang gnang byung ngo / /sprul
pa mchog gi mchan bur/ /shog byang khron pa 'di'i gting yang / /dpog pa'i rnam dpyod mi ldan par/ /chos tshul rgya mtsho'i klong gzhal ba'i/ /re ba byed pa e ma mtshar/
/rnam dpyod 'bring zhig gis shog byang de dal bur klags

pa nyid kyis gzhung der ji ltar bstan pa rig par 'gyur la/ de ltar mi go na ni bshad kyang mi go bas btang snyoms ngal gsor chug cig ces bris snang yang / de ni ye shes grub
pa'i le'u nyi shu yod pa'i bco brgyad yan dbang po rab/ bcu dgu pa 'bring / nyi shu pa tha ma'i skabs yin zhing / dbang po rab de dbang gis smin zin yin par bshad pas gzhung
la rnam dpyod ci yang ma zhugs bzhin du gdul bya blun po rnams kha drangs pa'i zol 'gros kyi tshig tshangs pas rta thul la bden gtam rlung la bskur ba'i tshig smras
pa dang chos mtshungs pa kho na ste/ rgyu mtshan ci'i phyir na ye shes grub pa'i le'u dang por/ rtog pa thams cad rnam spangs pa'i/ /ye shes mchog bzang thob pa yi/ /rdo
rje ye shes dbang bskur bas/ /dngos grub mchog gnyis grub par bya/ /yang dag ye shes kun ldan na/ /bris pa'i dkyil 'khor sogs gzhan du/ /dbang bskur ba ni len ce na/ /'di
ni dam tshig nyams par gyur/ /zhes ye shes grub pa'i byin rlabs rdo rje ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba/ zhes pa'i ming can sngar du dbang gi ye shes rgyud la skyes zin pas
bris sgrub la sogs pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang zhus shing bskur na dam tshig nyams par 'gyur zhes gdul bya de las dang po pa min par gsal bar bshad 'dug pa'i phyir ro/ /zhib
tu dpyod ldan yod na ye shes grub pa'i le'u nyi shu pa la gzigs shig /skabs der bka' drin mtshungs bral phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi dus kyi mchod pa mang ja rgyun chags kyi
rten/ bo dong bre chen gyi nas khal stong phrag gcig dang bcu gnyis btsugs/ mnyan yod bya gshongs su mdo'i 'chad nyan la mi gnod

pa byas/ gsung ngag lam 'bras yongs rdzogs lan drug tsam dang / 'khrid kyang thal tsam cig dang bdun bshad/ khog phubs bskyed rim phyi nang sogs la zin bris byed mkhan yang
mang po byung / spros med 'khrid lan gnyis/ gur gyi 'khrid/ tshe 'khrid/ ma gcig /sgrol dkar 'khrid rnams byas/ /yul bo dong 'dzin ma'i 'gram pa 'dir/ /lha bi shwa karma
babs pa bzhin/ /rten ngo mtshar bkod pa'i gtsug lag khang / /lha mir bcas lta ba'i mgron du byas/ /yul dbus gtsang dad 'dus blo gsal la/ /khong shAka sras chos 'khor bskor
ba bzhin/ /chos legs bshad bdud rtsi'i char pa bab/ /yid rab dga' bden pa mthong dang mtshungs/ /drin 'gran bral 'jam dbyangs bla ma de'i/ /drin khyer ba med kyang khyer
ba'i blos/ /rgya rkang 'thung btung ba rgyun gyi rgyur/ /'bru bzang po shel dkar phung por spungs/ /de nas sras mo ko ne'i bzhugs sa yin pas ko ne ma zer ba'i dgon pa
zhig na rje rdzogs chen pa zer ba mdo sngags nyams rtogs kyis brgyan pa/ dgung lo bdun cu don lnga bzhes pa zhig yod pa des dbang zhig la shog gsung phyin/ nged gzhon pa'i
dus nad la rkyen dang bsre thub pa zhig yod kyang kha rgas pas nad 'dis kyang tshur rngan chen byed pa zhig 'dug gsung / nged yang yod ba dang thug dbang byed long ni ma
byung / lam zab sogs brda sbyor phran bu ni byas/ rang gzhon dus nyams len ci byas kyang / /rkyen nad la thog rdzis thongs pa dka'/ /rang 'chi kar nad med smon lam thob/
/ci byas kyang bde'o grogs po rnams/ /de nub bya gshongs su sleb/ sang nyin snga ba la yong

rtsis byas/ blo bde gong kha thug grwa pa rnams kyis skyel ma byas blo bder sleb tsa na khong rnams kyis skad bton mchi ma byung rdzi chom chen po byung / rang dka~X' gnas
'khyur nas dga' tshor che yang 'bral mi phod pa'i snang tshul des sems skyo shas kyang chen po byung / rang dga' spro'i snang ba sag ge la/ /khong mig chus ja bskol skyel
ma byas/ /sems skyo yang khong nad ma zhugs par/ /rje bla ma srung ma'i bka' drin yin/ /grwa pa byings de nas log bya gshongs su sleb tsa na gling gseb skya thag ge ba sems
skyo phyod de ba byung zer/ grwa pa thog cig gis de nas kyang bcu pa rong thug phyin/ chos gling pa rnams kyis bcu pa 'og ma'i gsum mdo der sngon la phyin ja skol byas
'dug /gung tshigs de ru byas/ de nub la skog tu sleb/ grang mo che'i grwa pa dos pa rnams snga 'gros la thegs/ dpon slob rags bsdus rnams 'chos mar gdan 'dren byas phyin
zhag gnyis bsdad/ khong yab yum/ srang dbar chos legs yab yum sogs rnams la tshe bka' dmar po skor gsum sogs byas/ phyag dril hor dril dngos gtsang zhig phul ba de snga
gong yin/ de dus kyang 'bul ba shin tu bzang ba mdzad/ sang bye la'i chu mig thug phebs skyel gsol 'degs sogs byas/ de nub rgyang du chos rje tshul khrims pas shog gsungs
phyin/ de nas sang nyin grang chen chos 'khor yang rtser 'gro dus zhal ngo chibs rags dang bcas pas phebs bsu/ rgya gling dung chen dang bcas ser sbreng bzabs pa byas chos
'khor yang rtse'i bla brang gi dri gtsang khang du sleb/ de tshe sde srid dpon blon gyis/ /byin rlabs rten 'brel zab mo'i lam/ /ci dgos cho

ga rdzogs par bsgrubs/ /sems kyi ngal gso de ru byas/ /phag lo lo gsar la rnam rgyal stag rtse'i rtser shog gsungs phyin gsol ja/ bur ston/ go ra sogs bzabs ma dang bcas pa'i
thugs dgyes dgyes mdzad/ rogs ram 'jam dbyangs smra ba'i rgya mtsho dang / mang thos nam mkha' rnam rgyal gnyis rigs lung la slang ba'i dga' ston bzhad gad shin tu che
ba byung / me phag gi bgrang gzhi gsar pa la/ /'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i pho brang rtser/ /lugs gnyis mdzom dga' ston bsam mi khyab/ /gzhan rna ba'i rgyun gyur glu gar
rol/ /lo de la 'dar chos 'khor yang rtse ru gsung ngag dgos zer lo de'i zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer gsum la lam 'bras btsugs/ sems bskyed dang rgyu dbang gi tshe zhal ngo rnams
kyang phebs/ sras 'byor chen yang sku btsas/ me tog gi char mang po yang babs/ rten 'brel 'dzom zer ba yang byung / byang chub thugs bskyed smin byed byas/ /me tog char
babs sras yang 'khrungs/ /phyi nang gsang gsum rten 'brel 'dzom/ /snyan grags phyogs kyi mdzes ma'i rgyan/ /de dus lam 'bras la phyogs nas byon pa chos rje mdong rab 'byams
pa byams pa bde legs/ rkyang 'dur chos rje byams pa/ ra nam mkha' rnam rgyal/ dge slong mnga' ris pa spun/ chos rje 'khyog pa blor rgyam/ drung rams pa byams snying
/ chos mdzad skyab ma/ chos mdzad rgya rgod pa/ gzhan rnams gzhi ba/ nub dgon nas chos rje bzod rin/ ya ga chos sdings nas chos rje btsun grags/ dbon chen klu dbang / kun
dga' mchog grub

sogs rags bsdus la spros med kyi 'khrid zur du byas/ khong rnams mgur shin tu bzang bas spros med bla ma mchod chog de yang rgyun ldan du byed kyin 'dug /zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes
bcu khra rgyu ba'i nyin 'dar nas sa skyong mi dbang chos skyong lhun grub kyis lam 'bras sogs 'khrid chen po bdag gis mi 'chun/ tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po gshegs rjes/
tshe 'di phyi'i skyabs gnas 'phral phugs kyi blo rtse gtad rgyu'i bla ma khyed gcig pu yin pas lam zab kyi 'khrid cig dgos gsung dgongs pa dang sbyar/ zla ba de'i nyer
dgu'i nub rmi lam la ngam ring gi chos grwar dam bca' bzhag /gzhan dang 'brel tam byas pas rang nyid rgyal ba'i spobs pa spro sag ge ba dang spos shel gyi 'phreng ba shin
tu legs pa brgya rtsa gnyis skor lag tu brgyus/ rje bla mas lung bstan mang po mdzad pa'i nyams snang / zla ba lnga pa'i tshes gnyis kyi nub rmi lam na tshon si dmar
po gsar pa'i chos gos gyon pa'i rmi lam sogs shin tu bzang ba yang byung / lam zab phyi nang gi byin rlabs 'khrid dang bcas pa/ bla ma rigs lnga'i byin rlabs sogs mang po
phul thugs shin tu dgyes pa yang byung / 'khor 'bangs chos bzhin skyong ba'i mi dbang gis/ /zol min thugs kyi re ltos bdag la bcol/ /rang nyid gar 'gro'i nges pa mi 'dug
kyang / /dus kun mi 'bral snying gi dam bca' phul/ /bka' drin zla bral tshar chen chos kyi rje'i/ /mkhyen brtse'i gser gyi nyag thag gis sbrel ba'i/ /bdag dang bdag ltos
dad ldan sbyin bdag che/ /khyed bzhugs dag pa'i zhing der drongs mdzod cig /rang snying nas

bcags pa'i grib bsil gyis/ /khyed thugs kyi gdung skyong ma nus par/ /ngag gcam bu'i 'gyur mgugs snyan po yi/ /gzhan dad ldan bslu bar byed na 'tshangs/ /tshes gsum gyi nub
rmi lam la gzhan gyis phul ba'i gdugs gnyis tsam phub pa dang / khyad par khro phu gdung brgyud kyis phul zer ba'i gdugs chung ngu legs pa rang zhig 'dug pa de po ti rnams
kyi steng du 'buu ba bsam pa zhig byung / de mtshams rang khang pa dog ge ba zhig na 'dug /de'i steng na khyi gu chung ngu snum zul le ba 'dug pa de nged kyi mal du zhugs
byung 'di snying rje chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul yin bsam pa byung / rang gsar pa'i gos gyon gdugs rim phub/ /khong srung ma'i rnam 'phrul lus la 'khril/ /khyed sbyin
bdag bu slob dad ldan rnams/ /dus nam yang bslu bar ma gyur cig /yang tshes bzhi'i rmi lam la skas ring po zhig la rta zhon nas nged gsum gyis phyin g.yang za se ba la bgrod
khang pa tshoms dam po zhig tu sleb/ mi bdag dang bdag la blo gtad gsum/ 'gros mgyogs byed chu 'thung bzhon par zhon/ /lam 'khrul med thar pa'i skas la 'dzegs/ /gnas
dag pa'i zhing du son pas bde/ /yang de'i nub rmi lam la nged rang sangs rgyas kyi sku mang po par la 'debs kyin 'dug pa zhal phyag sogs gsal po byung / mi zhig gis dpar
de kun gsal po thebs song zer/ rje mkhan dang mjal ba'ang mang du rmi/ zab 'khrid legs gdams bdud rtsi'i khu ba 'dis/ /mi phyed dad thob sbyin bdag slob bu yi/ /snying la
lha yi par bzhin

'phos gyur nas/ /ci bsams bzhed dgu'i don rnams 'grub par nges/ /de'i lo lam 'bras kyang dbang byin rlabs/ lung so so/ 'khrid rnams cha lag tshang ba zla ba bdun tsam gyi bar
la rdzogs par grub/ 'khrid zur pa rnams kyang zla ba lnga pa'i nyer bzhi la grol/ de nas chos mtshams cung zad byas nye brgyud shin tu nye brgyud kyi 'khrid rnams kyang
rdzogs par btang / zla ba bdun pa'i nyer bzhi'i khra rgyu ba la zhal ngo rnams la rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs sngon 'gro'i 'khrid kyi rim pa rnams byas/ zla ba brgyad
pa'i tshes bcu la grol/ de skabs rmi lam DA dril dang bcas ye shes dbab pa'i rim pa shin tu gsal ba rang byung / bsam mi khyab thun mong ma yin pa shin tu zab zer ba
de yang byas pa yin/ rje ngo mtshar blo gsal rgya mtsho yis/ /mtshan 'od gsal ngang nas lung bstan bzhin/ /gnas chos 'khor yang rtse'i chos kyi khrir/ /chos slob bshad
zab mo'i 'brug sgra bsgrags/ /khong dad ldan sa skyong yum sras mched/ /thugs rab dgyes bdud rtsi'i lo tog smin/ /gzhan bskal med 'byung po'i bya rnams longs/ /thugs ma 'khrug
blo mun sros na bde/ /lam 'bras kyi skabs dbyar mthongs lcong shol klu sdings su byas/ grwa pa rnams dang sde srid kyi mang ja so so/ gor/ bur ston sogs shin tu bzabs
pa byung / rab 'byams pa rkyang 'dur byams pa dang byams snying gnyis kyis 'bel gtam bzhad gad sogs shin tu che ba byung / lam 'bras skabs su zin thun mang po btang /
drung rams pa nam mkha' rnam rgyal gyis dam tshig /tshogs

'khor/ dbang chu/ rab gnas kyi cho ga bzang drug /rten bzang po'i khyad chos gzungs bzhugs 'jug tshul/ pho 'khor mo 'khor sogs la dogs gcod dang bcas pa'i zin bris shin tu
gsal ba byas/ rang gis kyang slob bshad 'khrid rim de de dus brtsams pa yin/ khong ngur smrig 'dus pa'i dge 'dun sder/ /chos legs bshad dgag dang sgrub pa 'phel/ /gnad che
ba rnams la zin thun byas/ /rang bstan pa'i dmigs rgyan de tsam yin/ de nas phag lo zla ba bcu gcig pa la thub bstan dge 'phel du phyin lam 'bras dgos zer gzhi ba rnams
dang / phyogs nas 'bum chen bstan pa dar rgyas/ nyang stod pa tshe dbang dpal 'byor/ shag tshal pa 'bum pa chos dar/ shrI nas dge slong dkon bzang / smad chag pa dbon btsun/
bya gshongs pa kun gzhon/ cha lung nas sgrub pa bcu gcig /shar phug pa sgrub pa gsum rnams yod/ de rnams la lam 'bras slob bshad cha lag yongs rdzogs/ spros med kyi
dbang 'khrid yongs rdzogs rnams byas/ gnas thub bstan dge 'phel chos grwa cher/ /chos slob bshad brgyud pa gsum ldan dang / /gzhan brgyud pa gnyis ldan spros med 'khrid/
/rje tshar chen bstan pa'i dpal du dar/ /'bum chos dar ba dang phu rab 'byams pa zhig gis zin bris kyang tho re ba byas 'dug /cha lung sgrub pa bcu gcig gis gzhi bsnyen dang
sbyin sreg rdzogs par byas/ deng sang kyang lam bsdus 'chag med byed kyin 'dug /de nas rang gi bsam tshod la rje kun

dga' mchog ldan la sngar ma thob pa'i chos 'dra zhus na bsam pa yod pa la 'ga' zhig gis de mi rigs zer ba mang du byung kyang rang re bya gshongs pa nang 'tshogs yin pa dang
/ bslab pa bgres pa dang mdo sngags kyi sku yon chen po yod pa tshun/ rang gis ma thob pa'i chos zhu ba la phan yon ma gtogs mi rigs pa gcig kyang med snyam rang gis rbad
bcad snyan zhus 'bul du btang bas zhal bzhes byung / de dus rmi lam gyi mtshan ma gsal po byung ba ni/ lo byi ba zla ba dang po'i tshes/ /dus yar ngo rdzogs pa gnyis pa
la/ /rje bla mas zhal bzhes byung ba'i tshe/ /mtshan rmi lam mtshan ma 'di ltar mthong / /gnas gyang rim se rol khang rnying du/ /don chu mig 'don snyam phug tu zhugs/
/rogs bden pa'i tshig gis 'di skad zer/ /gnas sa 'og rim pa mang po na/ /klu gtsug na nor bu'i chu klung skad/ /gsung snyan snyan mang po sgrog go skad/ /der gang phug nyams
dga' rdo ro~Xm can/ /phyogs 'di ni sa gnyan yin no zer/ /cung 'jigs 'jigs byed kyang 'jigs mi snyam/ /skyabs gsum dang rtsa brgyud bla ma la/ /phyag 'tshal zhing rdo
rim bsal ba la/ /phug sa rdos khengs pa'i gnas shig mthong / /chu gtsang ma sa 'og shor ro snyam/ /grogs rnams kyis g.yam bag lag cha yis/ /sa phung po bshas pa'i 'og cig
na/ /phug zab mo g.yam pas bcad pa mthong / /de bsal tshe sa phug yangs se ba/ /mdog ser skya khrol le ba zhig snang / /chu ma mthong rang sems nongs pa'i tshe/ /slar de
nang g.yam leb gcig bsal bas/ /de

'og gzhir sa phug nyams dga' bar/ /chu sngon po thol gyis rdol ba mthong / /'di rten 'brel legs snyam rab dga' shar/ /don de la'ang chu 'gro mi 'dug pas/ /chu 'gro sa shing
rtas lam gtod pa/ /chu lhung lhung snyan par 'bab pa'i skad/ /khong gnyis 'thung dga' ba'i skad 'dra bas/ /dus rgyun chad med par 'bab bo snyam/ /sems rab dga'i bdud rtsi
ci yang thob/ /rmi lam de ltar byung bas de don mang po zhig gi brda yin pa 'dug snyam sems rab tu dga'/ rje bla ma dgon par spyan drangs/ chos 'brel gyi thog ma tshe dpag
med dze tA ri'i dbang byed pa ngor pa'i srol yin gsung de ga bzhin zhus/ de nas 'khor lo bde mchog lo nag dril gsum las nag po pa'i dbang rje dam pa la thob zin pas/
lo yi pa dang dril bu pa'i dbang zhus/ sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang gi rim pa rdzogs par thob/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang yang zhus/ de nas phu'i chab la dpon
slob cab mthun phebs chab khar gsang 'dus sgron gsal/ mdor byas/ mdo bsre sogs kyi lung gnang / mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang yang zhus/ de mtshams rtse chen nas lam 'bras la yong
dgos gsung ba'i pho nya ba sleb/ rje bla ma dpon slob rnams phu nas skyid gshongs su zhag gcig bzhugs/ de nas phebs skyel byas/ rje bla ma kun dga' mchog ldan la/ /dbang
rjes gnang mang po'i bka' drin zhus/ /phyis rmi lam zab mos mtshams sbyar nas/ /chos mang du thos pa'i rten 'brel bsgrigs/ /rang re grang chen du phyin/ smyung gnas/ dbang

mo che sogs kyi brel ba chod mtshams shar la phyin de nub la lkog tu bsdad/ sang nyin bya gshongs su sleb/ grwa pa rnams kyis dres ma nas ser sbreng byas bsus/ mang ja gnyis
byas/ shar rtse chen rgyal po'i pho brang du/ /kha za 'dod kyi ltogs brel ma yin kyang / /khong sbyin bdag gi dad sun mi 'byin phyir/ /chos slob bshad spel snyam shar re
phyin/ /de nas sang nyin ber chen bla brang du sleb/ khong rnams la tshe dbang sogs byas/ de nas sang nyin bde chen rtse'i gla tshal du tsha ba la sleb/ de nas yom lag
bla brang gi mdun gyi thang kar bla brang nas gsol ja bzang ba/ rogs rnams la skom sing sogs shin tu smar ba byung / rdzi la bud tsam gyi la thog zer ba'i grong pa zhig tu
bsdad/ de phan chad la rtse chen pas gsol 'degs rtswa gzan sogs yong gin/ de nas srad pa ngur du bsdad/ srad rgyud pa ba'i bla brang de nas gsol ja rgyugs byung / rang
res kyang ja ltir rgyugs byas/ sang snga bar langs yongs pas srad do dpe nas gsol ja 'bul ba sogs byung / chu shar brgyud der rta babs byas yud tsam bsdad/ de nub dbang ldan
du sleb drung chen drung gis dgon pa rdzong gi chu tshan de dga' mo yod pas 'phrod po yong gsung / gur sogs mthun rkyen bsgrigs zhag gsum chu tshan der bsdad/ de nas
gang la la byas rtse chen pa rang gi gzhis ka yin zer ba'i khang pa zhig tu bsdad/ sang gsol 'degs kyi gsol ba de ru ka byas/ sde pa dpon blon chibs khrom mang po dang bcas
phebs bsu/ grong gsar thad kyi rtsi kha yangs po der gur chen po phub gsol

ja gsum sbrel gyi bar bsdad/ de nas rtse chen pho brang du sleb rang gi gzims chung nor rgyas su byas/ lam 'bras snang gsum gyi chos dus tshes bzang ba la btsugs/ chos 'chad
sa rab gsal bar ma ring mo zhig 'dug pa der byas/ de'i dus sde pa phun tshogs nas kyang bu gte'i grol cha cung zad byung gsung phebs 'dug pas/ lam 'bras rang la ni sdod
skabs ma byung ba yong ngam zur du spros med kyi 'khrid cig dgos gsung de ga bzhin phul/ de dus bde gzar gyi gzhi ma zhig thing yod 'dug pas phun tshogs drung gi phyag rdzas
rags rim kyang rtse chen du sleb 'dug /khyad par sprul sku bsod dpal bas bris pa'i rten gtso kha che paN chen/ sa paN sogs kyi sku thang shin tu legs pa/ de bas kyang
sa skya paN chen gyi rdza sku/ kha che paN chen gyi rdza sku las kyang ches lhag pa mig gi bdud rtsir gyur pa de tsho mthong / de nas snang gsum dang spros med grol/ rang
gi bsnyen pa kha gso byas/ rgyu dbang gi skabs su rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs pa phyis gshegs gsol byas chus yang yang bkrus kyang ma dag par khra lam me 'dug zer/
rgyu dbang gi rim pa grol/ sngags lam ma tshugs tsam la dbang ldan nas chos mdzad gro dpe ba gnang byung nas/ dbang ldan sde pa sku bgres pa sogs sha dug gi skyon byung
dbang ldan du chog dpon la yong dgos gsung gsang ba'i tshul du mdzad kyin 'dug /bdag gis gzim lags la gnas tshul zhus pas/ spyir dbang ldan pa sbyin bdag yin pa dang /
khyad

par drung chen dad stobs kyi slob ma phyag phyi 'grub che ba nas gsang 'di la yud tsam cis kyang phebs rigs gsung / dbang ldan la phyin dbang ldan rtse'i gzims khang du dgyes
pa rdo rje'i dus tha ma'i cho ga dpon slob lngas btang / mtshan byang bsregs/ tshogs su cho ga'i bsngo ba sogs la yud tsam phyin/ rta sga chas rna ba'i pad kor sogs 'bul
cha nyi shu rtsa gcig tshan cig byung / gnas bsngo ba gson gshin rjes su 'brang / /ci bsngos pa'i 'bras bu don bzhin 'grub/ /gnas min pa'i bsngo ba blo sbyong tsam/ /'di
phyed pa 'jam dpal sa skya'i drin/ /don ma shes mgrin pa'i gzengs mtho yang / /khyi rgan po'i gsung dbyangs sgrog pa la/ /khyi'i bu chung 'gram pa 'degs pa yis/ /khong
mgron po sa mthar bskrad pas ci/ /lha dgyes pa rdo rje'i ye shes mes/ /khong gnyis snang 'khrul pa'i bud shing bsregs/ /sems rang gsal dag pa'i zhing du bskyal/ /dus tha
ma'i cho ga'i 'phrin las yin/ /gnad mi shes me chog phaT sgrogs kyang / kho khugs na gson po a tsha tsha/ /gzhan phan gnod med pas yon gyi sdig /tshe phyi ma'i khrel thum
bor la thong / /de lta bu'i bya ba tshar nas de nub bar tsho shag tu bsdad/ sang nang par sde srid dmag dpon drung gis rtser shog gsung gzims chung dga' mo zhig tu zhag
gcig bsdad/ khong dpon blon sogs la tshe bka' phul/ de'i sang rtse chen du yongs sngags lam man chad sgrol ma lha khang du btsugs/ lam 'bras la dbus pa dka' bcu pa zer ba
rgyal chen gling pa zhig yod pa de rnam dpyod shin tu che yig gzugs

legs pa/ brda dag po byas pa zhig 'dug pa des lam 'bras slob bshad 'di shin tu legs pa zhig 'dug /slob bshad yod pa'i lung rigs kyi sgrub byed cig zin thun gnang dgos skyor
'go yang nga rang gis byed zer de bzhin byas pa'i dpe yang da lta lag na yod pa 'di yin/ khyed rang gi gsung rtsom rnams kyi nang nas rab gnas dpe 'di shin tu legs pa mkho
che ba zhig 'dug zer 'pho thabs byas song / snang gsum la rtse chen sde srid/ dpon sa lha sras/ bdag mo yum gzims lags khu dbon/ lhan skyes drung nas kun bsod/ rkyang
'dur bar dkon tseg /grong gsar nas sogs lnga bcu skor yod/ sgrol ma lha khang du lam 'bras pa byings la slob bshad dbang 'khrid byin rlabs sogs cha lag yongs rdzogs/ zhal
ngo dpon blon rnams la gser chos bcu gsum/ dze tA ri'i dbang / 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dbang / mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang / gzungs gra lnga'i rjes gnang / gur zhal gyi rjes gnang
/ sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang tshe 'khrid dang bcas pa/ rjes gnang sogs mang du byas/ lha sras kyis rtser gsol ja bzhes spro sogs gnang ba yang yang phebs/ dpon sa yum gyis
'bras kyi sim sag sogs ka To ra theg tsam yang yang 'di gsol ja la thob las bzhes gsung / gsol ja ser nag gi rtse thum mang po bskyal/ sbyor khyed rang mkhas pa 'dug pas
de ru skol la khyed rang yang bzhes 'dir yang skyol gsung / mkhar nyang stod sgrol ma'i lha khang du/ /chos slob bshad gser chos bcu gsum sogs/ /dpal

sa skya'i gsung ngag bdud rtsi phab/ /khong skal bzang rnams lhag bsam tshim nas song / /sgrol ma lha khang gi nged rang gi gzims chung zur 'phyong dang bcas pa zhig 'dug pa
de'i mal gyi 'khris na blo skar sgo sgrigs dang bcas pa zhig gi stegs bu la rgyun gtor bzhag yod/ tho rengs lam bsdus byas/ nam gsal le ba la gtor ma'i dkyil na myu gu
'dra ba zhig sngo lhag ge 'dug /mchod g.yog pas ljang pa zhig gtor ma la btsugs pa 'dra bsam gzhigs nas bltas pas btsugs pa min par ljang pa zhig skyes 'dug /gtor zan la
nas rdog shor na ma la'i stabs kyis myu gu skyes pa yin pa 'dug bsam zhag 'ga' song tsa na myu gu sngo rong nge ba bcu tsam skyes rtse la me tog se chom me ba thon pa yid
spro sing nge ba byung / mda'i tshoms na gtor sgrub byed pa'i gtor ma lnga tshar/ rnam sras/ dmag zor ma/ dur khrod bdag po rnams la'ang gtor ma re yod/ zhag 'ga' nas mda'i
dur khrod bdag po'i gtor ma la myu gu skyes 'dug zer/ myu gu dur khrod bdag po'i nus pa yin pa 'dra bsam pa byung na'ang de mtshams gtor ma thams cad kyi snying po dang
mtheb skyu sogs la dbyar gyi rtsi kha skyes skyes myu gu sngo rong nge ba grangs med skyes byung / dpon sa yum drung gi gtor ma de yang rgyun ring song yong ran gsung
/ phud phye dkar rgyan sogs bskyal song / rogs rnams kyis 'di 'dra ya mtshan 'di ma spos pa dga' ba 'dra zer rnying pa rnams bzhag /gsar pa zur du btsugs phyis gsar pa rnams
la'ang sngar bzhin myu gu sngo rong nge ba bsam gyis mi khyab

pa thon byung / phyis lhun rtse zhabs drung bkra shis stobs rgyas dang mjal tshe de 'dra'i lo rgyus byung bas gtor ma la spu nag skyes pa 'di sbyong ma thub pa'i skyon/ myu
gu skyes pa mchog 'grub pa'i rtags su bshad/ dbus phyogs su sa skya pa'i bla chen zhig gi gtor ma la'ang myu gu zhig skyes gsung rnam thar la btab 'dug gsung / rang re'i
mgon pod kyi gtor ma'i bkra brtag pa'i skabs na myu gu skyes pa la khams gsum dbang du 'du ba dang / chos skyong bran du 'khol ba'i rtags zer ba sogs snang / de man chad
rgyun ldan du myu gu skye ba zhig ni 'dug /de nas bde gzar g.yos re che byung / rong pa/ rtse chen pa/ gser ma sogs phyogs gcig /gtsang byang phyogs gcig yin pas gtsang
byang gi dpung nyang stod la bcug /rtse chen gyi 'og ting ting rdzong du sgar rgyag pa'i lugs yin 'dug na'ang rtse chen pas de gong rdzong ro la mkhar las byas/ de bsrung
cha bcug tshar bas de nas slar log gzhung der gtsang byang gi sgar rgyag sang nyin rgyal rtse'i 'khor gyi tsher ma la me rgyag byas/ du lding nam mkha' 'grib pa tsam byung
/ skya thor la phyin pa 'dra la rgyal rtse nas sne logs cung zad thongs/ slar log tsho gcig gis chu la rab 'don grabs byas/ tsho gcig gis rtse chen zam pa la 'tshang drag
byas/ rang re sgrol ma lha khang na gtor sgrub la yod na'ang rtse chen sde srid nas dmag chu thon yong ba 'dug pas gtor ma brdeg dgos gsung / rang gis gtor ma rgyag rgyag
byed pa'i bla ma zhig min/ gtor bskul 'phrin bcol tsam gyis thus zhus/

rab la 'don mkhan rnams kyis rab khungs mchod par log dgos pa byung / de nas zam pa la 'tshang drag pa rnams kyang 'tshang drag ma khyad par log dgos pa byung / rtse chen na
bzang ra dang / bzang ngu gnyis lha yang yang 'bab/ bzang ngan gyi lung ston pa zhig 'dug pa de yon mchod dpon blon gyi bzhugs gral du byung / gri rmog sogs bzhag nas phyag
'bul byas/ mda' dar g.yas g.yon du khur nas pus btsugs mdun du bsdad/ nged kyis kyang dar mdung dkar po zhig sbyin kho mgu nas song / rang re'i dkar phyogs rnams kyi
bla ma'i byin rlabs kyi mthus de ma thag tu chu mdog dmar po rba tshub dang bcas pa zhig tu 'gyur song bas chu la ma thar song zer/ de 'phral rtse chen pa rnams kyis sgrol
ma lha khang gi rtser dkar dung / dung chen/ rgya gling / 'phyar dar mang po dang bcas lha rgyal 'bod kyin 'dug rang gi bsam pa la dgra la snying khrag blud pa lta bur
song / sang nyin 'tshang drag tu btang yong ngam snyam pa shar/ nyang stod pa rnams kyis sgar brdung sogs byed pa'i rtsom pa mi 'dug na'ang rang rang gi bsod nams kyi mthus/
pha rol pa rnams de nub sgar brdung yong ba 'dug zer brda zhogs chen po byas mtshan zang thag gnyid bcag /spre nyal byas bsdad/ ku co cung zad tsam la 'ur zhogs chen
po byed dgos byung zer/ sang nam langs nas sgar phyir thegs song / bdag rang phyogs bsod nams dpung chen dang / /lha dkar phyogs chos skyong srung ma'i mthus/ /dgra nag
