phyogs srog dang ma bral yang / /snying kha ru 'tshangs pa'i sdug bsngal myong /

/khong rtse chen yab yum sras bcas dang / /blon nor bu tshe brtan sku 'khor bcas/ /thugs rab dga' bde chen phugs su chud/ /snyan grags dkar gyi ba dan 'phyar la brtson/ /de
nas sgra zin legs par phye/ /chos ldan gyi 'phrin las kyang de tsam yin/ /yar phyogs la 'gro bsam pa'i grol cha yang yang zhus pa/ gzim lags drung gis 'di na gser zer ba'i
dben dgon spro mo zhig kyang yod/ lo 'ga' bzhugs dgos de tsam ma byung na yang thugs lhod tsam cis kyang gnang dgos gsung / sngar gra lnga nyin byed dbang po bde gzar
gyi 'gros la brten rwa lung phyogs su phebs dgos byung tshe/ rang gis mi sna nyis sbrel btang / gsol ja 'bul ba tsam thub kyang zhal dngos mjal ba zhig ma byung de rtse chen
phyogs na bzhugs yod 'dug pas dngos su mjal/ gra lnga nas la tshe bka'/ sgrol dkar gyi tshe 'khrid rjes gnang dang bcas pa grub/ gnang sbyin yang tshad med mdzad kyin
'dug /rang res kyang sgrol ma lha khang du spyan drangs sems dkar mtshon byed 'bul ba mtshon tsam yang byas/ snyan ngag sogs 'bel ba'i gtam yang mang po byung / snyan ngag
pa lha mthong ba dpal sgang pa sogs kyang snyan ngag tshig sbyor shin tu legs kyang dper brjod ngos ma zin pa cho le ba yod pa 'dra/ khyad par rdzas dang rigs kyi shan
ma phye/ dbyangs can ma rigs su byas pa dang rdzas zhes pa thod pa gri gug sogs ding sang gi dngos spyad la rdzas su bsam pa mang po 'dug zhus/ bdag gis kyang dper brjod
byas pa yod de/ dbyangs can ma rigs su

sbyar bas gzigs 'bul ma nus/ sgrol dkar tshe 'khrid la gsung rtsom zhig gnang dgos gsung / rang gis kyang phran bu zhig byas phul/ yul tshong 'dus kyi gra lnga nyin byed de/
/grogs dbus gtsang gi gros phugs 'dri ba'i yul/ /dus deng sang cha chod ras su 'bor/ /dus 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal gzhan gtso'ang gzob/ /'o yug dka' bcu pa spun de nged rang
la gus shing legs pa'i mthun sbyor byas/ sde pa gzim zhal ngo rnams kyis dang thog nas thugs dkar zhing de'i bar du nyal 'gro'i rgyun bzhin gus zhabs che ba rang mdzad/
bsnyen cing bkur ba'i khri la yang yang bzhag /mkhar rtse chen gros 'debs sngon rab 'ga'/ /yul lang ka'i rtsub 'gyur tshal mtshungs kyang / /khong ci 'dod nor bus kha
sgyur bas/ /dus 'gyur ba'i rnyog ma sangs nas song / /de nas yong khar lha sras drung gis bkra shis kha btags kyis gtsos pa'i bdun tshan/ sde pa ma nas bkra shis kha btags/
dngul dkar gzugs/ dkar rgyan/ ja sigs/ gos phyi nang / gon ma/ ras yug /gzims zhwa rgya tshos/ gzan li khri/ ring 'gag dngos gtsang / rta/ gzim lags kyis bkra shis kha
btabs/ ja rtse rdum/ dar ljang yug /sngon gyi spen 'dab dngos gtsang bubs/ ar skya sdong po/ dngul phor/ rten khebs/ gding ba li khri/ sde pa phun tshogs nas kyis gong ma'i
rten sgam shan mtshon mdangs legs pa dang bcas pa bcos nas phul/ phyi ba ling 'o ma'i rgya mtsho cher/ /nang dam tshig dri ldan myu gu 'khrungs/ /bar lta ba phyag chen
me tog 'bar/ /'khor chos srung bung ba thibs se thib/ /de nas

sde pa dpon blon gyi chibs rags mang po dang bcas te khro mda' nor bu sgang thug phebs skyel byas/ gur mang po phub gsol ja gnyis sbrel bzhes spro sogs bzabs par byung / bdag
mchod yon shar nub so so yang / /dad 'dun dang mkhyen brtse'i srad bus sbrel/ /dus nam yang shis pa'i cho ga bstar/ /chos lugs gnyis dar ba nyams re dga'/ /de nas dgon
pa rdzong la byas dbang ldan du sleb/ dbang ldan rtser sde pa dmag dpon drung la tshe dbang sogs byas/ de dus drung chen bsam rtser bzhugs dgos byung / rgyan drung gang
ci la gnang byung / rgyan drung gi sgos gzhis dbu rir zhag gcig bsdad khong rnams la tshe dbang sogs byas/ sang nang so tshe bdag drung dang / la 'khrud mkhan mang pos tang
tang la la skyel thud byas/ srad phu do dper zhag gcig bsdad/ khong rnams la tshe dbang sogs byas/ de nas sang srad gzhung lam la yongs pas rlung 'tshub dper mi bzod pa
langs/ do dpe nas mi sna zhig gis lam sna byas pa ma gtogs lam dang rab khungs mi chod pa lta bu byung / dmag zor ma dgyes pa'i cho 'phrul yin pas rlung 'tshub la dga'
bar byas zer ba 'dug pas bzod zer gyin yongs/ lha dmag zor rgyal mo 'phreng ba'i rlung / /srad lung pa dog kyang rlung gis spos/ /rlung rba rlabs che yang reg bya 'jam/ /kho
mi sdod mgyogs po 'gro yo byas/ /de nas chu thon tsam gyi la kha zer ba zhig tu bsdad/ gsol 'degs rtsa gzan sogs kyi mthun 'gyur rtse chen nas mdzad kyin 'dug /sang nang
par snga bar langs lhun rtser phyin/ sde

srid gser ma ni sgar thog bzhugs/ lhun rtse na chos rgyal bkra shis stobs rgyas drung dang / sde srid dpal bkras gnyis bzhugs 'dug /dpal bkras drung gi drung 'khor rta pa de
'dras bsu ba spos sna sogs byas rtser phyin/ sde pa dpal bkras drung gis bkra shis kha btags dkar po dang bcas phyag 'bul mdzad kyin 'dug /chos rgyal bkra shis stobs rgyas
drung dang mjal thugs bag phebs pa'i 'bel gtam sogs shin tu 'phel ba byung / sang nyin 'gro rtsis sang nyin cis kyang bzhugs rang re gnyis 'jig rten phyogs kyi gtam tshig
gcig kyang byas re dag bton pas chog gsung / chos rje dpal sdings rig 'dzin pas sgo spe steng du bos tshur phyag 'bul mdzad/ nyams char gyi bzhad gad chen po dang bcas
thugs nang dag pa rang byung / de nas sde pa dpal bkras drung gis gzims chung rten mchod shin tu bzabs pa/ rang la gdan brtsegs mthon pa'i steng du 'bul skyes gya nom
pa dang bcas bzhugs gral chen po zhig tu ra nam mkha' dang dga' ldan pa zhig rigs lung la bslangs/ khos khyed byang ba rdud na ngas shes zer/ rab 'byams pas byang pa thams
cad gcig na med/ kha ri ngom tshul 'di khur nas ngo gdong bteg bteg byed zer ngad langs pa'i thal mo brdabs pas 'phreng ba 'thor gral pa rnams bzhad gad thag pa byung /
drung rams pas rbad chen po'i sgo nas mchod yar rgyas pa byas/ de nas sngags 'chang bkra shis stobs rgyas drung gis gzims chung du bos 'bel gtam shin tu smrar/ ngas

sa phyogs kun tu phyin yang spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa/ sgos dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa byang phyogs 'di na ga 'dug /gzhan na gzugs brnyan tsam du snang gsung / dbang
bskur gyi tshe rjes zlos dgos pa dpon slob kun gyis dus mnyam byed pa 'di e dag gsung / 'dul mngon gyi lugs la ni/ mdzod rang 'grel las/ 'bogs pa po'i sngar yang smra
bar mi bya la/ kha mnyam ste yang smra bar mi bya ste/ de ltar na gzhan las nos pa yin gyi gzhan du na 'bog pa dang nos pa 'grub par mi 'gyur ro/ /zhes bshad pas rjes zlos
dus mnyam du mi rung zhing / sngags la yang de 'dra zhig dgos rgyur 'dug kyang ding sang dus mnyam byed pa cung zad nyams pa yin pa 'dra zhus/ de 'dra'i lung kha gsal
yod phyin dus mnyam mi rigs pa 'dug gsung / nged kyi bu tsha zhig kyang khyed kyi rtsar slob gnyer la gtong gsung / gtor ma'i myu gu'i skor kyang sngar bzhin gsung / de dus
rje dbon 'phags mchog dang / ra dkyil khang sogs kyang 'dug pa rang phyogs zhen gyi mthun rkyen legs po byas/ dkyil khang pa de dus shin tu na ba byung bas/ 'og tu yong
ma khyod steng gi g.yabs chung zhig tu phyin ja dang 'bul ba sogs byas/ srid zhi'i dpal ster rig 'dzin utpal can/ /zur tsam gyis kyang rang gzhan yid 'dzin na/ /rnam dkar
mdzad 'phrin skyong na lta ci snyam/ /ngo mtshar yid kyi ri mo ci yang 'bri/ /sde srid dpal bkras ying 'ong des pa'i gzugs/ /gzhon nur gyur kyang 'jig rten gzhung lugs
skyong / /phun tshogs

'dod dgu 'byung ba'i bsti gnas der/ /dpal dang 'byor pa'i yo lang ci yang byas/ /sang snga bar ber chen bla brang du sleb tshe dbang sogs byas/ sang rdzing lung du gung tshigs
la sleb sbyin bdag rnams la tshe dbang sogs byas/ de nas bya gshongs su dge 'dun rnams kyi ser sbreng gis bsus te sleb/ mang bskol sbyi 'bul rta rnams byas/ de dus chos
rgyal nam mkha' rgyal po lha dbang rtse na bzhugs pa dang mjal/ dpon rigs thor chags la tshe dbang byas/ de nas mtshed du bstan 'dzin rin po che dang mjal/ rje grub chen
nas brgyud pa'i zhal dang phyag bzhi pa'i rjes gnang zhus/ lha khang ka gnyis ma'i rten mchod thugs nang dag pas phod kha 'chams chas sogs dang / gsol dpangs chen mo gser
zho brgya zi zer ba sogs kyi ltad mo sna tshogs kyang gzigs 'bul gnang / bod kha ba can pa'i grub thob dngos/ /rje grub chen gyi gdan khri skyong ba'i rje/ /chos gzhan
la med pa'i ngo mtshar gtam/ /gsung bdud rtsi myong ba skal pa bzang / /de nas rong tshor shog gsung chu byang brgyud nas gruu la thon nas phyin zhag 'ga' bsdad/ dbang
byin rlabs/ rjes gnang sogs mang du byas/ rong tsho byang pa'i der tshe dbang / gzungs gra'i rjes gnang sogs mang du byas/ de nas bya gshongs su sleb/ bo dong gnyer pa mus
nas kyi nang so chos rje la bya gshongs su byon nas tshe dbang phul/ grwa pa rnams la tshe dbang dang / rab 'byams pa kun bsod la phyag rdor rjes gnang byas/ sang la lkog
tu sleb sa lung nas nang so sku mched gzhon nu gnyis kyang mjal du

byung / de nas pho brang lha rtser sleb/ lha sras sa skyong rgyal mo dang mjal/ de dus lha rtse na 'dar nas mi dbang rnam dpyod dang ldan pa dgra 'dul don 'grub bzhugs yod
bas de'i bzhugs mtsher du shog gsung zhag gnyis bsdad/ nor rgyas tshe pas gsol ba btab nas dpon rigs mang po la tshe dbang byas/ rtse de la 'gro 'dug 'tsher bas grol cha
yang yang zhus/ rigs phun tshogs nam mkha' tshe dbang de/ /sku gzhon yang lugs gnyis rnam dpyod 'dzom/ /byang khri skor gyi mdun ma grub bo snyam/ /sems dga' spro rab dga'i
sa thob bzhin/ /de nas grang chen nas nam yong gi gsal len mi yang yang byung / grwa rigs 'ga' zhig gis thel bsdus byas rgan pa'i lugs gcig bton pa 'dra zer ba thos skyug
log /de rigs byas nas dus ngan pa'i shan gyis/ bla ma/ dpon po sogs la'ang rim gyis 'byung nye bas sa phyogs der nged mi yong byas/ ser sbreng grabs byas yod pas cis
kyang 'byon dgos zer byung / nged la ser sbreng gis don med byas/ rags rdzong du chos rje bstan pa dar rgyas bzhugs pa'i sar phyin zhag gcig bsdad/ grang chen nas yang yang
'bod mi byung yang ma phyin/ rjes su rgan pa 'dra byung byings la skyon med tshul mang po gleng gin 'dug /de nas gzhan gyis kyang bskul lcag yang yang byas pas ser sbreng
ni byed ma bcug rang gis bde thal gyis phyin/ 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i mnga' 'bangs der/ /khrims 'jam dar gyi bde skyid dar na yang / /khrims med pa'i spyod pa 'chol
dogs nas/ /rang

ri khrod du bse ru'i sems bskyed kyang / /khong chos ldan gyi sde srid zhal ngo yi/ /thugs dkar ba'i lcags thag bzang po btags/ /rang rbad chod kyi snying stobs zhan pas na/
/khong dad ldan la chags nas zhol le lus/ /de nas sa lung nas lha bzang drung dang skyed 'phrang drung la sde srid nas bka' skyon yod pa 'dug pas zhu ngo dgos zer/ lha
rtser 'dul lags bzhugs pa'i rnam sras gling du phyin/ skyid 'phrang nas cung yangs pa 'dug /lha rtse rtse'i byang phyogs de na lha bzang lags bzhugs 'dug pas der phyin thugs
gso gang yong byas/ rtser sde srid chos rgyal nam mkha' rgyal po la zhu snyan phul/ hor khrims mi yong ba'i zhal bzhes bzang po byung / der mi dbang dpyod ldan grags
pa lags sogs kyi rnam thar dpal gyi 'khri shing 'di dpag bsam 'khri shing gnyis pa yin pas 'phro rdzogs pa zhig rtsom dgos gsung shin tu nan chags pa dang / mi dbang dgra
'dul don grub kyis bzang dar kha gru/ gser zho gang / gon ma sogs gnang nas dpal gyi 'khri shing gi yal 'dab phyi ma gnyis dang / rgyu phra cha gsum snyan ngag gi dper brjod
'dra rtsom dgos gsung bskul lcag gnang gin 'dug /sa mo glang de'i lo shing mang sgrub sder shog zer phyin/ khong rnams la ma gcig khrid dang / zhen pa bzhi bral gyi
'khrid dgos zer/ mkha' 'gro sde lnga'i dbang / nam mkha' sgo 'byed kyi dbang / ma gcig zab don lugs kyi 'khrid sogs byas/ gsol 'debs dang DA ma ru'i khrol shang ni shin tu
che ba 'dug /'ga' zhig gnyan khrod kyang 'grim gyin 'dug

zer/ zhen pa bzhi bral gyi 'khrid kyang rgyas pa byas/ ngan song gsum gyi sdug bsngal bsams pa'i tshe nges 'byung rnam dag skyes pa los yin/ sgrub pa mo rnams kyi mgrin pa'i
'brug sgras mig chu'i char 'bebs mang du byas lab khe'u gad sgron ma'i phaT dbyangs kyis/ /gnyan lha 'dre rnams kyi rna ba bskul/ /rang 'jigs pa med pa'i lta stangs mtho/
/ma lab sgron chos lugs ngo mtshar che/ /chos pha rol phyin pa'i yang snying mchog /gnad zhen pa bzhi bral zab chos 'dis/ /blo chos dang lam du 'khrul pa yi/ /lam 'khrul
med snying gi dkyil du chongs/ /de'i dus sa lung nas zhal snga nas lug ra ba yang chos la yod pas/ khong ni rdzong lugs kyi glegs bam ma bu gnyis phul ba yang phan che/
gnas der rtogs brjod dpal gyi 'khri shing gi yal 'dab lhag ma nyi shu pa yan dang / yongs bsngo'i thad kyi 'grel pa rnams brtsams/ de dus bde gzar yang 'khrug nyams pa
yod pas/ rong pa'i dpung rgyan du yong ba 'dug go zer/ srod la rgyang nas grwa bgres shig byung rab phyag phebs/ tha na'ang bsrung yig tsam dgos zer/ tho rengs snga bar lha
rtse nas chos rgyal nam mkha' rgyal pos phyag rtags phebs/ khyed kyis rong pa'i sgar sar byon na rgyang 'di spyi mchod du 'gro ba 'dug pas legs tshogs che gsung / de dus
rang re yang khams bde mo med kyang nam langs la rta kha sgyur/ lug ru'i gdong der sleb tsam na rgyang phyogs na du ding chen po 'dug /sgar bteg 'gro yin yod pa 'dug zer/
'dar du sleb khar 'dar pa rnams kyang dmag grab

sag ge byas lha rtse sogs la byung na dor stod la 'gro zer nged kyi bla brang du sleb tsa na rin spungs dpung snga ba la bteg song zer 'gro ma dgos/ rang re'i zhu yig rgyang
pa'i grwa pa des phul bas 'di 'phyis nas da ma byung gsung zer/ rtsod dus kyi mgron po brel dus 'dir/ /phyogs gnyis phyogs su snying rtsa 'dar re ba/ /khong rgyal pham
gyi res 'jog thor re ba/ blo chos song rnams gcer nyal long nge 'dug /de nas rang lus ma bde bas sa lung chu tshan la de 'phral phyin/ /rab rgyang drung 'tsho nas kyang mjal
du byung / /rtswa me shing sogs 'dar nas bka' lung byas sems mtsher nas byung / sngar phan sa lung chu tshan du chu dkar mcher mi yong na'ang de dus phu'i chu dkar ma
zhig 'dra ba'i chu dkar ma nyin gcig byung yul sa lung rang byung tsha ba'i chu/ /thag ring yang lus zungs 'tsho ba'i sman/ /rtsa ser nag skol na 'chi med chab/ /khrus rdzing
bu ngo mtshar de nas skyis/ /de dus gtsang pa'i dpung sa lung du sleb/ lha bzang drung la skyon chen po yong ba 'dug pas byang sems a mdzes drung gis yong dgos gsung
phyin/ lha rtser sleb tsa na lha bzang drung da nang thegs de 'dra'i skyon mi yong ba yod zer slar log /de nas yun ring po ma lon par lha bzang drung dus la babs zer thugs
dam 'dogs sleb byung / mi phal cher gsol ba yin zer gtam smra yin 'dug /dus snyigs ma lnga bdo'i mjug ma 'dir/ /mi drag pa las kyis 'das na yang / /zas ngan pas yin zer
'chol gtam smra/ /gtam dang du ma len rna ba dgab/ /de nas drang

srong don grub kyis bram phur 'ja' sa ngo mtshar drug gi leb bris mdzad pas rab gnas la yong dgos gsung phyin/ zhag bcu skor bsdad/ dbang byin rlabs rab tu gnas pa'i me tog
gi char bab/ ngo mtshar drug gi ri mo mig gi dga' ston du gyur pa la rna ba'i rgyan du gyur pa'i snyan tshig gi sbyor ba yang byas/ mi grags ldan don grub rgyal po des/
/yul rgya nag yig tshang las btus pa'i/ /sngon gtam du ma grags 'ja' sa drug /de bgod la rab gnas me tog gtor/ /de nas sgro lung du rdo rje 'dzin pa kun dga' mchog ldan drung
du phyin/ sku nas stabs kyis gsung chos mang po ma byung ba yong ngam/ sngar ma thob pa'i sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang lung phran bu zhu snyam pa byung / ma chen skal
bzang gis rang re la ched gtad kyi khang pa gsar pa zhig kyang bcos 'dug /sgrub thabs rgya mtsho song mtshams ma chen gyis mtshams sbyar/ khyed rang gi thugs la yod pa'i
bka' babs so so'i dbang dang / rgyud bshad sogs kyang zhus na gnang ba zhig yong ngam zer/ rang yang sems dga' spro'i ngang nas de bzhin zhus zhal bzhes byung / thog mar
'grel pa lugs kyi dbang / mtsho skyes lugs kyi dbang / nag po lugs kyi dbang / bka' rim pa bzhi/ gur rigs bsdus kyi dbang / saM bu Ta rdor dbyings kyi dbang / gsang 'dus
'jam rdor gyi dbang / gsang 'dus spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang / rgyud bshad la rgyud kyi sngon 'gro gsum/ dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi bshad pa/ lung tsam ma yin par tshar gsum
gsum dogs gcod

gsed bkrol dang bcas te gnang / dbang de dag la dgos pa'i yig cha so so'i lung / mthar rnam sras ser chen gyi rjes gnang dang bcas te rdzogs par gnang shin tu bka' drin che/
rang yang rgyud man ngag gi bdag por gyur snyam sems gzengs mtho ba rang byung / de dus rang gi rgyun gtor rdo leb gcig gi steng na yod pa de la myu gu sngon po me tog
se sding ba dang bcas pa gtor ma'i snying po mi mthong ba de 'dra skyes/ de dus gdong dga' nas zhabs drung sku mched gnyis mi bzhugs yod kyang zhal bkod kyis khyab pa yin
nam/ bdag mo rtse chen mas thab chas shin tu bzang ba/ de bar gyi bzhugs shing rnams 'bad med du gnang / rags rdzong slob gnyer ba rnams kyi ri la zhag nyal byas pa'i shing
bu ser skam ma shin tu mang ba bskyal/ de rje rin po che sa skya la phebs pa'i bar la gdong dga' rtser shog gsung zhag gsum bsdad/ ban gtsang pa rnams la mgon po'i rjes
gnang / rtse chen bdag mo/ yum tshe dpal drung / bkra shis rtse pa sogs la tshe dbang / gzungs sgra sogs mang du byas/ de nas sgro lung du sleb mtshams rmi lam shin tu
dga' ba zhig byung / rtse chen bdag mo dang / yum drung gnyis spro lung du yang byon nas 'bul ba sogs shin tu bzabs pa mdzad/ yum drung gis ba gzhon ma gcig kyang gnang
gsol ja dang / 'jam sdor la phan pa gyis gsung / de skabs su bde kye gsang gsum sogs kyi mngon dkyil rnams 'jam pa'i rdo rje dang / byams rgyan gnyis kyis bris dbang de dag
gi dkyil thang rnams phyogs

mtha' nas btsal te sprul sku rnam sras kyis bris/ gnas skyid phug sgro lung yang dben du/ /rje kun dga' mchog ldan zhabs pad bsten/ /rgyud bka' babs dbang gi srad bus sbrel/
/rgyud sngon 'gro dngos gzhi'i bshad 'brel thos/ /rjes dpal ldan sa skya'i zab pa'i chos/ /rgyud man ngag zab dbyangs sgrogs pa der/ /sngags rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa
dar/ /chos 'di 'dra'i ngo mtshar skal ba bzang / /mdo rgyan drug gzhung la nges pa brnyed/ /sgos 'phags pa klu sgrub gzhung la 'dris/ /spyir rdo rje theg pa'i bag chags sad/
/sgos rje btsun gong ma'i gsung la 'dris/ /chos rnyed par dka' ba'i rgyud man ngag /dus da res rang skal rim gyis brnyed/ /rang skal par 'tsham pa'i gdul bya rnams/ /yid
dga' ba sgoms shig snying gi bu/ /spyir gdong dga' nas mi dbang rnam rgyal rdo rje dang thog nas thugs 'dris/ mi dbang bstan pa lags kyis bya gshongs la 'gro pa'i lam
bar rags rdzong rtser shog gsung / chos kyi 'bel gtam shin tu 'phel zhing thugs dgyes/ gzims chung dngos mar sdod gsung zhag gcig 'gor/ sku mdun chos rje'i drung dang yang
bya gshongs su mjal thugs bag phab pa'i snying gtam mang po shod pa gnang / tshe ring lags kyis gdong dga' grwa tshang gi 'dzin bdag dgos gsung phyag rtags yang yang phebs/
tshe brtan lags dpon blon gyis lha rtser de mthun bka' lung nan chags gnang gin 'dug /gdong dga' grwa tshang de mdo sngon song gi grwa rigs mang

bas chos 'chad pa la spro mo yin pa 'dug kyang / rang na tshod stabs kyis chos 'chad mi thub cing ming gis skyong ba tsam la phan yon med bsam grol cha zhus/ khong mi dbang
gdong dgar zhal ngo mched/ /chos 'jig rten rnam dpyod ches bkra zhing / /dad 'dun pa'i lhag bsam dkar na yang / /rang zhi bde'i cho gar zhen zhing chags/ /de nas stag lo
grang chen chos 'khor yang rtser bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang / gur rigs bsdus kyi dbang la mi dbang dgra 'dul don grub sogs zhal ngo rnams kyang bzhugs/ de nas dge bdun
rnams la mgon po'i 'khrid dgos zer mgon po'i rjes gnang phyi 'khrid/ khyad par brag rdzong ma'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi 'khrid rnams rdzogs par grub/ nang 'khrid dgos zer
na'ang de skabs ma grub/ dpal mgon po'i yang gsang phyi nang 'khrid/ /gnyan khro bcu 'dra cog byas so zer/ /chos rang la med pa'i sdug gnong gis/ /gzhan chos spong las
ngan ma sog gcig /de nas shar ri phug tu chos 'chad la yong dgos zer phyin sgrub sde rnams la rnal 'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs 'khrid dang bcas pa/ zhen pa
bzhi bral gyi 'khrid byas/ gdong dga' bas tshe ring lags chab la phebs pa'i lam kha nas shar phug tu phebs/ sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang dgos gsung phul/ gnas der mai tri mkha'
spyod kyi mngon dkyil dang / indra mkha' spyod kyi mngon dkyil rnams kyang de dus brtsams pa yin/ gzims chung phug na gtor ma rnams yod pas myu gu sngon po me tog se
chem me ba grangs med pa skyes

gtor ma de rnams ma bsdus par gtor kha gsos la chab re sbyongs shig byas pas yang yang myu gu thon gyin 'dug zer/ rnal 'byor ras rkyang pa la zhen pa bzhi bral la sbyar ba'i
mgur ma dgos zer/ mgur tshan pa gnyis brtsams/ der zla phyed skor bsdad/ zangs gzhon nu 'bar gyi dben gnas mchog /de 'phos pa shar ri phug tu grags/ /rje blo gsal rgya
mtsho'i chos kyi khrir/ /mi khos kyang chos bshad yang yang byas/ /de nas thub bstan dge 'phel du phyin/ tshogs pa rnams la bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang dbang tshan lnga tsam
byas/ beg gdong lcam dral gyi rjes gnang yang dbang tshan yang kha re byas/ gnas thub bstan dge 'phel ri bo'i spor/ /rje sa paN bskrun pa'i yul gnas der/ /dpal 'khor
lo bde mchog nag po pa'i/ / dbang chu rgyun dri med yang yang spel/ /de nas cha lung du sgrub chen bde legs dpal 'dzom gyis spyan drangs nas phyin/ nged rang gis rje btsun
grags pa'i sgrub gnas shing sgo mar bsdad/ chos 'chad sa tshoms ma g.yabs gsar bcos shig 'dug /lam 'bras ni mi rdzogs spros med dgos gsung / nged rang gi brgyud pa 'di
brgyud pa gnyis ldan yin pas thog mar gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang / de nas 'khrid btsugs/ spros med rgyun gyi byin rlabs byas/ byin rlabs de tsam ngor lugs la'ang 'dug /de
nas theg chen pa nas brgyud pa'i rnam rtog 'od gsal gyi byin rlabs byas/ de nas sems bskyed pa drug gi 'khrid

dang bdud rtsi byin rlabs byas/ der rjes bar chad bsal ba sogs 'khrid rdzogs par byas/ theg chen pas mdzad pa'i spros med tshig rkang gi rnam 'grel dang / rje ngor nas mdzad
pa'i spros med mdzes rgyan sogs lung rnams kyang cha tsam song / de dus phyag chen rtsod spong gi 'go thor tsam la padma dkar pos mchan bu gnang 'dug pa'i yang lan spyan
dbye ba'i cho ga de yang de dus brtsams pa yin/ rje grags pa mkha' spyod spyan 'dren pa'i/ /shel skas rings btsugs pa'i padma'i gdan/ /rje bla mas rta mgrin zhal gzigs
pa'i/ /gnas bzang po rang byung rdo'i phug par/ /rje rnal 'byor dbang phyug bi rU'i srol/ /rang cig car 'khrid pa'i lam gyi mchog /chos spros pa med pa'i gdams pa byin/ /nyams
rtogs pa'i rdzing bu khol bar shog /de nas stag gi lo de la mi'i dbang po dgra 'dul don grub kyis rgyud gnang dgos gsung nan gyis bskul/ chos mnyan pa zhabs drung gtso
bor bzhugs pa'i/ chos rje gtsang tshul/ rgyang rab 'byams pa byams pa rgyal mtshan/ byang rab 'byams pa nam mkha' rnam rgyal/ lhas sdings rab 'byams pa mang thos dga'
ba'i bshes gnyen/ gong dkar rab 'byams pa byams pa snying po/ gcung rab 'byams pa dbon byams pa rgyal mtshan/ mtsho sgo dge slong pa/ grang chen pa sum cu skor yod/ de rnams
kye rdor man ngag lugs kyis smin pa yang 'dug kyang rang gi rgyud bshad thog ma yin pas man ngag lugs kyi dbang yang byas/ rang re sa lugs kyi rgyud bshad 'di man ngag
lugs

dang 'grel pa lugs zung 'brel yin pas/ 'grel pa lugs kyi dbang yang 'brel chags snyam nas dbang de yang byas/ de nas rang re sa skya pa'i phyag srol sngon 'gro tshul bzhin
dang / rgyud kyi dngos gzhi gnyis nges par dgos pas thog mar bshad bya'i rgyud bshad thabs kyi man ngag des ji ltar 'chad tshul gsum tshang ba ni rgyud sde spyi rnam yin
pas de'i zin thun btang / de rjes rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa lag tu blang ba'i rim pa ni mngon rtogs ljon shing yin pas de'i zin thun btang / 'di rnams kyi zin thun gtong
ba la spyir mdo sngags zung 'jug /khyad par du grub mtha' smra ba bzhi'i rnam bzhag legs par phyed pa'i rnam dpyod dang ldan pa zhig ma byung na mgrin pa thung bsril 'gro
bas/ gzhan gyis brtsams chos la klog sgrogs re ba tsam las mi 'byung ba yin no/ /rgyud sngon 'gro'i zin thun byed pa la/ /mdo sngags kyi pha rol son nas kyang / /khong
grub mtha'i rnam dbye phyed pa dgos/ /de mi byed klog sgrogs mchod gnas tsam/ /de nas gsol phu nas zhabs drung chen mo sku tshe ma brtan pas yong dgos gsung bang chen byung
/ rje bla ma kun dga' mchog ldan la bang chen 'di ltar byung / sngon 'gro dngos gzhi'i mtshams shig 'dug pas yud tsam phyin na e khyab zhus pas rgyud ni shin tu gnyan/
sbyin bdag ni sku khag shin tu che ji ltar rigs dgongs pas gcod pa zhu gsung / rang za 'dod ltogs brel ma yin yang / /khong sbyin bdag snying nas dad ldan yin/ /chos sngon
'gro

dngos gzhi'i bar 'di la/ /cung 'gal ba med snyam shar la chas/ /de nas rong tshor phyin/ sbyin bdag gshegs bzhugs kyi dgongs pa'i re ba bskang / zhag bcu tsam la mgyogs skor
byas/ rgyud kyi dngos gzhi btsugs/ zla ba gsum tsam song de bar la chos ja tshogs 'khor sogs shin tu mang ba byung / rgyud sngon 'gro dngos gzhi gnyis la zin bris byed
mkhan yang bdun tsam byung / khyad par rtse zhabs drung dang dge slong byams chos pa gnyis bsgrigs pa'i zin bris dang / ra nam mkha' rnam rgyal gyis bsgrigs pa'i zin bris
gnyis rang gis kyang 'pho thabs byas tshig don 'byor po byung bar nges/ rang gis kyang 'grel pa dag ldan/ rnam bshad nyi 'od 'phags mchan rnams gdan du bting / 'grel ba
lugs dang / man ngag lugs gnyis so sor dbye/ rang gi rnam dpyod kyi nus pa gang thon byas pas mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa thob par sems so/ /rgyud brtag gnyis mkha' 'gro'i bka'
yis gdams/ /khong mkhas rlom gzhan gyis sgo ma phyed/ /rang bla ma mkha' 'gro'i byin rlabs kyis/ /gnad bkrol nas skal bzang rnams la sbyin/ /de'i dus ra byams chos pa 'jam
dbyangs dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyis dpal ldan sa skyar rgyud kyi gra skor la phyin par skabs su rgyud kyi gra skor gyi srol 'di chad 'dug pas sa skya gong ma bu slob rnams
kyang shin tu dgyes tshor che ba mdzad/ drung rams pas rgyud zin thun gyi steng nas bshad pa nyi ma gsum byas pas khong rnams 'di lta bu'i bshad pa ngo mtshar che ba
yi

ger 'khod pa med/ khong bla ma mkhas pa dang mjal bas yin pa 'dug /skal pa bzang zer/ lo de la 'brum pa thor cha yod pas zhabs drung 'dul lags kyang thugs zem me yod/ rgyud
ma grol bar du su gang la yang skyon ye ma byung / rgyud grol nas re thu byung / 'on kyang drag pa rnams la skyon ye ma byung / de mtshams drang srong don grub rgyal pos
drang srong bon skyabs shin tu thu ba yod pas yong dgos gsung phyin/ de nub dger mda' ru bsdad de nas phram phur sleb drang srong bon skyabs sku tshes ma zin 'dug pas dus
tha ma'i cho ga btsugs/ kun rig cho ga pa chos rje gshongs chen pa/ rdza re'i bla ma/ drang srong gsung gi rje gshongs chen pa 'di dad 'dun shin tu che ba 'dug pas phyag
'bul la 'byon pa 'dug pas/ de lugs kyi bdag rkyen gnang dgos gsung kho bos kyang phyag lan byas sgrol dkar mgon po'i rjes gnang sogs gsan/ drang srong sku ngo rnams la
tshe bka' sgrol dkar sogs mang du byas/ kun rig stong tshar gyi 'go ma la sdod dgos gsung na'ang 'dar nas zhabs drung chen po sku khams cung ma bde bas grol cha zhus yod/
khong drang srong mi dbang rgyal po yis/ /thugs dad pas spyan drangs zhi gshegs rnams/

/gnas mthon por spor dang sku tshe lhan/ /thugs bsam don 'grub pa'i smon lam btab/ /de nas nged mang mkhar rmu na yod tsa na zhabs drung chen mo sku bsnyel du song nas 'bod
mi gcig 'thud gnyis 'thud shing mangs nas byung / gang mgyogs 'gro ba'i lugs byas kyang rta mchog kho 'gro 'thad po mi 'dug pas rnam rtog che ba tsam byung / chos rje dpal
bzang po gcig po khrid nas nang du phyin byin rlabs bka' bsgo 'dra byas pas thugs rig dngas su song zhag gsum bsdad/ tshe bka' rjes gnang sogs du ma byas pas dngas skyed
chen po byung nas 'dar rtser phebs thub/ 'dar mi dbang chos skyong lhun grub kyis/ /thugs dad 'dun skya rengs kyis drangs pas/ /rmongs mun rum sel ba'i nyin byed shar/
/rtsi bzhad pa'i pad dkar tshal rnams bzhad/ /rang la nus pa cher med kyang pha rol po des thun mong min par blo gtad na 'bras bu cung zad mthong bar nges te/ rang cag gi
tsha mo zhig drod shod na mi chos la yod pa des nub cig 'khrul snang la rang gi gtan grogs kyi mas drag tu labs pas thon 'gro snyam pa'i snang ba shar/ sgor thon tsam na
mi zhig gis ske nas khrid 'gro ba'i snang ba shar/ gzhan nus pa ma byung a khu chos rje mkhyen zer ba zhig thon/ lha 'dre rgan rgon gnyis kyi sar sleb zhag bzhi tsam bsdad/
khyod rang song btsun pa gcig gis mig ngan lta ba sogs mi 'dod pa sna tshogs byed kyin 'dug zer/ de snga 'gro 'dod kyang 'gro mi thub 'tshol mkhan byung tshe rang gis
'tshol mkhan mthong

kyang 'tshol mkhan gyis rang mi mthong / de rjes rta pa zhig byung bas phan tshun gnyis car gyis mthong / rang yul du sleb zer/ de yang mo rang gis a khu chos rje mkhyen zer
ba'i tshig thon pa de'i nus pa yin pa 'dug zer/ rang gzhan skyobs kyi dri bzhon dal na yang / /gzhan dad mos kyi rlung zer sir tsam gyis/ /sa thag ring gi nye du gdon las
skyabs/ /chos rten 'brel gyi gnad 'di ngo mtshar che/ /de nas gcung ca lam du rang gi pha spun tsha bo gser dpon skye ma 'brum pa la brten nas tshes ma zin zer gcung la
phyin/ chos gling pa rnams kyis kun rig gi chog gra btsugs/ rang gi dgyes mdzad kyi dus mtha'i cho ga byas/ ming byang bsgral/ khong mi ngo rnams la tshe dbang rjes gnang
sogs du ma byas/ de dus chos rje 'bum pa dpal 'byor shes rab kyang bzhugs 'dug pas sngar bya gshongs su 'dris stabs kyis dad mos dga' ba chen po mdzad/ sngar lam 'bras
thob phar yang cung zad bshad da sgrub pa lung sbyin/ brda chig brgyud/ gsang bcu'i rgyas 'debs sogs cha lag mang po ma thob/ rje zhi dgon pa la zhus pas khyed dang nged
bla ma mi gcig mi yong gsung / da khyed kyis mdzad na e yong zer/ spyir bla ma gcig la ka yongs su rdzogs pa dga' de ma byung na bla ma gcig mi gcig gi rtseg 'gram chen
po ni mi dgos pa 'dra zhus/ de nas 'bum pas rgyu dbang / lam dbang / lam zab/ mgon rkyang / brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin

sogs zhus/ mig chu 'dzag pa'i dad shugs chen po mdzad kyin 'dug /e dang khri mkhar rnams su yang phyin/ tshe bka' rjes gnang sogs mang du byas/ khri mkhar du chos rje sa 'bog
pa'i drung yang 'dug khong gis kyang mkhan chen 'bum pa la lam 'bras thob kyang sgrub pa lung sbyin sogs cha lag rnams ma thob/ rje dbon mchog grub sogs kyis ched gtad
zhus kyang nga la yang bla ma bsod nams rtse mos 'di las ma byung 'dis yong gsungs nas lung gcig las ma byung da khyed kyis mdzad na e yong zer/ lam 'bras 'chad na med thabs
mi 'dug pas cis kyang byed byas rdzogs par phul/ chos gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa ni/ /dar ches pa'i tshe na nub bo zhes/ /khong rgan pos lung bstan de tsam nye/ /thugs
dpyod ldan mdzod cig che btsun rnams/ /de nas rang gi chos gling grwa tshang du shog zer nyin khor zhig la phyin/ grwa pa rnams kyi ser sbreng sgra rol cha sogs kyis
bsus rang gis mang skol byas/ grwa pa so sos ja ltir rgyugs nyi shu tsam spyi so so nas 'bul ba rnam grangs mang po byung / khyad par legs bzang gi rgyas sku shin tu legs
pa zhig phul/ byams pa'i sku shin tu che ba zhig bslus 'dug pas rab gnas bkra shis mnga' gsol rgyas par byas/ rang lcang lo'i zur phud mchod pa'i gnas/ /chos 'khor lo bskor
ba'i bsti gnas der/ /sngon dkar ba'i bag chags slar yang sad/ /chos legs bshad sa bon sar 'debs byas/ /de nas ca lam du yongs/ e khang gsar mdar yang tshe dbang zhig
la phyin

thang sku'i ras gzhi la med thabs med pa'i ras sgong shun zer ba yug gcig phul/ mi gces pa skye ma 'od 'tsho de/ /tshe dus babs dbang gis mtho ris song / /nged bla ma rnams
la ra mda' bos/ /lam 'khrul pa med la lam ston byas/ /mtho thar pa'i stegs bur sleb bo snyam/ /de nas shar lam dang ldan tshe 'phel drung gi gro lung du shog zer phyin thugs
shin tu dgyes pas zhag gcig bsdad/ tshe bka' sogs phul mdo spe chos sder rje dpon nam mkha' drung la gson byang dgos zer/ sa skya pa phal cher de mi rung zer na'ang
spyir btang dmigs bsal gyi gnad shes dgos/ gson po'i rnam shes bkug nas gnod pa byas tshe gnod nus na gson po'i rnam shes bkug nas sdig pa sbyangs na ci'i phyir mi phan snyam
nas byas/ de nas rang gi sbyin bdag rnying ma bya mchur shar lam shog gsung phyin/ khong rnams la rtog bcas kyi sgo khyi gsa' yis bsad pa dang / sras chung ba legs pa
zer ba de la zung 'dzugs kyi ra pho rwa bzhi pa zhig yod pa des gtam yang cung zad labs pa yin nam zer/ gang na'ang rtog bcas shin tu che ba 'dug pas zhag 'ga' re sdod
dgos zer nan chags byed kyin 'dug /sras chung ba de yang sems la skyo snang chen po byas ya nga mo 'dug /shug khrod nas grwa pa 'phrad mkhan mang po yang byung / chos rje
bla ma thugs rje rnam rgyal yang spyan gsal po med kyang mjal du byung / dmag zor nye brgyud kyi rjes gnang dgos gsung de ga'i dkyil 'khor

gtor ma mchod pa rnams bshams/ bdag mdun sgrub pa byas chos rje'i drung de nub sku khams bsnyel du song / de nub phebs ma thub/ de nas cung zad nas 'gal rkyen ci yang med bzhin
du dmag zor gtor ma de manydzi'i steng nas sa la brul byung / khong yon bdag gang rung zhig la mi dga' ba'i ltas yin pa 'dug snyam/ bskang gso/ gtor sgrub srung 'khor
sogs ched gtad byas/ zhag gsum bsdad sras de yar skyed chen po byung / chos rje bla ma'i drung phyis spyan gsal po ma byung zer/ ltas ngan pa'i cho 'phrul mang na yang
/ /khong mi phyed dad pa'i lhag bsam dang / /nged srung ma'i mthu stobs rten 'brel 'dzom/ /dus skad cig glog bzhin yal nas song / /de nas rims pas 'dar du sleb de nas stag
lo phu'i chu tshan la 'gro ba'i yar res shig skyid gshongs don grub pa la dgon pa seng rdzong phyogs 'di ru nged thugs dam byed pa'i khang chung zhig bzos na e khyab zer
ba bzhad gad la byas pas don grub pas de dgongs par yod na zhus pas chog zer/ yum byang sems a mdzes la zhus pas dgongs pa la yod na los byed/ rnal 'byor pa zhig bzhugs
kyin yod pas de la ni bzhugs gnas gzhan zhig byin pas chog /btsun ma 'dra yod de zhing la'u 'dra gzhan du byin pas chog gsung ngo zer/ de nas rnal 'byor pa de yang sku gshegs
byung / de 'dar khang gsar ba tshang yin pas khang gsar bzo rigs bkra shis pas kyang seng rdzong bzhugs gnas la 'bul zer byung / byang

sems a mdzes drung gis phul ba de bzhes pa'i lugs mdzod cig gsung / thugs dkar ba'i sbyin bdag zhal ngo rnams bka' bgros/ cha zhabs la dge bskul las mi bskul bda' mdzad pa'i
'go tshugs byang sems a mdzes drung gis gzims khang la sgo nyi shu byas pa zhig dges pa 'dug go /sgo rnams ngas 'bul lo de lugs mdzod gsungs/ de dus rang gi bsam tshod
sgo nyi shu byas pa'i khang pas don mi 'dug snyam pa byung ste/ 'jig rten gzhung lugs la mkhas pa'i dpyod ldan dam pa'i gsung phyis thog tu khel byung / ma mkha' 'gro bzhi
yis byin brlabs pa'i/ /yum chos ldan mi yi dbang mo yi/ /thugs dkar ba'i zhal bkod thog tu babs/ /ngo mtshar ba'i rten 'brel 'grig par nges/ /de nas dus bzang po ba santa'i
zla ba bzhi pa bdag cag gi ston pas dus bzang po gsum gyis byin gyis brlabs pa dkar phyogs rdzogs pa lnga pa la phyi nang gi mkha' 'gro srung ma la gtor 'bul/ 'phrin
bcol smon lam bkra shis rgyas par byas/ zla ba de ga'i dkar phyogs bzang po gsum pa'i tshes la 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i drung 'khor zho shas 'tsho ba rnams kyi dad blangs
kyis rtsig mal gzhi bting / zhabs drung a mdzes rgyal mos skabs chang / sprul sku legs bshad 'khor bcas dang / sprul sku nor bu spun gnyis kyis rtsig gyang gi bzo dang
/ shing rkos shing bsgrigs sogs nged rang spun gnyis kyi phyags phyi bsgrubs gzhan mi dgos zer nyin mtshan

med par 'khri shing lcug phran gyi bzo'i rig byed legs par bsgrubs/ 'dar cha zhabs kyi grong re nas zhag brgyad brgyad kyi dge bskul brgyugs/ cha zhabs kyi grwa tshang bzhi/
sgrub pa pho mo'i sgrub sde rnams kyis kyang dge bskul yang dang yang du rtsol bas thon pa byas/ sa skyong mi dbang chos lhun drung gis gzims chung gi rgyug pa 'bul gsung
ba la rgyug pa rnams bla brang rang nas sgrub pa dang / 'bul mkhan so sos thus tsam 'dug pas nas mkho ba 'dra gsung nas nas khal lnga bcu phul/ mi dbang bsod nams lhun
chen sku mched kyis bzo rigs pa las 'go pa sogs la zla phogs rgya ri dang bcas pa dang / ka bzhi ma zhig gi rgyug phul/ sku mdun byams pa lags kyis nas khal nyi shu phul/
bde gling nang nas sku mdun a rgyal bu khrid drung gis gdung chen mo gnyis gnang ba la/ ka ba drug /gzhu ring drug rnams byung / bzo rigs 'go lung pa dang bcas pa la nas
zho gang dang ja thum/ grang chen bgres pas bzo rigs 'go lung pa la ston mo/ /grang chen las mi rnams la yi dam rgya mtsho dang / blo gsal chos skyong gnyis kyis skabs
chang / dgen rgyam pas skabs chang / rmu pa dpon po bas skabs chang dang zho gang gi rgyug pa/ skyid gshongs nas gzims chung ka gnyis ma'i rgyug pa dang bzo rigs pa la skabs
chang / phu grwa tshang nas bzo rigs las 'go pa la ja bur ston/ sbyin pa bas phu grwa tshang las mi la skabs chang / bsam grub gra tshang las mi la dgon pa spe bla brang
nas

skabs chang dang / rna 'u bas skabs chang dang gdung gcig /dar rgyas gling las mi la gra tshang rang nas skabs chang / zur khang dge slong pas gdung gcig /ru byang pas gzhu
ring gsum/ gzim lags kyi rgyug rtsa bcu/ dgon phug nas rgyug bcu/ sngon mo rdzong pas rgyug bcu/ khab gong pas rgyug bzhi/ cha lung sgrub chen mas bzo rigs las 'go dang
bcas pa la ston mo/ /bla brang rang nas bzo rigs las 'go dang bcas pa la ston mo kha re song / ma chen 'gro bas bzo rigs las 'go ba dang bcas pa la skol ja nyag bdun/ de
rnams kyi las byed kyi 'go ma zhal ngo rnams kyi bkas khyab pa dang / rang gis kyang bcol gdams byas/ grwa pa rnams la nyi ma blo gsal dang / dpal ldan tshul khrims gnyis
kyi 'go mi dang khong gnyis la bla brang nas shing cha nyo ba'i do dam yang bcol/ mi skya rnams la gzims dpon kun dga' zhes pa des 'go ma byas/ zla gsum zhag po bcu'i ring
la khang pa 'gram bting nas thog phubs/ spos zhal dang bcas pa/ gzims chung ka bzhi ma/ rab gsal ka bzhi ma/ dbang khang ka bzhi ma/ gzims chung 'phral dgos gdung khang
ma/ g.yabs shar nub/ shag mig tha dad/ lho na shag mig de rnams tha dad la kun spyod dang bcas pa/ ja khang ka gnyis ma shing mdzod dang bcas pa/ phug na gnyer khang ka
gnyis ma shag mig dang bcas pa/ yang shar nub gnyis na shag gnyis/ gung na me tog ldum ra/ de'i mtha' rdo bcal

gyis bskor ba/ lho 'khris la rkang 'thung gi do ra dang bcas pa rnams legs par grub/ ming du slob bshad nor bu gling zhes btags/ zas gtsang sras la rgyal byed tshal zhes khang
bzang phul la 'gran pa bzhin/ /mgon med zas sbyin snying stobs mchog la co 'dri byed pa'i mi dbang che/ /dgra phyogs 'dar byed rigs rus phun tshogs dpal rtsal 'dzom pa'i
dad ldan gyis/ /nA gA rdzu nar nor bu'i gling mchog dad pas phul 'di rab brtags gsal byed kyi rgyan/ ngo mtshar gnas/ rang gi rnam dpyod nyi mas gdungs pa'i blo gros
mig ldan gnyis 'thung che/ /legs bshad khrus la rings par chas nas sde snod rgya mtshor zhugs pa de/ /nyi ma'i bu mo gzhung lugs pad ma'i tshal rab ma lus 'joms so snyam/
/rab rtog rgyan 'phreng nor bu'i do shal mi dbang mgul du mdzes gyur cig /las dpon mgron po'i tshogs rnams la/ /bsnyen bkur mgron gyis tshim byed rnams/ /ci 'dod 'dod dgus
tshim byas nas/ /bde ba can der bgrod par shog /las byed pho mo 'di dag kun/ /lus ngag ngal ba khur byas pas/ /'di phyir ngal ba kun spangs nas/ /'chi med gnas bzang bgrod
par shog /zas gtsang sras der gtsug lag khang chen gyis/ /rab dgyes skyed phyed wa ra NA si yi/ /khyim bdag dge bzang yus kyi brnangs byed pa'i/ /khengs pa 'phrog byed
sa skyong 'dar nas rgyal/ /'brug lo ston byang sems yum a mdzes rgyal mo dang / dpon sa dbang ldan ma rdo rje dpal mdzom bu khrid/ chos lags chos bzang

lags/ dge slong byams chos pa/ dge slong rje btsun/ dge slong chos dbang legs pa/ chos mdzad chos 'phel sogs bcu skor la ni gu dgos gsung / ni gu'i smin byed rgyud sde lnga'i
gtso bsdus kyi dbang / bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang / chos drug gzhung shing gi bka' dbang brgyad sogs/ rje dam pa las thob pa'i byin rlabs nyer lnga/ gzhan yang phyag rdor
dza li ma/ rnam 'joms sogs rje dpal 'bar rgyal mtshan la thob pa'i byin rlabs sogs sum cu skor dang / mdor na rtsa ba phyag rgya chen po/ sdong po ni gu chos drug /yal
ga 'chi med 'phyug med/ lo 'dab lam khyer rnam gsum/ 'bras bu mkha' spyod dkar dmar sogs dang / de rnams kyi phyag rgya chen po ga'u ma dang / chos drug la nyams 'khrid
dang / gzhan rnams la lung tsam dang / 'khrid yig 'jag bsam gnyis kyi 'khrid kyi steng nas bshad bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar gyi lung sogs/ rang gis gang thob kyi lung
rnams kyang byas/ rtse zhal ngo rnams kyis tshogs 'khor/ chos pa rnams la mang ja sogs ther chags su rgyun mi 'chad pa gnang gin 'dug /chos rje byams chos pas zin bris kyang
mang po byas par 'dug /rang gis ni gu'i brgyud 'debs de yang de dus byas pa yin/ sems nying 'khrul rmi lam 'khrul pa'i grong / /dus lan cig 'khyams pas 'dod pa'i don/
/yid ci bsam nor bu'i gter rnyed pa/ /snying padma bzhad pa'i dga' ston yin/ /thugs dad ldan yum sras mchid sogs

kyis/ /rdzas 'dod dgu 'dod yon dpal gyis mchod/ /rje shangs pa'i gser chos bcal du bkram/ /chos don gnyer rgyan du mdzes pa yin/ /de nas mi dbang dgra 'dul don grub kyis sngar
rtsa rgyud sngon 'gro dang bcas pa legs par thob zin kyang / da man ngag cig 'dod bya che bar yod gsungs pa nas khong sum cu skor la lam 'bras 'phral du btsugs/ lam 'bras
ring brgyud cha lag dang bcas pa rdzogs par grub/ lam 'bras nye brgyud/ lam sbas bshad/ phra sgrub dang bcas pa dang / shin tu nye brgyud brda don gsal ba 'khrid dang
bcas pa rjes su gnang dgos gsungs/ bdag yon mchod dpon slob 'khor dang bcas pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo bkra shis mnga' gsol mchod 'phrin smon lam shis brjod dang bcas pas
rang gzhan dgyes pa chen po'i dpal la bkod pa yin no/ /de'i tshe gzhung bshad zin thun dgos gsung zin thun byas/ rang re'i rnam 'grel bcu gcig /gzhung bshad dmar nag /dge
rgan ma sogs legs pa'i cha btus/ gzhung gshad 'di la paN chen bo dong pas mgo mjug tshang ma la mkhas pa'i rnam dpyod ldan pa'i skyon gtong dka' ba 'dug na'ang / gnad che
chung ci rigs pa'i zar zir shin tu mang ba 'dug pa la/ mkhas pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan pas kyang lan mang du mdzad 'dug pa bzhin kho bos kyang rang lugs kyi rnam bshad dang
/ pha rol po'i rtsod pa zlog pa'i rnam bshad zhib tu byas/ chos zab don rdo rje tshig rkang 'grel/ /zhal snyan lam brgyud

pa ma nyams par/ /gzhan rtog ge'i tshig 'phreng smig rgyu la/ /chu bden par 'khrul rnams a re 'tshang / /yul rgya gar rgyal po'i paNDi ta/ /chos dpag bsam 'khri shing sgrun
byed mkhan/ /rigs dge dbang zla dbang snyan grags mkhan/ /phyi rig pa'i gnas la mkhas pa tsam/ /mi dpyod ldan nag phyogs dgra 'dul ba/ /nang rig mchog rgyud dang man ngag
'dzin/ /phyi rig gnas 'byed pa'i zur mig can/ /mkhas dregs ldan dbus na re re tsam/ /mi dbang lhun chen drung yang gsung ngag la thugs brel gyi stabs phebs skabs ma byung
yang / lam zab kyi rigs kun dgos gsungs/ lam zab phyi nang gsang ba/ bla ma rin 'byung sogs rigs lnga rnams phul/ zhabs drung sku mched kyi mang ja tshogs 'khor 'bul ba
rnam gzhag shin tu bzang ba/ gzhan yang zhal ngo rnams so so nas mang ja rnam grangs mang po dang / de dag gi skabs su rdor glu gar rol mo sogs mchod pa'i bye brag bsam
gyis mi khyab pa'i dga' ston byas/ de'i skabs su chos 'chad kyi tshe gzhung bshad la bo dong pas dgag pa re gzug 'dug pas 'di'i lan ngo red mi grub pa 'dug pas sang nyin
byed do byas pas/ chos nyan pa dge slong legs bshad zer ba nyams 'tshar ba zhig yod pa des sang nyin chos bsgugs kyi dus de ring 'thab dus chen po dgos yod pas ltad mo chen
po yod zer/ chos nyan pa rnams bzhad gad thag ge byung zer/ de ga bzhin dgag sgrub kyi spros pa shin tu 'khrug pa byung

ba de yi ger bkod pa de bzhin yin/ 'dir brgyud ldan rnam bshad glegs bu la/ /gzhan ngan rtog ri mos bsgribs mthong nas/ /lan legs bshad khrus kyi cho ga bstar/ /bzhir mdzes
ldan ngo 'dzum mthong na mdzes/ /de nas 'brug lo dbyar chos 'tshog pa la nye ba'i tshe byang rigs ldan chos kyi rgyal po'i pho brang chen po nas/ dpon sa lha gcig phun tshogs
chos kyi rgyal mos/ 'phags ma'i skye bo dpyid kyi pho nya khri'u mkhar nang so chos rje dang / gling nas nang so tshe dbang pa gnyis mngags/ bka'i glegs bu gnang skyes
dang bcas pa'i sgo nas/ dpal g.yas ru byang gi ngam ring chos sde chen po'i mkhan por dpyod ldan gzur gnas kun mthun grub cing mo brtag sogs kyang legs par chud pas sleb
pa byed dgos gsung ba phebs/ rang la de 'dra'i dpe bya yong bsam pa yang med cing / tshe mjug 'di la sos gang dal rnam g.yeng gang chung byed bsam pa ma gtogs/ de 'dra'i
'dod bya ye med pas grol bya zhu bsam de ga'i lugs byas kyang / khong mi sna gnyis po da lan grol bya ci zhus kyang yong ba med/ de bas bka' dang blangs mdzad na thugs
dgyes pa zhig yong gsungs/ de ltar yin kyang gnas tshul 'di snyan du thengs pa zhig dgos pa 'dug /rang gi lo bdun cu lon/ lo de tsam lon nas mkhan por bskos pa sngar yang
med/ khyad par lus po 'di bab theg ye med pa nas gnas tshul 'di snyan du thengs na dgongs grol mi yong kha med yin byas kyang khong

gnyis ma gsan par dbyar chos steng du phyin/ dbyar thog 'di dgag dgos stabs nas dbu mdzad legs pa 'dug gsung / snga so'i dbu mdzad rnams las gdan rnams kyang shin tu mtho ba
legs pa'i cha mang du bsgrigs nas bsko gzhag gnang / sngar phan dbu mdzad tsam la khyud med kyang chos sde'i che bgres slob dpon las 'dzin dang bcas pa thams cad kyis phyag
'bul mdzad/ rtse nas phyag phyi drung 'khor drag zhan thams cad kyis kyang phyag 'bul mdzad kyin 'dug /dbyar chos de la mang ja nas 'bo 'gyed sogs bsnyen bkur/ chos
rigs lung sogs shin tu 'phel ba phyi'i gra skor ba cher ma byung yang / nang nas bshad pa sogs kyang 'phel ba/ sa phyogs kun tu sa gtsang ba sogs legs tshogs shin tu che
ba byung / lha padma DA ki'i mtshan rtags can/ /bka' 'khor lo sgyur ba'i dpal mo yis/ /snyan grags dkar chos sde chen po yi/ /dbu gtsug tor mdzes pa'i rgyan du bkod/ /shar
lam ya ga chos sdings la phyin/ /dge 'dun la mang ja/ rje mkhan gyi dngul gdung la snyan dar yug dkar me sogs phul/ chos rje kun dpal sogs slob dpon mang po la rnam sras
sgrol dkar sogs kyi rjes gnang mang po byas zhag 'ga' bsdad/ rje 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i mkhyen brtse'i thugs/ /nub bde ldan zhing du gshegs pa'i gnas/ /gdung rings bsrel
phung po bzhugs pa'i rten/ /khang rim brtsegs dngul gyi mchod rten mjal/ /lam zab mo'i

rnal 'byor gsal 'debs zhus/ /rdzas dgra gnyer bar ma'i zhen pa spangs/ /phyi lus dngos phongs med mchod par 'bul/ /dbang bzhi ldan sku bzhi'i dngos grub stsol/ /de nas gur
la brgal te bar kar bsdad/ sang nyin chu rab med la grus bsgral te 'dar skyid phug tu sleb/ sang nyin bar 'dar chab srid kyi rta thogs kyis 'khor gyis skor ba'i zhal ngo
rnams dang / grwa tshang gsum sogs ngur smrig khrims ldan rnams kyis dar gdugs 'phan rgyal mtshan phye phur sgra rol mo dang bcas te 'dar chos 'khor yang rtser son/ chos
dang zang zing gi dga' ston rgya che ba la rol/ de nas rang gi bsti gnas slob bshad nor bu gling du sleb/ de dus rje shrI ba blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis rang la thugs brtse
bas bstan gtso zangs thang ma/ sa skya bka' 'bum sogs zhal chems kyi bka' stsal nas bzhag 'dug pa de yang sleb/ bka' 'bum gyi lung 'di yang dkon po 'dug pa nas/ gro mo
lung nas 'jam mgon bla ma kun dga' mchog ldan spyan drangs spyan gsal po rang mi 'dug kyang / ma chen skal bzang gis legs pa'i mtshams sbyar/ khong la 'di'i lung 'phrod na
mig shor yang bzod gsungs/ rang la thugs brtse ba dang / sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i khur chen po bzhes/ zla ba phyed gnyis tsam la dka' 'bum gyi lung yongs rdzogs/ 'jigs byed
rwa lugs kyi dbang / las gshin gyi rjes gnang yig cha'i lung sogs ma tshang ba med par gnang bas bka' drin zla med par gyur/ kho bo rang

gis kyang bka' 'bum lnga'i brgyud 'debs dang / thob yig /rje bla mas ngor chen dkon cog lhun grub pa'i gsan yig nang bzhin gnang / 'on kyang kho bo rang gis sngar thob zin
pa rnams de'i tshe bzlas te zhu ma dgos so/ /de'i tshe 'jigs byed mngon dkyil/ las gshin rjes gnang sogs 'jam pa'i rdo rjes bzabs te bris/ dkyil thang sprul sku rnam sras
kyis bris/ rje sa skya gong ma'i zhal lung gis/ /gnas 'chi med mal las legs 'ongs pa'i/ /gsung bdud rtsi'i ganggA'i chu bo'i rgyun/ /bdag ma dros chu gter che ru 'khyil/
/khong kha 'bab bzhi nas phyogs bzhir babs/ /yul dbus gtsang ljongs su g.yas skor nas/ /sems ma dag 'khrul pa'i dri ma bkrus/ /kun bde ldan zhing du 'khrid par shog /de
nas ngam ring dgun chos la phyin/ tshes bdun gyi mtshan rmi lam du 'du khang chen po zhig gi nang du phyin rgya mthong na mdung dar khra thib se mang po bslang nas bzhag
'dug /khyams stod de na rang gi bla ma zhig yin snyam pa'i bla ma brjid can cig gis khyed la mda' e dgos gsung ba la dgos zhus pas/ mda' gsar pa bcu phon gcig gnang byung
langs 'gro ba'i tshe mda' phon po de lag tu khur/ mdun na po ti mang po 'dug pa de rang gi rogs la bskur nas khur yongs pa rmis/ de'i tho rengs sa g.yos re che ba zhig kyang
byung de yang dge ba'i ltas yin zer mkhan ni 'dug /'brug lo zla ba bcu gcig

pa'i yar ngo tshes brgyad la rgyal phur 'dzom/ kho bo mkhan po'i khri thog tu 'don gsung / sde srid rgyal po nam mkha' tshe dbang phun tshogs dbang gi rgyal po sku shin tu
gces pas/ sa mi gtsang gi dogs 'dzem mdzad sku mtshams dam par yod/ de'i dgongs rgyal po'i mtshan lam la byams chen gyi rtser rgyal mtshan gsar pa btsugs pa sogs mtshan lam
bzang po byung zer/ dpon sa lha gcig phun tshogs rgyal mo drung 'khor rags bsdus dang bcas bsko bzhag la tshogs su phebs/ khri ston la mang ja gsum sbrel/ nas khal 'gyed
dkar spro'i 'gyed/ bur 'gyed/ che bgres slob dpon phyi'i grwa skor ba dang bcas pa la dar 'gyed ngos su 'degs rten bkra shis kha btags gser srang phyed/ dngul phor/ rten
khebs/ gos chen/ ras dkar yug /'dar nas zhal ngo rnams kyis khri ston/ mang ja nas 'bo bkra shis kha btags/ gser zho lnga/ gos chen ring 'gag /rgyud 'brel po ti sogs stobs
che ba/ rtse chen nas dpon blon rnams kyi mang ja 'degs rten bkra shis kha btags/ dngul phor/ gu ge shel gyi ka to ra/ gos phyi nang / gdan rdor gdan ma sogs stobs che
ba/ sde pa drang srong don grub kyi mang ja nyis sbrel/ 'degs rten bkra shis kha btags/ ber thul skyer kha/ ja sigs sogs stobs che ba/ phyag g.yog 'khor bcas rnams kyis
thon si ja rdum/ rdum phyed sogs bsdoms pas spobs rtse tsam/ rang gi stod thung / mtha' dmag bzlog

pa'i smon lam sogs 'dzugs pa la mang ja bzhi sbrel/ bstan 'dzin rin po ches khri ston yin no gsung mang ja/ gnang sbyin bkra shis kha btags/ gu ge shel gyi dkar gzugs/ thon
thi'i pang khebs dngos gtsang / srab chen gyi chos gos/ gos phyi nang sogs stobs che ba/ gzhan yang dkar chos 'degs rten rong tsho nas/ bde gling nas sogs dang / gzhan yang
dad 'dun gyi slob bu sbyin bdag sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pas bgrang gis mi lang ba byung / khyad par khri thog tu sleb tsam gyi tshe/ rang lus la nyi ma shar ba dang /
me tog gi char sbrang char zim pa lta bu yang 'bab kyin 'dug zer/ rang phyogs 'dras bstod pa'i lugs yin nam bsam ste/ steng nang so'i jo gdan bzhi sde pa rnams 'bab nges
pa can yin/ phyogs 'di nas byung dus 'di la byung / yun 'di tsam byung / nges dag rang shod kyin 'dug pas bden pa e yin bsam/ mkha' 'gro'i rigs can mdzes ldan lha mi'i tshul/
/'dus pa'i tshogs su rin chen khrir bkod tshe/ /'dod yon dpal gyis mchod dang lhan cig tu/ /lha rnams dge ba'i me tog dga' char phab/ /dad ldan sbyin bdag lhag bsam
dar bab pas/ /'dod yon mchod sprin sna tshogs phung por spungs/ /tshe dang bsod nams yar ngo'i zla dbang ltar/ /dar rgyas yun ring gnas pa'i bkra shis shog /ngur smrig tshul
khrims dri yis phyogs kun gyi/ /dad ldan bung ba'i tshogs kun bskrad kyang 'khor/ /mgrin

rnga snyan pa'i dbyangs kyis yid 'phrog pa'i/ /byams gling chos sde ngo mtshar dpal gyi gzhi/ /de'i tshe rab brtan lhun grub spe'u nas dad ldan mi'i dbang po kun dga' bkra
shis kyis dad 'dun bdag rkyen snga phyi kun tu mdzad pa zhig byung / khyad par khri chen po de la skas dngos gtsang po mi 'dug pas 'bab 'dzeg shin tu dka' sbyin bdag chen
pos 'di 'dra 'o brgyal gsungs nas shing gi sgam skas bab thag shin tu legs pa zhig bcos nas gnang ba de sems rab tu dga' ba zhig byung / de'i tshe dpal nang so/ /e sde pa/
sku drung dpal rtse/ yol gdong drung chen/ sde pa grags pa sogs phyag g.yog drung 'khor mang pos tshes dbang rjes gnang sogs mang po zhu yin 'dug /lhag bsam rab dkar mi
dbang dga' ba'i mtshan/ /tshe rabs sngon nas 'grogs pa'i bag chags sad/ /bsnyen bkur bsngags pa'i khri la 'gyur ba med/ /tshe dang bsod nams dar ba'i bkra shis shog /de
nas phar lam rngod la phyin/ yul khang shin tu 'jam yongs ru'i dar la thon pa 'dug gsung 'dar nas pho nya byung / phar lam dar shin tu bzang ba brling ba thag chod pa byung
/ 'dar nas dpon blon mnga' srid skya btsun thams cad kyi bsu ba sngar bas kyang ches bzabs pa rang mdzad kyin 'dug /lam bar nar kyang zam ma chad pa'i shong dkar rtse
mo'i btung ba rgyun ma chad pa 'khor 'das dbyer med lta ba'i rgyan du che ba byung / 'dar gyi rdzong 'gram ri phug gi skyed mos tshal du zhal ngo rnams kyis gsol

ja/ bzhes spro sogs rig pa'i dwangs cha thon pa byung / de nas chos 'khor yang rtse'i dri gtsang khang du tshar chen chos kyi rgyal po'i sku gdung ring bsrel bzhugs pa'i gser
'bum la phyag mchod snyan dar sogs phul/ nged kyi snga skad dar la thon dgongs phyogs dar de shor zer/ sems med 'byung bzhi sems dang ldan pa bzhin/ /la chen 'jam rlung
nyi mas drod kyis bskyangs/ /chu chen bsil rlung dar gyis skyel ma byas/ /e ma sgyu ma'i rten 'brel ngo mtshar che/ /sa 'og klu rnams dga' bas rtsi bcud 'phel/ /sa steng
mi rnams rab dga' glu dbyangs 'tsher/ /sa bla lha rnams dgyes pas lo phyugs rgyas/ /rgyal khams kun tu phan bde dar bar shog /de nas phu rang byung gi chus lus zungs gsos
te/ mang mkhar bde gling pa de rang la snying nas dad 'dun gyi sbyin bdag yin pas lam bar du zhag 'ga' ngal gso dang dbang lung rjes gnang 'dra byas/ de nas rang gnas
nor bu gling du sleb/ zla ba gcig gi bar la mtshams se byas/ skabs gseng la klu sgrub bstod 'grel de brtsams/ nub gcig 'phags pa klu sgrub yin zer ba'i paNDi ta paN zhu bsnams
pa zhig dang mjal/ chos kyi bgro ba mang du byung ste tshig rigs ni mi dran/ de nas rang cung zad g.yengs pa'i bar la klu sgrub mi bzhugs 'dug /klu sgrub gar phebs
byas pas thegs song zer/ phebs pas mi yong ba yod/ gsung gling 'dra dgos pa yod byas pas da sku rjes ma zin pa yod

zer/ de bden khong 'phags pa yin pas 'phur nas byon bde ba can gyi zhing du phebs nges bsam pa byung / phebs shul 'od kyi lam lta bu skya thal le ba zhig 'dug /de nas 'phags
pa klu sgrub kyi lta ba la mkhas pa snga phyi mang po dag gi spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i gnad zab mos khong du chud pas/ mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang rdzun du ma gyur tsam yod/
dpal 'phags pa klu sgrub gzhung lugs la/ /lung rigs pa zab mos nges par 'drongs/ /gzhan zer lo'i rjes zlos mi dgos par/ /gnad snying po longs pa kho bo tsam/ /de nas
stag rtse nub dgon nas chos mdzad cig dang nyang stod rkyan ngur nas grwa pa zhig gnyis chos don du gnyer nas rjes 'brang du yod pa de gnyis sogs shes ldan 'ga' re la/ gshed
dmar lha lnga'i dbang / brgyud pa gnyis ldan gyi spros med kyi 'khrid byin rlabs so so dang bcas pa tshang 'grig byas/ de nas rong tsho nas dad ldan gyi sbyin bdag mi
dbang nam mkha' dpal 'byor drung gis sku nas stabs kyis phyin chad 'byon thub pa dka' bas/ da lan khong cig yong dgos gsung snga so nas bka' lung nan chags gnang gin 'dug
pa nas/ phebs bsu'i chibs pa sogs sleb byung ba nas shar la phyin lam bar bya gshongs su zhag gcig bsdad/ mang ja dar 'gyed dang bcas pa byas/ dpon slob rnams tshe dbang
dgos zer chos grwa phyir tshogs pa la tshe dbang byas/ sngon gyi bag chags sad pa lta bus grwa pa rnams spyan chab mang po bsil gyin 'dug

zer/ gling tha dad nas sgos mjal ja ltir rgyugs 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa byed kyin 'dug /de nas rong tshor phyin zhal ngo rnams la tshe bka'/ sgrol dkar rjes gnang dgyes
mdzad dbang tsam byas/ na so'i stabs kyis ngal dub byung gi dogs rnam grangs mang po zhu ba mi gnang 'dug /de'i dus karma sku gzhogs grwa tshang pa la zla ba gcig gi sbyin
bdag gnang 'dug pas/ khong rnams kyis kyang gsol ja zhus 'bul ba sogs byas/ rang res kyang mang ja gcig byas/ grwa tshang de yang slob gnyer ba sha stag /tshogs su dbu
ma 'jug pa'i gzhung 'don sogs dngos gtsang po 'dug /rang re'i drung rams pa byams chos pa dang / drung rams pa byams snying gnyis kyis kyang rigs lung la btang ma la phyin/
khong rnams kyis mthong dga' tshor chen po byed kyin yod par 'dug /de nas rong tsho byang du nub gcig bsdad/ khong rnams la tshe dbang sogs mang du byas/ de nas rong
tsho rtser phyin/ dang thog ma nas mdza' bo snying ltar gces/ /don ci 'dod bzhed dgu'i dpal gyis mchod/ /thugs dkar ba'i lhag bsam dag pas 'khyud/ /dus gtan gyi bshes su
bdag gyur cig /rong tsho nas snang gsal rdzong mdun du gsol 'debs/ sku mched gnyis kyis mdo thug phebs skyel mdzad/ de nas bya gshongs su cal ma zhig bsdad/ de nas la lkog
tu yongs/ spe bzang nas chos legs 'khor bcas la tshe dbang dgos gsung de bzhin byas

sa lung nas sras chung ba gnyer pa dang bcas dkon gnyer dge slong sogs kyang byung 'bel ba'i gtam yang smra/ sang nyin mtsho bo lho sgor bsdad/ khang pa gsar pa la rab gnas
dang tshe dbang sogs byas/ chos rje rgyang pa yang phebs byung / 'bel ba'i gtam sogs 'phrod pa'i gtam mang du glengs/ de nas 'dar chos 'khor yang rtse sogs su phyin/ skabs
shig shing mangs su sgrub sde la zhen pa bzhi bral gyi 'khrid dgos zer byas/ de'i tshe sngar dbang dril nyer lnga'i phal cher grub kyang / 'phro cung zad yod pa dge slong
byams chos pas grogs ldan byas rdzogs par grub/ de skabs nub cig rmi lam du dpal ldan a ti sha yin zer ba da lta'i sku 'dra la ji ltar bris pa'i rnam par can gyi paNDi
ta phyag na bstan gtso'i sku legs po bsnams pa zhig dang mjal/ a ti sha thugs dam 'phel lam byas pas pha la pha la gsung / de nas phyag g.yog pa zhig gis a ti sha gsang
chab dro yin 'dug zer bltas pas zhal nas 'o ma lta bu zhil skya rgyang rgyang 'ong gin 'dug /kho bos kyang lag pa bzed pas yol mo gang 'thungs pas ro mchog dang ldan par
gyur/ rten 'brel bzang snyam dga' ba chen po byung / rang re rong tsho la 'gro ba'i tshe snga sor nas rje btsun sa paN gyi rnam thar thang kha/ thang kha lnga la thus pa
zhig snying la 'dod bya che bar yod pa nye bar sprul sku yang sleb/ ras 'dul skya ris rnams kyang rang gis bkod pa byas shar la 'gro gong grub/ sprul sku de

chang la sred pa che bar 'dug na'ang / ri mo ma grub bar chang bcad/ de bar gyi skol ja sogs kyang bzhag grang mo cher 'brir bcug pas ro tsho'i bar la phal cher grub cung mgyogs
pa'i skyon yin nam zhu na 'ang / rang blo kha rdzogs po byung / 'phro rnams nor bu gling du grub par byas/ gong gsham sogs bzo'i bya ba legs par grub pa nas dgyes rdor
cho ga bzang po drug pa'i sgo nas rab tu gnas pa bkra shis mnga' gsol dang bcas gnas mchog slob bshad nor bu gling du grub pa yin no/ /de'i tshe dkar me bzung nyin mtshan
kha re thub pa byung / rje sa paN rnam thar ngo mtshar gtam/ /gzugs ri mor bkod pa tshon gyi bkra/ /mig bdud rtsir sim pa yid bde'i dpal/ /don ci bsam re ba rdzogs par
shog /mi'i dbang po 'dar nas khu dbon gsum gyi gzims chung rab gsal steng 'og gsum yod pa'i 'og ma mi dbang lhun chen gyi gzims chung la brgya byin pho brang / bar ma
mi dbang chos skyong lhun grub kyi gzims chung la shing rtsi legs par byas/ lam zab la thugs dam gtso bor mdzad pas logs bris la rang nyid gtso bor byas pa'i lam zab brgyud
pa'i bla rim/ chos skyong nor lha sogs kyis bskor ba legs par bzhengs de la rab gnas la shog gsung / 'brug lo hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes bcu gcig gi nub sta gon btsugs/
tshes bcu gnyis la dngos gzhi/ tshes bcu gsum gyi nyi rtser smin drug rgyu ba'i dus rab gnas dngos gzhi'i me tog gtor/ dkyil 'khor rdul

tshon la brten pa/ cho ga kye rdor bzang po drug pa nub gnyis nyin gsum pa'i cho ga kha lag tshang bar byas/ 'on kyang dkyil 'khor sbyin sreg dang ma 'brel bas rab tu gnas
pa'i cho ga yongs su ma rdzogs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pas rab tu gnas pa rgyas pa la dkyil 'khor rdul tshon dang sbyin sreg dgos par bshad/ mjug chog sbyin bdag bsgo ba'i tshe
zhal ngo rnams rgyan sku chas bzabs pa dang bcas bsgo ba'i cho ga bkra shis rdzas brgyad mnga' gsol dang bcas pa legs par bgyis/ tshogs 'khor tshim drug cho ga ci bzabs
kyi steng du chos rje 'jam dpal dga' ba'i bshes gnyen gyi bshad pa'i tshig bkra legs pa dang / tshig don phun sum tshogs pa byas de'i tshe me tog mang po phul 'dug pa la/
rgya lcam pa'i me tog cig sprul lo sa ka zla ba'i dus kyang ma bskams pa'i steng du rkang dang 'dab sngon po gsar du skyes pa'i sngo sol le ba de nas kyang rgyun ring du
bsdad/ de ngo mtshar bar 'dug pas 'di la tshigs su bcad pa zhig rtsom dgos gsung kho bos kyang tshigs su bcad pa 'di rnams byas/ lhag bsam sa 'dzin yangs pa'i lte ba cher/
/dad dang 'dun pa'i chu lud mtshams sbyar ba/ /'dren pa'i byin rlabs char gyis smin pa'i mthus/ /dpag bsam ljon pa'i lo 'dab gsar du 'khrungs/ /rten 'brel zab mo'i gser
skud thag pa yis/ /tshe rabs kun tu 'bral med dam du bcings/ /gar bzhugs chos dbyings dag pa'i zhing khams su/ /zab don chos kyi bdud rtsis

ngoms par shog /gnas skabs lo 'dab gsar 'khrungs rten 'brel 'dis/ /tshe dang bsod nams 'khor 'bangs dpal 'byor 'phel/ /bla ma lhar bcas dkar phyogs srung ma yis/ /'bral med
bsrung skyob dar ba'i bkra shis shog /ces sbyar ba yin no/ /de nas gzims chung de'i ming la lam zab phug ces grags/ steng ma mi dbang dgra 'dul don grub kyi gzims chung
yin la de'i ming ni rigs gnas yang rtse zhes grags/ kho bo cag gis ni dga' ldan gyi lha bu dam pa tog dkar gyi gzims khang la rgyal mtshan mthon po zhes btags 'dug /de'i
rigs 'gres ding sang phyogs kun na rgyal mtshan mthon po'i ming btags pa mang po 'dug de bas na rig gnas yang rtse mdzes pa'i rgyal mtshan snyan pa'i ba dan kun tu g.yo ba
zhes pa zhig kyang thob snyam mo/ /de gsum ga la shing rtsi skyang nul sogs 'chi med kyi skyed tshal la 'gran bzod pa yod/ dbyar dus rtsi shing me tog 'bar ba la/ /khrel
bzhin dgun dus grang reg gos gyon pa'i/ /lo 'dab gsar 'khrungs sngo ljang bu mo'i 'dzum/ /shor ba'i mod la sos ka'i dpal rnams bzhad/ /chos bzhin sa skyong dgyes pa'i 'od
'bum dang / /lhan cig 'gro la phan bde'i nyin byed shar/ /rgyu 'bras dus mnyam 'di 'dra ngo mtshar nas/ /dga' ba'i bro 'khrab glu dbyangs de nas dar/ dpe'i rab brtags
rgyu rgyan/ mi dbang chen po'i bsod nams mthu yin zhes/ /lha rnams smras

kyang rmongs pas ma go nas/ /dus min 'dab gsar sngo ljang ban bun gyi/ /brda 'di nam mkha'i dbyings nas smra dang mtshungs phra mo rgyan no/ /brgya phyin pho brang spo la gdan
chags pa'i/ /mi dbang lhun po'i zil dngar 'di mthong tshe/ /'chi med lha dbang gnas 'dir bzhugs so snyam/ /nye dbang 'khor rnams sa 'dir lhag par nges rab rtags gsal
byed/ /mdo rgyud man ngag snying po bsdus pa'i chos/ / lam zab skyong ba rdo rje snying por mtshungs/ /snyan grags pad mtshor ngang mo 'du ba bzhin/ /lam zab phug gis rdzing
bur bskrad kyang 'khor rang bzhin rgyan/ /phyi nang rig gnas sgrog pa'i skyed mos tshal/ /dbyangs can dri za'i rgyud mangs kyis bos bzhin/ /rig gnas yang rtser mkhas
pa'i legs bshad gtam/ /rgyun mi 'chad la ngo mtshar su mi byed/ rab brtags rgyan/ /dbus gtsang phyogs 'dir rnam par rgyal ba'i srid/ /dpa' bo stag ltar rngam pas rtsa zhing
rgod/ /khu dbon yab yum sras 'bangs 'khor dang bcas/ /rdo rje'i tshe brtan chab srid dar rgyas shog /shis brjod rgyan/ /sa 'dzin yangs pa'i skyed tshal gzhan spangs nas/
/phyogs 'di'i utpal rdzing bur mig gtad pa/ /dad ldan sbyin po'i snying stobs dri bsung la/ /chags pa'i spu long ci yang g.yo bar gyur/ rnam pa'i phra mo'i rgyan/ e ma
phyogs 'di'i skyed tshal la/ /dga' bas mig gi bdud rtsi 'dzag /gangs kyi ri sul la reg pa'i/ /ma la ya klung 'dir 'ongs sam/ cha'i rgyan no/ /de nas sprul lo dbyar chos
la phyin

phyi nang gra skor ba yang shin tu mang / chos rigs lung sgrigs rnam gzhag sa gtsang dus bde sa 'jam sogs phun sum tshogs/ khyad par chu lho byang gi sgrub mchod chen po'i
thad du bsnyen bkur dar 'gyed nas 'gyed sogs dus gsum khebs zhes snyan par grags/ bla brang rang nas kyang gong dkar sgrub mchod kyi thad du mang ja nas 'bo/ che bgres slob
dpon las 'dzin phyi'i gra skor ba dang bcas pa la bkra shis kha btags kyi 'gyed dang bcas pa bsgrubs chu lho byang sgrub mchod chen po 'di/ byang khri skor sgrub mchod
yin zhes grags/ /de ming bas lhag tsam don la khel/ /phyogs kun tu mdzes ma'i rna rgyan 'chang / de nas gong dkar dpon slob rnams bka' bgros/ chos sde'i sgrub mchod ni dpyod
ldan gyi thugs la gsal ba bzhin 'bad pas bsgrubs/ da lhag cung zad byung ba 'di log 'tshor ma song tsam dgos pa 'dug pas/ da lo dbyar ston 'di gsung ngag 'chad pa la
phebs dgos de'i cha rkyen du 'bul gsung pa byung bas/ kho bo rang gis kyang sngar lam 'bras mang du bshad kyang chu byang phyogs 'dir cher ma song ba dang / khyad par byang
phyogs 'di shes ldan gzur gnas don gnyer can shin tu mang ba dang / skyon yon gyi rtog dpyod kyang shin tu chug pa zhig 'dug bsam/ sems spro ba dang bcas pas khas blangs
de ga'i lugs byas na'ang / 'dar nas zhal ngo / dmangs skya btsun kun rang la thugs dad rtse gcig pa yin pa dang / khyad par sa skyong chos skyong lhun grub da lo rtog
bcas shin tu

che ba yod pa dang / yang sgos lo sri thu mo yod pas dbang bka' yang yang dgos pa 'dug lags pas/ gsung chos nyan 'dod yod pa rnams 'dir 'bod pa gnang de rnams la gnas khang
gur bcas shing bu chas mthun rkyen 'di rang nas bsgrubs pas gsung chos 'chad sa nor bu gling rang du gnang dgos gsung nan chags pa dang / bde gling nas kyang de bzhin gsungs
byung ba nas sbyin bdag stobs ldan gyi dad pa sun dbyung yang ma bde/ khong dge 'dun gyi bka' yang bcag tu med pas byed dka' se byung yang / dge 'dun la gsed bkrol byas
khyed rang don du gnyer ba dang / long skabs yod pa rnams tshur byon pa legs tshul phul bas/ khong rnams thugs 'pham me ba la bde grol byas/ nor bu gling du lam 'bras
btsugs grang chen pa dang / phu thub bstan dge 'phel ba/ phyogs nas bya rgod gshongs/ ya ga chos sdings/ stod mnga' ris/ dgun lhas sku skye dpon slob/ rma bya shug khrod
pa/ chos rje 'jam dpal dga' ba'i bshes gnyen sogs cha lung pa du ma ste de sogs phyogs kun nas 'dus pa'i lam 'bras pa brgya zin tsam byung / snang gsum gyi 'khrid/ brgyud
pa gnyis ldan gyi sems bskyed/ slob ma rjes 'dzin/ bsnyen pa kha gso/ yab kyi smin byed 'khor 'das dbyer med lta 'khrid/ rgyu dbang lam byed yum gyi dbang bka'/ phyi bskyed
rim 'khrid/ lam dus dbang nang bskyed rim/ yum gyi byin rlabs brgyud pa ma nyams pa/ khyab byed rlung dang khyab bya gtum mo ste 'dus pa dang po'i 'khrid/ pho nya'i
lam ste

'dus pa bar pa'i 'khrid/ rdo rje rba rlabs te 'dus pa tha ma'i 'khrid/ ring brgyud kyi 'khrid phal mo che rdzogs nas 'dul lags kyang phebs sngar ma gsan ba'i nye brgyud lam
sbas bshad kyi byin rlabs dang 'khrid/ phra mo brgyad dang grub chen bcu pho brang sbas bshad sogs dang / lam 'bras shin tu nye brgyud brda don gsal ba'i byin rlabs/ dmigs
pa rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi 'khrid/ zhar byung gi 'khrid bzhi sogs dang / de dag gi skabs su lam zab phyi nang gsang gsum/ tshar gsum khug pa bla ma rin 'byung / bir
srung rnam gnyis rnam 'joms bir lugs/ gA ya'i mgon rkyang / brda chig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ lung sbyin nas gsang ba bcu'i rgyas btab/ 'khrid kyi skabs su dbang bzhi
dang 'brel ba'i bskyed rim sogs kyi 'khrid bzhi/ lam bzhi dang 'brel ba'i nyams bzhi la phyag chen ngo sprad nas skyong ba'i 'khrid bzhi/ de spyod pas bogs dbyung ba'i
'khrid bzhi/ de bogs dbyung ba las grub mtha' bzhi snyogs tshul/ grub mtha' ma snyogs na dbang bzhi dang sbrel ba'i 'da' ka ma 'pho ba'i 'khrid bzhi 'pho ba ma thebs na
dbang bzhi dang 'brel ba'i bar do sbyong byed kyi 'khrid bzhi/ lam gyi tshod 'dzin rmi lam dang sgyu lus kyi 'khrid bzhi/ de ltar byas pas 'gros bzhi thim nas sku bzhi mngon
du byed pa'i tshul rnams kho bo cag gi lam 'bras 'di la bzhugs pas tshang 'grig byed pa 'di'i lugs yin pas skal bzang yid tshim par gyis la snying dbus padmar gces par

mdzod cig /de'i tshe gsung ngag pa rnams la mang ja/ bsnyen bkur bsam gyis mi khyab/ khyad par zhabs drung chen mos mang ja/ phyogs pa rnams la phogs zhib khal phyed gsum ma/
lnga dbar sha khog pa re/ khye 'dren lags kyi tshogs pa la mang ja nyis sbrel/ nas 'bo 'gyed gnyis/ zhabs drung sku mched kyi tshogs pa la mang ja nas 'bo bzhi 'bo/ yum
drung gis mang ja glum dkar 'khur ston dang bcas pa phyogs pa rnams la 'jam tsha bre re/ dpon sa dbang ldan lags/ chos lags rnam gnyis kyis mang ja re/ bde gling nas mang
ja gsum/ nas 'bo/ zhib 'bo/ go ra/ legs/ 'khur 'gyed sogs/ skyid gshongs pas mang ja/ ru spe nas mang ja/ rmu bas mang ja/ zhib 'bo/ khab gong pas zhib 'bo/ chos 'dzad
mar mes mang ja/ mnga' ris rje drung gis mang ja/ mnga' ris slob dpon pa'i mang ja/ chos rje byams chos pas mang ja/ dgun lhas sku skye bas mang ja/ gdan non/ bla brang
nas mang ja gsum/ phu bgres pas mang ja/ grang chen bgres pas mang ja zung sbrel/ tshogs 'khor shin tu bzang ba/ rdo rje'i glu dang gar la sogs pa lha mchod pa dang mi rnams
dga' ba bskyed pa'i spros pa sna tshogs pa yang byas/ gnas slob bshad nor bu'i gling mchog 'dir/ khong dad ldan sbyin bdag phul du phyin/ /chos rgyud dang man ngag bstan
pa dar/ /phyogs dge zhing shes pa'i ngo mtshar spel/ /sbrul lo sangs rgyas kyi 'phel gdung mthe bong tsam zhig yum byang sems a mdzes drung gis

phyag na yod pa de la/ mi dbang lhun chen drung gis zhal bkod mdzad nas gser zangs las grub pa'i dri'i gtsang khang rnam rgyal mchod rten bzo rigs mkhas pa khang gsar bkra
shis pas khri gdan bang rim gsum gser zangs las grub pa/ de'i steng du seng khri grub bzhi lcags bskos gser tshags ma/ shar gyi dbus na rdo rje/ g.yas g.yon gnyis na dpal
be dang 'khor lo/ lho'i dbus na rdo rje/ g.yas g.yon gnyis na padma dang rgyal mtshan nub kyi dbus na rdo rje/ g.yas g.yon gnyis na gdugs dang bum pa/ byang gi dbus na rdo
rje/ g.yas g.yon gnyis na gser nya dang dung dkar/ de thams cad gser tshags bzabs brkos seng khri'i kha khyer la mi mchog rgyal ba gang dag sogs rkang pa bzhi dang / sgrol
dkar gyi sngags legs sbyar gyi skad lanytsha'i gzugs su bkod pa/ de'i steng du gser zangs las grub pa'i pad gdan 'khor lo/ de'i steng du bang rim gsum gser zangs las
grub pa/ bum pa zlum po'i smad dngul ljang brdung / stod shel/ sgrigs mtshams gser ljang brdungs kyi 'bu sgril dang bcas pa/ de'i nang du ring bsrel gyi gong bu phyi gsal
nang gsal du mthong ba/ sgo khyim gser g.yu las grub pa'i nang du kA ma rU pa'i rdo las grub pa'i ston pa gtso 'khor gsum bzhugs pa/ de'i phyogs bzhir gser tshags las grub
pa'i shar du bhrUM dang hUM/ lhor aM/ nub tu dzriM/ byang du khaM ste rigs lnga'i sa bon/ de'i steng du gdugs rim pa bcu gsum gser

tshags las grub pa pad gdan dang bcas pa/ de'i steng du char khebs 'gan jir tog dang bcas pa gser zangs las grub pa/ mu tig gi zar tshags dang ldan pa shin tu ngo mtshar ba
mthong bas yid 'phrog pa zhig bcos grub gnang 'dug pa de la rab gnas dgos gsung / chu mo sbrul gyi zla ba bdun pa'i nyer gsum gyi nyin me tog gtor bas rab gnas bzang po
drug pa gang rgyas byas/ de'i tshe nam mkha' nas me tog gi char yang 'bab kyin 'dug zer/ de'i steng du mi dbang lhun chen drung gi phyag 'bun gnang ba rnams la sngar nas
drug bde yod pa la bcag nas/ de la brten zhal ngo gzhan rnams dang / cha zhabs byin rnams kyis kyang drug bde chag 'bun len mi rnams la bsod nams kyi tshogs shin tu che ba
byung gzhan yang nor bu gling gtsug lag khang 'di bzhengs phyin chos gzhis dgos pa 'dug gsung / blo khud kyi zhing rnams kyang chos gzhis la phul/ de rnams la bsngo bas
rgyas 'debs dgos gsung thugs bsam rnam par dag pas dge rtsa stobs che ba de 'dra la rang gis bsngo ba ci shes dang / khyad par 'dar nas sbyin bdag chen po zhal ngo spyi
dang / bye brag ched du bstad pa'i gnas skabs kyi tshe 'di'i bzhed don 'grub pa dang / mthar thug sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa'i bsngo ba smon lam bkra shis rgyas 'debs
ci yang byas/ 'dar nas mi dbang chos bzhin sa skyong ba/ /dgos 'dod lhun grub bsod nams ye shes tshogs/ /yar ngo'i zla ltar lhun grub ches cher 'phel/ /bdud dpung dgra
'dul lhag bsam don kun grub/ /yum mchog a mdzes

mi dbang dpal 'byor mtshan/ /rdo rje ltar brtan dpal kun phyogs nas 'dzom/ /chab srid 'jam dar phun tshogs dpal du bsngo/ /lhag bsam rab dkar gangs ri'i dum 'khrigs las/ /legs
'khrungs bsod nams lhun po'i spo chen por/ /rab 'khyil mngon mtho dge legs chu gter che/ /lugs gnyis srid kyi lo tog smin par bsngo/ /'bru tshogs skyes kyis dbul 'phongs
sdug bsngal bsal/ /zhing bzang mchod pa'i 'bru tshogs phung por spungs/ /rgyal ba'i gdung la ngo mtshar khang brtsegs phul/ /bzhed don yid bzhin 'grub pa'i bkra shis
shog /rten bzang po la rab gnas bgyis nas yun ring ma lon par dad ldan gyi sbyin bdag bsod nams khye 'dren gyis bdag la sa paNDi ta'i yungs 'bru'i ring bsrel 'bul bar brtsams
pa na brtsams pa de las lhag tsam gsar du 'phel ba dang bcas pa phul bas/ rang sa skya paN chen la sngon gyi las 'phro sad pa lta bu'i dad 'dun dngos dang rmi lam du
yod pa nas dga' zhing spro ba sa rab dga' thob pa lta bur gyur/ slob bshad nor bu gling nas chos nyan pa rnams kyis dar gdugs sgra rol mo dang bcas pas ser sbreng gis bsu
ba legs par byas nas gnas su bzhugs su gsol/ dad 'dun bsod nams bsags pa'i sbyin po yi/ /tshe rabs kun tu bogs dang khye 'dren pa'i/ /rgyal ba'i ring bsrel las lhag phul
ba 'di/ /dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa'i ched du bsngo/ /rang nyid la bsrung skyob byed pa'i 'dun pa cher med kyang pha rol po nas bsam pa dag pa nas blo gtad na nus cung
zad yong gin yod par snang ste/ rang gi tsha bo

ngos ma bzhis gtso byas dpon g.yog sum cu tsam gyis byang thang mi med la gser la phyin pa'i tshe/ tsha bo lha mo dbang ldan zer ba zhig gi mtshan gyi rmi lam du a khu chos
rje'i bang chen btang ba yin zer ba zhig gis 'phrad dgos zer phrad pas nged kyi yi ge yin zer yi ge rten bcas mang po sprad byung / khyad par tsha bo btsan lha dar po'i
sog po thul ba'i dkar chol yin no zer gser zho gang sbyin pa sogs rmi lam mang po rmis/ snga dro nam langs nas gser las la phyin tshur 'gugs 'phral rgyang ring po nas rta
pa 'dra mthong rkun gser ba yin pa 'dug rdung du 'gro zer phyin pas/ rta pa zhig gi zhwa mo sa la lhung song ba mgo reg tu mthong nas da rkun gser ba min pa 'dug zer log
pas/ ra lug 'tsho ba'i bu tsha gnyis yod pa la bstad nas byung ba bu tsha gnyis kyis bros pa la gcig 'gyel ba la rta kha nas go snyob byas bzung nas rta 'gab tu skyon song
/ de nas sog po yin par shes nas khong rnams kyis sgrigs byas da bud med dang bu tsha lang long rnams kyang ma bskyur/ gur dang chas phal cher bzhag /sog po ri bzung ba
la bstad nas tsha bo lha mo dbang ldan mdang nga la rmi lam bzang po byung ci yang skyon mi yong zer ri la 'dzigs pas sog po rnams yar ri rtse la bros/ de nas sa sros mtshams
mtshan bcod byas bros pas skyon med du thar ba sogs legs tshogs che ba rang byung / de nas nang par tsha bo gnyis g.yog gcig dang gsum gyis snga ma'i bsdad shul bskor
ba la yongs pas tsha bo lha mo dpal gyi rta nyal nas 'gro ma 'dod/ bslang bas lang ma 'dod/ rta de na ba yin 'dug zer log yongs pas na ba med par thad bzhin 'gro zer
de

nas phar phyin na sog po dang thug nas skyon chen po yong ba'i snga ltas yin par 'dug zer/ de nas khong rnams kyis kre ba'i ru ba la bsnyegs nas yongs pas sog pos khong gi
sngon la kre ba'i ru ba la rgyugs 'dug pa dang yang cung zad thug sog pos mda' tshur zhus pa rogs shig gi rkang pa la phog /rang gi tsha bos phar mda' rgyab pa de kho la
'phog la khad byung ba khos bar snang nas bzung song zer/ de nas phan tshun glags ma rnyed/ de nas rang phyogs rnams kyis tshur yongs la zhig gi phag na snga sor chu mig
cig yod pa der tsha ba la sdod grags byas pas chu bskams nas med par sdod thabs ma byung / de nas yongs pas la zhig gi pha na sngar chu med kyang chu gsar pa zhig rdol 'dug
pas der bsdad zer/ sngar gyi chu yod sa der bsdad na sog po dang thug pa'i skyon chen po yong ba 'dug cing / chu med par chu byung de yang dkon cog gi thugs rje rang du
byung zhing / de rnams kyang nged rang gi chos srung gis bskyabs pa kho nar 'dug zer ro/ /pha bla ma'i byin rlabs snying la zhugs/ /bka' bstan bcos zab don sems la 'phos/
/khong chos srung rnams brtse skyob 'bral ba med/ /bdud sog po'i 'tshe ba skyabs la ltos/ /chu sbrul gyi dgun chos steng du phyin gra skor ba karma pa'i sngags kyi gra
skor ba gnyis dang sgra rams pa gcig the bas zhe lnga tsam byung / gra skor ba mangs pas bshad pa mang po byed skabs mi 'dug kyang nyung na mig ltos la gnod dogs tshad ma'i
snga ldang ba rnams la khor gsum gsum phar phyin pa la gnyis gnyis/ 'dul ba la yang gnyis gnyis/ pod phran la re re sbyor bkod tshun tshogs chen

rang du grub pa byas/ sngags rams pa rnams la bshad pa thun gnyis gnyis/ 'bum rams pa sogs la bshad khor re/ che bgres pa rnams la gzhung zhu re tshogs lang tho re ba ma gtogs
thams cad la byed skabs ma byung / gra skor ba khams pa 'ba' ro zer ba des tshogs su mang ja gsum/ che bgres slob dpon gra skor ba sogs la dar 'gyed gnyis byas bshad
pa yang dga' mo yod pa zhig 'dug /gzhan 'bras yul ba/ gzha' ri ba/ thub bstan pa ngag dbang sogs kyis yang bshad pa legs par yong gin 'dug /dpon sa lha gcig phun tshogs rgyal
mos mang ja brgyad/ che bgres slob dpon gra skor ba sogs dar 'gyed bzang po dang nas khal gnyis ma/ bsngo rten shin tu bzang ba dang bcas pa/ gdan sa chen po nas mang
ja bsngo rten dang bcas pa/ sde pa gtsang pas mang ja zung / spyi 'bul bsngo rten bdun tshan bzang po/ rtse chen nas ma dang lha sras drung gis mang ja re re/ shangs dgra
'dul nas mang ja sogs bsnyen bkur stobs che bar byung / de skabs su nub dgon pa dgu/ rjes su skyar skya pa'i bla ma gcig dang bcas pa bcus bsnyen rdzogs sa paN nas brgyud
pa'i sdom rgyun gtsang ma yin/ lhun grub spel nas dus rgyun du bzhes spro gsol ja bda' ba dang bcas pa gnang / mgon po'i bskang bshags rtsom dgos gsung yang yang bskul/
gur zhal phyag drug pa/ legs ldan phyag bzhi pa/ dur khrod bdag po/ las gshin/ dmag zor/ rnam sras/ beg tse/ tshe ring mched lnga sogs la bskang bshags mchod sprin sogs
rgyas par brtsams/ de'i lung phul rjes gnang dgos gsung de snga ma grub rjes su 'bul

pa byas/ chu mo sbrul gyi dgun chos 'dus tshogs la/ /mchod sbyin bsnyen cing bkur ba bsam mi khyab/ /legs bshad skyes 'bul phyogs kyi grwa skor bas/ /bstan la phan pa'i bshad
pa'i rgyud mang sgrogs/ /dgun chos steng du sde pa rong pas 'bras yul rab 'byams pa zhig dang / rtse chen nas dpon sa skye rgod pas rang dang rtse chen sogs su dbyar chos
la 'khor tsam byas pas chog yong dgos gsung ba byung kyang rtsol ba ma byas/ de nas dgun chos grol mtshams rang gnas su sleb/ 'dar nas zhabs drung chen mo la sku dog
shin tu che bas tshe dbang brgya tshar re zla re la dgos gsung / lhun chen drung la yang sku dog che bas rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg dang / tshe bka' dgos gsung phu chu tshan 'khor
rtser phyin rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg dang khu dbon gnyis la tshe bka' brgya tshar byas/ 'dar nas 'dir sleb/ shing pho rta lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad la gtor sgrub
btsugs tshes dgu'i nub rmi lam du dur khrod bdag po yab yum yin zer ba'i a tsa ra gnyis gshibs nas bzhugs na bza' nang ma gnyis pus gong du brdzes pa 'dra ba/ phyi nas
na bza' dkar po gsar pa skya 'jol leb bsnams pa gnyis mthong bas sems dga' ba dang spro ba shin tu che ba byung / de'i 'khris na kham bu'i sdong po chen po nam mkha' la zeng
nge ba zhig 'dug pa la de lag g.yas nas bskor lho nub phyogs kyis yal ga nas 'di na smin par yod zer btogs kyin zos pa rmis so/ /mtshan rmi lam yin yang mngon sum bzhin/
/lha dur khrod bdag po yab yum mjal/ /'bru bzang po smin pa'i ro

mchog myong / /sems rab dga' lus kyi spu long g.yo/ /de nas nor bu gling du 'dar nas mi dbang dgra 'dul don grub dang / chos rje byams chos pa 'jam dpal dgyes pa'i bshes gnyen/
ya ga chos sdings pa chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan grang chen nas ra ngag dbang / nub dgon nas khong gsum sogs ched bstad yong / rgyud bshad dgos gsung rang gi blo
'dod gur sam gang rung la zin thun bshad pa zhig byed bsam pa yod kyang khong rnams kyis sku nas stabs yang yang yong ba lkog pas rgyud gsum char la da lan ka gnang thub
pa zhig byung na legs tshogs che ba 'dug zer/ khong rnams kyis kye rdor man ngag lugs gur rigs bsdus kyi dbang rnams rang gis sngar du byas zin pa mang ba 'dug pas/ rdor
dbyings lha sum cu so bdun gyi dbang zla ba de ga'i tshes bcu gnyis la sta gon/ bcu gsum la dngos gzhi/ tshes bco brgyad la rgyud bshad kyi 'go btsugs/ mi dbang dgra 'dul
don grub kyis mang ja nyis sbrel dang tshogs 'khor bzang po mdzad/ rtsa rgyud 'phags pa'i bsdus don dang sa gzhung sbyar ba'i bshad pa/ gur la rje btsun gyi bsdus don dang
sa gzhung sbyar ba'i bshad pa/ sambu Ta la 'phags pa'i bsdus don dang sa gzhung sbyar ba'i bshad pa rnams tshang 'grig sngon du 'gro bar byas nas/ sambu Ta la 'phags pa'i
bsdus don sa bcad gzhir bzhag /'bru non rnams sa paNDi ta'i mtshan ma gtso bor byas/ de'i cung ma thus pa rnams rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pas TIka chen rin chen 'bar
ba dang / rje btsun grags pa'i slob ma dbang phyug dpal

gyi TIkka las kyang cung zad gsal bar byas te zin thun btang / zin thun byed mkhan mi dbang dgra 'dul drung dang / chos rje byams chos pa gnyis kyis gcig /chos rje kun rgyal
bas gcig /drung rams pa ngag dbang gis gcig /grang chen dka' bcu pa rgyan rin gyis gcig /nub dgon pa rnams kyis gcig rnams byung / sambu Ta'i rtsa rgyud la brtag pa bcu/
brtag pa re re la rab byed bzhi bzhi yod pa'i brtag pa dang po'i rab byed bzhi la zin thun legs par grub/ mi dbang dgra 'dul dang chos rje byams chos pa'i zin thun la shog
bu gdong bton brgyad cu gya brgyad byung 'dug cing / gzhan rnams la yang kha dras kyi stabs kyis bdun cu skor re byung 'dug /de dag gi skabs su rmi lam la rtsa ba'i bla
ma gsum sogs bla ma rnams ther chags kyis yong ba zhig 'dug /nub cig stong nyid bcu drug gi grangs sgrong gin 'dug pa la/ phyi stong pa nyid sogs 'go nas kha cig chad
stong du 'dug snyam/ de man chad stong pa nyid mtshan nyid pa yin pa 'dug /zung 'jug rang du 'dug snyam pa zhig shar/ de dag gi skabs su rje bla ma kun dga' mchog ldan thugs
