mnyes pas mang ja/ rang nyid la gnang sbyin bzang po/ sa skyong mi dbang chos skyong lhun grub kyis mang ja zung / tshogs 'khor bzang po/ sde pa lhun chen lags kyis mang
ja nas 'bo/ byang sems yum gyis mang ja glum dkar/ go ra/ bur ston dang bcas pa/ dpon sa rdo rje dpal 'dzom gyi mang ja/ bsod nams khye 'dren gyis mang ja bzhi/ byams
pa lags kyis mang ja/ chos bzang lags

kyis mang ja/ mi dbang dgra 'dul lags kyis chos nyan pa rnams la slar yang mang ja/ phogs khal phyed gnyis ma/ bde gling nas mang ja zhib 'bo rgyar bcas/ slar yang mang ja/
yang mang ja zhig 'bo rgyar bcas/ ru spes 'khur ba/ glum dkar/ mang ja/ skyid gshongs pas mang ja/ rmu pas mang ja/ nub dgon pa rnams kyis mang ja/ grang chen nas mang ja/
phu bgres pas mang ja/ ka spe bas mang ja/ grol ston la sde pa ma gnyer khang nas mang ja/ tshogs 'khor bzabs pa sogs legs tshogs cher bar byung / rgyud kyi glegs bu chu
shel mdangs/ /tshig 'bru'i me tog tshom bu bkra/ /blo gsal mkhas pa'i rgyan 'phreng mdzes/ /shes ldan su zhig yid mi tshim/ /shes ldan sems kyi tsha gdung bsil yang skal
med phrag dog gdung bas smyo/ /dad ldan mchod pa'i me tog 'thor yang skal med ser sna'i mdud pa dam/ /gzur gnas rna ba'i rgyan du mdzes kyang skal dman rna ba'i bug pa
'gags/ /nag phyogs yi mug rgyal mtshan bsnyal yang dkar phyogs legs so'i rgyud mangs brel/ /rgyud bzang lha lam yangs pa la/ /legs bshad sprin gyi sngo sangs 'thibs/ /sbyin
po'i mchod rdzas char rgyun phabs/ /rgyal bstan lo tog smin 'di mtshar/ /lo de'i rgyud grol 'tshams de la mi dbang lhun chen drung gis phyag rtags rten bcas gnang / zha
lu sku zhang pa 'dir phebs/ der gsung chos shig zhu 'dod 'dug pas/ khong rang 'dod pa'i gsung chos gnang dgos gsungs byung / de ga bzhin sku zhang rang gi thugs 'dod rab
zha lu ba'i lugs kyis 'khrid chen bzhi

de min gshed dmar spros med zhu 'dod 'dug pa ltar 'khrid chen bzhi'i dbang rnams mi grub pa 'dug pas/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang byas/ spros med rgyun gyi byin rlabs te dbang
dang byin rlabs rnam bzhi rdzogs pa byas/ spros med 'khrid kyi rim pa rnams kyang cha tshang rdzogs par grub pa yin/ yul zha lu sku zhang chos rje la/ /'khrid zab mo
shin tu spros med lam/ /dbang byin rlabs 'khrid rim ma tshang med/ /dus myur bar phul 'di dge zhing shis/ mi zad pa zhes pa me pho khyi'i lo zla ba drug pa'i nyer gnyis la
bya gshongs nas lha dbang rtse'i chu tshan la phyin pa'i tshe/ chu tshan gyi 'og gzhi bye ma 'bol le 'dug pas bye ma la gre mo btsugs chu tshan dug pas de'i rkyen byas
gre mo la chu bur cig byung / zhag 'ga' nas de la ngas kyi rnam pas zug gzer cung zad skyes/ chu tshan gyi 'gram na brag dang gad pa dmar sra le ba 'dug pa de gnyan po rang
yin zer ba nas cung zad rnam rtog skyes mtshan mo nyal ba'i tshe de la gtad pa'i dmigs pa dang / sngags bzlas mang du byas pas mtshan phyed tsam nas rmi lam du kha nas
sbrul gcig 'thon grabs byed kyin 'dug /lag gis 'then pas phyed tsam nas sbad de chad song gnyid sad de ma legs sam/ de la dmigs pa gtad yang nyal bas rmi lam du sngar gyi
sbrul gyi 'phro de kha nas 'thon grabs 'dug pas yang chad nas 'phro ma cung zad lus/ gnyid sad da dung ma legs sam dmigs

pa shugs drag tu gtad nas nyal bas sngar gyi sbrul gyi 'phro de kha nas 'thon grabs 'dug pas de 'then pas sbrul gyi rnga ma phra sang nge ba de rdzogs par thon song blo bde
tsam byung / sngar gyi zug gzer de yang chag nas mi 'dug de'i rten 'brel gyi sngar nas yod pa'i sha bu 'bar 'bur de gtan nas ma byung / klu bdud btsan gyi gnod par gzas
pa'i tshe/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i sngags bzlas me 'od kyis/ /sprul gdug lan gsum bcad nas phyi la bsgyur/ /klu bdud gdon las grol snyam rab dga' skyes/ /de gong rtse chen du
chos rje bstan pa la mgon pod me 'bar ma'i lung dgos gsung rgyal rtse nas dpe g.yar nas lung byas/ de rjes 'dar du chos rje dkon cog legs 'dzin sogs la me 'bar ma'i lung
dgos zer lung byas/ rang khams nyog ge yod pa de yang bde sang song / yang bya gshongs su phu gsum nas grwa pa chos rje kun bzang pa sogs sum cu skor la chos dgos zer kye
rdor gyi rgyu dbang / gur zhal rnam sras sogs kyi rjes gnang byas/ yang chos rje nam mkha' chos rje gtsang tshul/ chos rje tshe ring pa rnams la dmar po skor gsum la rjes
gnang gi rnam grangs bco lnga tsam dang / rje tshar chen gyis dkar chag nang bzhin gyis po ti gsum gyi lung rnams shin tu zhib par byas/ 'brug pa'i dbu che spo sa skya'i
gdan sa chos rje chos 'phel ba bsnyen rdzogs la byon nas bsnyen rdzogs byas/ ma gcig ni gu 'khrid lung mang du byas/ yang bya gshongs su mkhar las kyi ring la chos rje
bstan pas gsol ba btab/ chos rje bstan pa/ nyang stod pa

sngags 'chang / bla chen sogs sum brgya skor la lam 'bras yongs rdzogs/ gsol phu nas chos lags la rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang 'khrid sogs mang du byas/ bya gshongs su chos
rje snye mo ba sngar chos zhu rtsis mi 'dug kyang / tshes bcu'i nub cig mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis DA ma ru'i sgra 'khrol ba dang bcas ni gu la sogs pa'i chos rnams bla
ma gser pa la zhus zer ba'i lung bstan rmi lam du byung ba la brten chos zhu ba la byon dad ldan mang po la bshed dmar spros med yongs rdzogs/ dmar po skor gsum sogs byas/
ni gu dgos zer na'ang byed skabs ma byung / bya gshongs nas chu mo lug lo re gcig pa la/ 'tshed bla brang du bstan 'dzin nyi zla bzang po'i zhabs drung du/ rje btsun thams
cad mkhyen pa'i 'khrid brgya de la dgos pa'i cha lag dang bcas pa/ grub thob nye brgyud kyi tshe bka'/ dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang yig lung dang bcas pa/ 'phags pa
brgyad stong pa'i lung rje grub chen gyis snar thang du gnas brtan ba ku la dang / yan lag 'byung la gsan pa de'i lung / seng gdong can gyi rjes gnang / bram nag bshan
pa drug skor gyi rjes gnang rnams zhus/ yang bya gshongs su nub cig rmi lam du rje mkhan blo gros rnam rgyal khri mthon po la bzhugs pa zhig gis tshe dmag zor ma'i rjes gnang
zhus/ sbyor dngos rjes gsum gyi rjes gnang rdzogs/ mchod g.yog pa'i dkyil 'khor bsdu ba'i tshe/ dkyil 'khor de ji lta bu zhig yod lta dgos pa

'dug snyam ston dang byas pas/ dkyil 'khor 'di na yod zer ras 'dul la dkyil 'khor bris pa mang po 'dug pa'i gseb nas bton nas bstan byung ba bltas pas/ chos 'byung gru gsum
pa'i nyis brtsegs zur g.yas g.yon re re na zur phran de yod pa mtha' me ris kyis bskor ba zhig bstan byung / de'i tshe rang ja zhig 'thung gin 'dug pas lag pa g.yon na dkar
yol/ g.yas na dmag zor ma'i sku zhal gdong gsum brtsegs byas pa zhig 'dug /zhal gdong gsum po ci yin snyam tsa na/ 'og ma dmag zor/ bar ma dbyangs can/ steng ma rigs
bdag gshin rje gshed kyis yin zer ro/ /mtshan dus 'od gsal ngang du bla ma rjer/ /sngon med dmag zor lha mo'i rjes gnang zhus/ /dkyil 'khor sku brnyan ngo mtshar ltad mo
mthong / /byin rlabs snying la zhugs snyam dga' ba skyes/ /bya rgod gshongs su bsnyen rdzogs pa chos rje 'ga' rong pa/ /chos rje 'bum pa sher blo ba/ chos rje cha lung pa/
chos rje rkyang 'dur byams pa/ chos rje grags pa/ chos rje gtsang tshul/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs pa/ chos rje bo dong grags byang pa/ chos rje 'brug pa spos skya pa/ chos
rje nam mkha' pa/ chos rje bo dong ring mo/ chos rje las chen mngon dga' shar pa/ chos rje bstan pa dar rgyas/ chos rje nyi ma bkra shis/ chos rje nyang stod nyi ma ba/
chos rje nyang stod 'jam dbyangs pa/ chos rje sngags 'chang pa/ chos rje bsam gtan pa/ chos rje rtse chen grags pa/ chos rje hor rgyal mtshan pa/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal
mtshan pa/ chos rje'i 'od zer lhun grub pa/ chos rje zur chen dge rgyam pa/

chos rje 'dzim chen bsod nams grags pa rnams des snga bla ma'i gong 'phang thob pa rnams dang / gzhan yang grwa shar mang po bsnyen par rdzogs pas mkhan po bgyid pa/ sa skya
paN chen gyis sdom rgyun dri ma med pa yin de rjes dpa' ldan brang mo che ru/ dge slong chos dbang legs pa/ dge slong dkon cog rgyal mtshan/ dge slong legs bshad/ dge slong
rje btsun/ dge slong shAka seng sogs bcu phrag yod pa rnams gzhi ba/ ya ga chos sdings nas dge slong btsun grags/ dge slong klu dbang / dge slong mchog grub sogs mang
po dang / phu nas dge slong bzod pa sogs dge slong mang po'i mkhan po bgyid pa rnams sa paN nas brgyud pa'i sdom rgyun gtsang ma yin/ nub dgon nas chos rje nags dgon pa
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan grang mo che ru ched bstad byon/ sngar mdo phyogs kyi slob ma kho na yin pa'i zhen gyi bsnyen rdzogs zhu 'dod zer bsnyen rdzogs byas/ snga phyir
gser srang gang lhag tsam sogs 'bul ba yang bsam gyi mi khyab pa byas bstan la yongs su rdzogs pa'i ngur smrig sde/ /bgrang bar mi bzod mkhan po'i cho ga bgyis/ /'di tsam
gyis kyang sa skya paNDi ta'i/ /tshul khrims dri yis phyogs kun khyab gyur cig /bya rgod gshongs su 'chad nyan lo skor byas pas/ rab 'byams smra ba gsar 'phel drug cu lhag
byung 'dug zer/ dka' bcu yan chad gsar 'phel bgrangs pas brgya phrag lhag tsam thon/ ya ga chos sdings dang chos gling du yang 'chad nyan byas pas bka' bcu dang rab 'byams
smra ba sogs mang du byung / rgyan drug

mchog gi gzhung lugs bshad byas pas/ /bka' dang rab 'byams smra bas mgrin pa brgyan/ /blo gsal ngang mo bzhad pa'i 'phur lding gis/ /sa dang bar snang khyab 'di bla ma'i drin/
/rtse chen du byi lo phyin skabs/ chos rje gur pa de rang nyid la dbang rjes gnang mang du zhus pa'i slob ma yin kyang / khong gis dbus la byon sngar ma thob pa'i chos
mang po thob 'dug pas/ rang gi gsang ba'i bla ma bcol/ zhal gyi khyung zhal can/ tshe 'phel dkar po sogs thob yig nang bzhin mang du zhus/ khong sngags 'chang kun dga'i
mtshan can la/ /rang khengs dregs che 'dod ma yin kyang / /khong sbyin bdag ma dad 'gog pa'i phyir/ /snying dad pas gsang ba'i bla ma bcol/ /nor bu'i gling gi mkha' las
grub 'phral gyi tshe/ rin chen mkha' 'gro'i mtshan rtags dang ldan pa'i rje btsun ye shes drung 'dir phebs zhag gcig bzhugs/ sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang gsan/ de gang grang
chen bla brang du dpon sa smon 'gro ma dang gnyis byon pa'i tshe tshe bka' gsan/ de dus rang khams nyog ge ba zhig yod pa la thugs phral chen po gnang gin 'dug /stag lo
'dar rtse nas sbyin bdag mdzad sprul sku kun bzang rog sa ngor pa gcig gnyis kyis phyag chen rtsod spong par du bzhengs/ de rjes rim pa bzhin du phyag chen yang lan/ rgyud
man ngag gi brgyud 'debs/ klu grub kyi bstod pa/ rab gnas kyi rtsa ba/ bzang drug gi lag len/ bzang drug gi rten/ bzang po'i khyad chos/ klu sgrub stod 'grel sogs brgya
phrag lhag

pa par du brkos/ chos rje tshe ring drung gis jo mjal la byon pa'i tshe yang rin spungs zhabs drung nas khyed rje rin po che klu sgrub pa'i zhal slob mthil mar 'dug /stong
ye tshor mi nyams med tsho rje rin po che klu sgrub ba las 'brug nas sprul sku rin po che mkhas zer ba yod 'dug ste/ sprul sku rin po che'i gsung gis rje rin po che klu sgrub
pa'i gsung gi phyogs su yang mi sleb gsung ba dang / da snga zhu shog rim pas phul kyang phebs pa zhig ma byung / de phyogs kyang 'gro don che bar yod 'dug kyang / de
bas kyang 'di phyogs che ba zhig yong pas byon gsung pa nan chen phebs kyang / na tshod stabs kyis 'gro 'dug mangs pa mi dga' ba 'dug pas dgongs grol zhu zer ba byas/ yang
zha lu sku zhang drung gis 'jam dkar gyi rjes gnang zhig zhu gsungs nas chos nyan pa rnams la 'jam dkar gyi rjes gnang legs par byas/ lugs gnyis ldan gyis gzhu shing
sdong po la/ /tshul rnam dpyod kyi shes rab mchog tu gces/ /skyes sbyang dang yi dam lha'i sbyin pa'i/ /don 'jig med kyis spobs pa thob par shog /de ltar rang nyid chu mo
lug la btsas nas don gnyis pa shing pho rta lo yan gyi ji ltar bgyis pa'i lo rgyus rnams yi ger bkod pa la dgos pa cher mi 'dug kyang / rang la dad ldan gyi sbyin bdag chen
po 'dar nas sa skyong mi'i dbang po chos skyong lhun grub zhal ngo yab yum rtse 'dzom gyis/ 'dar rnam rgyal stag rtse'i gzims chung lam zab phug tu rkang 'thung rtse
mo'i btung ba gya nom pa 'bul rten dang bcas pa mdzad/ sngar khyed

kyis gsung rtsom mang po mdzad rung / nged kyis go ba dang phan pa cher mi 'dug /da nged la phan thogs nges shes pa khyed rang bla ma rnam gnyis kyi rnam thar/ khyad par khyed
rang gi rnam thar rgyas pa zhig dgos zhes nan gyis bskul ba la brten/ chu sbrul hor zla bdun pa nas rtsom pa'i mu la zhugs pas tshe yang bar skabs zhal ngo rnams kyis
gsol ja dang bcas gsol 'debs yang yang mdzad/ de mthun grang mo che nas grwa bgres rnams kyis kyang gsal btab/ cha tsam rdzogs pa'i tshe yang sku mched gnyis kyis gsol ja
dang bcas bskul lcag mdzad/ bsod nams khye 'dren drung gis gsol ja/ gser gyi maNDal gos chen yug dang bcas pa phul nas/ da 'di'i 'phro ma lus pa myur ba zhig rtsom dgos
zhes gsungs shing bskul/ khyad par sa skyong mi'i dbang po chos skyong lhun grub kyis gug gser zho gang phul nas 'di la bcu chab mdzad dam gang mdzad kyang yongs su rdzogs
pa zhig dgos gsung bskul ba nas/ shing pho rta lo zla ba lnga pa'i dkar phyogs kyi tshes brgyad la slob bshad nor bu gling gi skyed tshal yangs par rdzogs par grub pa
dge zhing bkra shis/ sprul sku snang rtse bas khyung tshang brag nas spyan drangs pa'i lung bstan las/ da lta'i lcog ro klu yi rgyal mtshan 'di ma 'ongs pa sa zhes bya bar
rnal 'byor pa bsod nams rtse mo bya bar skye/ de nas bde ba can sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyong / de nas lnga brgya tham ma'i dus der dge slong klu sgrub bya ba stod
du lam 'bras spel/ de 'brel tshad don dang

ldan pa yin pas de la kun gyis 'dud cing mtha' dmag mi 'byung ba'i smon lam gdab tu 'jug dgos/ des phan che'o zer ba yang 'dug /'chi 'pho skye ba dngos su gzigs pa yi/ /spyan
mig gsal ba padmA ka ra yis/ /ma 'ongs lung bstan bsam gyis mi khyab par/ /log lta spangs nas gsol gdab byin rlabs 'jug /mang du thos pa'i mgon po klu sgrub de/ /rgya
mtshor klu rgyal gdan drangs smin grol mdzad/ /kha ba can 'dir klu sgrub rgya mtsho zhes/ /mkhas grub du mas lung bstan der phyag 'tshal/ /zhes pa 'di zhwa lu sku zhang chos
rjes rnam thar gyi gseb tu 'jug dgos zer bris pa'o/ /de ltar rtsom po rang nyid kyis zog dang rdzun dang hab 'gros spangs te legs par sbyar ba'o/ /rang gi lo rgyus gtam
gyi mu tig 'phreng / /snyan tshig dar gyi srad bu la brgyus te/ /dad ldan sbyin dang bu slob rgyan du 'bul/ /rab dang sa rab dga' ba 'thob gyur cig/ //sarba mangga laM//
